Nkpo okle kafɔɔ mimbuɛ ku kolesɛtũ bilɛ, ‘Alokonkyɛ lɛsɛɛ kayi lefuu nioso kanto manɔɔ.’ Minfuo mmle kaayi mate ni otofo nse bienyu osi.
Kafɔɔ biloofuo atuosaa ya ninkɔwa ni di obe wɔ mmle kamɛ kasɔ onu!
Aye miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle kpile, bitookple di Yaa nkpaamaa, biomiɛ bilɛ mbla dituosaa ntuo ye.
Oowo!
Bilabanya dituosaa kuniwii dilenkee Yona lele le okle.” Nkpo oso Yesu ladiɛ ma aasifi.
Yesu Lakpee Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Kufiofa Di Farisi Batii Ku Saduki Batii Asaa Otuo Suoto.
Obe wɔ di basaateketetɛ nwu lataalɛ lɛpanta nwu nkpo baalaadu ni kayɛ nyɔɔfa yi, ni baanyuma alɛ baayɔ bloblo kuonwii bakle nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu nwaa di Farisi batii ku Saduki batii kɔfa ko mankpee ni di nnaafũ kamɛ nintaka ni suoto.” Ninfɛ baakyako obuɛ kaamɛ lɛma alɛ, “Mmle munan-yɔ bloblo kuonwii bukle ni oso obuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle?” Yesu latofo ɔlaa wɔ baatoobuɛ nii, nioso aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be oso biobuɛ kaamɛ bilɛ biɛyɔ bloblo kuonwii bikle?
Ofũ onu lee lɛtɛ kuɔwa kasɔ lo!
Ni biifuo otofo?
Ni biloonyuma obe wɔ labɛbɛɛ bloblo akudi anɔɔ lasɛ ni batii nkpe nnɔɔ?
Nkyikyɛ nsɛ kɔkyɛɛ kɔkyɛɛ ko biasiisa ni layii?
Diɛkyakaa nii, bloblo akudi akuɛnsĩ ya layɔ lata ni basuɔtɔ nkpe nna mɔ?
Nkyikyɛ nsɛ biasiisa kɔkyɛɛ kɔkyɛɛ nwu biayiisa?
Ni be oso minoofuo otofo bilɛ diele bloblo suoto kɔkakatɛ nta ye nlɛ, ‘Bilolaa binyu nwaa di Farisi batii ku Saduki batii kɔfa ko mankpee ni di nnaafũ kamɛ nintaka ni suoto’?” Nfa nfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lanu kasɔ alɛ diele kɔfa ko mankpee ni di nnaafũ kamɛ nintaka ni suoto ɔɔkakatɛ anta ma.
Kafɔɔ di asaa ya di Farisi batii ku Saduki batii ntuo ni suoto alaka.
Petro Ladiki Aabuɛ Otii Wɔ Di Yesu Nwu Nkpo Nle Nii.
Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasifi ntɛɛ be niɛtɛɛtɛɛ ni Kaesarea Filipi okpoo.
Nfa aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Owe baatii kobuɛ alɛ ami, Otii Obi nwu, nle?” Ni baadiki kanya alɛ, “Bawo kobuɛ alɛ Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane.
Bawo kafɔɔ kobuɛ alɛ Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Elia fale.
Fiɛ baawo kafɔɔ kobuɛ alɛ Yeremia ee Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ bamba owo fale.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ni aye mɔ?
Owe biobuɛ bilɛ nle?” Ninfɛ di Simon Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Kristo nwu nkpo nɛ, Yaa wɔ ninkpe ni nkpa Obi.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Yaa ntoowii fɔ lɛyɔɔ, Simon, Yona obi.
Diekye diele otii kuonwii niediki nle mmle eetuo fɔ, kafɔɔ Teemi wɔ ninkpe ni di osi niediki eetuo fɔ.
Nkpo oso kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ afɔ ninle Petro di lɛsɔdiki ninle ni difuɔnkpaa.
Difuɔnkpaa le mmle suoto kamatofo bafũbanutɛ nii dikudi nɛ.
Bia kukpi osie dilɔbafuo ma olenkee.
Kamayɔ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ osie nta fɔ.
Lɛsaa lele feenii kaasɔ ka mmle suoto yi, Yaa kafɔɔ manii ni di osi.
Lɛsaa lele kafɔɔ feefukuti di kasɔ ka mmle suoto yi, Yaa kafɔɔ mafukuti ni di osi.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakpee basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kufiofa alɛ, “Bitantɔkɔ otii kuonwii bilɛ ami ninle Kristo nwu.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Aakyeko Dibuo Nɔɔ Ku Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Diayɔ ni di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yesu lakye kasɔ aatɔɔtɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo alɛ, “Dikpe ni lɛkyɛ Yerusalem lɛlaafe diibuo kpinwu kamɛ di okpoo banɔɔfo ku oleɔta banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Babalo mi, kafɔɔ dii tiɛfa Yaa masɛnkɛsɛɛ ankyeko bakpi kamɛ nsiɛ nkpa.” Ninfɛ di Petro lakpaa Yesu aasifiko ɔlɔɔkɔ aalaasĩ ɔlaa aatɔɔ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, Yaa ata nle mmle dikyɛ di okyo.
Diidii nle mmle dilabawafɔ di suoto!” Yesu lamunikĩi aatɔkɔ Petro alɛ, “Abonsam, kyɛ mi di ɔlɔɔkɔ fasifi!
Fale disukutĩisaa fɛɛtɛɛ, diekye disibu le fakle ni yi, diele Yaa nfũ diekye.
Otii disibu dile.” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Nse otii owo komiɛ alɛ awa abatikankoe, ni dikpe nii ansĩ suoto nɔɔ, an-yɔ aatoo nɔɔ, antikankoe.
Diekye otii lele nikomiɛ alɛ ata nkpa nɔɔ, abayu mi, kafɔɔ otii lele nieyu nkpa nɔɔ ta ami oso yi, nwaako abawɛ mi.
Obe nfasũ di otii mawɛ nse ɛɛwɛ kayi ka mmle asaa amuu eeyu nkpa nɔɔ?
Ee lɛsaa lewo nkpe di otii kafuo ni ɔyɔ ɔkyɛlɛnsa ofũ nkpa nɔɔ?
Diekye Otii Obi nwu nkpo kamawa di Ote lɛkpa kamɛ ku Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ, abata otii biala koto di nkpa nɔɔ be eesiɛ ni kanya.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, batii bawo nsi ye kaamɛ ninfũ, blɔwa ɔbakpi fiɛ babanya Otii Obi nwu nkpo kɔwa fɛ ɔka.”
Kakyi Kawo Lawa Di Yesu Suoto.
Ayi akuɔ sɛmaa, Yesu lakpaa Petro, Yakobo ku obilɛma suɔtɔbi Yohane baasifi kobokote takale kunwii osi.
Ni baalaasiɛ ninfa lete lɛma nɛ.
Di obe wɔ baasiɛ ni ninfa, baanya nii, Yesu letembi ntookyi.
Anu nɔɔ lakpa fɛle kufĩ, awu nɔɔ kafɔɔ lapu aatoosese di anu.
Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo batiɛ lanya Mose ku Elia bɔɔkakatɛko Yesu nɛ.
Nioso Petro latakatɛsa sɛlɔ katoo aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, diɛtɛ dilɛ alɛ buɔwa nfũ!
Nse feetuna yi, mapɛ akpanta atiɛ.
Alefɔ anwii, Mose ale anwii, Elia ale kafɔɔ anwii.” Di obe wɔ ayɛ ɔɔkakatɛ ni yi, dituntũ le niɛkpa ni lawa diabafukuti diatĩi ma di suoto.
Ni sɛɛlɔ ladie diituntũ nwu kamɛ siabuɛ alɛ, “Obi nii bɔmbɔtɛ ninle nwɔ mmle nɛ.
Nintuna nwɔ di suoto, oobuo mi anu nwaa.
Bikyɔɔ nwɔ atoko!” Di obe wɔ baasaateketetɛ batiɛ nwu nkpo lanu ni sɛlɔ se mmle yi, lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ ma osie kanya, ni baafuusa anu kaasɔ nɛ.
Ni di Yesu lakple aawa ɔkyɛ lɛma abakpanko ma aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitaka!
Bitanyɛkɛ!” Ninfɛ baatakatɛsa anu katoo nɛ, batasinya otii kuonwii dilenkee Yesu lete.
Di obe wɔ nfɛ boosoo mankye ni kobokote nwu nkpo suoto manwa nii, Yesu lakpee ma kufiofa alɛ, “Bitantɔkɔ otii kuonwii dituosaa le beediki beetuo ye ni ninfũ, diɛlaase di obe wɔ bɛɛtakatɛsa ni ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, beekyeko ni bakpi kamɛ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Ni obe oso di kufiofa batuotɛ labuɛ alɛ dikpe ni Elia lelekatũ ɛɛwa fiɛ di asaa ya mmle lɛwa kaanya?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako dile alɛ Elia lelekatũ ɛɛwa ɛɛba lololaa lɛsaa biala ɛɛtɛ.
Kafɔɔ kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ Elia ntɔɔwa kofokofoko, kafɔɔ batii diɛnyɔɔ batɛ nsũ, ni baabla nwɔ amumu fɛ mmle dilɛ ma ni nɛ.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ bababla Otii Obi nwu amumu nɛ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo latofo alɛ Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane suoto ɔɔkakatɛtɛ anta ma nɛ.
Yesu Latososa Ninwuna Kpile Ninwii Di Osuɔtɔbi Onwii Kamɛ.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasoo baabadu ni batii dikudi nwu nkpo nfũ yi, osuɔtɔ onwii lawa Yesu nfũ aabapɛ akunkyi kaatũ nɔɔ.
Ni aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, nya obi nii suɔtɔbi wɔ mmle nyaami.
Kakpibubu nsi nwɔ kɔɔnwɔtɔ nwɔ osie kanya.
Obe lele ɔɔnɔɔ ambuo di ntu ku ɔtɔ kamɛ.
Lɛkpaa nwɔ lɛwako basaateketetɛ lɛfɔ, kafɔɔ baafuo nwɔ ofiɛ ɔnyɔɔsa.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Aye miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle, be oso minoofũ mi binu, bikpe otokopĩ nkpo?
Ɔmɛmbe okle kakpee otu nnanfi ye nnaase?
Namasiɛ ye di ɔkyɛ obe lele!
Bikpaa obisɔ nwu nkpo biwakoe ninfũ!” Ninfɛ di Yesu lasĩ ɔlaa aata ninwuna kpile le niasiɛ ni di obisɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ, ninfɛ diadie nɛ.
Nfanwu ni di ofiɛ nwu nkpo layɔɔ nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lawa Yesu nfũ babakaalɛ nwɔ buɛɛ alɛ, “Be oso munanfuo ninwuna kpile nwu nkpo otososa odiki?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Diekye ofũ onu lee diɛpɔ.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse ofũ onu lee nte fɛ alesaa kubi biibii yɛntɛle yi, biafuo kobokote takale ko mmle ɔtɔkɔ bilɛ, ‘Taka ninfũ fasifi kamaa nwu falaayila!’ Kubasifi.
Lɛsalɛsaa kuninwii ɔbla dilaba lenkee ye!
Nse diele kanya onii ku ɔlaa ɔpɛ ɔta Yaa, bilaafuo ninwuna le mmle okle otososa odiki.” Yesu Lakple Aakakatɛ Di Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Di obe wɔ baasaateketetɛ nwu nkpo bamuu labasi ni di Galilea yi, Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Babayɔ Otii Obi nwu nkpo mankpee di batii nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Babalo nwɔ, kafɔɔ dii tiɛfa, Yaa makple ansɛnkɛsa nwɔ ankyeko bakpi kamɛ.” Nioso, basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo labuo nyaami.
Yesu Ku Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Lata Yaa Olekatakɔ Koto Ko Baatii Nta Nii.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lababuo ni Kapernaum, Yuda batii Olekatakɔ ato bafuntɛ labakaalɛ Petro alɛ, “Saatuotɛ lee kafɔɔ nta Olekatakɔ koto nwu nkpo?” Ninfɛ di Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Be Oso.
Anta!” Nkpo oso obe wɔ di Petro lakyɛ aalaabuo ni leyo, ni di Yesu lalekatũ aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Simon, lɛfɛɛnya?
Bawe dikpe ni bɛɛta akpooto ku kale ato bɛɛta kayi ka mmle baka?
Kale babi ɛɛ, sɛɛ bafɔɔ?” Ninfɛ di Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bafɔɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Dilɛ.
Nse dinaa alɛ kale babi kata fiɛ!
Kafɔɔ noomiɛ nlɛ buwolaa batii ba mmle kaanya, tɔɔkyɛ lekpo nwu nkpo kotoko falaataa dadiwa.
Kakpaku ka kasale fabadiki ni yi, nyu ka kanya kamɛ, fabanya koto kowo nimawo ni ami ku kole ye fanta ni Olekatakɔ nwu koto.
Diki koto nwu, faayɔ falaata koto ko busiko ma ni.”
Yesu Ladiki Otii Wɔ Ninlenke Ni Aatuo.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lawa Yesu nfũ babakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Owe ninle otii finle di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu lalɛɛ obisɔ biibii onwii aabayila ma di anu nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye ntikiti nlɛ, nse biekyisa letembi lee bite fɛ babisɔ yi, diidii, bilababuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo.
Otii wɔ niefũ kɔya alenke ni di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo ninle, otii wɔ niɛwakosa ni suoto kasɔ, eekyi eete fɛ obisɔ wɔ mmle okle.
“Otii wɔ nimafũ ni obisɔ biibii wɔ mmle okle di leyooto nii kamɛ yi, ami eefũ.
Tannanfi Otii Wo Lɛfɔ Faakpee Di Okpile Kamɛ.
“Nse Otii owo lɛta alɛ babisɔ ba mmle nwu nkpo onwii lɛma leyu ofũ onu nɔɔ kaamɛ nii, nse bɔɔyɔ kukuɔ dibinte beenii bɛɛsakasa nwɔ siimu beesoosa nwɔ beekpee di lekpo kakyofolekɔ ɛɛmɛ ntu eekpi yi, dibalɛ nwɔ ninlenkee.
“Kayi ka mmle batii bayɔɔsa di asaa ya nimata batii n-yu ni ofũ onu lɛma.
Asaa nwu nkpo nnya obe lele abawa.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ suoto abafe anwa nii, ayɔɔsa!
“Nkpo oso nse kɔnɛɛ lɛfɔ, ee kɔkpaa lɛfɔ mata alɛ fambla okpile yi, faabudi kũ fayu.
Dilɛ dilenke alɛ faayɔ kɔnɛɛ kunwii ee kɔkpaa kunwii fambuo di nkpa nwu kamɛ, alɛ faawɛ nnɛɛ nnyɔ ee nkpaa nnyɔ, man-yɔ fɔ manfuki mankpee di kawɔɔ ɔtɔ wɔ ninnaa ni kaloo kamɛ.
Nse kafɔɔ, ninu lɛfɔ nikɔta fɔ fambla okpile yi, faadiki ni fayu.
Diekye dilɛ dilenke alɛ, faayɔ ninu ninwii fambuo nkpa nwu nkpo kamɛ alɛ, faawɛ anu anyɔ man-yɔ fɔ manfuki mankpee di kawɔɔ ɔtɔ wɔ ninnaa ni kaloo kamɛ.
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Foso Wɔ Nieyu Ni Suoto.
“Bilolaa binyu nwaa bilɛ bienyu babisɔ wɛkyɛ wɛkyɛ ba mmle nwu nkpo bilɛ baadie lɛsalɛsa di anu lee.
Diekye nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye ntikiti nlɛ, bakpe Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ ba nin-yɛ ni di Teemi wɔ ninkpe ni di osi anu obe lele.
Diekye ami, Otii Obi nwu, lɛwa nlɛ kɔmadiki batii ba nieyu nii, nta ma nkpa.
“Lɛ biɛnya, nse otii nkpe bafoso kɔlafa di onwii leyu kaamɛ, ɔlabadiɛ afosi anaasĩ banaasĩ ba niebu ni koobokote osi batoole alesaa asifi alaawolaa onwii nwu nkpo nieyu ni?
Nwaako nse ɛɛnyɔɔ yi, abanya suoto lɛyɔɔ di onwii nwu nkpo suoto anlenkee afosi anaasĩ banaasĩ nwu nkpo niebu nii.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di Teeye wɔ ninkpe ni di osi yi, oloomiɛ alɛ babisɔ ba mmle wɛkyɛ wɛkyɛ onwii lɛma ayu nɛ.
Nya Osuku Wɔ Suoto Dikpe Ni Fɛɛkyɛ Ni Nse Ofũ Onutɛ Wo Lɛfɔ Lɛbla Fɔ Okpile.
“Nse ofũonutɛ wo lɛfɔ lɛbla fɔ okpile yi, kyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ falaadiki okpile wɔ ɛɛbla fɔ ni fatuo nwɔ.
Faata ɔlaa nwu kusiɛ di batii lee banyɔ ntɛɛ lete.
Nse eenu fɔ kasɔ yi, ni minko nwɔ kasiɛ ntookple kɛɛlɛ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nse aanu fɔ kasɔ yi, ni faamiɛ otii onwii ee banyɔ fakyakaa di suoto biɛkyɛ, baanuko fɔ ɔlaa nwu nkpo fɛle kamaa bayilatɛ, fɛ mmle okle bɛɛkpana ni Kɔɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ.
Nse mma kafɔɔ aanu ma kasɔ yi, ni faata ɔlaa nwu kudu bafũbanutɛ ba ninkpe ni kaasiisakɔ nwu nkpo.
Nse aanu kasiisakɔ nwu nkpo batii kafɔɔ kasɔ yi, ni faadiɛ nwɔ fɛle otii wɔ ninanfũ anu ni ee kpileblatɛ wɔ ninayikyisa ni nkpa.
Yesu Lata Bafũbanutɛ Nwu Nkpo Osie.
“Nkpo oso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, lɛsaa lele bienii kaasɔ ka mmle suoto, Yaa n-yɛ ye kamaa di osi.
Lɛsaa lele kafɔɔ biefukuti di kasɔ ka mmle suoto, Yaa n-yɛ ye kamaa di osi.
“Kokple ntɔkɔ ye kafɔɔ nlɛ, nse batii lee banyɔ biɛbla kanya kanwii lɛsaa lele suoto kaasɔ ka mmle, biɛkaalɛ, Teemi wɔ ninkpe ni di osi mabla anta ye.
Diekye kakɔ lele batii banyɔ ee batiɛ lɛbla onwii leeyooto nii kamɛ, nsi ma nintɛɛ.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Kpɛmblatɛ Onwii Wɔ Nintayɔ Owo Nɔɔ Okpile Aakyɛ Nwɔ Ni Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Petro lawa Yesu nfũ aabakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, nse owo nii kɔbla okpile di suoto nii, sɛsɛ kayɔ nkyɛ nwɔ?
Sikuɛnsĩ ɛɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Diele nkpo!
Kafɔɔ faayɔ fankyɛ nwɔ afosi akuɛnsĩ, sikuɛnsĩ.
“Nle mmle oso Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nte fɛ Ɔka wɔ ninkomiɛ alɛ ablako ni batii nɔɔ ba nikɔblako nwɔ ni ɔkpɛ nkuntaa.
Di obe wɔ aanya aakye ni kasɔ, ni baakpaa osuɔtɔ onwii ninsiko nwɔ ni koto kpinwu baawako ɔkyɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Di obe wɔ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo nnaa lɛsalɛsaa abayɔ anta ni koto nwu oso, Ɔka nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, bayɔ nnwɔɔ ku ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ ku babi ku lɛsaa biala ninkpe nwɔ basunsu bata koto nwu nkpo.
“Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lapɛ akunkyi di Ɔka nwu nkpo katũ aatikiti nwɔ lekoto osie kanya alɛ, ‘Wɛ otu fatɛɛ, mata koto nwu nkpo kumuu!’ Osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo ɔlaa lakpɛ Ɔka nwu nkpo nyaami, nkpo oso aayɔ koto nwu nkpo aakyɛ nwɔ, aadiɛ nwɔ aasifi.
“Di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle ladie aasifi nii, ni aakyɛ aalaakyakako kpɛntɛ wo nɔɔ wɔ ninsiko nwɔ ni koto kafuii nɛ.
Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lamufũ kpɛntɛ wo nɔɔ nwu nkpo siimu osie kanya aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Tɛɛ koto nii ko kumuu fasikoe ni!’ “Ninfɛ di kpɛntɛ wo nɔɔ nwu nkpo latikiti nwɔ lekoto aatɔkɔ alɛ, ‘Wɛ otu fatɛɛ, mata fɔ koto nwu nkpo komuu!’ “Kafɔɔ aasĩ, ni aata baakpaa kpɛntɛ wo nɔɔ nwu nkpo baalaatɛ leeyo alɛ diediki ɛɛta koto nwu nkpo kumuu fiɛ baadiɛ nwɔ.
Nkpo oso, obe wɔ di bakpɛntɛ bamba lanya ni lɛsaa le di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo labla nii, suoto ditayɔɔ ma ni baasifi baalaatɔkɔ Ɔka nwu nkpo lɛsaa le di osuɔtɔ nwu labla ni fɛɛ nɛ.
“Nkpo oso Ɔka nwu nkpo lakpee baalaalɛɛ osuɔtɔ nwu baawako nwɔ ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Otii kpile fale.
Di obe wɔ faatikiti mi ni lekoto, layɔ koto ko kumuu fasikoe nii lɛkyɛ fɔ.
Nse nkpo okle dikpe ni afɔɔ fan-yɔ fankyɛ kpɛntɛ wo lɛfɔ nwu fɛ mmle okle lanya fɔ ni nyaami nɛ.’ Nni nkpo oso ɔblɔ lafiɛ Ɔka nwu nkpo osie kanya, ni aata alɛ bakpaa osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo balaatɛ leeyo, baananfi nwɔ kootoko dilaase di obe wɔ ɛɛta ni koto nwu nkpo kumuu.” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɛntɛ ɔlaa nwu alɛ, “Nkpo okle di Teemi wɔ ninkpe ni di osi mabla aye ba ninan-yɔ bikyɛ ni bafũbanutɛ wo lee di situ lee kamɛ nɛ.”
Yesu Latuo Asaa Aakyeko Sɛsa Ku Sɛsɔfɔ Osĩ Suoto.
Obe wɔ di Yesu labuɛ sɛlaa se mmle simuu aaloo nii, ninfɛ aadie di Galilea aasifi Yudea ntɛɛ nwu di Yordan okle sɛmaa nɛ.
Ni baatii dikudi ninwii kpinwu latikanko nwɔ nɛ, ni aayɔɔsa bamuu lɛma sifiɛ ninfa nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Farisi batii bawo lawa nwɔ ɔkyɛ baabawolaa nwɔ kaanya nɛ.
Ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Mose kufiofa lɛta osuku alɛ osuɔtɔ kafuo ɔsɔfɔ osĩ di lɛsaa lele suoto?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Biika di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, kaasɔ kakyekɔ osuɔtɔ ku ɔsanko di Yaa labla?
Ninfɛ di Yaa labuɛ alɛ, ‘Nle mmle oso, osuɔtɔ madie di ote ku ɔya suoto ansifi manko ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ manaabla onwii, banyɔ lɛma mankple suoto sina sinwii.’ Nle mmle oso, baasinle batii banyɔ, kɔfɔɔ otii onwii nfɛ bale.
Nkpo oso, dinaa alɛ otii lɛblasa lɛsaa le di Yaa ntoomufũ ɛɛbla ninwii.” Ninfɛ di Farisi batii nwu nkpo lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni be oso di Mose lata osuku alɛ, osuɔtɔ kafuo ɔsɔfɔ kusinkũ ɔta ansĩ nwɔ antɔɔ ansifi?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Mose lata ye osuku alɛ biasĩ ɔsanko ta otokopĩ lee oso.
Kafɔɔ kaasɔ kayekɔ di Yaa labla ni kayi yi, ditate nkpo.
Kafɔɔ nunua kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse osuɔtɔ owo lesĩ ɔsɔfɔ ninanle asɔnɔ eekpee, eekple ɛɛlaayɔ ɔsanko bamba, atookpee asɔnɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu basaateketetɛ latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse nkpo dite di ɔsa ku ɔsɔfɔ ntɛɛ, ni diɛlɛ alɛ, baayɔ bawo.” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Diele otii lele nimafuo asaa otuo ya mmle ofũ, diediki otii wɔ di Yaa lɛyɔ ɛɛta ni lete.
Diekye lɛsaa le oso di basuɔtɔ bawo nle ni balɛma nkpe ate ate.
Bawo yi, nkpo bɛɛtɛ beelofo ma nɛ.
Bawo kafɔɔ yi, batii niɛbla nkpo.
Fiɛ baawo kafɔɔ mma bamu niɛbla suoto balɛma, ta Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɔkpɛ nwu oso.
Otii wɔ nimafuo ni nle mmle ɔbla yi, aabla.” Batii Lakpaa Babisɔ Baawako Yesu Nfũ Aawii Ma Lɛyɔɔ.
Batii bawo lakpaa babisɔ baawako Yesu Nfũ alɛ atika ma nnɛɛ di suoto aapɛ ɔlaa ata Yaa diisi lɛma.
Kafɔɔ basaateketetɛ lasĩ ɔlaa baata batii nwu nkpo.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo alɛ, “Bita babisɔ bawa ɔkyɛ nii, bitantũi ma osuku.
Diekye batii fɛ babisɔ ba mmle okle kale ninle Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo.” Yesu layɔ kɔnɛɛ aatika ma di suoto aapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa diisi lɛma, nni kamaa, ni aasifi aadiɛ ma nɛ.
Dibawɛ Osie Ninta Basaawɛntɛ Fiɛ Bababuo Yaa Sɛka Kalekɔ Nwu Nkpo.
Dii ninwii osuɔtɔ onwii lawa Yesu ɔkyɛ aabakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, lɛmɛnsaa biene kabla fiɛ di Yaa katɛɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ.
“Be oso fɔɔkaalɛ mi ɔlaa fankyeko lɛsaa biene ɔbla suoto?
Yaa lete ninle otii biene.
Nse foomiɛ falɛ fawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo yi, ni faale afiofa nɔɔ nwu nkpo.” Ni di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔmɛnfiofa?” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tanlo otii, tankpee asɔnɔ, tan-yu, tanyila sɛlaa kuafunu kamaa, bu teefɔ ku yaafɔ, bɔmbɔ owo lɛfɔ, fɛ mmle okle fambɔmbɔ ni suoto lɛfɔ.” Ninfɛ di okosopo nwu nkpo latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Ntoole afiofa ya mmle amuu.
Lɛsaa lewo lebu kakple mbla ni?” Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse foomiɛ falɛ fawo nimu yi, tɔɔkyɛ flaayɔ asaa ya amuu ninkpe fɔ ni fasunsũ, faayɔ koto nwu nkpo fata bapiitɛ, ni fabakple saawɛntɛ di Yaa kafa.
Nni kamaa, faawa fabatikankoe.” Obe wɔ di okosopo nwu nkpo lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle yi, suoto ditayɔɔ nwɔ, ni aasifi nɛ.
Diekye saawɛntɛ aale osie kanya.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, dibawɛ osie fiɛ di basaawɛntɛ makyɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo.
Kokple nse ye lɛtɔkɔ kafɔɔ nlɛ, diɛtɛ diɛyɔɔ diɛta kapupɔnkɔ alɛ aafe di paniɛ dituɛ kamɛ, dilenke alɛ saawɛntɛ kabuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo.” Di obe wɔ baasaateketetɛ lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle diatɛ diabla ma ɔkpɛ.
Nkpo oso baakaalɛ alɛ, “Ni se nkpo kute mɔ, owe nfɛ babata nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu layu ma di anu tuwĩi aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii kuonwii dilabafuo nle mmle ɔbla.
Kafɔɔ Yaa nnwɔɔ lɛsalɛsaa nnaa nwɔ osie ku ɔbla.” Ninfɛ di Petro lakakatɛ aabuɛ alɛ, “Nyu lo!
Buodiɛ lɛsaa loo biala buɔtɛ butikanko fɔ.
Ni be bubawɛ?” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse Otii Obi nwu nkpo lɛbasiɛ di lɛkakpomii nɔɔ suoto, leeklekle kamɛ, di kayi fɔle ka nikɔwa ni kamɛ, aye lefosi batii banyɔ ba nintikankoe nii, ayee bibasiɛ di akakpomii suoto minkanko Israel batii, lefosi nfaabi nnyɔ nwu nkpo.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niediɛ ayo ee babilɛma suɔtɔbi ee babilɛma sankobi ee ote ee ɔya ee babi ee afe ɛɛtɛ ta ami oso, abawɛ nya akyuu kɔlafa anlenkeesa bia.
Yaa matɔɔ kafɔɔ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Kafɔɔ batii ba kpinwu ninle ni batunletɛ, makple bamaakpitɛ.
Bamaakpitɛ kafɔɔ makple batunletɛ.
Bakpɛmblatɛ Labla Ɔkpɛ Di Dii Kɔkpɛnto Kanya.
“Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nte fɛ nle mmle okle.
Obe onwii kamɛ, osuɔtɔ onwii lataka ku kolesɛtũ alɛ, ɔlaamiɛ batii bawo manaabla dii kufĩ ɔkpɛ di awosobi ya mambla ni nta kofe mantɔɔ.
Kofe saate nwu nkpo ku bakpɛntɛ nwu lale ɔkpɛ nwu kɔya.
Lɛsɔnu lawa diatɔɔ alɛ abata ma dii kɔkpɛnto koto fututu kunwii.
Ni aakpaa ma aasifiko kofe nwu nkpo nɛ.
“Di obe wɔ diapɛ ni abombo anaasĩ, osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lakple aadie aakyɛ lɛkpaka, aalaanya basuɔtɔ bawo n-yɛ ninfa blɔbla lɛsalɛsaa.
Nkpo oso, aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Aye kafɔɔ bitɔɔkyɛ kofe nii bilaabla ɔkpɛ, mata ye koto ko niesiɛko ni ɔkpɛ nwu.’ Nkpo oso baasifi kofe nwu nkpo.
“Aakple aadie aakyɛ lɛkpaka di abombo lefosi anyɔ ku abombo atiɛ kamɛ aalaabla nkpo kafɔɔ.
Ditoobu kɛkɛɛ di abombo anɔɔ kapɛ nii, aakple aadie aakyɛ lɛkpaka, ni aalaanya basuɔtɔ bamba bawo n-yɛ ninfa.
Ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, ‘Be niɛwa fiɛ biɛlalaasa dii kufĩ kumu minambla ɔkpɛ kuonwii?’ “Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Otii kuonwii diɛwa abayɔ wo alɛ bubabla ɔkpɛ.’ “Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Ni bitɔɔkyɛ kofe nii biɛlaabla ɔkpɛ.’ “Obe wɔ kɔɔtɔɔfɔ lawo nii, ni koofe nwu nkpo saate latɔkɔ kofe nwu nyuntɛ alɛ, ‘Lɛɛ bakpɛntɛ nwu nkpo faata ma koto lɛma.
Kyekasɔ di mba niɛnyɛntɛ ni ɔwa falaase di bakasale suoto.’ “Ninfɛ aayɔ koto fututu ninle ni dii kɔkpɛnto kunwii kunwii aata batii ba niawa ni kɔtɔɔfɔ abombo anɔɔ kamɛ nɛ.
Nioso obe wɔ diadu ni batii ba niasifi ni kofe nwu nkpo ku olesɛ yi, baanyu alɛ babafũ koto manlenkee bawo lɛma.
Kafɔɔ mma kafɔɔ koto nwu nkpo fututu kunwii kunwii baafũ nɛ.
Di obe wɔ baafũ ni koto nwu nkpo yi, baakyako ɔkakatɛ di kofe nwu nkpo saate suoto alɛ, ‘Batii ba mmle niɛwa ni kofe lɛyɛntɛle, lebombo ninwii lete bɛɛbla ɔkpɛ.
Awo ba niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ dii nimu, kuufĩ lɛpɛ wo nii, koto nwu kunwii fɛɛta wo!’ “Ninfɛ di kofe nwu nkpo saate latɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Basiɛwo, binu kasɔ, nintafaa ye!
Munko ye niele ɔkpɛ kɔya bienu suoto kasɔ bilɛ, bibafũ dii kɔkpɛnto ninle koto fututu kunwii.
Nkpo oso yi, bifũ koto lee biɛtɔɔkyɛ leyo.
Ami omu ninlɛ kɔta batii yɛntɛle ba mmle koto okle lɛta ye nii.
Nkpe osuku mblako koto nii ɔkpɛ mmle okle dilɛ mi nii.
Nkpo oso yi, bitanta ɔblɔ lafiɛ ye di sifutulɛ nii se lɛbla ni suoto.’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɛntɛ alɛ, “Nioso batii yɛntɛle mawa mamale bakasale, bakasale kafɔɔ mawa mamale bayɛntɛle.” Yesu Lakple Aabuɛ Kukpi Nɔɔ Ɔlaa Dii Tiɛfa.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoofe ni Yerusalem, aalɛɛ ma di ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ.
“Binu lo!
Buofe Yerusalem, nfa babayɔ ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo mankpee di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Babalo nwɔ kukpi lɛpɔɔ.
Babayɔ nwɔ mankpee di batii ba ninanle ni Yuda batii nnɛɛ kamɛ, babama nwɔ, babapɛ nwɔ, mampɛ nwɔ sibuɛ mankaasa di kowoso suoto.
Kafɔɔ di dii tiɛfa suoto, Yaa masɛnkɛsa nwɔ aakyeko bakpi kamɛ, ansiɛ nkpa.” Yakobo Ku Yohane Ɔya Lakaalɛ Yesu Alɛ Akyakaako Babi Nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Sebedeo ɔsɔfɔ lakpaa babi nɔɔ suɔtɔbi banyɔ aawako Yesu nfũ, abapɛ akunkyi kaatũ nɔɔ aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, akyakaako ma.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be lɛsaa foomiɛ?” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Komiɛ nlɛ, fabla fatɛɛ alɛ, nse fɛɛwa sɛka lɛfɔ ole yi, babi nii ba mmle banyɔ yi, onwii masiɛ di oletannɛɛ kyɛ lɛfɔ, onwii kafɔɔ masiɛ di kɔmɛntunnɛɛ kyɛ lɛfɔ.” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bieye lɛsaa le biɔkaalɛ nii.
Bibafuo dibuo le kamanya ni ɔnya?” Ninfɛ baadiki kanya alɛ, “Yii, bubafuo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako, bibafuo.
Kafɔɔ nnaa osuku ndiki otii wɔ nimasiɛ ni di oletannɛɛ kyɛ nii ku kɔmɛntu nnɛɛ kyɛ nii.
Nsiɛkɔ be mmle nwu nkpo yi, dile batii ba nle di Teemi lelolaa ɛɛtɛ ɛɛta nii.” Di obe wɔ di basaateketetɛ lefosi bule lanu ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo yi, ɔblɔ lafiɛ ma osie kanya di basuɔtɔbi nwu nkpo banyɔ ninle ni bawo babilɛma suoto.
Nkpo oso Yesu lalɛɛ ma aasiisa ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biye bilɛ batunletɛ ba nikole ni sɛka di batii ba ninanfũ banu nii, bakpe osie di suoto lɛma mantuo suoto mankpee ma.
Bitanta diate nkpo okle di kamɛ lee.
Nse onwii lee komiɛ alɛ ale ɔnɔɔfo kaamɛ lee yi, ni dikpe ni eele kpɛmblatɛ ɛɛta babule.
Nse onwii lee kafɔɔ komiɛ alɛ ale ɔkasale yi, ni dikpe ni ɛɛbla suoto fɛ obisɔ ɛɛta babule.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di Otii Obi nwu nkpo diɛwa alɛ batii katɔɔbla sɛkpɛ mantɔɔtɔɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nnwɔɔ ɛɛwa alɛ ɔɔbla sɛkpɛ anta batii alɛ aayɔ nkpa nɔɔ kafɔɔ antɛ kaasɔ andiki batii kpi.” Yesu Latikiti Banumbiɛtɛ Banyɔ Banwii Anu.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ladie di Yeriko baatoosifi nii, batii dikudi kpinwu latikanko ma.
Basuɔtɔ banyɔ banwii di anu labiɛ ma ni lasiɛ di osukulɔɔkɔ, ni baanu alɛ Yesu kɔwaalɛ anfe.
Ni baakyako ɔfaa osie kanya baabuɛ alɛ, “Ɔka Dawid Obi ee!
Nya wo nyaami!” Batii dikudi nwu nkpo lasĩ ɔlaa baata banumbiɛtɛ nwu nkpo osie kanya alɛ bamaasa kanya.
Kafɔɔ mia nwu nfɛ baatɛ baafaa osie kanya baabuɛ alɛ, “Saate loo!
Ɔka Dawid Obi ee!
Nya wo nyaami kyu woo!” Yesu layila ni aalɛɛ ma aawako ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be biomiɛ bilɛ mbla nta ye?” Ninfɛ baadiki kanya baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, buomiɛ bulɛ fata wo butɔɔnya.” Ɔlaa lɛma lakpɛ Yesu nyaami, ni aakpanko ma anu nɛ.
Nfanwu ni baakyako ɔnya nɛ.
Ninfɛ baatikanko Yesu nɛ.
Yesu Labuo Yerusalem Fɛle Ɔka Ku Suoto Lɛyɔɔ.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kɔtɛtɛɛ ni Yerusalem, babadu ni Betfage di Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote ɔlɔɔkɔ yi, Yesu lakpee basaateketetɛ nɔɔ banyɔ alɛ balekatũ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ kakpaayotũ ka ninte ye ni siitũ kamɛ, bibanya bɔkɛɛ wɔ ninte ni fɛ pɔnkɔ antuka ni aatoo beekpee nwɔ okũ, diibi kafɔɔ n-yɛ nwɔ ni di ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Bidiki nwɔ di okũ biɛkpaa ma biwakoe.
Nse otii owo lɛkaalɛ ye ɔlaa owo yi, biɛtɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ, ‘Saate nwu nikomiɛ ma.’ Abakplesa ma kafɔɔ anwako ye nunua.” Nle mmle lawa kaanya fɛ mmle okle di Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ onwii labuɛ aatɛ ni alɛ, “Bitɔkɔ Sion batii bilɛ, ‘Binyu!
Ɔka lee kɔwa ɔkyɛ lee.
Ɛɛwakosa suoto kasɔ asi di bɔkɛɛ wɔ nintuka ni atoo ku dibi suoto ɔɔwa.’ ” Nkpo oso basaateketetɛ banyɔ nwu nkpo, lakyɛ baalaabla fɛ mmle okle di Yesu lakpee ma alɛ balaabla nii.
Ni baakyɛ baalaakpaa bɔkɛɛ wɔ nintuka ni atoo ku dibi nwu nkpo baawako nwɔ nɛ.
Ni baablɛfɛsa abula lɛma baatika di suoto lɛma, ni di Yesu layie aasiɛ ma di suoto nɛ.
Ni baatii kpinwu di batii dikudi nwu nkpo kamɛ latɔtaa siwidi baadiki abula lɛma baatɛ di osuku suoto.
Ni baawo kafɔɔ labudi sɛkaafɛ baatɛ di osuku suoto nɛ.
Ninfɛ di batii dikudi le niale Yesu katũ ku mba niakpi ni sɛmaa latɔɔtaa siwidi alɛ, “Bitansa Ɔka Dawid Obi nwu!
Yaa lekusɛkusɛsa otii wɔ nikɔwa ni di Saate leyooto kamɛ!
Bitansa Yaa!” Di obe wɔ di Yesu labuo ni Yerusalem, kudu niamu di okpoo omuu.
Ni baatii latɔɔkaalɛ alɛ, “Owe dile?” Ninfɛ di batii dikudi nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, “Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yesu wɔ niekye ni Nasaret di Galilea kasɔ suoto dile!” Yesu Latososa Asaa Basunsutɛ Aadiki Di Yaa Olekatakɔ Kamɛ.
Yesu lakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ ni aalaatososa batii ba bamuu niatoosunsu ni asaa ku mba niatɔɔya ni asaa ninfa odiki leeyo nwu kamɛ nɛ.
Aatutukusa koto babiɛtɛ siipunu aayu.
Aatukusa mba ninsi boosunsu ni ablonuma kafɔɔ akpomii aayu.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bɛɛkpana di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, ‘Baalɛɛ mi leyo alɛ ɔlaa ɔpɛ katakɔ.’ Kafɔɔ aye, bitɔɔyɔ biɛbla bayu kawofakɔ!” Ninfɛ di batii bawo lakpaa banumbiɛtɛ ku abafa baawako nwɔ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo nɛ.
Ni di Yesu layɔɔsa ma sifiɛ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ lanya sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ aabla nii ku mmle okle di babisɔ latɔɔfaa batoobuɛ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu kamɛ alɛ, “Bitansa Ɔka Dawid Obi nwu nkpo” yi, ɔblɔ lafiɛ ma osie kanya.
Nkpo oso baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Foonu ɔlaa wɔ baabisɔ nwu nkpo kobuɛ ni?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Lenu.
N-ye kafɔɔ nlɛ bitɔɔka di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, ‘Fɛɛbla babisɔ ku babifɔɔle alɛ baayɔ katansa ka niewo ni niimu manta fɔ.’ ” Di nni nkpo kamaa, Yesu ladiɛ olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nwu nkpo ku kufiofa batuotɛ aadie di okpoo, aasifi Betania, aalaate nfa.
Yesu Lakpaani Kole Woso Kunwii.
Obe wɔ kaale ntɔɔsɛ nii, di Yesu ntɔɔpɛ ankple ansifi ni okpoo ku kuolesɛtũ yi, kɔka laklee nwɔ.
Ni aanya kolewoso kunwii di osukulɔɔkɔ nɛ, ni aakyɛ kũ ɔlɔɔkɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ atanya lɛwosobi kuninwii, dilenkee afata lete.
Nkpo oso aatɔkɔ kowoso nwu nkpo alɛ, “Diɛyɔ di miɛ diesifi nii, flabasintika abi diidii.” Nfanwu, kolewoso nwu nkpo niayɔɔ.
Obe wɔ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lanya ni nle mmle, diabla ma ɔkpɛ osie kanya.
Ni baakaalɛ alɛ, “Lɛ diɛbla fiɛ koolewoso ko mmle lefuo ɔyɔɔ nkpo wla?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse biefũ bienu siitu lee kamɛ, minanta dibla ye ɔtanfũ onu, bibafuo lɛsaa le lɛbla ni kolewoso ko mmle ɔbla.
Diele bia nle mmle lete, kafɔɔ, bibafuo kobokote ko mmle ɔtɔkɔ bilɛ, ‘Taka ninfũ falaabuo di lekpo kamɛ,’ dibawa kaanya.
Lɛsaa lele biɛpɛ ɔlaa biɛkaalɛ Yaa di ofũ onu kamɛ, bibafũ.” Baakaalɛ Yesu Nfũ Ɛɛwɛ Osuku Fiɛ Ɛɛbla Ni Asaa Nwu Nkpo Okle.
Yesu lakple aakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo.
Di obe wɔ ootuo ni asaa, ni di Yaa olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo lawa nwɔ ɔkyɛ babakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔmɛnsuku fakpe fɔɔbla asaa ya mmle?
Owe kafɔɔ niɛta fɔ osuku nwu nkpo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bitɛɛ nkaalɛ ye ɔlaa onwii, nse biediki kanya yi, ni amii matɔkɔ ye osuku wɔ nkpe fiɛ kɔbla ni asaa ya mmle nwu nkpo.
Ɔfɛ di Yohane lawɛ osuku fiɛ aatookpeesa batii Yaa ntu?
Yaa nfũ kuakye ɛɛ, sɛɛ batii nfũ kuakye?” Ninfɛ baamumufũ ɔlaa nwu nimanima baanyu alɛ, “Be nfɛ buabuɛ?
Nse buobuɛ bulɛ Yaa nfũ kuokye yi, abakaalɛ wo alɛ, ‘Ni be oso bitafũ Yohane bianu mɔ?’ Kafɔɔ nse buobuɛ bulɛ ‘otii nfũ kuokye’ yi, buɔyɛkɛ bulɛ batii ba mmle mabla wo lɛsaa, diekye bamuu lɛma beefũ beenu alɛ Yohane yi, Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ aale.” Nioso baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Buoye.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di amii, namatɔkɔ ye otii wɔ niɛtɛɛ ni osuku fiɛ kɔbla ni asaa ya mmle nɛ.
Yesu Latuo Asaa Aakyeko Basɔtɔbi Banyɔ Banwii Niale Ni Bawo Babilɛma Suoto.
“Bibu ɔlaa wɔ mmle disi binyu.
Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ babi suɔtɔbi banyɔ banwii.
Ni aakyɛ aalaatɔkɔ ɔnɔɔfo le alɛ, ‘Obi, kyɛ falaabla ɔkpɛ koofe nii miɛ.’ “Ninfɛ di obi nwu nkpo latɔkɔ ote alɛ, ‘Namafuo ɔkyɛ.’ Kafɔɔ sɛmaa, aakyɛlɛnsa disibu nɔɔ, ni aakyɛ nɛ.
“Ninfɛ di ote nwu nkpo lakyɛ obi nyɔɔfa nfũ, aalaatɔkɔ nwɔ ɔlaa nwu nkpo okle kafɔɔ.
Ni aatuna alɛ, ‘Teete lenu, makyɛ.’ Kafɔɔ atakyɛ.
“Di babi ba mmle banyɔ kamɛ, owe niabla ote dibiesaa?” Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Obi nɔɔfo le nwu nkpo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, akpooto bafuntɛ ku basɔnɔkpeetɛ makaye Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo obuo.
Diekye Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane lawa abatuo ye osuku biene wɔ suoto biafe nii, kafɔɔ bitafũ nwɔ bianu.
Kafɔɔ akpooto bafuntɛ ku basɔnɔkpeetɛ lafũ nwɔ baanu.
Kuntɛ bianya nle mmle, bíekyisa disibu lee bifũ nwɔ binu.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Aakyeko Kofe Nyuntɛ Kpile Onwii Suoto.
Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bikple binu lɛkpa bamba.
Fekpɛntɛ onwii lakpɛ awosobi ya man-yɔ mambla ni nta kofe, ni aakpee kɔba aakyisa kofe nwu nkpo nɛ.
Aabla lɛba le manka ni awosobi nwu nkpo mandiki ni nta.
Aatofo lɛba le niataka ni kle, baayila mantoonyu ni kofe nwu.
Ninfɛ aayɔ kofe nwu nkpo aakpee di bakpɛntɛ banwii nnɛɛ kamɛ alɛ batoonyu, ni aadie aasifi osuku nɛ.
Di obe wɔ di awosobi nwu nkpo ɔtɛsɛbee lawo nii, kofe saate nwu nkpo lakpee bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ alɛ bakyɛ kofe nwu banyuntɛ nfũ baalaafũ kalekɔ nɔɔ bawako nwɔ.
“Kofe nwu nkpo banyuntɛ lamufũ bakpɛmblatɛ ba mmle, baapɛ onwii, baalo onwii, baasafɔ onwii kafɔɔ afuɔ.
Nni sɛmaa kofe nwu nkpo saate lakple aakpee bakpɛmblatɛ bamba niapɔ baalenkee ni bakasale.
Kafɔɔ kofe nwu nkpo banyuntɛ lakple baabla mankpo kafɔɔ laakpa nwu.
Lɛyɛntɛle, aakpee ma nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ obi, aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Lefũ lenu nlɛ babata obi nii nwu dibu.’ “Kafɔɔ obe wɔ di kofe nwu nkpo banyuntɛ lanya ni obi nɔɔ nwu nkpo yi, ni baatɔkɔ bawo alɛ, ‘Nnya kofe saate obi wɔ nimale ni atesaa ninle nwɔ mmle nɛ.
Biwa biɛta bulo nwɔ di atesaa nɔɔ nwu nkpo akple wo ale.’ Nioso baamufũ nwɔ baafuki baayu di kɔba nwu nkpo sɛmaa, ni baalo nwɔ nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ni, nse kofe nwu nkpo saate lɛwa mɔ, be bienyu bilɛ ababla kofe nwu nkpo banyuntɛ?” Ninfɛ baadiki nwɔ kanya alɛ, “Abalo kofe banyuntɛ kpile nwu nkpo an-yɔ kofe nwu ankpee di bayuntɛ bamba nnɛɛ kamɛ, mba nimatɔɔ ni kalekɔ nɔɔ di nta awosobi nwu nkpo ɔtɛsɛbee kamɛ di obe kanya.” Ni di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Biika di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ binya?
Beebuɛ alɛ, ‘Difuɔ le baayotofotɛ lesĩ alɛ diɛlɛ nii, nni nintɔbakple difuɔ le niefĩ dilenke ni nɛ.
Saate niɛbla lɛsaa kplɛ le mmle.
Nioso diɛbla wo ɔkpɛ osie kanya!’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nkpo oso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Yaa maklee sɛka kalekɔ nɔɔ nwu nkpo anfũ ye di nnɛɛ kamɛ, an-yɔ anta batii ba nimabla nwɔ ni dibiesaa.
Otii lele niɛnɔɔ ɛɛpɛ diifuɔ le mmle suoto mafefee kukuii kukuii.
Kafɔɔ nse difuɔ nwu nkpo lɛkpa diɛpɛ di otii owo suoto yi, abakuɔ muɛmuɛ.” Nioso di Olekatakɔ banɔɔfo ku Farisi batii lanu ni Yesu akpa ya mmle yi, baatofo alɛ mma alaka.
Nkpo oso baamiɛ alɛ boomufũ nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ baayɛkɛ batii dikudi nwu nkpo, diekye batii kpinwu lafũ Yesu fɛle Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ.
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Ɔsanko Ɔyɔ Dii Ole Suoto.
Yesu lakple aatuo ma asaa di akpa kamɛ aabuɛ alɛ, Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nte fɛ nle mmle.
Di obe onwii kamɛ, ɔka onwii lale ɔsanko ɔyɔ dii aata obi suɔtɔbi nɔɔ.
Ni aakpee bakpɛmbla nɔɔ alɛ bakyɛ baalaalɛɛ batii ba ɛɛkyaka ni di ɔsanko ɔyɔ nwu nkpo dii kalekɔ bawako.
Kafɔɔ baasĩ alɛ bɔlɔɔwa.
“Nkpo oso aakple aakpee bakpɛmblatɛ bamba alɛ balaatɔkɔ batii nwu nkpo alɛ, ‘Dii ole alesaa nwu ntoobe, lelo nankyue suɔtɔ ku obiibii wɔ ninsi ni lɛla, lɛsaa biala ntoosi.
Biwa ɔsanko ɔyɔ dii nwu kalekɔ.’ “Kafɔɔ batii ba baakyakako ni nkpo, kuonwii lɛma ditakyɔɔ lɛlɛɛ nwu kotoko, baasifi sɛkpɛ lɛma mmɛ.
Onwii lasifi kofe, onwii kafɔɔ lasifi asaa kasunsukɔ.
Bawo kafɔɔ lamufũ bakpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo, baapɛ ma, ni baalo ma nɛ.
Ɔblɔ lafiɛ ɔka nwu nkpo osie kanya ni aakyesee bakpɛtɛ nɔɔ baakyɛ baalaalo batii lotɛ nwu nkpo bamuu, ni baakpee okpoo lɛma nwu nkpo ɔtɔ baawɔɔsa nwu nɛ.
“Ninfɛ aalɛɛ bakpɛntɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Obi nii ɔsanko ɔyɔ alesaa nwu nkpo ntoosi, kafɔɔ batii ba lɛkyakako ni diesiɛko dii nwu nkpo kalekɔ.
Nkpo oso nunua yi, bitɔɔkyɛ akpaka biɛlaalɛɛ batii lele biɛnya bilɛ bawa ɔsanko ɔyɔ dii kalekɔ nwu.’ Nioso bakpɛntɛ nwu nkpo ladie baasifi akpaka baalaalɛɛ batii ba bamuu baanya nii, babienetɛ ku bakpiletɛ baawako.
Nioso ɔsanko kayɔkɔ nwu nkpo layii pɔ ku batii.
“Ni di ɔka nwu nkpo lawa alɛ ɔɔbaanyu batii ba bɛɛkyakako bɛɛwako ni nfa, ni aanya osuɔtɔ onwii diekpee ɔsanko ɔyɔ awo.
Ni di Ɔka nwu nkpo lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Siɛwo, lɛyiɛbla fiɛ fɛɛwa nfũ fanankpee ɔsanko ɔyɔ awo?’ Kafɔɔ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo ditafuo kanya odiki.
“Ninfɛ di ɔka nwu nkpo latɔkɔ bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ alɛ, ‘Binii nwɔ nnɛɛ ku nkpaa biefuki nwɔ biyu kaayi diitunu nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Nfũ kaaku owi ku anyɛɛ owee nkpe ni.’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɛntɛ ku lɛkpa le mmle alɛ, “Yaa lɛlɛɛ batii kpi, kafɔɔ, basɛɛ eediki kaamɛ.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Di Akpooto Ɔta Suoto.
Farisi batii bawo lakyɛ baalaabla disibu mmle okle baayɔ Yesu omu kanya kamɛ ɔlaa manwɛ nwɔ nii.
Nkpo oso baakpee basaateketetɛ lɛma bawo ku batii ba nintikanko ni Herode baakyɛ Yesu nfũ.
Obe wɔ baakyɛ ni ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buye bulɛ nwaakotɛ falɛ, fantuo kafɔɔ Yaa ɔlaa nwu ninle ni nwaako ɔlaa, diekye fánnyu batii di anu faabla lɛsaa.
Faayɔ nwu ole di batii sɛlaa se mambuɛ ni kafɔɔ.
Nkpo oso, tɔkɔ wo disibu lɛfɔ.
Kufiofa loo lɛta osuku alɛ buata akpooto munta Roma batii Ɔka Nɔɔfo ɛɛ, sɛɛ dinaa alɛ buɔta?” Kafɔɔ Yesu latofo disibu kpile le bakle ni di suoto nɔɔ, nioso aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Be oso biɛwa biowolaa mi kaanya?
Bitɛɛ koto ko min-yɔ mintɔɔta ni akpooto nwu nkpo ninnyu.” Ninfɛ baayɔ koto nwu nkpo baawako nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Owe kunyii ku leyooto nintika di koto ko mmle suoto?” Ninfɛ baadiki kanya alɛ, “Ɔka Kplɛ Kaesare dile.” Nioso Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ni biyɔ lɛsaa le ninle ni Ɔka Kplɛ Kaesare lele yi, bita Ɔka Kplɛ Kaesare.
Biɛyɔ lɛsaa le kafɔɔ ninle ni Yaa lele yi, bita Yaa.” Obe wɔ baanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle yi, diabla ma yaaa, ni baasifi baadiɛ nwɔ nɛ.
Yesu Latuo Asaa Alɛ Bakpi Makple Mantaka Kuukpi Kamɛ.
Dii nwu nkpo kale, Saduki batii ba nimbuɛ alɛ bakpi dilabasintaka bakye ni bakpi kamɛ lawa Yesu nfũ.
Ni baabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, Mose latɔkɔ wo alɛ, nse osuɔtɔ owo lekpi eediɛ ɔsɔfɔ manko nwɔ banaa babi kubanwii yi, osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo obilɛma kafuo kpisɔfɔ nwu nkpo ɔyɔ, manko nwɔ manlofo babi.
Ni baayɔ babi nwu nkpo mambla fɛ osuɔtɔ wɔ ninsinaa ni babi.
Obe onwii, babilɛma suɔtɔbi bakuɛnsĩ banwii lawɛ wo kaamɛ ninfũ.
Ni di ɔnɔɔfo le layɔ ɔsanko batalofo babi, ni aabafe aakpi nɛ.
Ninfɛ di maatɛle labayɔ kpisɔfɔ nwu nkpo nɛ.
Lɛsaa nwu nkpo kafɔɔ labla obilɛma suɔtobi nyɔɔfa nwu nkpo ku otiɛfa, dialaase di okuɛnsĩ le suoto.
Kuonwii lɛma ditalofo ku ɔsanko nwu nkpo fiɛ baakpi.
Yɛntɛyɛntɛ, ɔsanko nwu nkpo kafɔɔ labafe aakpi.
Nimɔ, di dii le baakpi makple mantaka nii, owe lɛma ɔsɔfɔ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo male di obe wɔ baakuɛnsĩ lɛma nwu layɔ nwɔ ni?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Diele nkpo dibate saa.
Lɛnya nlɛ bienu ɔlaa wɔ mmle kasɔ, diekye bieye sɛlaa se ninsi ni diɛ Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ, ee Yaa osie.
Diekye di obe wɔ di bakpi mataka nii, babate fɛ Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ di osi, nioso sɛsa ku sɛsɔfɔ dilabasinwɛ.
Biika lɛsaa le di Yaa labuɛ aatɔkɔ ye ni diekye ni baakpi okple ɔtaka osiɛ nkpa suoto?
Aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Ami ninle Abraham Yaa ku Isak Yaa ku Yakob Yaa.’ Nle mmle kotuo alɛ, nnwɔɔ ninle batii ba ninkpe ni nkpa Yaa, diele bakpi Yaa ale.” Di obe wɔ di batii dikudi nwu nkpo lanu ni asaatuo ya mmle yi, diabla ma ɔkpɛ osie kanya.
Yesu Latuo Asaa Di Kufiofa Ko Niefĩ Kulenke Ni Suoto.
Di obe wɔ di Farisi batii lanu alɛ Yesu sɛlaa kanya didikibi lata alɛ Saduki batii nwu nkpo ditasinfuo ni kanya ɔbɛ yi, baakple baabasi.
Ni di onwii kaamɛ lɛma ninle ni kufiofa tuotɛ lawolaa Yesu kaanya aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, kɔmɛnfiofa niefĩ kulenke di Mose afiofa nwu nkpo kamɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bɔmbɔ Saate Yaa lɛfɔ ku otu lɛfɔ omuu, ku ninwuna lɛfɔ nimuu ku disibu lɛfɔ nimuu.
Nko mmle ninle kufiofa ko niefĩ kulenke ni, kule ni kɔkasale nɛ.
Nko niekple kutikanko ni kuodie ni kɔkasale ninle alɛ, ‘Bɔmbɔ owo lɛfɔ fɛ mmle okle fambɔmbɔ ni suoto lɛfɔ.’ Afiofa ya mmle anyɔ suoto di Mose kufiofa ku Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ asaa otuo nkyɛ nɛ.” Owe Ninle Kristo Nwu Nkpo?
Obe wɔ di Farisi batii bawo lasi ni dikudi, Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Lɛ ninle ye disibu di Kristo nwu nkpo suoto?
Owe leyo kamɛ eekye?” Ni baadiki kanya alɛ, “Ɔka Dawid leyo kamɛ eekye.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Nse nkpo kute mɔ, ni lɛ diɛbla fiɛ di Yaa Ninwuna lata Dawid lalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ Saate?
Di Dawid nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa latɔkɔ Saate nii alɛ, “Siɛ di oletanɛɛkyɛ nii ninfũ dilaase di obe wɔ mayɔ balo lɛfɔ nkpee fɔ ni ninkpaa kalɔ.” ’ Ni nse Dawid lalɛɛ Kristo nwu nkpo alɛ Saate, ni lɛ diɛbla fiɛ ale Dawid leyo kamɛ obi?” Otii kuonwii kaamɛ lɛma ditafuo Yesu ɔlaa nwu nkpo kanya odiki.
Diayɔ ni di dii nwu nkpo kamaa, kuonwii ditasinkpee otu aakaalɛ Yesu ɔlaa kuonwii.
Yesu Ladiki Kufiofa Batuotɛ Ku Farisi Batii Ɔsaabla Kayi.
Nni nkpo sɛmaa, Yesu lakakatɛ aata batii dikudi nwu nkpo ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii ninle mba bɛɛta osuku alɛ baadiki ni Mose kufiofa nwu nkpo kasɔ.
Nkpo oso bibla lɛsaa lele bɛɛtɔkɔ ye, biemufũ biklee osie kanya.
Kafɔɔ bitantikanko ɔsaabla lɛma nkpaamaa, diekye baasi nkpa di asaa ya bootuo ni suoto.
Beekpee atoo ya ninkpe ni onutũ beetukasa batii diisi alɛ batuka.
Kafɔɔ mma bamu bolootuna alɛ bɔɔyɔ bia lɛnɛɛbi lɛma ninwii mankyaako batukatɛ nwu alɛ baatuka.
“Mambla lɛsaa biala baatii kanya ma ni fɛle Yaa bakpɛmblatɛ nwaa bale nii.
Asaa ya man-yɔ mannii ni disi ku nnɛɛtũ lɛma lɛbla blɛfɛɛ, bɛɛkpana Kɔkpana Klekle sɛlaa beetika nya di suoto.
Bɛɛbla kafɔɔ awu sɛkpaalɛ abinte beetika di awu lɛma suoto.
Mambɔmbɔ osiɛ di nsiɛkɔ kplɛ di dii nlekɔ ku aba kplɛ osiɛ di Yuda batii nsiisakɔ kamɛ.
Mammiɛ alɛ batii katɔwakasɔ mantɔɔsɛɛsa ma ku dibu laakpaka, mantɔɔlɛɛ ma kafɔɔ alɛ Basaatuotɛ.
“Kafɔɔ aye bafũbanutɛ yi, bitanta baalɛɛ ye basaatuotɛ, diekye saatuotɛ onwii lete ninkpe ye.
Aye yi, bawo babilɛma bile.
Bitanlɛɛ otii kuonwii kafɔɔ kaayi ka mmle bilɛ Teete, diekye Teete onwii lete ninkpe ye di osi.
Bitanta baalɛɛ ye kafɔɔ alɛ Batunletɛ.
Diekye otii onwii lete ninle ye tunletɛ, nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo nɛ.
Kaamɛ lee, nwɔ ninle ni ɔnɔɔfo yi, dikpe nii eele kpɛmblatɛ ɛɛta bayɛntɛle.
Otii wɔ niɛtakatɛsa ni suoto katoo yi, Yaa mawakosa nwɔ kasɔ.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ niɛwakosa ni suoto kasɔ yi, Yaa matakatɛsa nwɔ katoo.
Yesu Lalo Kufiofa Batuotɛ Ku Farisi Batii Lɛpɔɔ.
“Biyɔɔsa, aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Biɛsɛɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ kayokontũ biekpee batii bilɛ batambuo.
Aye bamu kafɔɔ biesĩ bilɛ biloobuo.
Bietĩi mba kafɔɔ nikokpee ni okyiini alɛ boobuo ni osuku.
Biyɔɔsa aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Minkyɛ bakpisɔfɔ nfũ bilɛ biɔkyakaako ma, kafɔɔ minkyɔnkyɔ ma minfũ ma asaa ninnɛɛ.
Mimpɛ ɔlaa minklɛsa kafɔɔ bilɛ biɔyɔ minkyɔnkyɔ ma.
Ta nkpo oso letokonanfi lee matɛ nimpɔ.
“Biyɔɔsa aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Mintaalɛ lekpo minkyɛ minkyi kayi aba aba mimmiɛ otii onwii minta Yaa.
Nse bitɔɔwɛ otii nwu bieloo, mintuo nwɔ asaa anlalaa anlenkee bia aye bamu lee sɛnyɔ, alɛ aakyɛ kawɔɔ ɔtɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ!
“Biyɔɔsa aye batunletɛ ba di anu lebiɛ ni!
Mintuo bilɛ, ‘Nse otii lɛka Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo yi, diɛbla lɛsalɛsaa, kafɔɔ nse otii lɛka koto sɛɛle ko ninte ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, dikpe nii eediki ntam nwu nkpo.’ Banumbiɛtɛ babuutɛ!
Lɛmɛnle niefĩ dilenke, koto sɛɛle nwu ɛɛ, sɛɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ ka niɛta koto sɛɛle nwu nkpo nte ni klekle?
Biokple mintuo bilɛ, ‘Nse otii owo lɛka oleɔta akyikye nwu nkpo yi, diɛbla lɛsalɛsaa.
Kafɔɔ nse ɛɛlɛɛ oleɔta wɔ nintika ni di oleɔta akyikye nwu nkpo suoto yi, ni dikpe nii eediki ntam nwu nkpo.’ Banumbiɛtɛ biɛtɛ bile nwaako!
Lɛmɛnle niefĩ dilenke, oleɔta nwu ɛɛ, sɛɛ oleɔta akyikye ya niɛta oleɔta nwu nkpo nte ni klekle?
Nkpo oso, nse otii owo lɛlɛɛ oleɔta akyikye nwu nkpo yi, ni atɔɔlɛɛ oleɔta akyikye nwu nkpo ku oleɔta wɔ omuu nintika nya ni di suoto.
Nse ɛɛlɛɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ kafɔɔ yi, ni atɔɔlɛɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu ku Yaa wɔ ninsi ni ninfa.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ nse otii owo lɛka osi yi, ni atɔɔka Yaa lɛkakpomii ku Yaa wɔ omu ninsi ni di lekpomii nwu suoto nɛ.
“Biyɔɔsa aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Biye mmle okle manta ni apasalɛbi ku kayee ku abulaa dikyuu lefosile nɔɔ manta ni Yaa, kafɔɔ biesĩ kufiofa asaatuo finle ya ninle ni batii ɔtannyu di anu ku nyaami ɔnya ku ote tinini biɛtɛ.
Asaa ya mmle dikaatɛ alɛ biɛka ɔbla fiɛ biɛyɔ nnya nkpo kafɔɔ biɛkyakaa nɛ.
Batunletɛ banumbiɛtɛ!
Mindiki kabɔkɔbii biibii di nta anu, kafɔɔ asaa ya mimmɛ ni lemuɔ alenke kapupɔnkɔ!
“Biyɔɔsa aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Minfoto sipũ lee ku awansaa lee sɛmaa klekle, kafɔɔ kamɛ ninya leyii pɔ ku lɛkpɔnɔnfɔ fɛ mmle okle bieyii ni ku ditiitafaa ku onumbɛbɛɛ.
Afɔ Farisi otii numbiɛtɛ, foto opũ lɛfɔ kamɛ lɛkasale, ni sɛmaa kafɔɔ makpa.
“Biyɔɔsa aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Bite fɛ sɛkya se beekpiitaa ni ku akaaloo siɔlɛ ni onyu kaayi osie kanya.
Kafɔɔ kamɛ leyii pɔ ku bakpi buule ku akufi.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ biɛbla suoto fɛ batii biene baatii anu nɛ, kafɔɔ kamɛ lee leyii pɔ ku sɛlaa kuafunu ku sikpile.
Yesu Labuɛ Kufiofa Batuotɛ Ku Farisi Batii Letokonanfi Aatɛ.
“Biyɔɔsa aye kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii!
Aye anu di anu basaablatɛ!
Mimbla sɛkya biene minta Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ, minlolaa kafɔɔ batii ba niesiɛ ni nkpa biene sɛkya osie kanya.
Mimbuɛ kafɔɔ bilɛ, ‘Nse minsiɛ nkpa di bawa lee obe kamɛ yi, nse biɛbla onwii ku mma bilo Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nwu nkpo.’ Kafɔɔ nwaako ɔsaabla lee kodiki kuntuo alɛ batii ba nialo ni Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nwu nkpo banantii bile.
Nkpo oso yi, bibla bikyɛnko, biɛyɛntɛ lɛsaa le baawa lee lakye ni kasɔ.
“Batii kpile bile!
Bite fɛ basaanwu ku abi!
Bienyu bilɛ bibafuo otoso odie di Yaa letokonanfi le abananfi ye ni di ɔtɔ kawɔɔ kamɛ?
Nle mmle oso, makyesee ye Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ ku banumbentɛ ku kufiofa batuotɛ, bibapɛ bawo minkaasa di kowoso suoto mankpi.
Bibapɛ bawo kafɔɔ kowesee di nsiisakɔ lee, mintikanko babamba kafɔɔ mindiki di okpoo minsifiko okpoo bamba kamɛ.
Di ɔsaabla wɔ mmle oso, batii ba ninte ni tinini bamuu ntɔ be batooyiwii ni kaasɔ suoto, matika ye diisi.
Dibakye kasɔ di otii tinini Abel ntɔ suoto, ninaase di Barakia obi nɔɔ Sakaria wɔ bialo ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ kamɛ ku oleɔta akyikye obo.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, ntɔ be mmle beewii nii letokonanfi mawa di aye ba ninkpe ni nkpa miɛ disi.
Kafutu Lanu Yesu Di Yerusalem Suoto.
“O Yerusalem, Yerusalem, afɔ nialo Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ, faasafɔ batii ba kafɔɔ di Yaa lakpee fɔ ni ɔkyɛ aafuɔ faalo!
Obe kpinwu ntoomiɛ nlɛ kosiisa babi lɛfɔ di afoko nii kalɔ fɛ mmle okle di kɔɔkɔɔbi ɔya nkpaa abi ankpee ni di afoko nɔɔ kalɔ, kafɔɔ floonu kasɔ!
Ta nle mmle oso, Yaa madiki okpoo wɔ mmle atoko manwɔɔsa nwu.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, biloosinwa mi ɔbanya diediki diɛlaase di obe wɔ biebuɛ bilɛ, ‘Yaa lekusɛkusɛsa otii wɔ nikɔwa ni di Saate leyooto kamɛ.’ ”
Yesu Labuɛ Alɛ Bɔɔwa Yuda Batii Olekatakɔ Nwu Nkpo Obiɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu ladie di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo ninfa aatoosifi nii, ni di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ babatootuo nwɔ Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo ku ayo ninya.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bilolaa asaa ya mmle nwu nkpo binyu nwaa.
Diekye kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ bababiɛ nya amuu, bia difuɔ ku ninwii dilababu ditika di lewo nini suoto alɛ baasamiisa nya batɛ kaasɔ.” Yesu Latɔkɔ Batikankotɛ Nɔɔ Obe Wɔ Babawɛ Ni Dibuo.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu lasifi aalaasiɛ ni di Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote suoto yi, ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ buɛɛ babakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔkɔ wɔ ɔmɛmbe di asaa ya mmle mawa kaanya?
Obe kafɔɔ nimale dituosaa alɛ fɔɔwa, ni kayi kalookɔ kafɔɔ ntoowo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu nwaa alɛ otii kuonwii diɛkyɔnkyɔ ye.
Diekye batii kpinwu mayɔ leyooto nii manwa ɔkyɛ lee, mamatɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Ami ninle Kristo nwu!’ Mankyɔnkyɔ batii kpinwu.
Bibanu kakpɛ kudu sɛɛlɔɔkɔ lee ku kakpɛ sɛlaa fanfa, kafɔɔ bitanta lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ ye.
Dikpe nii, asaa ya mmle okle lɛwa kafɔɔ dilootuo alɛ kayi kalookɔ ntoowo.
Nnle mataka baawo suoto, sɛka nlekɔ kafɔɔ mataka baawo suoto.
Nsɔ matũkũ di aba aba.
Aka siene kafɔɔ makpɛ di aba aba.
Asaa ya mmle amuu nte fɛ mmle lɛɛmɛ nkye kasɔ nintoonu ni mɛlakatɛ nintɔɔtɛ nii.
“Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, balo lee mata mammufũ ye mambla ye amumu, manlo ye bia.
Batii bamuu makyidi ye ta ami oso.
Di obe nwu kamɛ yi, batii kpinwu madiɛ ofũ onu lɛma.
Babadiki bawo lɛma manta, mankyidi bawo lɛma kafɔɔ.
Balaatɛ Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ kpinwu madie mankyɔnkyɔ batii kpinwu.
Sikpile ɔbla mapɔ osie kanya di batii kamɛ alɛ batii kpinwu ditiibɔmbɔ mawa kasɔ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimakpee otu anaase ni kaayɛntɛlekɔ kamawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Batii mayie Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɔlaa biene nwu nkpo lɛkya kaayi kamuu kamɛ, alɛ otii biala kawɛ osuku annu, fiɛ nfɛ di kayi kaloo nwu nkpo mawa.
Ditikanko Kplɛ Le Mmle Okle Nimawa Ni Lɛɛyɛkɛ Nsi Ni Diiwa Diidii.
“Nse biɛnya abusufɔɔsaa yɛkɛle ya di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Daniel labuɛ aatɛ ni n-yɛ di Kakleklekɔ nwu nkpo yi, ni afɔ wɔ nikɔka ni kukũ ko mmle yi, nu kasɔ nwaa!
“Ni biɛta batii ba ninkpe ni di Yudia batoso basifi abokote osi balaawofa.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ nintika ni di leyo nɔɔ osi, atantɔkɔ alɛ oosoo anwa amayɔ lɛsalɛsa nɔɔ leeyo kamɛ ansifiko.
Otii wɔ ninkpe ni koofe, atasinkple aatɔkɔ alɛ ooyie ammayɔ akleesaa nɔɔ leeyo.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, dibatɛ ninwɛ osie ninta basanko ba ninlaka ni amɛ ku mba nikɔta babi nyɛɛfu nii.
Bipɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa bilɛ, otoso osifi wɔ mmle nwu nkpo diɛwa di lɛwɔɔfɔ obe ee Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto!
Diekye dibuo kplɛ le nimawa ni di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ malenkee nle okle nintɔwa diɛbafe ni di obe wɔ kaayi lakye ni kasɔ diɛbase ni diɛ miɛ dii le mmle.
Dibuo le mmle okle kafɔɔ dilabasinwa diidii.
Kafɔɔ Saate lɛkɔkɔlɛ ayi nwu nkpo.
Se diele nkpo ɛɛbla se otii kuonwii dilababu.
Kafɔɔ ta batii nɔɔ ba eediki ɛɛta ni suoto oso, ɛɛkɔkɔlɛ ayi nwu.
“Nioso se otii owo lɛtɔkɔ fɔ alɛ, ‘Nyu!
Nnya Kristo ninfũ!’ ee ‘Nyɔɔ ninfa!’, tanfũ nwɔ faanu.
Diekye batii mataka manlaa mambuɛ alɛ mma ninle Kristo nwu nkpo, bawo kafɔɔ mabuɛ alɛ Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ bale.
Bababla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni sɛkpɛ ku atuosaa ate ate mantuo alɛ, nse dialɛ yi, baayɔ mankyɔnkyɔ bia batii ba di Yaa lediki eese ni lete.
Binu!
Nkpo oso ntoole katũ lɛtɔkɔ ye sɛlaa se mmle fiɛ di obe nwu mawo nɛ.
“Nse batii lɛtɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Binyu!
Akpe di ɔfaafuu’ yi, bitankyɛ nfa.
Ee nse bɛɛtɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Asi leeyo kamɛ’ yi, bitanfũ bianu.
Diekye Otii Obi nwu nkpo mawa fɛ mmle okle di kanto mmunaa ankye ni kufĩ katunkɔ amafe ni kufĩ kamɛɛkɔ.
Nkpo oso bitanyee bilɛ nfũ di lɛsaa lekpi dite nii, nfa di alente nsi nɛ.
Asaa Ya Awo Nimatuo Alɛ Kayi Kalookɔ Ntoowo Nii.
“Diibuo kplɛ nwu nkpo kamaa, kufĩ mata ditunu, kɔwɛntɛ kafɔɔ dilabapu.
Awɛntlɛbi kafɔɔ makpa ankye osi, osi asaa kafɔɔ matididi di aba ya atika nii.
“Nfanwu Otii Obi nwu nkpo dituosaa makyɔɔ di osi, kasɔ ka mmle batii bamuu mawi kaku di obe wɔ baatii manya Otii Obi nwu makyɔɔ ni di alokonkyɛ kamɛ ɔɔwa ku osie kplɛ di leklekle kamɛ.
Abata manfɛ dikyukyoo kplɛ nwu nkpo.
Abakyesee Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ di kayi ka mmle nkyakakɔ nwu nkpo nna, mansiisa batii nɔɔ ba eediki ni mankyeko kaasɔ disi le diɛlase ni diisi le.
Yesu Latuo Asaa Aakyeko Kolewoso Kunwii Suoto.
“Bitekete lɛsaa bikyeko kolewoso suoto.
Nse obe wɔ biɛnya bilɛ nfɛ kuodie ni sɛla fɔle kuokpee ni afata fɔle yi, mintofo bilɛ kanto ɔnɔɔbee nfɛ kowo.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ nse bienya asaa ya mmle nkpo amuu yi, bietofo bilɛ Kristo obe nwu nkpo ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ, nfɛ ayɛ di kayokontũ.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ asaa ya mmle amuu mawa fiɛ di batii ba bamuu ninsi ni nkpa nunua maloo okpi.
Osi ku kasɔ mafe, kafɔɔ sɛlaa nii nsĩ, silabafe diidii.
Otii Kuonwii Dieye Dii Le Ku Obe Wɔ Di Yesu Makple Anwa Nii.
“Otii kuonwii dieye dii nwu nkpo ku obe wɔ kamɛ dibale nii.
Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ ba ninkpe ni di osi dieye.
Bia Obi nwu nkpo omu dieye, Ote lete ninnye.
Otii Obi nwu nkpo ɔwabee mate fɛ lɛsaa le niawa ni di Noa obe kamɛ.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ fiɛ di kanto labanɔɔ aayii ni kayi yi, batii latoole baatoonyi.
Basanko ku basuɔtɔ latoodiki bawo baatɔɔyɔ.
Baatɔɔyɔ bawo kafɔɔ baatɔɔta asa, dialaase di dii le di Noa labuo ni di oklo nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ batatofo lɛsaa le niatɔɔwa nii, dialaase di obe wɔ di kanto lanɔɔ ntu labayɔ ni bamuu lɛma.
Nkpo okle dibate nse Otii Obi nwu nkpo lɛwa nɛ.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, basuɔtɔ banyɔ matɔɔbla ɔkpɛ koofe Yaa makpaa onwii andiɛ onwii.
Basanko banyɔ kafɔɔ mawɛ di nnaafũ kakuɔkɔ, Yaa makpaa onwii andiɛ onwii.
“Nkpo oso bita anu lee ate kesekese, diekye bieye dii le di Saate lee kamawa nii.
Nse fɛ leyo saate n-ye obe wɔ kamɛ di yu kamawa nii yi, biye bilɛ atabasiɛ ku anu kesekese ansoko nwɔ.
Atabata yu nwu nkpo abiɛ kakɔkakɔ abuo nwɔ leyo kamɛ.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ dikpe nii biɛta anu lee lete kesekese obe lele nɛ, diekye Otii Obi nwu nkpo kamawa di obe wɔ kamɛ minoonyu osuku bilɛ abawa nii.
Dikpe Nii Kpɛmblatɛ Lɛbla Asaa Di Osuku Suoto.
“Nimɔ owe ninle kpɛmblatɛ wɔ niebe ni anu ambla ni asaa di osuku suoto?
Nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ di saate nɔɔ leyɔ nwɔ eese ni di bakpɛmblatɛ wo nɔɔ kanya alɛ aata ma ni alesaa di obe kanya nɛ.
Nwaako suoto matɛ sinyɔɔ kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo nse saate nɔɔ lɛwa ɛbanyɔɔ alɛ ɔɔbla lɛsaa le aatɔkɔ nwɔ nii.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, saate nwu nkpo mayɔ kpɛmblatɛ wɔ mmle anse di asaa nɔɔ amuu kanya.
Kafɔɔ nse kpɛmblatɛ kpile ale yi, ababuɛ antɔkɔ suoto alɛ, ‘Sua!
Saate nii dilabawa nunua!’ Nkpo oso abakye kasɔ antɔɔpɛ bakpɛmblatɛ wo nɔɔ nwu nkpo.
Nse atɔɔkyako ole, onyi ku batasiɛntɛ.
Nse Saate nwu nkpo ntookple ɛɛwa di dii le ku obe wɔ di kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo diloonyu osuku aatɔɔ nii.
Saate nwu nkpo mananfi kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo kootoko osie kanya, antɔɔ kalekɔ nɔɔ di anu di anu basaablatɛ kamɛ.
Nfa di kaku owi ku anyɛɛ owee kamawɛ nɛ!
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Kokpeelebitɛ Lefosi Kowo Suoto.
“Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo mate fɛ mmle okle.
Di obe onwii kamɛ, kokpeelebitɛ lefosi kowo layɔ bakandiɛ lɛma alɛ bɔɔlaakyakako ɔkafɔɔsa.
Banɔɔ kaamɛ lɛma lale babuutɛ.
Banɔɔ bule kafɔɔ lale banumbentɛ.
Babuutɛ nwu nkpo layɔ bakandiɛ lɛma kafɔɔ bataklee nnɔfɔ kunwii baakyakaa.
Kafɔɔ banumbentɛ nwu nkpo mma baabla nnɔfɔ baakpete di asaa kamɛ baakle baata bakandiɛ lɛma.
Ɔkafɔɔsa nwu nkpo laklɛ ku ɔwa, nkpo oso kokpeelebitɛ nwu nkpo lakyako sɛkyɔsĩ ɔkpa, ni baakyɔsĩi nɛ.
“Nkyɛntɛɛ fiɛ kuudu ladie alɛ, ‘Ɔkafɔɔsa nwu ntɔbabuo kyu woo!
Bidie biwa biɛbakyakako nwɔ!’ “Ninfɛ di bakpeelebitɛ lefosi nwu nkpo lataka wla baayiensa bakandiɛ lɛma nɛ.
Ninfɛ di babuutɛ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ banumbentɛ nwu nkpo alɛ, ‘Bitika wo nnɔfɔ lee nwu nkpo nnwo, diekye bakandiɛ loo ba bukle ni nfɛ konii.’ “Ninfɛ di banumbentɛ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Oo, nnɔfɔ be bukle ni dilabawo awo ku aye.
Nkpo oso bitɔɔkyɛ basunsutɛ nfũ biɛlaaya.’ “Nkpo oso babuutɛ nwu nkpo lasifi nnɔfɔ nwu nkpo kayakɔ.
Obe wɔ baasifi ni osifi ni di ɔkafɔɔsa nwu nkpo lawa nɛ.
Ninfɛ di kokpeelebitɛ kɔnɔɔ ko nialoolaa ni suoto latikanko nwɔ baabuo ɔsanko nwu kayɔkɔ nɛ, ni baasɛɛ leyo nɛ.
“Nni sɛmma, kokpeelebitɛ bulɛ nwu nkpo kafɔɔ lawa, ni baabuɛ alɛ, ‘Ɔnɔɔfo, Ɔnɔɔfo!
Sɛkɛtɛ wo buobuo!’ “Ninfɛ di ɔkafɔɔsa nwu nkpo latɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Oowo!
Ninye ye.’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɛntɛ ku lɛkpa nwu alɛ, “Nkpo oso bita anu lee ate kesekese, diekye bieye dii nwu nkpo ee obe wɔ di Otii Obi nwu mawa nii.
Dikpe Nii Buololaa Asaa Ya Di Yaa Lɛyɔ Eekpee Wo Ni Di Nnɛɛ Kamɛ Buoklee.
“Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu kamate fɛ nle mmle okle.
Obe onwii kamɛ osuɔtɔ onwii lalolaa suoto aatoofe osuku, ni aalɛɛ bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ, aayɔ ma aase di asaa nɔɔ kanya nɛ.
Aata obiala lɛma lɛsaa le aafuo ni okle di osei nɔɔ kanya.
Aata onwii koto fututu nkpe nnɔɔ, ɔbamba kafɔɔ aatɔɔ koto nkpe nnyɔ, ɔbamba kafɔɔ aatɔɔ kakpe kanwii.
Ni aadie aasifi osuku nɛ.
Kpɛmblatɛ wɔ niafũ ni koto nkpe nnɔɔ, nfanwu aasifi aalaayɔ koto nɔɔ aakpee di ɔkpɛ ɔbla kamɛ aawɛ koto nkpe nnɔɔ atikasa.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di kpɛmblatɛ wɔ niafũ ni koto nkpe nnyɔ lawɛ koto nkpe nnyɔ aatikasa nɛ.
Kafɔɔ kpɛmblatɛ wɔ niafũ ni koto kakpe kanwii lasifi aalaakutu kasɔ aayɔ Saate nɔɔ koto aakookaa ninfa.
“Ayi kpinwu sɛmaa, bakpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo Saate lɛma lakple aawa aabablako ma koto nwu nkpo nkuntaa.
Kpɛmblatɛ wɔ niafũ ni koto nkpe nnɔɔ, layɔ koto nkpe nnɔɔ bamba aakyakaa, ni aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Ɔnɔɔfo, faatɛɛ koto nkpe nnɔɔ kafɔɔ lɛwɛ nkpe nnɔɔ bamba letikasa.’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nɔɔ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Oo!
Kpɛmblatɛ biene, fɛɛbla lɛsaa di osuku kanya nwaako!
Di obe wɔ feelolaa fɛɛbla, feelolaa koto ko mmle kafuii feekle ni oso yi, mayɔ fɔ nse di koto kplɛ kanya.
Wa fabasiɛ di suoto lɛyɔɔ nii kamɛ!’ “Ninfɛ di kpɛmblatɛ wɔ kafɔɔ baata ni koto nkpe nnyɔ lawa ababuɛ alɛ, ‘Ɔnɔɔfo, faatɛɛ koto nkpe nnyɔ, kafɔɔ lɛwɛ nkpe nnyɔ bamba letikasa.’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nɔɔ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Oo!
Kpɛmblatɛ biene, fɛɛbla lɛsaa di osuku kanya nwaako!
Di obe wɔ feelolaa fɛɛbla, feelolaa koto koto ko mmle kafuii feekle ni oso yi, mayɔ fɔ nse di koto kplɛ kanya.
Wa fabasiɛ di suoto lɛyɔɔ nii kamɛ!’ “Ninfɛ di kpɛmblatɛ wɔ kafɔɔ baata ni koto kakpe kanwii lawa ababuɛ alɛ.
‘Ɔnɔɔfo, n-ye nlɛ fale otii wɔ di ɔlaa lɛfɔ nkpe ni osie, fanfiɛlɛ ninfũ fanankpɛ nii.
Fantɛsɛ ninfũ kafɔɔ fanampɛ ni lɛsalɛsaa.
Kɔyɛkɛ ni oso, layɔ koto lɛfɔ nwu nkpo lalakutu kasɔ layɔ lakookaa.
Nnya lɛsaa lɛfɔ.
Fũ!’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nɔɔ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Afɔ kpɛmblatɛ kpile, fakpe nkyɔkɔ lo!
Faye falɛ nfiɛlɛ ninfũ ninankpe ni kowee, ntɛsɛ kafɔɔ ninfũ ninampɛ ni lɛsalɛsaa.
Ni be oso fanan-yɔ koto nii nwu nkpo falaatɛ di koto katɛkɔ alɛ nse lɛwa kafũ koto nwu nkpo nwɛ lɛsaa ntikasa?’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nɔɔ nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, ‘Bifũ koto nwu nkpo di nnɛɛ nɔɔ biɛyɔ bita otii wɔ ninkle ni koto nkpe lefosi.’ Diekye otii wɔ ninkpe ni lɛsaa yi, nnwɔɔ babakple mankyakaa mampɔɔsa nɛ.
Alɛ lɛsaa le ninkpe nwɔ ni kakple nimpɔ ninlenkee.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ ninnaa ni lɛsaa yi, kɛɛkɛɛ wɔ bia ninkpe nwu nii yi, babakle manfũ nwɔ ninnɛɛ kamɛ.
Kpɛmblatɛ wɔ mmle diesinlɛ ata lɛsalɛsaa ɔblako, nkpo oso biyɔ nwɔ bifuki binyu kaayi di ditunu nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Nfa abawi kaku anwee anyɛɛ nɛ.
Otii Obi Nwu Nkpo Nimakanko Batii Bamuu Kaayi.
“Nse Otii Obi nwu nkpo lɛwa fɛ Ɔka, di Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ lɛmana nwɔ beekyi yi, abasiɛ di lɛkakpomii nɔɔ suoto.
Abasiisa nnle mmuu batii di anu nɔɔ, nse atɔɔsɛ ma ntɛɛ di akyuu anyɔ fɛ mmle okle di babɔkɛɛkpatɛ nsɛ ni batie ku bafoso ntɛɛ.
Abata batii biene nyila di oletanɛɛkyɛ nɔɔ, anta batii kpile kafɔɔ nyila di ɔmɛtukyɛ nɔɔ.
“Nse Ɔka nwu nkpo ntɔɔtɔkɔ batii ba nin-yɛ nwɔ ni di oletanɛɛkyɛ alɛ, ‘Biwa, aye ninle batii ba di Teemi lewii ni lɛyɔɔ nɛ!
Biwa biɛbasiɛ di sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo di Yaa lelolaa ɛɛta ye ni, diɛyɔ ni di kayi kasɔ kakyekɔ.
Diekye di obe wɔ kɔɔka laklee mi nii, biatɛɛ alesaa lale.
Obe wɔ di otukɔnsɔ laklee mi nii, biatɛɛ ntu lanyi.
Obe wɔ kafɔɔ lababuo ye ni kɔfɔɔ, biafũ mi ku otu biene.
Obe wɔ lakyɛ ni lɛkyɔtɔ, biatɛɛ asaa laklee.
Obe wɔ latoofiɛ nii, bianyu mi.
Obe wɔ kafɔɔ late ni leeyo, biawa biabanyu mi.’ “Nfa nfɛ di batii biene nwu nkpo makaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Saate, ɔmɛmbe buanya fɔ kɔka laklee fɔ buata fɔ alesaa faale, ee ɔmɛmbe di otukɔnsɔ laklee fɔ buata fɔ ntu faanyi?
Ɔmɛmbe faabuo wo kɔfɔɔ buafũ fɔ ku otu biene, ee faakyɛ lɛkyɔtɔ buata fɔ asaa faaklee?
Ɔmɛmbe faatoofiɛ buawa buabasɛɛsa fɔ, ee faate leeyo katenkɔ buawa buabanyu fɔ?’ “Nfa nfɛ di Ɔka nwu nkpo madiki kanya alɛ, ‘Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, di obe wɔ biɛnya biɛbla nle mmle biɛta ni babiloo ba mmle yɛntɛle onwii lɛma kamaa, ami biɛbla biɛta.’ “Nfa nfɛ abatɔkɔ batii ba nin-yɛ nwɔ ni di ɔmɛtukyɛ alɛ, ‘Bikyɛ mi di ɔlɔɔkɔ bisifi aye ba di Yaa lɛkpaani ntika ni di suoto!
Bitɔɔkyɛ kawɔɔ ɔtɔ wɔ ninnaa ni kaloo di Yaa lelolaa ɛɛtɛ ɛɛta ni Abonsam ku batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ kamɛ!
Diekye kɔka laklee mi, kafɔɔ bitatɛɛ alesaa lale.
Otukɔnsɔ laklee mi, kafɔɔ bitatɛɛ ntu lanyi.
Labuo ye kɔfɔɔ, kafɔɔ bitafũ mi.
Lakyɛ lɛkyɔtɔ, bitatɛɛ asaa laklee.
Latoofiɛ bitawa biabasɛɛsɛɛ.
Late leeyo kafɔɔ bitawa biabanyu mi.’ “Nfa nfɛ babakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Saate, ɔmɛmbe buanya fɔ kɔka laklee fɔ, ee otukɔnsɔ laklee fɔ, ee faabuo wo kɔfɔɔ, ee faakyɛ lɛkyɔtɔ, ee faatoofiɛ, ee faate leeyo fiɛ butakyakaako fɔ?’ “Nfa nfɛ di Ɔka nwu nkpo matɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ di obe wɔ bitabla dibiene biata ni babiloo ba mmle yɛntɛle yi, ami bitabla biata.’ ” Yesu layɛntɛ alɛ, “Batii ba mmle nwu nkpo masifi dibuo le ninnaa ni kaloo kamɛ.
Batii biene kafɔɔ masifi nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo kamɛ.”
Yuda Batii Batunletɛ Lakpee Asi Baawo Alɛ Boolo Yesu.
Di obe wɔ kamɛ di Yesu ntooloo ni asaa ya mmle amuu otuo yi, aatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Biye bilɛ ditoobu ayi anyɔ bubale ni Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii nwu nkpo.
Babayɔ Otii Obi nwu nkpo manta mampɛ mankaasa di kowoso suoto.” Ninfɛ di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo balaasi di Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo Kaiafa leyo nɛ.
Ni baalaabla disibu mmle okle babamufũ ni Yesu di lɛwofa kamɛ manlo nwɔ ni nɛ.
Ni baabuɛ baatɔkɔ bawo alɛ, “Ditanwa alɛ buɔbla lɛsaa le mmle di ayi ya buole ni kamɛ.
Se diele nkpo, batii manya ɔblɔ mantaka wo di suoto.” Ɔsanko Onwii Lakpete Nnɔnyi Kɔnɔkɔnɔ Nnwii Di Yesu Suoto Di Betania.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, Yesu lakyɛ Simon wɔ niafiɛ ni ofiɛ sɛɛle leyo di Betania.
Yesu lawɛ di Betania okpoo diɛ Simon wɔ niafiɛ ni ofiɛ sɛɛle leyo.
Ɔbe wɔ di Yesu lasiɛ aatoole ni alesaa, ɔsanko onwii lawa nfa.
Aaklee difuɔ kylɔkylɔ lebo ninwii di nnɔnyi kɔnɔkɔnɔ be niefũ ni kɔya osie kanya lasiɛ ni kaamɛ.
Ni aanyɛɛnɛ nnɔnyi nwu nkpo aakpete di Yesu disi nɛ.
Obe wɔ baasaateketetɛ nɔɔ lanya ni nle mmle yi, ditaayɔɔ ma kafutu, ni baakaalɛ alɛ, “Be lɛsaa oso ɛɛlalaasa nnɔnyi be mmle, nkpo okle?
Baafuo nnɔnyi be mmle osunsũ ku kɔya kplɛ, man-yɔ koto nwu nkpo manta bapiitɛ fiɛ!” Yesu lanu ɔlaa wɔ baatoobuɛ nii, ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Be oso biokpee ɔsanko wɔ mmle kubuɛ?
Lɛsaa biene ninle nle mmle ɛɛbla ɛɛtɛɛ nii nɛ.
Bapiitɛ nsi ye kaamɛ obe lele.
Kafɔɔ ami, diele obe lele kamawɛ ye kaamɛ.
Nnɔnyi be mmle di ɔsanko wɔ mmle lɛyɔ eekpete mi ni di suoto yi, ololaa eelolaa mi ɛɛta okookaabee nii.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, kakɔ lele beeyie ɔlaa biene wɔ mmle lɛkya di kayi ka mmle kamɛ yi, lɛsaa le di ɔsanko wɔ mmle lɛbla nii, bababuɛ nwu man-yɔ mannyuma nwɔ.” Yuda Iskariot Latuna Aafũ Koto Aadiki Yesu Aata.
Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ lefosi banyɔ nwu nkpo onwii lɛma wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Yuda Iskariot ladie aasifi olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nfũ nɛ.
Ni aalaakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be bibatɛɛ nse lediki Yesu lɛta ye?” Ninfɛ baaka koto fututu afosi atiɛ baatɔɔ nɛ.
Diayɔ di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ diasifi nii, Yuda latoomiɛ osuku wɔ suoto abafe andiki Yesu anta nii.
Yesu Ku Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Lale Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii Alesaa Nwu Nkpo.
Diɛ Bloblo wɔ Ninantaka ni Dii ole kamɛ, di dii kasale suoto yi, basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lawa Yesu nfũ babakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔfɛ foomiɛ falɛ bulaawa Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole alesaa nwu buta fɔ?” Ni aakpee ma osuɔtɔ onwii nfũ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ okpoo kamɛ biɛlaatɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ, ‘Saatuotɛ alɛ, “Obe nii ntoowo.
Ami ku basaateketetɛ nii, leyo lɛfɔ bubale Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa nwu nkpo.” ’ ” Nkpo oso basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo labla fɛ mmle okle di Yesu latɔkɔ ma nii, baalaawa Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa nwu nkpo baase.
Di obe wɔ kɔɔtɔɔfɔ lawo nii, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi batii banyɔ nwu nkpo lasiɛ kaasɔ alɛ boole alesaa.
Obe wɔ boole ni alesaa nwu nkpo, Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii onwii kaamɛ lee madiki mi anta.” Ɔlaa nwu nkpo lakpanko basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo di otu kamɛ osie kanya ni baakyako nwɔ ɔkaalɛ onwii onwii alɛ, “Saate, nwaa n-ye nlɛ diele ami falaka, sɛɛ ami dile?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Otii wɔ niekpee ni kɔnɛɛ kaasɛfɛ ku ami, nimadiki mi anta.
Ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, makpi fɛ mmle okle di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ labuɛ nii.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimadiki ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, anta nii, ayɔɔsa.
Nse bia batanlofo nwɔ, nse dilɛ nwɔ dilenke!” Ninfɛ di Yuda wɔ niadiki nwɔ aata ni kafɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, nwaa n-ye nlɛ diele ami falaka, sɛɛ ami dile?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nnwu fatoobuɛ nɛ.” Baale Kɔtɔɔfɔ Alesaa Ya Nikotuo Ni Yaa Kanya Ninii Fɔle Nwu.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nsi boole ni alesaa yi, ni aayɔ bloblo nɛ.
Ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, aafee nwɔ, aayɔ aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ, aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bifũ bile.
Nle mmle ninle suoto nii sina nɛ.” Ninfɛ aayɔ opũ, ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, aayɔ aata ma aabuɛ alɛ, “Bamuu lee bifũ binyi.
Nle mmle ninle ntɔ nii be bɛɛyɔ beese ni kaanya di Yaa kanya ninii le eenii ni ku batii nɛ.
Beewii mi kaasɔ di batii kpinwu disi alɛ Yaa kayɔ sikpile lɛma ankyɛ ma.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, namasinnyi nta be mmle okle diidii diɛlaase di dii le di ami ku aye bubanyi ni nta fɔle di Teemi sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ.” Ninfɛ baasa onu onwii baatansa Yaa, ni baadie baasifi Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote suoto nɛ.
Yesu Labuɛ Aatɛ Alɛ Petro Masĩ Nwɔ.
Nfa nfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Miɛ kakyɛ yi, bamuu lee bibatoso mindiɛ mi nimbu lete nii.
Diekye Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ labuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa malo bafosokpatɛ nwu nkpo se bafoso nwu bamuu ntɔɔsamii.’ Kafɔɔ nse beekple bɛɛsɛnkɛsɛɛ bɛɛwako nkpa kamɛ yi, male ye katũ nsifi Galilea.” Ninfɛ di Petro latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Mintɛ bawo nii bamuu matoso mandiɛ fɔ yi, ami diidii namatoso ndiɛ fɔ!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ Petro alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, kakyɛ ka mmle fiɛ di kɔɔkɔ mabo nii, fababuɛ sitiɛ simu falɛ faaye mi.” Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nse bia olo alɛ booloe munko fɔ yi, diidii namabuɛ nlɛ ninye fɔ.” Basaateketetɛ bule bamuu kafɔɔ labuɛ nkpo.
Yesu Lapɛ Ɔlaa Aata Yaa Di Lɛba Le Bɔɔlɛɛ Getsemane.
Nfa nfɛ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo lasifi lɛba le bɔɔlɛɛ ni Getsemane.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bisiɛ ninfũ ninkyɛ sitũ naapɛ ɔlaa nta Yaa.” Ni aakpaa Petro ku Sebedeo babi banyɔ nwu nkpo aakyakaa di suoto nɛ.
Ditaklɛ ni aabuo nyaami, aakyako otũtũkũ di suoto nɔɔ kamɛ nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Konu dibuo di otu nii kamɛ osie kanya fɛle kukpi ninkle mi.
Aye bisiɛ ninfũ bietoonyunkoe.” Ninfɛ aakyɛ sitũ kɛɛkɛ nɛ, ni aapɛ akunkyi aafuusa anu kaasɔ aapɛ ɔlaa alɛ, “Teete, nse diaalɛ yi, faata dibuo opũ wɔ mmle nwu nkpo kufe mi.
Kafɔɔ diele mmle okle komiɛ nii, kafɔɔ bla di dibiesaa lɛfɔ suoto.” Ni aakple aawa basaateketetɛ nɔɔ batiɛ nwu nkpo nfũ nɛ, aabanya ma baatɔɔkyɔsĩi.
Ninfɛ aakaalɛ Petro alɛ, “Ni bilaafuo osiɛ otoonyunkoe lebombo ninwii pɛ?
Bita anu lee ate kesekese biɛpɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa alɛ bilaabuo di ɔsɔ onyu kamɛ.
Ninwuna komiɛ ɔbla, kafɔɔ suoto sina nnaa osie.” Nni sɛmaa Yesu lakple aasifi lɛnyɔɔfa aalaapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa alɛ, “Teete, nse dibuo le mmle dilabawaalɛ mi dife, dikaatɛ alɛ lefe ni kaamɛ, dile fɔ dibiesaa yi, faata diwa kaanya.” Obe wɔ aakple aawa ni basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo nfũ, aabanya ma baatɔɔkyɔsĩi, batafuo bia anu otikiti.
Yesu lakple aadiɛ ma aatɛ, aasifi aalaapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa ditiɛfa aabuɛ sɛlaa se okle aabuɛ abafe nii.
Ninfɛ aakple aawa basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo nfũ, aabakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Sɛkyɔsĩ biɔkyɔsĩi mintɛ ɔnyɛɛ nkpo nɛ?
Binyu!
Obe nwu ntoowo alɛ baayɔ ami Otii Obi nwu nkpo mankpee di bakpileblatɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Bitaka buosifi.
Binyu, otii wɔ nikodiki mi anta ni ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ.” Yuda Batii Banɔɔfo Lamufũ Yesu.
Yesu lakple aayila aatɔɔkakatɛ ko ma fiɛ di Yuda wɔ ninle ni lefosi batii banyɔ nwu nkpo onwii lɛma lawa.
Batii dikudi le di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo ladiki ni latikanko nwɔ baatɔɔwa.
Baaklee nwosoku ku mpamii.
Otii wɔ niadiki Yesu aata ni latɔkɔ ma aatɛ alɛ, “Otii wɔ kamaminiko mbla ni atuu yi, nnwɔɔ ninle nwɔ biowolaa ni nɛ.
Biemufũ nwɔ.” Di Yuda lanya ni Yesu, ni aakyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ aalaatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, atoko ɔkyɛ ole disiɛko fɔ.” Ninfɛ aaminiko nwɔ aabla nwɔ aatuu nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Siɛwo, lɛsaa le oso fɛɛwa ni ta dipɛsɛwa!” Ninfɛ di batii nwu nkpo ladie baawa Yesu nfũ, ni baamufũ nwɔ, baakle kpinkpĩ nɛ.
Ni baatii ba niawɛ ni di Yesu ɔkyɛ, onwii lɛma ladiki kapamii nɔɔ di kotofo kamɛ aasafɔ Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo kpɛmblatɛ kotoko aakpa nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kplesa kapamii lɛfɔ fakpee ninfũ feediki ni.
Batii ba niɛyɔ ni kapamii yi, kapamii kanya manka.
Sɛɛ bieye bilɛ kafuo Teemi ɔlɛɛ nkaalɛ lɛkyakaako, nfanwu ankyesee mi batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ ba ninkpe ni kaatoo, mba ninlenke akudi lefosi anyɔ?
Kafɔɔ nse bɛɛwa bɛbakyakaakoe, ni lɛyibabla fiɛ di ɔlaa wɔ Kɔɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ ɛɛtɛ alɛ diawa ni, kawa kaanya?” Nni kamaa, ni di Yesu lamunikĩi aakaalɛ batii dikudi nwu nkpo alɛ, “Be oso di mpamii ku nwosoku bikle biɛwa mi omufũ fɛle kpileblatɛ nɔɔfo nle?
Lasiɛ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo dii biala latuo batii asaa, kafɔɔ bitatɔkɔ bilɛ biomufũ mi.
Asaa ya mmle amuu lɛwa kaanya alɛ diata alɛ sɛlaa se di Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ lakpana ni di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ kawa kaanya.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ bamuu latoso baadiɛ nwɔ nɛ.
Baakanko Yesu Di Yuda Batii Kankankɔ Kplɛ.
Ninfɛ di batii ba niamufũ ni Yesu lakpaa nwɔ baasifiko Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo Kaiafa leyo nɛ, nfũ di kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo lasi nii.
Petro latikanko nwɔ sɛɛmaa fanfa aalaabuo Yaa Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo nwu leyo kaflɔnkɔ di bawo kalɛɛkɔ.
Aakyɛ aalaasiɛ di asaa banyuntɛ ɔlɔɔkɔ aatoonyu mmle okle di ɔsaabla nwu nkpo mate kunfe nii.
Olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku bakantɛ nwu nkpo niawɛ ni ninfa bamuu lamiɛ alɛ boobudi kanya mantika di Yesu suoto mmle okle baafuo nwɔ ni olo.
Kafɔɔ batawɛ ɔlaa kuonwii di suoto nɔɔ, nu batii kpinwu ladie baabudi nwɔ kanya.
Lɛyɛntɛle, batii banyɔ banwii ladie, bababuɛ alɛ, “Otii wɔ mmle labuɛ alɛ, ‘Kamabiɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ ka mmle, ninni kamaa, mayɔ ayi atiɛ nse ni letofo.’ ” Ninfɛ di Oletatɛ ɔnɔɔfo lataka aayila aakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Feenu ɔlaa wɔ beebuɛ ni di suoto lɛfɔ?
Ɔmɛnlaa ninkpe fɔ fambuɛ?” Kafɔɔ Yesu lamaasa kanya, atabuɛ ɔlaa kuonwii.
Ninfɛ di Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo lakple aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛka Yaa wɔ ninkpe ni nkpa lekpete fɔ nlɛ tɔkɔwo, nse afɔ ninle Kristo nwu nkpo, Yaa wɔ ninkpe ni nkpa Obi.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ɛɛ!
Nwu fatoobuɛ fɛ mmle kute ni nɛ.
Kafɔɔ kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, diɛyɔ di nua diesifi nii, bibanya Otii Obi nwu nkpo nsi di Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni oletanɛɛkyɛ.
Bibanyɔɔ kafɔɔ eekye osi ɔɔwa di alokonkyɛ kamɛ!” Obe wɔ di Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, ni aabɛ awu nɔɔ aabuɛ alɛ, “Bienu!
Ebuɛ mbusuo ɔlaa!
Diesinfĩ alɛ otii kuonwii kayila ɔlaa owo kamaa!
Lɛ biɛnya?” Ni baamuu lɛma baadiki kanya alɛ, “Eekpi lɛpɔɔ, dikpe ni eekpi!” Ninfɛ baatufa sita baakpete nwɔ di anu, ni baapɛ nwɔ nɛ.
Bawo kafɔɔ lapɛ nwɔ nnɛɛ di atokosi.
Ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Kristo nwu nɛ?
Tɔkɔ wo, otii wɔ niɛpɛ fɔ ni!” Petro Lasĩ Yesu Aalaa Aabuɛ Alɛ Aaye Nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ Petro lasiɛ kaayi di leyo nwu kaflɔnkɔ fiɛ di Olebatatɛ ɔnɔɔfo kpɛmblatɛ ɔsankobi onwii lawa abatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔɔ fatikanko Yesu wɔ niekye ni Galilea kasɔ!” Kafɔɔ Petro lasĩ di batii nwu nkpo bamuu anu aabuɛ alɛ, “Ninye ɔlaa kuonwii nkyeko ɔlaa wɔ foobuɛ ni suoto.” Ninfɛ aadie aalaayila di kaflɔnkɔ nwu nkpo kayokontũ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di kpɛmblatɛ ɔsankobi bamba lanya Petro, ni aatɔkɔ basuɔtɔ ba niayila ni ninfa alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle kafɔɔ latikanko Yesu Nasaret Otii nwu nkpo.” Ninfɛ di Petro lakple aasĩ aaka di asaa aabuɛ alɛ, “Ninye osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo kama!” Ditaklɛ saa, ni di basuɔtɔ ba niayila ni ninfa lawa Petro nfũ babatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nwaako, afɔɔ, onwii lɛma fale.
Diekye mmle okle fɔɔkakatɛ nii, ditoodiki dietuo klekle.” Ninfɛ di Petro labuɛ alɛ, “Lɛka nlɛ nwaako kobuɛ!
Yaa ananfi mi kootoko nse ɔlaa kɔlaa!
Ninye osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle.” Nfanwu, ni di kɔɔkɔ labo nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Petro lanyuma alɛ Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Fiɛ di kɔɔkɔ mabo nii, fabasĩ mi sitiɛ fambuɛ falɛ, faaye mi.” Nkpo oso aadie aasifi kayi aalaawi kaku osie kanya.
Yuda Banɔɔfotii Lakpaa Yesu Baakyɛnko Pilato Nfũ.
Kaleesɛ ku kolesɛtũ, olebatatɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo bamuu, baabla disibu alɛ babalo Yesu.
Bapɛ nwɔ lekpo ni baakpaa nwɔ baalaakpee di Roma Abaa Nɔɔfo Pilato nnɛɛ kamɛ nɛ.
Yuda Lalo Suoto.
Obe wɔ di Yuda wɔ niadiki Yesu aata ni lanu alɛ beelo nwɔ ni kukpi lɛpɔɔ, diabuo nwɔ suoto osie kanya.
Nioso aakplesa koto fututu afosi atiɛ nwu nkpo aakyɛnko olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo nwu nkpo.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Lɛbla okpile di obe wɔ lediki otii wɔ ninambla ni okpile lɛta nlɛ balo nii.” Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nnwu nkpo diɛkaako wo.
Ɔlaa lɛfɔ kule!” Ninfɛ di Yuda layɔ koto nwu nkpo aawii di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo ninfa, ni aasifi aalaakpee suoto okũ nɛ.
Ni di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nwu nkpo lakyɛ baalaasɛsɛɛ koto nwu nkpo ni babuɛ alɛ, “Yinaa alɛ buɔyɔ koto ko mmle buɔkpɔtɔɔsa di nko ninte ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ lɛlakaa kamɛ, diekye otii ntɔ koto kule.
Kufiofa loo kafɔɔ diɛta osuku.” Di obe wɔ baakpee ni asi baawo, baatuna alɛ babayɔ koto nwu nkpo man-ya dibukii blatɛ kasɔ, nfa kafɔɔ babatookookaa bafɔɔ nɛ.
Nle mmle oso, bia miɛ bɔɔlɛɛ kasɔ nwu nkpo alɛ Ntɔ Kasɔ nɛ.
Nioso ɔlaa wɔ di Yaa Ɔlaabuɛtɛtɛ Yeremia labuɛ aatɛ ni lawa kaanya nwaako.
Aabuɛ alɛ, “Baayɔ koto fututu afosi atiɛ ko di Israel batii latuna alɛ baata ni diisi nɔɔ, baaya dibukii blatɛ kasɔ fɛ mmle di Saate latɔkɔ mi nii.” Pilato Lakaalɛ Yesu Sɛlaa.
Baakpaa Yesu baalaase di Roma batii abaa ɔnɔɔfo Pilato anu.
Ni aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Yuda batii Ɔka nwu nɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nnwu fatoobuɛ nɛ.” Kafɔɔ obe wɔ di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo nwu nkpo layila baatoobudi nwɔ ni kanya yi, Yesu ditakpee ma kanya.
Ninfɛ di Pilato lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni floonu sɛlaa se boobuɛ mantika fɔ ni di suoto?” Kafɔɔ Yesu lasĩ atabɛ kanya adiki ɔlaa kuonwii kanya.
Nioso diabla abaa nɔɔfo nwu nkpo ɔkpɛ.
Pilato Lalo Yesu Kukpi Lɛpɔɔ.
Di Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole biala yi, Roma batii abaa ɔnɔɔfo wɔ mmle ndiɛ Yuda batii leyo batentɛ lele baatii nwu lɛkaalɛ ni anta ma.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, leyo tentɛ onwii lawɛ ma baatii n-ye nwɔ ni osie kanya ta ɔsaabla nɔɔ lalaale oso.
Baatɔɔlɛɛ nwɔ Baraba.
Nioso obe wɔ baatii dikudi labasi nii, Pilato lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Owe biomiɛ bilɛ ndiɛ nta ye?
Baraba ɛɛ, sɛɛ Yesu wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Kristo?” Aakaalɛ ma ɔlaa nwu nkpo diekye aatofo alɛ onunsɛɛ kanya oso di Yuda banɔɔfotii lakpaa Yesu baawako nwɔ.
Di obe wɔ di Pilato lawɛ ni di kakankɔ, ɔsɔfɔ lakpee nwɔ otii alɛ, “Diki nnɛɛ lɛfɔ di otii wɔ ninambla ni okpile ɔlaa kamɛ.
Diekye kɔsa kukakyɛ, diɛ alaafɔ nii kamɛ, diabuo mi ta nnwɔɔ oso.” Kafɔɔ olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo nwu nkpo lakpee batii dikudi nwu nkpo ɔtɔ alɛ, baakaalɛ Pilato alɛ adiɛ Baraba ata ma, aalo Yesu.
Ninfɛ di Pilato lakaalɛ batii dikudi nwu nkpo alɛ, “Batii ba mmle banyɔ, ɔmɛnle lɛma biomiɛ bilɛ ndiɛ nta ye?” Ninfɛ baadiki kanya alɛ, “Baraba!” Ni di Pilato lakple aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe biomiɛ bilɛ mbla Yesu wɔ manlɛɛ ni Kristo nwu?” Ninfɛ di bamuu lɛma baakyako ɔfaa obuɛ alɛ, “Pɛ nwɔ sibuɛ fakaasa koowoso suoto nɛ!” Kafɔɔ Pilato lakple aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ɔmɛnkpile ɛɛbla fiɛ?” Kafɔɔ mia nfɛ baakple baatɔɔfaa osie kanya baatoobuɛ alɛ, “Pɛ nwɔ sibuɛ fakaasa koowoso suoto nɛ!” Di obe wɔ di Pilato lanya alɛ ɔlɔbasinfuo ni lele kuniwii ɔbla, kafɔɔ kudu nfɛ nimadie ni yi, ni aayɔ ntu, aafoto nnɛɛ nɔɔ di batii nwu nkpo dikudi anu, aabuɛ alɛ, “Nnɛɛ nii diesi di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle kukpi kamɛ lo!
Oleye kule lo!” Ninfɛ di batii dikudi nwu nkpo bamuu labuɛ alɛ, “Kukpi nɔɔ lɛkpaani ditika di awo ku babiloo disi!” Ninfɛ di Pilato ladiɛ Baraba aata ma nɛ.
Kafɔɔ obe wɔ aata baapɛ Yesu ku mpile baaloo nii, ni aayɔ nwɔ aakpee ma ninnɛɛ alɛ balaapɛ nwɔ bakaasa di kowosa suoto nɛ.
Roma Batii Bakpɛtɛ Nwu Nkpo, Lakpee Yesu Sinunsɔ.
Ninfɛ di Pilato bakpɛtɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo lakpaa Yesu baasifiko abaa nwu kaflɔnkɔ, ninfɛ di bakpɛtɛ nwu nkpo bamuu lamana nwɔ baakyi nɛ.
Ninfɛ baaklee nwɔ akpeele baadiki di suoto, ni baayɔ awu sɛɛle ya niefũ ni kɔya wua baakpa nwɔ nɛ.
Ni baabla sɛkansi lɛkakoto baatũkũsɔɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ baayɔ ɔkyɛnwoso onwii baakleesɔɔ di koletanɛɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ baapɛ akunkyi kaatũ nɔɔ baama nwɔ baatɔɔtaa siwidi alɛ, “Yii yiiduu!
Yuda batii Ɔka, asiɛ nkpa aklɛ!” Ni baatufa sita baakpete nwɔ di suoto nɛ, ni baafũ owoso ninnɛɛ nɔɔ baatɔɔpɛ nwɔ diisi nɛ.
Di obe wɔ baaloo nwɔ ni ɔma, baadiki nwɔ awu sɛɛle nwu di suoto baakplesa awu nɔɔ amu baakpee nwɔ.
Ninfɛ baakpaa nwɔ baasifiko alɛ bɔɔlaapɛ nwɔ sibuɛ mankaasa koowoso suoto nɛ.
Baapɛ Yesu Sibuɛ Baakaasa Koowoso Suoto.
Di obe wɔ batoodie boosifi nii, ni baakyakako osuɔtɔ onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Simon nɛ.
Aakye Kirene kasɔ.
Ninfɛ di bakpɛtɛ nwu nkpo layila nwɔ di suoto alɛ afũ Yesu kowoso nwu nkpo atuka nɛ.
Ni baakpaa Yesu baalaadu lɛba le manlɛɛ ni Golgota lɛɛsɔdiki ninle ni alɛ Otii Disi Dikufi.
Ninfɛ baayɔ nta be bɛɛkpɔtɔɔsa ni ku kɔfa lonle baata Yesu alɛ anyi nɛ.
Kafɔɔ obe wɔ aatu aanyu nii, aasĩ mi onyi.
Ninfɛ di bakpɛtɛ nwu nkpo lapɛ nwɔ sibuɛ baakaasa koowoso suoto nɛ.
Nni kamaa, baayɔ awu nɔɔ baasɛ bawo di obe wɔ baawii ni atrebi baatofo n-ya di obiala lɛma kayɔ nii.
Nni kamaa, ni baasiɛ ninfa baatoonyu nwɔ nɛ.
Ni baayɔ kataabookyɛɛ baapɛ baakaasa di lɛkantosi nɔɔ, ni baakpana lɛsaa le oso beelo nwɔ nii alɛ, “Nnya Yesu Yuda Batii Ɔka Nwu Ninle Nwɔ Nɛ.” Baapɛ bayu banyɔ kafɔɔ sibuɛ baakaasa di awoso suoto diɛ Yesu ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Onwii lakaa diɛ oletanɛɛkyɛ nɔɔ, onwii kafɔɔ lakaa diɛ ɔmɛntukyɛ.
Batii ba niatoofe ni ninfa bamuu latũkunsa asi, baatufa Yesu baabuɛ alɛ, “Afɔ niabuɛ falɛ fababiɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ ka mmle, fanse ni letofo di ayi atiɛ kamɛ nɛ!
Nse Yaa Obi fale nwaako, faasoo koowoso nwu fawa, faafũ suoto lɛfɔ nkpa buonyu!” Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo nwu nkpo kafɔɔ lama nwɔ alɛ, “Aafũ batii bamba nkpa, kafɔɔ oloofuo suoto nɔɔ odiki.
Diele nnwɔɔ ninle Yuda batii Ɔka nwu nkpo nɛ?
Asoo koowoso nwu nkpo suoto awa buofũ nwɔ bunu!
Eetika Yaa disi, ɔɔlɛɛ suoto kafɔɔ alɛ Yaa Obi ale.
Nse nwaako Yaa mbɔmbɔ nwɔ yi, ni aabafũ nwɔ buonyu!” Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di bayu banyɔ ba baapɛ baakaasa ni di awoso suoto ku nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ latufa nwɔ nɛ.
Yesu Lakpi.
Kakũ lefosi elomu ɛnyɔ lebe, kayi kamuu lawɔfɔ, dialaase di kɔtɔɔfɔ elomu etiɛ kamɛ.
Di kɔtɔɔfɔ elomu etiɛ kamɛ okle, Yesu lafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Eli, Eli, lama sabaktani?” Lɛsɔdiki ninle alɛ, “Yaa nii, Yaa nii, be oso feediɛ mi nnɛɛ nkpo?” Batii ba bawo niayila ni ninfa, baanu ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, “Ɔɔlɛɛ Elia!” Nfanwu onwii kaamɛ lɛma latoso aalaayɔ oleteku aanyɔ di nta nyankale kamɛ, aayɔ aatũ di owoso suoto, aamiɛ alɛ ɔɔyɔ ankyɔɔ nwɔ annyi.
Kafɔɔ batii bamba labuɛ alɛ, “Bita buyila buonyu, nse Elia kamawa amadiki nwɔ di kowoso suoto.” Yesu lakple aafaa lɛyɛntɛle, ninfɛ niinwuna nɔɔ ladie nɛ.
Nfanwu, dibula le ninsaka ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ niabɛ di akyuu anyɔ diakye di osi dialaase kaasɔ.
Kasɔ kafɔɔ latukũ, afuɔ labibiɛ.
Sɛkya kafɔɔ labɛ siatikiti, Yaa batii klekle ba nintookpi bɛɛbafe ni bawo lataka baakye bakpi kamɛ.
Baadie di sɛkya lɛma kamɛ obe wɔ di Yesu lakple aataka aakye ni bakpi kamɛ yi, baasifi Yerusalem okpoo klekle nwu nkpo kamɛ baalaadiki suoto baatuo batii kpinwu.
Di obe wɔ di bakpɛtɛ ɔnɔɔfo ku bakpɛtɛ nwu nkpo niayila baatonyu ni Yesu lanya mmle okle kaasɔ latukũ ni ku aasaa ya amuu niabla ni yi, lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ ma osie kanya!
Ninfɛ baabuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako, Yaa Obi ninle otii wɔ mmle!” Basanko ba kpinwu kafɔɔ niatikanko Yesu baatɔɔkyakaako nwɔ ni, baakye ni Galilea lawɛ ninfa.
Baayila kaakyonkɔ baatoonyu asaa ya niatɔɔwa nii.
Basanko nwu nkpo bawo kaamɛ lɛma niale Maria Magdalene, Maria wɔ ninle ni Yakobo ku Yosef ɔya ku Sebedeo ɔsɔfɔ.
Yosef Wɔ Niakye Ni Arimatea Lakookaa Yesu Kpi.
Obe wɔ kɔɔtɔɔfɔ lawo nii, osuɔtɔ onwii niale ni saawɛntɛ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Yosef lawa, aakye Arimatea.
Yesu saateketetɛ aale.
Aakyɛ Pilato nfũ alɛ ayɔ Yesu kpi atɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Pilato lata osuku alɛ balaayɔ kpi nwu nkpo batɔɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yosef lasifi aalaayɔ kpi nwu nkpo, ni aayɔ dibula fututu aamiminisa nwɔ di suoto nɛ.
Ninfɛ aayɔ nwɔ aalaakokaa di ofuɔntuu ɔkya fɔle wɔ aakutu aata ni suoto kamɛ nɛ.
Ninfɛ aamunusa difuɔ dibinte ninwii aatĩi ofuɔntuu nwu kanya nɛ.
Ni aasifi nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Maria Magdalene ku Maria nyɔɔfa lasiɛ ninfa baakyɔɔ ɔkya nwu nkpo anu nɛ.
Basaanyuntɛ Layila Baatoonyu Yesu Ɔkya Nwu Nkpo.
Kaleesɛ niale ni Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi yi, olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku Farisi batii lalɛɛ bawo di Pilato nfũ.
Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, buonyuma bulɛ obe wɔ di laatɛ nwu nkpo lasiɛ ni nkpa yi, aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Nse lekpi yi, makple ntaka nkye bakpi kamɛ di ayi atiɛ kamɛ.’ Nkpo oso ta falɛ basaanyuntɛ lɛlaayila beenyu ɔkya nwu nkpo osie kanya diɛlaase di ayi atiɛ kamɛ.
Nse faata babla nle mmle yi, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ makyɛ manayu nwɔ mansifiko, manatɔkɔ batii alɛ, ‘Atɔɔtaka eekye bakpi kamɛ.’ Nse diɛwa ninkpo yi, sɛlaa kuafunu se babakple malaa ni malenkee lɛkasale.” Ninfɛ di Pilato latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bita bakpɛtɛ bakyɛ balaayila banyu ɔkya nwu nkpo fɛ mmle dikaatɛ ni.” Ninfɛ baakyɛ baalaatĩi ɔkya nwu nkpo kanya osie kanya baatɛ nwu nsũ nɛ.
Ninfɛ baadiki bakpɛtɛ baase baatoonyu ɔkya nwu nkpo nɛ.
Yaa Lasɛnkɛsa Yesu Aakyeko Bakpi Kamɛ.
Obe wɔ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi ntɔbafe nii, di Kɔsida kolesɛtũ, Maria Magdalene ku Maria wɔ nyɔɔfa lakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaanyu Yesu ɔkya nwu nkpo.
Nfanwu, kasɔ latũkũ osie kanya.
Ni di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ onwii lasoo aakye osi aawa, abamunusa difuɔ nwu nkpo di ɔkya kanya, ni aasiɛ ni di suoto nɛ.
Suoto nɔɔ odiki otuo late fɛ ɔplalaa nimunaa, awu nɔɔ kafɔɔ lapu fɛle oleteku.
Lɛyɛkɛ lamufũ basaanyuntɛ nwu nkpo osie kanya, baakyako otũtũkũ baaklee baabla fɛ bakpi.
Ninfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ basanko nwu alɛ, “Bitanyɛkɛ.
N-ye nlɛ Yesu wɔ baapɛ sibuɛ baakaasa ni koowoso suoto biowolaa.
Anaa ninfũ.
Atɔɔtaka akpe nkpa fɛ mmle aatɔkɔ ye nii.
Biwa biɛbanyu lɛba le baatɛ nwu ni.
Kanunua bipɛsɛwa biɛtɔɔkyɛ bilaatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ bilɛ, ‘Aatɔɔtaka eekye bakpi kamɛ.
Atoole ye katũ oofe Galilea.
Nfa bibanyɔɔ nɛ.’ Binyuma ɔlaa wɔ lɛtɔkɔ ye ni!” Nkpo oso baapɛsɛwa baakyɛ di ɔkya nwu katũ baasifi.
Baatɔɔyɛkɛ, kafɔɔ suoto latɔyɔɔ ma baatoso alɛ bɔɔlaatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ɔlaa nwu nkpo.
Nfanwu, Yesu lakyakako ma di osuku.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Atoko ɔkyɛ ole disiɛko ye.” Ninfɛ baakpukuti baatɛɛtɛ nwɔ, baamufũ nwɔ nkpaa, baasumu nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitanyɛkɛ.
Bitɔɔkyɛ biɛlaatɔkɔ babiloo bilɛ, batɔɔkyɛ Galilea, babanyɛɛ ninfa.” Basaanyuntɛ Nwu Nkpo Lakyɛ Baalaabuɛ Lɛsaa Le Baanya Nii.
Di obe wɔ di basanko nwu nkpo ntɔɔkyɛ boosifi nii, basaanyuntɛ nwu nkpo bawo niatoonyu ni ɔkya nwu nkpo, baasifi okpoo kamɛ baalaatɔkɔ olebatatɛ banɔɔfo asaa ya amuu niawa ni ninfa.
Ninfɛ di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nwu nkpo ku okpoo banɔɔfo, lalɛɛ bawo baabla disibu nɛ.
Ni baata basaanyuntɛ nwu nkpo koto dikudi kplɛ ninwii nɛ, ni baatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bibuɛ bilɛ obe wɔ bite biɔkyɔsĩi ni ku kakyɛ, ni baasaateketetɛ nɔɔ labayu nwɔ baasifiko nɛ.
Nse Abaa Nɔɔfo lenu ɔlaa wɔ mmle kafɔɔ yi, bubablako nwu ɔkpɛ, muntɔɔ annu kasɔ bulɛ, diele aye ninkyɛnko.” Basaanyuntɛ nwu nkpo lafũ koto nwu nkpo baabla fɛ mmle okle baakpee ma nii.
Nioso ɔlaa lɛma nwu nkpo labiɛ kuabuo di Yuda batii kamɛ diɛbase bia miɛ.
Yesu Ladiki Suoto Aatuo Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi onwii nwu nkpo, lakata baasifi Galilea di kobokote ko suoto di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ basifi ni nɛ.
Di obe wɔ baanyɔɔ nii, baase akunkyi kaasɔ baasumu nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ batii bawo kaamɛ lɛma ditafũ baanu alɛ nnwɔɔ diale.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakpukuti aatɛɛtɛɛ ma ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Yaa lɛyɔ osi ku kasɔ osie omuu eekpee mi di nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Nkpo oso bitɔɔkyɛ kayi ka mmle nnle mmuu kamɛ, biɛlaabla batii basaateketetɛ nii.
Biekpeesa ma Yaa ntu di Ote, Obi, ku Ninwuna Klekle leyooto kamɛ.
Bietuo ma bilɛ bakyɔɔ asaa ya amuu letuo ye ni atoko.
Nwaako kamasiɛko ye obe lele ninaadu bia kayi ka mmle kalookɔ.”
Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane Layie Lɛkya.
Nnya ɔlaa biene wɔ niekye ni Yesu Kristo Yaa obi suoto kasɔ kakyekɔ.
Binyu!
Diawa fɛ mmle di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yesaia lakpana aatɛ ni kofokofoko alɛ, “Makyesee tɔkyɛntɛ nii anle fɔ katũ, aanaalolaa osuku antɛ fɔ.
Otii nwu matooyie lɛkya di ɔfaafuu antoobuɛ alɛ, ‘Bilolaa osuku bitɛ bita Saate nwu ɔwabee.
Bikyɛkyɛsa abaya abafe ni bitɛ nwɔ.’ ” Yohane Lakpeesa Yesu Yaa Ntu Di Yordan Okle Kamɛ.
Tɔkyɛntɛ nwu niale Yohane nɛ.
Aawɛ di ɔfaafuu aabatookpeesa batii Yaa ntu.
Aatɔɔtakɔ ma alɛ, “Bidiɛ sikpile lee ɔbla baakpeesa ye Yaa ntu, ni Yaa mayɔ sikpile lee ankyɛ ye.” Batii kpinwu lakye Yudea kasɔ ku Yerusalem okpoo kplɛ baakyɛ ɔfaafuu baalaanu Yohane ɔlaa.
Baadiki sikpile lɛma baabuɛ ni aakpeesa ma Yaa ntu di Yordan okle kamɛ nɛ.
Di obe wɔ mmle kamɛ Yohane lakpee kapupɔnkɔ sinwini awu, ni aayɔ bɔkɛɛ kukũ okũ aatika ofiamɛ nɛ.
Alesaa nɔɔ niale akpakyekyee ku bablɔ.
Ɔlaa wɔ aatoobuɛ ninle alɛ, “Otii wɔ nimawa ni sɛɛmaa nii nlenke mi.
Ale Otii wɔ ninansiɛko alɛ bia kadiki nwɔ ni ntokota fɛ kpɛmblatɛ.
