Ami ntu kɔyɔ nkpeesa ye Yaa ntu, kafɔɔ nnwɔɔ abayɔ Ninwuna Klekle ankpeesa ye kaamɛ.” Ditaklɛ, Yesu lakye Nasarɛt diɛ Galilea kasɔ aawa, ni di Yohane lakpeesa nwɔ Yaa ntu di Yordan okle kamɛ nɛ.
Nfanwu di Yesu latoodie ni di ntu nwu kamɛ, aanya kolo lasɛkɛtɛ, ni di Ninwuna Klekle latoosoo di suoto nɔɔ fɛ mmle di lɛlaapɔɔ nsoo ni nɛ.
Ni baanu sɛɛlɔ lakye osi siabuɛ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Obi nii wɔ suoto ninantuna ni nɛ, foobuo mi anu nwaa.” Nfanwu Ninwuna Klekle lakpaa nwɔ aasifiko ɔfaafu.
Ni aasiɛ ninfa lete nɔɔ ayi afosi ana Satana lasɔ nwɔ aanyu nse abatikanko nwɔ.
Babɔkɛɛ ba ninkpe ni kobe lawɛ ninfa, kafɔɔ di obe nwu kamɛ Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ lakye osi baabakpee nwɔ osie.
Yesu Ladiki Basaateketɛ Kasale.
Obe wɔ baatɛ ni Yohane leeyo katenkɔ sɛmaa, Yesu lakyɛ Galilea kasɔ aalaatoobuɛ ɔlaa biene wɔ niekye ni Yaa nfũ.
Aatoobuɛ alɛ, “Obe biene nwu ntoowo, Yaa sɛka ole bee ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ, bidiɛ sikpile ɔbla biefũ ɔlaa biene nwu binu!” Obe wɔ di Yesu latoofe ni di Galilea lekpo ɔlɔɔkɔ, aanya kɔkpaku badikitɛ banyɔ banwii, Simon ku obilɛma Andrea baatoodiki kɔkpaku ku asawu.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biwa biɛbatikankoe, matuo ye mmle mandiki ni batii.” Nfanwu ni baadiɛ asawu lɛma, baatikanko nwɔ nɛ.
Aakyɛ ni sitũ kɛɛkɛ, ni aanya babilɛma banyɔ banwii ninle ni Sebedeo babi Yakobo ku Yohane, baasiɛ di oklo kamɛ baatoololaa asawu lɛma.
Di Yesu lanya ma nii, ni aalɛɛ ma alɛ batikanko nwɔ nɛ.
Ni baadiɛ ote lɛma Sebedeo ku bakpɛntɛ nɔɔ di oklo kamɛ baatikanko nwɔ nɛ.
Yesu Latososa Ninwuna Kpile Di Osuɔtɔ Onwii Kamɛ.
Ni baasifi Kapernaum okpoo nɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yuda batii Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi nwu lawo nii, Yesu lasifi kasiisakɔ lɛma, ni aalaakya ko batii asaa otuo nɛ.
Asaa nɔɔ otuo labla ma ɔkpɛ, diekye aatuo ma asaa fɛ otii wɔ ninkpe ni otumi, ninanle ni fɛ mmle di kufiofa batuotɛ ntuo nii.
Nfanwu osuɔtɔ onwii di ninwuna kpile lasiɛ nii lawɛ kaamɛ lɛma, ni aafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Be foomiɛ di ɔkyɛ loo, afɔ Yesu Nasaret Otii ntɛɛ?
Ɔwɔɔsa fɛɛwa wo?
N-ye otii wɔ fale nii!
Afɔ ninle Otii Klekle wɔ di Yaa lekyesee ni nɛ!” Ni di Yesu lamuɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lo kanana, faadie nwɔ kaamɛ!” Ni di ninwuna kpile nwu latũkunsa osuɔtɔ nwu osie kanya, ni aafaa osie kanya, ni diadie nɛ.
Diabla batii ba niayila ni ninfa bamuu ɔkpɛ diata baatɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Be nɛ?
Asaa otuo fɔle ale?
Ɛɛyɔ otumi ootososa anwuna kpile annu!” Ta nkpo oso Yesu leyooto lakyaka Galilea kasɔ kamuu.
Yesu Lakya Batii Sifiɛ.
Nfanwu di Yesu ku batii nɔɔ ladie ni kaasiisakɔ nwu, baakpaa Yakobo ku Yohane baasifi Simon ku Andrea leyo.
Baabuo ni nfa batii bawo latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, Simon ɔmaato nte ofiɛ lɛwɔɔfɔ ofiɛ.
Nioso Yesu lakyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ aalaamufũ nwɔ kɔɔnɛɛ aatakatɛsa, ni di ofiɛ layɔɔ nwɔ nɛ, ni aataka aanyu ma kanya nɛ.
Obe wɔ kuufĩ ntɔɔmɛɛ nii, baakpaa bafiɛtɛ kpinwu ku mba di anwuna kpile nsi ni baawako Yesu ɔkyɛ alɛ ayɔɔsa ma sifiɛ.
Ni diɛ okpoo nwu batii bamuu labasi diɛ kayokontũ nwu baatoonyu nɛ.
Ni aakya batii ba bamuu niatoofiɛ ni sifiɛ ate ate sifiɛ.
Ni aatososa anwuna kpile atata nya osuku alɛ akakatɛ, diekye anwuna kpile nwu latofo otii wɔ okle ale nii.
Yesu Layie Ɔlaa Biene Nwu Lɛkya Di Galilea Kasɔ.
Yesu lataka kuyitatũ aadie leeyo aasifi lɛba le nialo ni lete nɔɔ, aalaapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa.
Sɛmaa Simon ku bawo nɔɔ lakyɛ baalaatowolaa Yesu.
Obe wɔ baanyɔɔ nii, baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Otii biala kowolaa fɔ!” Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bita busifi sekpoo bibii bamba se niɛtɛɛtɛɛ ni, ninaabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa ninfa kafɔɔ nta ma, diekye nni oso lɛwa nɛ.” Nioso aakyɛ aatookyi nsiisakɔ lɛma nwu diɛ Galilea kasɔ aatoobuɛ Yaa ɔlaa, aatootososa anwuna kpile baatii suoto.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Niatoofiɛ Ni Ofiɛ Sɛɛle Ofiɛ.
Ni di osuɔtɔ onwii niatoofiɛ ni ofiɛ sɛɛle lawa Yesu ɔkyɛ aalaapɛ akunkyi, aatootikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, “Nse dilɛ fɔ, faafuo ɔta suoto nii mbla klekle.” Ɔlaa nɔɔ lakpɛ nwɔ nyaami, ni di Yesu ladiki kɔnɛɛ aakpanko nwɔ, aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Letuna, suoto lɛfɔ siklekle!” Nfanwu, ofiɛ sɛɛle nwu layɔɔ nwɔ suoto nɔɔ laklekle.
Ni di Yesu ladiki nwɔ osuku aakpee nwɔ kufiofa alɛ, “Nyu, tanaabuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle faatɔkɔ otii kuonwii, tɔɔkyɛ falaadiki suoto fatuo Yaa oletatɛ, faata ole di mmle di Mose lekpee kufiofa ɛɛtɛ ni di suoto okleklesa suoto, diatuo alɛ ɔfiɛ nwu ntɔɔyɔɔ fɔ ni.” Kafɔɔ aasifi nii, aalaatoobuɛ ɔlaa nwu aatɔɔkyakasa osie kanya, ta nkpo oso Yesu ditasinfuo kayi otoodie di okpoo kuonwii kamɛ.
Ɔfaafuu aatoosiɛ, kafɔɔ batii lakple baakye aba aba batɔɔwa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Niafefee Aate Ni Ofiɛ.
Ayi asɛɛ sɛmaa Yesu lakple aasifi Kapernaum okpoo.
Di obe kakui kamɛ batii lanu alɛ akpe leeyo.
Ni baatii kpinwu lasi diɛ leyo le aabuo nii, diata alɛ baalaadu bia kayokontũ, bawo ditasinwɛ kayilakɔ.
Ni aabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa aata ma nɛ.
Ni baatii bana latuka fiɛtɛ onwii niafefee nii baatɔɔwako ɔkyɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Batii lɛpɔ oso batawɛ osuku baatɛɛtɛɛ Yesu di leyo le kamɛ aawɛ nii, nioso baasifi baalaayie lɛkya osi baalaadufu kutuɛ, baasoosa fiɛtɛ nwu ku ɔkla nɔɔ wɔ suoto aate nii baatɛ kaasɔ di Yesu anu.
Di Yesu lanya ni ofũ onu lɛma oso aatɔkɔ fefeetɛ nwu alɛ, “Obi nii, ntɔɔyɔ sikpile lɛfɔ bɛɛkyɛ fɔ.” Obe nwu kamɛ Yuda batii kufiofa batuotɛ bawo lasiɛ ninfa, baatoobu di disi lɛma kamɛ alɛ, “Lɛ oso ɔɔkakatɛ nkpo?
Eebuɛ mbusuo ɔlaa di Yaa suoto.
Yaa lete nikafuo sikpile ɔyɔ ɔkyɛ!” Nfanwu Yesu latofo disbu lɛma ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Be oso biobu disi kpile nkpo?
Lɛmɛnle niɛyɔɔ dilenke, alɛ baatɔkɔ otii wɔ niefefee ate ni alɛ, ‘Bɛɛyɔ sikpile lɛfɔ bɛɛkyɛ fɔ’ ɛɛ sɛɛ baabuɛ alɛ, ‘Taka, faayɔ ɔkla lɛfɔ faakyɛ’?
Ta biatofo bilɛ, Otii Obi, nkpe otumi kaasɔ ka alɛ aayɔ sikpile ankyɛ nii.” Ni aatɔkɔ otii wɔ niefefe ate ni alɛ, “Kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ taka!
Yɔ ɔkla lɛfɔ, faasifi leyo!” Nfanwu otii wɔ niafefee aate ni niataka aayɔ ɔkla nɔɔ, aadie ma kaamɛ aasifi.
Diabla bamuu lɛma ɔkpɛ ni baatansa Yaa baabuɛ alɛ, “Buunya nnle mmle okle bunya!” Yesu Lalɛɛ Lewi Alɛ Atikanko Nwɔ.
Ni di Yesu lakple aadie ninfa aasifi Galilea lekpo kotoko ni baatii kpinwu lawa nwɔ ɔkyɛ ninfa ni aatuo ma asaa nɛ.
Obe wɔ aatoofe ni lekpo nwu kotoko ninfɛ aanya Lewi, Alfeo obi, asi di akpooto kafunkɔ oofũ akpooto, ni di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tikankoe!” Nfanwu ni aataka aatikanko nwɔ nɛ.
Dii nwu kɔtɔɔfɔ Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakyɛ Lewi leyo alɛ, bɔɔlaaleko nwɔ alesaa.
Batii kpinwu latikanko nwɔ, batii ba niatikanko nwɔ ni nkpo bawo niale akpooto bafuntɛ ku bakpileblatɛ.
Nioso obe wɔ di kufiofa batuotɛ ba ninle ni Farisi batii lanya alɛ Yesu kole ni alesaa ku bakpiletɛ ku akpooto bafuntɛ, baakaalɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Lɛ oso ole alesaa ku akpooto bafuntɛ ku bakpileblatɛ bamba ba mmle?” Obe wɔ di Yesu lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ boobuɛ nii, ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Fablatɛ diefĩ batii ba ninoofiɛ nii, bafiɛtɛ di fablatɛ lefĩ.
Ninwa babienetɛ ɔlɛɛ, bakpileblatɛ oso lɛwa.” Akaalɛ Di Kanya Onii Suoto.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, di Yohane basaateketetɛ ku Farisi basaateketetɛ nnii ni kanya oso, ni baatii bawo lawa baabakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Obe oso fiɛ diɛ Yohane basaateketetɛ ku Farisi basaateketetɛ nnii ni kanya fiɛ baasaateketetɛ lɛfɔ ninannii kanya?” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Lɛ di ɔkafɔɔsa basiɛwo kanii kanya obe wɔ di ɔkafɔɔsa nkpe ma ni di ɔkyɛ?
Balaafuo kanya onnii di obe wɔ akpe ma ni di ɔkyɛ.
Kafɔɔ obe kɔwa babakpaa ɔkafɔɔsa mansifiko nii, obe nwu kamɛ babanii kanya nɛ.
Kuonwii nín-yɔ dibula fɔle kakyɛɛ aakaa aatĩi dibula kofole kabɛkɔ.
Se ɛɛbla nkpo, dibula fɔle nwu matuunii ninsifi lekofole kabɛkɔ nwu ninfoofoosa ninkyakaa.
Kuonwii nín-yɔ nta fɔle aakpete di kɔbɔkɛɛkũ kotofo kofole kamɛ, se diɛwa ninkpo, nta fɔle nwu mata kotofo nwu mbɛ, ninta alɛ nta ku kotofo nwu nlalaa.
Kɔbɔkɛɛkũ fɔle kamɛ man-yɔ nta fɔle mankpete.” Yesu Kristo Ninle Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi Saate.
Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoofe di atita kofe kunwii kamɛ.
Ni di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ, lafee atita nwu kɔɔne awo baatoowee nɛ.
Ta nkpo oso Farisi batii bawo Lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Nyu!
Be oso baasaateketetɛ lɛfɔ kɔbla nkpo, kuufiofa loo ninanta ni osuku di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Sɛɛ biika lɛsaa le diɛ Ɔka Dawid ku batii nɔɔ labla ni di Kɔkpana Klekle kamɛ binya, obe wɔ kɔɔka lakle ma ni?
Mmle aabuo ni Yaa Olekatakɔ diɛ obe wɔ di Abiatar lale ni Yaa Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo.
Aadiki bloblo klekle wɔ mananta osuku alɛ otii wɔ ninanle ni Yaa oletatɛ kale ni aale ni, aayɔ owo aata manko bawo nɔɔ ba kafɔɔ niakyɛ ni bale ni?” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii dibiene oso di Yaa lɛbla Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi, ni diele Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi oso ɛɛbla otii.
Nioso ami, Otii Obi, ninle Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi Saate.”
Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Ofiɛ Di Kɔɔnɛɛ Nɔɔ Lakatu Nii.
Yesu lakple aakyɛ Yuda batii kasiisakɔ kanwii, otii onwii kɔɔnɛɛ nɔɔ lakatu ni lawɛ ninfa.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, Yesu balo lawɛ ninfa.
Baatoonyu osuku alɛ abayɔɔsa osuɔtɔ nwu ofiɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi nwu suoto mmle baayɔ ni ɔlaa di suoto nɔɔ.
Yesu latɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu kɔɔnɛɛ lɛkatu ni alɛ, “Taka fawa sitũ ninfũ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ batii nwu niawɛ ni ninfa alɛ, “Kufiofa lɛta osuku alɛ, baabla dibiene di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi ɛɛ sɛɛ dikpile?
Baafũ otii nkpa ɛɛ sɛɛ baadiɛ nwɔ ankpi?” Kafɔɔ baalo kanana.
Yesu lanyunyu ma aafenko ku ɔblɔ.
Disi osie lɛma oso kafutu lanyiyii nwɔ, ni aatɔkɔ fiɛtɛ nwu alɛ, “Yilasa kɔnɛɛ lɛfɔ!” Ni aayilasa kɔnɛɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Nfanwu ni kualɛ nɛ.
Nioso Farisi batii ladie baalaakpee asi baawo ku Herodes batikankotɛ nɔɔ bawo mmle baalo ni Yesu.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Batii Kpinwu Sifiɛ Di Galilea Lɛpanta Kotoko.
Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ladie ninfa baasifi Galilea lɛpanta kotoko.
Ni batii kpinwu niakye ni Galilea latikanko ma nɛ.
Batii dikudi kafɔɔ lakye Yudea, Yerusalem, Idumea ku Yordan okle sɛmaa kuɛ Tiro ku Sidon ntɛɛ nwu baawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ.
Diekye baanu Yesu sɛkpɛ kplɛ se aatɔɔbla nii.
Ta batii dikudi nwu lɛpɔ oso Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ bamiɛ oklo owo batɔɔ aasiɛ kaamɛ mmle baatii dikudi nwu dilaba pimpi nwɔ ni.
Aakya batii kpinwu sifiɛ, nioso diata alɛ bafiɛtɛ ba niakyɛ ni nfa latikanko baatoomiɛ osuku alɛ bɔɔkpanko nwɔ siifiɛ lɛma nyɔɔ ma.
Batii bawo lawɛ ninfa di anwuna kpile lasiɛ ma ni kaamɛ.
Nioso nse diɛwa alɛ bɛɛnya Yesu, manɔɔ nwɔ di nkpaatũ, manyiisa kudu mambuɛ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Yaa obi!” Kafɔɔ Yesu lakpee anwuna kpile nwu kufiofa osie kanya alɛ batanta batii latofo otii wɔ okle ale nii.
Yesu Ladiki Basaateketetɛ Lefosi Banyɔ Aata Suoto.
Nni sɛmaa Yesu lasifi kabokotee osi.
Nfa aalaadiki basaateketetɛ ba omiɛ ni nɛ.
Aadiki lefosi batii banyɔ ba aata ni leyoto alɛ batɔkyɛntɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ntoodiki ye nlɛ biatikankoe obe lele.
Makpee ye kafɔɔ minaatoobuɛ mi ɔlaa biene.
Mata ye otumi kafɔɔ mintososa anwuna kpile.” Nya batii ba di Yesu ladiki ni.
Mma ninle Simon wɔ di Yesu lata ni leyoto alɛ Petro ku Yakobo ku obilɛma suɔtɔbi Yohane mba ninle ni Sebedeo babi ba di Yesu lata ma ni leyoto alɛ Boanege, lɛɛsɔ diki nɔɔ ninle ni ɔplalaa.
Banyɛntɛle kafɔɔ ninle Andrea ku Filipo ku Bartolomeo ku Mateo ku Toma ku Yakobo wɔ ninle ni Alfeo obi ku Tadeo ku Simon wɔ niabɔmbɔ ni kale nɔɔ osie kanya kuɛ Yuda Iskariot wɔ niadiki Yesu aata nii.
Batii Latufa Yesu.
Yesu ladie ni ninfa, aawa leyo ninwii kamɛ.
Ni baati kpinwu lakple baabasi ninfa nɛ.
Batii lɛpɔ oso Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ditawɛ kayaa baale alesaa.
Baanantii nɔɔ lanu nii, baakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaakpaa nwɔ, diekye batii latoobuɛ alɛ, “Disi kamɛ kɔkpɔtɔɔ nwɔ!” Kufiofa batuotɛ ba niakye Yerusalem baawa ni labuɛ alɛ, “Anwuna kpile ɔka Beelsebul ninsi di Yesu kamɛ.
Nni suoto anfe antososa anwuna kpile baatii kamɛ nɛ!” Nioso Yesu lalɛɛ ma aawako ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, ni aakakatɛ aata ma di akpa kamɛ alɛ, “Lɛ di Abonsam kafuo suoto otososa odiki baatii kamɛ?
Nse sɛka kalekɔ kawo lɛsɛ kɛtaka keeyila di suoto nɔɔ, ni sɛka kalekɔ nwu dilabafuo oyila.
Nkpo kafɔɔ sɛ leyo lewo lɛsɛ di akyuu anyɔ bɔɔkpɛko bawo ni leyo nwu dilabafuo oyila.
Nioso se Abonsam sɛka kalekɔ lɛsɛ ɛtaka eyila di suoto nɔɔ, kalaansifuo oyila, ni kalookɔ ni ka nɛ.
“Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii kuonwii dilaafuo sientɛ leyo kamɛ obuo ɔlɛ nwɔ asaa, diediki ɛɛka nwɔ omufũ onii fiɛ aafuo nwɔ asaa ɔlɛ.
“Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ Yaa mayɔ otii okpile lele ɛɛbla ku sibusufuɔlaa se eebuɛ ni di suoto nɔɔ ankyɛ nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ olele nimabuɛ obusufɔlaa di Yaa Ninwuna Klekle suoto, Yaa dilabayɔ akyɛ nwɔ diidii, diekye eekpi lɛpɔɔ, ɛɛbla okpile wɔ nnaa ni kaloo.” Yesu labuɛ sɛlaa se mmle, diekye baatoobuɛ alɛ, ninwuna kpile nsi nnwɔɔ Yesu.
Bawe Ninle Yesu Babilɛma Sankobi Ku Babilɛma Suɔtɔbi.
Di obe nwu kamɛ Yesu ɔya ku Yesu basuɔtɔbi lɛma labayila kaayi, ni baakpee otii alɛ balɛɛ nwɔ bata ma.
Batii dikudi lasiɛ baamana nwɔ baakyi, ni baalaatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nyu, yaafɔ ku babilee n-yɛ kaayi boowolaa fɔ!” Ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Bawe ninle yaami omu ku babiloo bamu?” Ni aanyu batii ba ninsi bɛɛmana nwɔ beekyi ni, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Binyu, yaami ku babiloo ninle mba ninsi ni ninfũ nɛ!
Otii lele nikɔbla Yaa dibeesaa, nnwɔɔ ninle obiloo ku yaami nɛ.”
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Alesaa Kubi Santɛ Suoto.
Yesu lakple aakye asaa katuosɔ diɛ Galilea Lekpo kotoko, batii dikudi lamana nwɔ baakyi.
Batii nwu lɛpɔ oso aalaayie aasiɛ di oklo wɔ niatika ni di ntu osi.
Batii dikudi nwu kafɔɔ layila di lekpo nwu kotoko.
Atuo asaa kpinwu diɛ akpa kamɛ.
Di asaa otuo nɔɔ kamɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Binu lo!
Obe onwii alesaa kubi santɛ onwii lakyɛ kofe aalaasa alesaa kubi.
Obe wɔ ɔɔsa ni alesaa kubi nwu nkpo koofe, kowo lakpete di osuku suoto, ni baakansiɛ lasɛsɛɛ kũ baamɛ nɛ kowo kafɔɔ lakpete di afuɔ kasɔ, nfũ kɔɔtɛ diɛpɔ nii.
Kɔtɛ ɔtampɔ oso, aawolaa ɔkɔntɔ.
Obe wɔ kuufĩ labadie nii aayɔɔ, aafiɛ diekye sidu nɔɔ diɛkyɛ kasɔ ta afuɔ nwu oso.
Kowo kafɔɔ labuo kakɔtɔkɔtɔ siiwuu kamɛ, ɔɔkɔntɔ anwa nii, siiwuu nwu kafɔɔ lakɔntɔ siafukuti siatĩi nya, nioso atafuo otika.
Alesaa kubi nwu kowo kafɔɔ lakpete di kasɔ biene suoto.
Nnya aakɔntɔ, aamuɔ aatika abi.
Awo latika afosi atiɛ, awo afosi akuɔ, awo kafɔɔ latika kɔlafa.” Yesu layɛntɛ ku sɛlaa se mmle alɛ, “Otii wɔ kuunutoko nkpe nii yi, aanu!” Yesu Ladiki Lɛkpa Nwu Kasɔ Aata Batikankotɛ Nɔɔ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lete nfɛ nsi nii, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ku lefosi batii banyɔ nwu lawa babakaalɛ nwɔ akpa nwu kasɔ.
Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Yaa lediki asaa ya ninsi ni di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɛɛta ye.
Kafɔɔ batii ba nsi ni sɛɛlɔɔkɔ, mma yi, akpa kamɛ babanu sɛlaa.
Nioso, ditɔɔwa fɛ mmle bɛɛkpana ni Kɔɔkpana Klekle kamɛ alɛ, ‘Babanya, mankple manya, kafɔɔ blɔbanya batɛnsũ.
Babanu, mankple manu, kafɔɔ blɔbanu kasɔ.
Nse beenu kasɔ, bɛɛnya bɛɛtɛ nsũ, babakyi siitu lɛma kamɛ, Yaa n-yɔ sikpile lɛma ankyɛ ma!’ ” Yesu Lediki Lɛkpa Le Aapɛ Ni Kasɔ Di Alesaa Kubi Santɛ Suoto Aata Ma.
Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Biénu lɛkpa le mmle kasɔ?
Ni lɛ bibafuo akpa bule amuu kasɔ onu?
Alesaa kubi santɛ kɔsa Yaa ɔlaa nwu.
Batii bawo nte fɛ alesaa kubi ko niakpete ni di osuku kotoko, nse beenu ɔlaa nwu, nfanwu Abonsam nwa amadiki ɔlaa nwu di situ lɛma kamɛ ansifiko.
Batii bamba kafɔɔ nte fɛ kubi ko niakpete ni di afuɔ kasɔ.
Nfanwu nse beenu ɔlaa nwu manfũ nwu ku suoto lɛyɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ ɔlaa nwu sidu nimmufũ kaasɔ nwaa.
Obe kakuii kamɛ ko manfũ nwu manu.
Diekye nse nimiina ee ditikanko lɛwa ma di suoto di ɔlaa nwu ofũ onu kamɛ, mankple nkpaamaa.
“Batii bawo kafɔɔ nte fɛ kubi ko niakpete ni di kakɔtɔkɔtɔ siwuu kamɛ.
Mma ninle batii ba ninu ni ɔlaa biene nwu, kafɔɔ kayi ka mmle amiina ku koto onumbɛbɛɛ, ku asaa bamba ɔkɔnsɔ oklee nfukuti kuntĩi ɔlaa nwu alɛ, kunfuo abi otika.
“Batii bawo kafɔɔ nte fɛ kubi ko niakpete ni kaasɔ nwaa suoto.
Baanu ɔlaaa biene nwu, baafũ nwu baanu baatika abi.
Awo afosi atiɛ, awo afosi akuɔ, awo kafɔɔ kɔlafa.” Kandiɛ Ɔkpɛ Wɔ Ambla Nii Ninle Alɛ Anta Lɛkpa.
Yesu lakple aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Nse bɛɛsɔ kandiɛ man-yɔ lɛsaa mantĩi nwɔ?
Ee mpa kalɔ manse wɔ?
Diele lɛsaa suoto man-yɔ mantika alɛ aakpa nwaa?
Lɛsaa lele beekookaa Yaa madiki ni kayi, lɛsaa lele kafɔɔ beetĩi Yaa matikiti ni.
Otii wɔ kunutoko nkpe ni, alolaa anu nwaa!” Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bikyɔɔ atoko nwaa di sɛlaa se bionu ni suoto!
Diekye leklapoosaa le biɛyɔ biɛklapoosa biɛta ni bawo lee, nninwu ke di Yaa mayɔ anklapoosa anta ye nɛ, bia lele ye malenkee.
Diekye otii wɔ niɛkyɔɔ mi ni ɔlaa kotoko abawɛ lɛsɔnu ankyakaa.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ ninankyɔɔ mi ni ɔlaa kotoko kɛɛkɛɛ wɔ aye nii, Yaa maklee anfũ nwɔ ni nnɛɛ.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Asaa Omuɔ Suoto.
Yesu lakple abuɛ alɛ, “Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nte fɛ mmle di otii nsa ni kamɔɔ kubi koofe.
Nse kale ntooloo otii nwu naate ankyɔsĩi, nse kale ntɔɔsɛ antaka, kafɔɔ aaye mmle diɛ kamɔɔ kubi nwu mbla fiɛ kunkɔntɔ kuntika ni abi ambe nii.
Kasɔ kamu ninta kamɔɔ kubi nwu mmuɔ kantika abi lɛnya.
Lɛkasale kankɔntɔ, afata ndie.
Sɛmaa kanlaka amɛ kandie kufuo, nni sɛmaa kansiɛ abi kanyi ntu kambe.
Nse abi nwu ntoobe, fɛkpɛntɛ nwu n-yɔ kasaka diekye ofiɛlɛ bee ntoowo.” Lɛkpa Diɛ Lewosobi Biibii Suoto.
Yesu lakple aabuɛ alɛ, “Be suoto kayɔ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nkaatɛɛsa?
Lɛmɛnkpa kayɔ ndiki ni kasɔ?
Dite fɛ lewosobi biibii lewo.
Fiɛ babapɛ ni nii, ninle lewosobi biibii diɛ awosobi kamɛ kaasɔ ka mmle suoto.
Kafɔɔ nse bɛɛpɛ ni nintaka, nimuɔ ninlenkee awoso amuu.
Kundie sɛla kplɛ, kunwɛ oyududu, ninwa alɛ bakansiɛ mbla ayo diɛ oyududu nɔɔ kalɔ masiɛ.” Yesu latɔkɔ batii nwu ɔlaa biene di akpa ya mmle okle kamɛ, ni mmle okle baanu nwɔ ni kasɔ.
Akpa lete kamɛ anfe ankakatɛ anta batii, kafɔɔ nse manko basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lete basi andiki asaa amuu kasɔ anta ma.
Yesu Layilasa Afɛɛfɔ Siene.
Diɛ dii nwu nkpo kɔtɔɔfɔ, Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bita butaalɛ busifi lekpo le mmle sɛmaa.” Nioso baadiɛ batii dikudi nwu baasifi baalaabuo di oklo wɔ di Yesu labuo aasiɛ nii, ni baakpaa nwɔ baasifi nɛ.
Seklo bamba kafɔɔ layila ninfa.
Nfanwu kɔfɛɛfɔ siene lakyako ɔfɛ, ntu kɔpɛ nimbuo diɛ oklo kamɛ diɛta alɛ ntu laloo oklo kamɛ oyii baamɛɛ nii.
Di obe nwu kamɛ Yesu omu lasiɛ diɛ oklo nwu sɛmaa lɛkyɛ, aatika disi di sumuyɛ aatɔɔkyɔsĩi.
Ni baasaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasɛnkɛsɔɔ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, faayɔ nwu ole falɛ buoloo okpi?” Nioso Yesu lasɛnkɛ.
Aataka aayila nii, aamuɛ kɔfɛɛfɔ nwu aabuɛ alɛ, “Diɛ ɔfɛ!” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ lɛkpo nwu alɛ, “Te kloklo!” Kɔfɛɛfɔ nwu ladiɛ ɔfɛ, ni dialo kanana nɛ.
Ni di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be oso biɔyɛkɛ nkpo?
Biefũ mi binu?” Lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ ma osie kanya ni baakaalɛ nimanima alɛ, “Omɛntii okle ninle nwɔ di kɔfɛɛfɔ ku lɛkpo nnu nwɔ ɔlaa?”
Yesu Latososa Ninwuna Kpile Di Osuɔtɔ Onwii Kamɛ.
Nni sɛmaa, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lataalɛ baalaadu Galilea lekpo nwu kakyɛ nyɔɔfa di Gadara batii kasɔ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lasoo ni di oklo kamɛ, otii onwii niinwuna kpile lasiɛ ni ladie aakye sifuɔntuu se kamɛ mankookaa ni bakpi aabakyakako Yesu.
Nfa ninle osuɔtɔ nwu kasiɛkɔ nɛ, otii kuonwii ninfuo kɔnyɛnɛ kukunwii ɔyɔ onii nwɔ.
Obe lele se beekpee nwɔ sɛkpɛnkyɛ ninnɛɛ ku ninkpaa anfee sĩ.
Nse kafɔɔ beenii nwɔ ku abɔɔsaa kɔnyɛnɛ ambudi kũ.
Sientɛ kuonwii ditawɛ anfuo nwɔ ni olenkee.
Ansiɛ di batii kakookakɔ ku abokote kakũ ku kakyɛ aakyɛ aatookyi, antooyiisa kudu obe lele.
An-yɔ afuɔ antɔɔkyankya suoto.
Obe wɔ aanya ni Yesu kaakyonkɔ aatoso aalaapɛ akunkyi kaatũ nɔɔ.
Ni aayiisa kudu osie kanya alɛ, “Be ɔlaa ninsi di awo ku afɔ ntɛɛ, Yesu, Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni obi!
Yaa oso, kotikiti fɔ lekoto, tannanfi mi kotoko!” Aabuɛ sɛlaa se mmle diekye Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninwuna kpile die nwɔ kaamɛ!” Ni di Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛ manlɛɛ fɔ?” Aadiki kanya alɛ, “Leyooto nii ninle dikudi, diekye buɔtɛ bupɔ!” Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle di ninwuna kpile nsi nii, latikiti Yesu lekoto osie kanya alɛ atantososa anwuna nwu aadiki nintɛɛ nwu.
Di obe nwu kamɛ aplakuo ɔlambu kplɛ onwii latoole asaa di kabokotee ɔlɔkɔ.
Nioso anwuna kpile nwu di osuɔtɔ nwu kamɛ latikiti Yesu lekoto alɛ, “Diki wo osuku buɔlaabuo diɛ aplakuo nwu kamɛ!” Ni aadiki nya osuku nɛ.
Nfanwu anwuna kpile nwu ladie di osuɔtɔ nwu suoto aalaabuo di aplakuo nwu kamɛ.
Aplakuo ɔlambu nwu omuu, nikawo ni fɛ nkpe nnyɔ latoso kitikiti aakye kabokotee nwu kalɔ aalaabuo leekpo nwu kamɛ aamɛ ntu aakpi.
Nioso batii ba kɔkpa ni aplakuo nwu latoso baasifi baalaabuɛ ɔlaa wɔ niawa ni baakyakasa afe ku sekpoo.
Ni baatii ladie baakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaanyu lɛsaa le niawa nii.
Obe wɔ baalaadu ni Yesu nfũ baanya otii wɔ kamɛ diɛ anwuna kpile dikudi nwu lasiɛ ni lakpee awu aasiɛ kasɔ, obe nwu ditɔɔkpa nwɔ.
Nioso lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ bamuu lɛma.
Batii ba niakasa ni otii wɔ kamɛ diɛ anwuna kpile nwu lasiɛ ni ɔnya latɔkɔ batii bamuu lɛsaa le niawa ni di osuɔtɔ nwu ku aplakuo nwu suoto.
Nioso batii nwu latikiti Yesu lekoto baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ adie ma kaasɔ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu latoobuo ni diɛ oklo kamɛ, otii wɔ kamɛ di anwuna kpile lasiɛ ni saa, latikiti nwɔ lɛkoto alɛ, tɛɛ ntikankofɔ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu ditatɔɔ osuku.
Ni ɔtɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔɔkyɛ leyo baatii lɛfɔ nfũ faadiki lɛsaa le di Saate lɛbla ɛɛta fɔ ni fabuɛ, faatɔkɔ ma ku mmle ɛɛnya fɔ ni nyaami.” Nioso osuɔtɔ nwu lasifi aalaabuɛ lɛsaa le di Yesu labla aatɔɔ ni diɛ ekpoo nwu lefosi aafenko.
Diabla batii ba nianu ni ɔkpɛ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Ɔnɔɔfo Yairo Obi Sankobi Ku Ɔsanko Onwii Ofiɛ.
Ɔbe wɔ di Yesu lasiɛ oklo aawaalɛ aakple aasifi ni lekpo sɛmaa, batii dikudi lakple baabasi nwɔ di suoto di lekpo kotoko.
Yuda batii kasiisakɔ ɔnɔɔfo onwii manlɛɛ ni Yairo lawa nfa.
Aanya ni Yesu, aapɛ akunkyi ninkpaatũ nɔɔ.
Aatikiti nwɔ lekoto osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Obi sankobi nii koloo okpi.
Lekoto wa faabatika nwɔ kɔnɛɛ di suoto di ofiɛ kuyɔɔ nwɔ, aawɛ nkpa.” Nioso Yesu latikanko nwɔ baakyɛ.
Batii dikudi latikanko nwɔ baamana nwɔ kpinkpĩ baakyi, Yesu lasiɛ ma nintɛɛ.
Ɔsanko onwii kafɔɔ lawɛ ma kaamɛ, asaa latoowii nwɔ fɛɛ lefosi alɛɛ anyɔ amu.
Diabuo nwɔ ku suoto kɔfa omiɛ di bafatɛ kpinwu nnɛɛ, aalalaasa koto nɔɔ kumuu, kafɔɔ ofiɛ nwu katoo ko kua tɔɔtaka.
Obe wɔ di ɔsanko nwu lanu ni Yesu lɛkpanko, aafe di Yesu sɛmaa baatii dikudi nwu kamɛ aakpanko Yesu awu.
Aabla nkpo diekye aabuɛ aatɔkɔ suoto alɛ, “Nse lɛkpanko nwɔ awu kamaa, ofiɛ mayɔɔ mi.” Nfanwu aakpanko ni Yesu awu nwu, asaa owii nwu labudi.
Nioso aatofo di suoto nɔɔ kamɛ alɛ ofiɛ nwu ntɔɔyɔɔ nwɔ.
Nfanwu, Yesu latofo alɛ osie owo ledie nwɔ di suoto.
Aakyi aakalɛ batii dikudi nwu alɛ, “Owe niɛkpanko mi awu?” Asaabateketɛ nɔɔ latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nyu mmle batii dikudi lɛmana fɔ kpinkpi beekyi ni, fiɛ fɔɔkaalɛ falɛ owe niɛkpanko fɔ awu?” Kafɔɔ Yesu latookpekpe anu aatoowolaa otii wɔ niabla ni lɛsaa nwu.
Difu lapɛ ɔsanko nwu, diekye aatofo lɛsaa le niɛwa ni di suoto kamɛ, nioso aayɔ lɛyɛkɛ ku ditũtũkũ aalaapɛ akunkyi di Yesu nkpaatũ ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ nwaako wɔ ninsi ni di ɔlaa nwu kamɛ nɛ.
Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Obi sankobi nii, ofũ onu lɛfɔ lediki fɔ.
Tɔɔkyɛ di suoto lɛyɔɔ kamɛ.
Ofiɛ lɛfɔ nwu kuyɔɔ fɔ.” Obe wɔ di Yesu lakple aatɔɔkakatɛ ni, batɔkyɛntɛ lakye Yuda batii kasiisakɔ nɔɔfo Yairo leyo baawa alɛ, “Obi sankobi lɛfɔ nwu ntookpi nioso ɔnɔɔfo, tansinkpɛnsa Saatuotɛ dibuo okpee.” Di Yesu lanu ni ɔlaa nwu aatɔkɔ ɔnɔɔfo nwu alɛ, “Tanyɛkɛ, afɔ fũ fanu!” Yesu ditatuna alɛ kuonwii atikanko nwɔ diediki Petro ku Yakobo ku obilɛma Yohane.
Obe wɔ baawa ni Yairo leyo Yesu lanya alɛ batii lesi ninfa boowi kaku ku kudu osie kanya.
Di Yesu labuo ni leyo kamɛ, ninfɛ aabuɛ alɛ, “Be ninle kudu ku kaku nwu biowi ni?
Ɔbisɔ nwu diekpi ɔkyɔsĩi ɔɔkyɔsĩi!” Batii nwu lama nwɔ ni aata batii bamuu ladie, ni akpaa obi ote, obi ɔya ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ batiɛ nwu ni baasifi nfũ diɛ obisɔ nwu lakpi aate ni nɛ.
Ni di Yesu lamufũ obisɔ nwu kɔɔnɛɛ aabuɛ seele lɛma alɛ, “Talita koumo!” Lɛsɔdiki ninle alɛ, “Okpeele, taka!” Nfanwu ɔsankobi nwu lataka aakyɛ.
Lefosi alɛɛ anyɔ obi aale.
Diatɛ diabla batii nwu ɔkpɛ osie kanya.
Yesu lakpee ma kufiofa osie kanya alɛ batanta otii kuonwii lanu, ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, bamiɛ lelesaa batɔɔ ale.
Baasĩ Yesu Di Nasaret.
Yesu ladie niinfa aawa okpoo lɛma, ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ.
Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi lawo nii, aakyako asaa otuo di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ.
Asaa otuo nɔɔ labla batii ba nianu ni ɔkpɛ, ni baakaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Ɔfɛ di otii wɔ lanu sɛlaa se mmle eekyeko?
Lɛmɛnsaatofo okle ninle nle mmle bɛɛtɔɔ ni!
Lɛ ɔbla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ nkpo?
Diele nnwɔɔ ninle Maria obi, saawolatɛ nwu?
Diele babilɛma ninle Yakobo, Yose, Yuda, ku Simon?
Babi lɛma sankobi kafɔɔ nsi wo kaamɛ.” Nioso baasĩ nwɔ.
Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Batii mbu Yaa Ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ di kakɔ biala diediki okpoo lɛma, kafaabi nɔɔ ku babi lɛma kamɛ manambu nwɔ.” Nioso atafuo lɛsaa le niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ ɔbla ninfa.
Diediki bafiɛtɛ basɛɛ afuo kɔnɛɛ otika aatakatɛsa ma siifiɛ.
Batii nɔɔ ɔtanfũ onu labla Yesu ɔkpɛ.
Yesu Lakpee Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Lefosi Banyɔ Kɔtɔ.
Yesu lakyi nkpayetũ be niawɛ ni di ntɛɛ nwu aatootuo batii ɔlaa biene.
Aalɛɛ batɔkyɛntɛ lefosi banyɔ nwu aasiisa, ni aasɛ ma banyɔ banyɔ aakpee ma kɔtɔ.
Aata ma osie diɛ anwuna kpile suoto.
Ni aakpee ma kufiofa alɛ, di osuku lɛma ɔkyɛ kamɛ batanklee lɛsalɛsaa diediki ɔkyɛnwoso, batanklee alesaa, kotofo ko mankaalɛ ni asaa, batanklee koto.
Bakpe ntokota kafɔɔ batanklee osi awu nyɔɔfa.
Aatɔkɔ ma kafɔɔ alɛ, “Nse kakɔ lele beefũ ye kɔfɔɔ, bisiɛ ninfa dilaase di obe wɔ bibadie ni di okpoo nwu.
Nse biɛɛkyɛ okpoo wɔ baatii diefũ ye nii, ee baanu ye nii ɔlaa, biesifi bidiɛ ma, kafɔɔ biɛfɛntɛ nkpaasɔ lee kɔtɛ bitɛ ma.
Nni nimatuo alɛ baasĩ ye ofũ nɛ.” Nioso baakyɛ baalaabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa baata batii alɛ, bikyi siikpile lee suoto, bietikanko Yaa sisuku.
Baatososa anwuna kpile kpinwu baatii suoto, baafifia bafiɛtɛ kpinwu nnɔnyi, baayɔɔsa ma sifiɛ.
Ɔka Herodes Lata Baabudi Yohane Disi.
Yesu leyooto lakyaka ntɛɛ nwu, Ɔka Herodes lanu, ni baatii bawo latoobuɛ alɛ, “Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ nwu bɛɛtakatɛsa beekyeko bakpi kamɛ, nioso akpe osie ɔɔbla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ nɛ.” Batii bawo kafɔɔ labuɛ alɛ, “Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Elia dile!” Babamba alɛ, “Yaa Ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ wɔ niedie ni saa Yaa Ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ owo ale!” Di Herodes lanu ni sɛlaa se mmle, aabuɛ alɛ, “Yohane wɔ lata baabudi ni disi bɛɛtakatɛsa beekyeko bakpi kamɛ nɛ!” Kaasɔ kakyekɔ, Herodes omu niata baamafũ Yohane baatɛ leeyo ta Herodia oso, diekye Herodes lafũ Herodia wɔ nle ni obi lɛma Filipo ɔsɔfɔ aayɔ.
Ni diɛ Yohane latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kufiofa diɛta osuku alɛ faafũ obilee ɔsɔfɔ fanyɔ!” Nioso, Yohane ɔlaa latoobuo Herodia suoto, ni aakyidi Yohane nɛ, aamiɛ alɛ oolo nwɔ, kafɔɔ atafuo ta Herodes oso.
Diekye Herodes n-ye alɛ Yohane nle otii biene ku otii klekle nkpo oso anyɛkɛ nwɔ, annyu alɛ lɛsalɛsaa diɛbla nwɔ kuntɛ sɛlaa nɔɔ ntofo nwɔ osie kanya ambɔmbɔ sĩ onu.
Dii ninwii lɛsaa le di Herodia komiɛ ni lawa kaanya.
Herodes lale lelofoyi dii nɔɔ.
Aatũ opunu, aakyakako banɔɔfo ku Galilea okpoo banɔɔfo ku kakpɛ kanya bayilatɛ banɔɔfotii aawa alesaa kalekɔ.
Herodia obi sankobi lakyɛ alesaa nwu kalekɔ, ni aatũ, diabuo Herodes ku batii ba aakyakako ni anu nwaa.
Ɔka Herodes latɔkɔ ɔsankobi nwu alɛ, “Kaalɛ mi lɛsaa lele ninlɛ fɔ, amii mata fɔ!” Aaka ntam aatɔɔ alɛ, “Mayɔ lɛsaa lele fɛɛkaalɛ mi nta fɔ, diɛlaase ni bia sɛɛka nii kalekɔ kakyɛ!” Ɔsankobi nwu ladie aalaakaalɛ ɔya alɛ, “Be ninkaalɛ?” Aatɔkɔ nwu alɛ, “Kaalɛ Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ disi!” Nfanwu ɔsankobi nwu lapɛsɛwa aawa ɔka Herodes ɔkyɛ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Komiɛ nlɛ budi Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ disi, faayɔ fakpee di bɛɛsi kamɛ fatɛɛ nunua!” Ɔlaa nwu labuo Ɔka Herodes suoto osie kanya, kafɔɔ diɛ ntam be aaka ni ku batii ba aakyakako ni oso, aata miɛ alɛ ɔwaalɛ ɔlaa wɔ aabuɛ aatɛ nii.
Nfanwu Ɔka Herodes lata disi buditɛ osuku alɛ akyɛ aalaabudi Yohane disi awako.
Ni aakyɛ aalaabudi Yohane disi diɛ leyo katenkɔ nɛ.
Aayɔ disi nwu aakpee di bɛɛsi aawako, aayɔ aata ɔsankobi nwu.
Ɔsankobi nwu kafɔɔ layɔ aakyɛnko ɔya.
Obe wɔ di Yohane basaateketetɛ lanu nii, baakyɛ baalaayɔ kpi nɔɔ nwu baalaakookaa.
Yesu Lata Batii Nkpe Nnɔɔ Alesaa Bale.
Batɔkyɛntɛ nwu di Yesu lakpee ni kɔtɔ lakple baawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, baabatɔkɔ nwɔ asaa ya baabla ni ku n-ya baatuo nii.
Nle mmle sɛmaa, batii kpinwu latɔɔwa ɔkyɛ lɛma diata alɛ batawɛ osuku bale alesaa, nioso Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biwa buɔlatɛ ɔnyɛɛ kɛɛkɛɛ.” Ni baabuo di oklo kamɛ baasifi lɛba le nialo ni nɛ.
Kafɔɔ batii lanya ma baatɛ nsũ nioso baakye sekpoo ate ate baatoso baatikanko ma baasifi nfũ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoofe nii, diata alɛ batii nwu lakasa ma obuo.
Obe wɔ di Yesu ladie ni diɛ oklo kamɛ aanya ni batii dikudi kplɛ nwu, ɔlaa lɛma lanu nwɔ kafutu, diekye baate fɛ bafoso ba di kpatɛ nnaa nii, ni aatuo ma asaa kpinwu nɛ.
Kɔɔtɔɔfɔ lawo nii, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lawa babatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nfũ bukpe ni lekyo ku okpoo, kale kafɔɔ nfɛ koloo.
Diki ma osuku baasifi sekpoo biibii ku nkpaayotũ be niɛmana wo diekyi ni baalaamiɛ alesaa baya bale.” Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye bamu bimiɛ alesaa bita ma bale!” Ni baabuɛ alɛ, “Ni ɔkyɛ buakyɛ munaayɔ otii awɛntɛ anɛ kɔkpento munaaya alesaa muwako ma manle?” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ biɛlaanyu bilɛ bloblo akudi asɛ ninte ye?” Baakple baabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Bloblo akudi anɔɔ ku kɔkpaku sɛnle kɔnyɔ ko kule.” Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ bata batii nwu basiɛ akudi akudi sɛɛfa lɛkɛtɛɛ kɔnle nwu suoto.
Nioso baasiɛ diɛ akudi kanya, akudi awo kɔlafa, awo kafɔɔ afosi anɔɔ.
Yesu layɔ bloblo akudi anɔɔ ku kɔkpaku nwu kɔnyɔ, ni aanyu osi aakusɛkusɛsa nya.
Aabɛbɛɛ bloblo nwu aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ basɛ bata batii nwu, ni aabɛbɛɛ kɔkpaku nwu kɔnyɔ kafɔɔ aata batii nwu bamuu nɛ.
Obiala lɛma lale aamiɛ.
Obe wɔ baasaateketɛ nɔɔ lasiisa ni bloblo ku kɔkpaku kɔkyɛɛ ko niabu nii, baawɛ lefosi nkyikyɛ nkplɛ nnyɔ.
Batii ba niale ni alesaa nwu basuɔtɔ lɛpɔ lawo nkpe nnɔɔ.
Yesu Lakyɛ Di Ntu Osi.
Nfanwu Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, babuo di oklo kamɛ wla baatɔɔsɔ okpoo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Betsaida di lekpo nwu sɛmaa.
Ninfɛ aadiki batii dikudi nwu kafɔɔ osuku nɛ.
Nni kamaa, Yesu omu kafɔɔ lasifi kabokotee osi aalaapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa.
Kɔɔtɔfɔ lawo nii, oklo nwu kafɔɔ ntoodu lɛpanta nwu ntɛɛ.
Yesu lete nfɛ niabu di kasɔ nwu suoto.
Yesu lanya alɛ oklo nwu ɔwa kɔwɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ osie, diekye kɔfɛɛfɔ latɔɔkyakako ma.
Di kuyitatũ elomu etiɛ kamɛ aakyɛ di ntu osi aatoofe ɔkyɛ lɛma, aamiɛ alɛ ɔɔwaalɛ ma anfe.
Obe wɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lanyɔɔ akyɛ ni di ntu osi ɔɔwa nii, ni baayiisa kudu alɛ, kpi ale!
Bamuu lɛma baanyɔɔ nii, ɔfɔɔ lasifi ma.
Ni di Yesu lakakatɛ ko ma aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bita situ lee site, biitanyɛkɛ!
Ami dile.” Ni aayie aabuo di oklo nwu kamɛ di anu lɛma, ni diɛ afɛɛfɔ nwu ladiɛ ɔfɛ nɛ.
Diatɛ diabla ma ɔkpɛ osie kanya!
Diekye batanu kasɔ di lɛsaatuo le ninsi ni diɛ bloblo wɔ aata ma baale ni kamɛ, ditabudi ma diekye batafũ baanu.
Yesu Lakya Batii Sifiɛ Di Genesaret.
Obe wɔ baataalɛ ni lekpo nwu baalaadu ni kakyɛ nyɔɔfa, baalaasoo diɛ Genesaret okpoo.
Ni baapɛ oklo nwu lekpo nɛ.
Obe wɔ batosoo ni diɛ oklo nwu kamɛ batii lanya Yesu baatɛ nsũ.
Nioso baatoso baalaatɔkɔ batii di ntɛɛ nwu, ta nkpo oso kakɔ lele beenu alɛ Yesu nkpe, mankɛnkɛ bafiɛtɛ ku atensaa lɛma manwako Yesu nfũ.
Kakɔ lele di Yesu lɛkyɛ, nkpayetũ woo, sekpoo woo, ee sefensuku, mankɛnkɛ bafiɛtɛ mamatɛ di asaa kayakɔ aba aba, mantikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, ata bafiɛtɛ nwu bakpanko awu nɔɔ kotoko.
Batii ba niakpanko nwɔ ni awu kotoko, sifiɛ layɔɔ ma.
Tansĩ Yaa Ta Fatikanko Ni Amanle Lee Oso.
Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ bawo lakye Yerusalem baawa baabamana Yesu baakyi.
Baanya alɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasiɛ baatoole ni alesaa, bawo ditafoto nnɛɛ fɛ mmle diɛ Farisi batii letuo batii alɛ batofoto nii.
Baafuo otofo ta Farisi batii ku Yuda batii latɔɔbla bawa lɛma amanle ya baadiɛ baatɛ ma nii.
Nioso diediki beefoto nnɛɛ lɛma fɛ mmle baatuo ma nii, fiɛ manle alesaa.
Se bɛɛya lɛsaa lele di asaa kasunsukɔ, dikpe ni beefoto nnɛɛ lɛma fiɛ beele.
Manle afiofa ya kpinwu bɛɛtaka bɛɛbatũ nii, fɛ mmle manfoto ni nkɔkɔɛ ku awambukii ku ntu adubukii.
Nioso Farisi batii nwu ku basaatuotɛ nwu lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Lɛ oso diɛ batikankotɛ lɛfɔ dilɔbla bawa loo amanle?
Manle asaa kuntɛ baafoto nnɛɛ kafɔɔ!” Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nwaako ɔlaa wɔ di Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yesaia labuɛ ni di balaatɛ lee suoto kute nkpo.
Fɛ mmle bɛɛkpana bɛɛtɛ alɛ, ‘Batii ba mmle kanya fukiti ko man-yɔ mantansɛɛ, kafɔɔ mámbɔmbɔ mi siitu lɛma kamɛ.
Kasakasa bɔɔbla mi ɔkpɛ.
Diekye bakle batii afiofa bootuo fɛle afiofa nii ale.’ Dietuo alɛ batɔɔyɔ Yaa afiofa beekookaa, bɛɛyɔ batii ablasaa bootuo ye.” Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biefe diɛ kakyɔnkyɔ osuku biediɛ Yaa afiofa biɛtɛ, biɔbla diɛ aye bamu lee saa amanle.
Diɛ ɔtɛ onyu kamɛ, Mose lakpee kufiofa alɛ, ‘Bu teefɔ ku yaafɔ.
Otii lele niɛkpaani ote ee ɔya, dikpe ni beelo nwɔ.’ Kafɔɔ biotuo bilɛ, nse otii owo nkpe lɛsaa alɛ ɔɔkyakaako ote ee ɔya, aafuo obuɛ alɛ, ‘Lɛsaa le nlɛ kɔta ye nii, ntoodiki ni lɛtɛ fɛ lɛsaa klekle nlɛ man-yɔ nta Yaa ole.’ Bilɔɔta ma osuku bilɛ bata balofotɛ lɛma asaa ya niefĩ ma nii!
Ote ko dite fɛle biɛyɔ bawa lee amanle biɔlalaasa Yaa afiofa.
Mimbla asaa bamba kpinwu fɛ n-ya mmle okle.” Nnya Sikpile Se Sewo Ninkpɔnɔnfɔsa Ni Otii.
Nni kamaa, Yesu lakple aalɛɛ batii dikudi nwu alɛ batɛɛtɛɛ nwɔ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bamuu lee bikyɔɔ mi atoko, bienu ɔlaa wɔ matɔkɔ ye ni kasɔ.
Lɛsaa lele di otii léle eekpee kaafutu dilaata alɛ akpɔnɔnfɔ di Yaa anu.
Kafɔɔ asaa ya nindie ankye ni otii otu kamɛ, nnya ninkpɔnɔnfɔsa nwɔ nɛ.
Bienu kasɔ.” Nni kamaa, obe wɔ aadiɛ ma aasifi ni leyo ninwii, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, adiki ɔlaa nwu kasɔ ata ma.
Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ni ayee bienu kasɔ?
Ɔlaa wɔ mmle diɛkpa kamɛ alɛ lɛsaa lele di otii lele eekpee kaafutu kamɛ dilaafuo nwu ɔkpɔnɔnfɔsa?
Diekye diele otii otu kamɛ nimbuo, kafɔɔ kafutu nɔɔ kamɛ nimbuo fiɛ ankyɛ ni andiki.” Nioso ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu kobuɛ ni ninfũ, kotuo alɛ alesaa amuu nlɛ alɛ baale.
Aakple aabuɛ aakyakaa alɛ, “Lɛsaa le nindie ninkye ni otii otu kamɛ, nni ninta ambla okpile nɛ.
Diekye otii otu kamɛ di disibu kpile nkye, nni ninta otii mbla asaa ya ninanlɛ ni nɛ.
Asaa nwu awo ninle otetee ku kayu ku batii olo kuɛ lɛsɔnɔkpee, onumbɛbɛɛ, disi osie ku ditii kyɔnkyɔ, suoto sĩna ɔkɔnsɔ akleesaa otikanko, batii odu okutu, onunsɛɛ, suoto katoo ɔtakatɛsa ku abuusaa ɔbla.
Sikpile se mmle simuu nindie sinkye otii kamɛ nɛ, nsĩ kafɔɔ ninta otii nkpɔnɔnfɔ nɛ.” Ɔsanko Onwii Niakye Foinike Kasɔ Lafũ Yesu Aanu.
Sɛmaa, Yesu ladie aasifi kasɔ ka niɛtɛɛtɛ ni okpoo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Tiro.
Aabuo leyo ninwii, kafɔɔ atamiɛ alɛ otii atofo alɛ akpe ninfa, atafuo owofa kafɔɔ.
Ɔsanko onwii, obi sankobi, ninwuna kpile lasiɛ nwɔ.
Ɔsanko nwu lanu Yesu lɛkpanko ninfa, ni aati nwɔ aakyɛ aalaapɛ akunkyi di nkpaatũ nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ aatikiti Yesu lekoto alɛ atososa ninwuna nwu di obi suoto.
Ɔsanko nwu Hela otii aale, kafɔɔ baalofo nwɔ di Foinike kasɔ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ta bata babisɔ alesaa bale bamiɛ fiɛ.
Diekye diɛlɛ alɛ baayɔ babisɔ alesaa manta baweewee alɛ bale.” Nfa diɛ ɔsanko nwu kafɔɔ kokpee nwɔ kanya alɛ, “Ao, Saate, baweewee ba nsi ni diɛ opunu kalɔ di alesaa kalekɔ, nwɛ osuku manle alesaa ya baabisɔ kole oowiwii ni kaasɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ta, kanya didiki le feediki ni ninfũ oso, tɔɔkyɛ leyo.
Fabalaanya falɛ ninwuna kpile nwu ntoodie di obi lɛfɔ suoto.” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu lasifi leyo nɛ.
Nfa aalaanya alɛ obi nɔɔ nwu nte kaatenkɔ nɔɔ ninwuna kpile nwu ntoodie diesifi.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Wɔ Ninoonu Nii, Ɔnɔɔkakatɛ Ni Kafɔɔ Ofiɛ.
Yesu ladie di Tiro ntɛɛ nwu aafe di Sidon, aasifi Galilea lɛpanta sɛmaa aalaata di ntɛɛ be diɛ ekpoo lefosi nkpe nii.
Nfa di batii banwii lakyeko osuɔtɔ wɔ ninoonu nii, onoofuo ni ɔkakatɛ nwaa kafɔɔ baawako Yesu nɛ.
Baatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ atika nwɔ kɔnɛɛ, aayɔɔsa nwɔ ofiɛ.
Nioso Yesu lakpaa nwɔ aasifiko lɛba le nielo nii baatii nnaa nii, ni di Yesu lakpee anɛɛ nɔɔ diɛ osuɔtɔ nwu atoko kamɛ nɛ.
Aatufa sita aatika kɔɔnɛɛ, ayɔ aatusa osuɔtɔ nwu di ɔkplalomii.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakplesa anu katoo aanyu osi ni aanwuna aadieko nwaa, ni aatɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu seele lɛma alɛ, “Hefata,” kasɔ ninle alɛ, “Tikiti!” Nfanwu, osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle atoko niatikiti, ɔkpalalomii nɔɔ okũ labudi ninfɛ aakyako ɔkakatɛ nwaa nɛ.
Yesu lasĩ aata batii ba niayila ni ninfa alɛ batantɔkɔ otii kuonwii lɛsaa le baanya ni ninfa.
Kafɔɔ batanu, bamuu lɛma baasifi baalaatoobuɛ mmle diawa nii.
Batii ba bamuu nianu ni sɛlaa nwu, diabla ma yaaa!
Ni baabuɛ alɛ, “Anlolaa asaa amuu ambla!
Anta bamumu nkakatɛ, batokotĩitɛ kafɔɔ nnu!”
Yesu Lata Batii Nkpe Nna Alesaa Baale.
Ditaklɛ saa fiɛ baatii kpinwu labasi ninfa.
Ta lɛsalɛsaa ditabu ma baale ni oso, Yesu lalɛɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ baawa nwɔ katũ ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Batii ba ɔlaa konu mi kafutu diekye batɔɔwɛ di ɔkyɛ nii ayi atiɛ amu.
Kafɔɔ lɛsalɛsaa diebu baawɛ manle nii.
Nse lediɛ ma nlɛ batɔɔkyɛ, loo babalaatookpi kɔka diɛ osuku.
Diekye bawo lekye nkyonkɔ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Di ɔfaafuu wɔ mɔ, ɔfɛ di otii mawɛ alesaa anta batii ba mmle alɛ bale bamiɛ?” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Bloblo akudi asɛ bikle?” Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Bloblo akudi akuɛnsĩ bukle.” Yesu latɔkɔ bamuu lɛma alɛ basiɛ kaasɔ.
Ninfɛ aayɔ bloblo akudi akuɛnsĩ nwu, aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, ninfɛ aabɛbɛɛ nwɔ kɔkyɛɛ kɔkyɛɛ aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ bayɔ bata batii nwu bamuu.
Mma kafɔɔ, baayɔ baasɛ ma fɛɛ.
Baanya alɛ kɔkpaku kɔsɛɛ kafɔɔ labu nii, Yesu layɔ kũ kafɔɔ ninfɛ aapɛ sɛfa nɛ.
Aayɔ kũ aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ bayɔ basɛ ma kafɔɔ.
-Batii ba lale alesaa nwu baamiɛ.
Basuɔtɔ lete lɛpɔ labla nkpe nna.
Baale baaloo nii, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasiisa kufii ko niabu nii baawɛ nkyikyɛ nkplɛ nkuɛnsĩ.
Sɛmaa, Yesu ladiki ma osuku baasifi.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ labuo di oklo kamɛ baataalɛ ntu baasifi kasɔ ka bɔɔlɛɛ ni Dalmanuta.
Farisi Batii Lakaalɛ Yesu Alɛ Abla Atuosaa Atuo Ma.
Farisi batii lawa Yesu ɔkyɛ alɛ bɔɔbakaalɛ nwɔ sɛlaa mansɔ nwɔ mannyu.
Nioso baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ abla atuosaa atuo ma baanya alɛ Yaa nfũ eekye.
Kafɔɔ Yesu lanwuna faa, ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe lɛsaa oso diɛ nunua babi komiɛ alɛ batɔɔnya atuosaa?
Oowo, kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ nɔɔmatuo ye lɛsaa le biomiɛ bilɛ binya ni ninfũ!” Ninfɛ aasifi aadiɛ ma aakple aalaabuo di oklo kamɛ aataalɛ lɛpanta nwu aasifi kakyɛ nyɔɔfa.
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Aakyeko Lɛnyanka Suoto.
Obe wɔ baatoofe nii, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ layee batakelee bloblo, dikudi ninwii ko niabu diɛ oklo kamɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu laka ma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu biemufũ suoto lee biklee di Ɔka Herodes ku Farisi batii mmɔle nyankale suoto.” Basaateketɛ nɔɔ labuɛ baata baawo alɛ, “Ta nle munankle bloblo apɔ ni oso oobuɛ ɔlaa nwɔ nɛ?” Kafɔɔ Yesu latofo ɔlaa wɔ baatoobu ni oso aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe oso biobuɛ bloblo ɔwɛnlaa?
Diɛbase ni di nunua, biifuo ɔnya ɔtɛ nsũ, biinu kasɔ?
Atoko nkpe ye opĩ nwaa!
Bikpe anu, kafɔɔ bilɔɔnya!
Bikpe atoko, kafɔɔ biloonu!
Bitanya obe wɔ labɛbɛɛ bloblo akudi anɔɔ lata ni batii nkpe nnɔɔ baale ni?
Nkyikyɛ nsɛ di kɔkyɛɛ kɔkyɛɛ ko niabu ni layii?” Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nkyikyɛ lefosi nnyɔ.” Yesu lakple aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Di obe wɔ kafɔɔ lasɛ ni bloblo akudi akuɛnsĩ lata ni batii nkpe nna, kɔkyɛɛ kɔkyɛɛ nwu niabu nii, nkyikyɛ nsɛ kuayii?” Baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nkyikyɛ nkuɛnsĩ.” Ni aakple aakalɛ ma alɛ, “Ni bia nua biinu kasɔ?” Yesu Latikiti Numbiɛtɛ Anu Di Betsaida.
Obe wɔ baakyɛ baalaadu ni Betsaida, batii banwii lakpaa numbiɛtɛ onwii baawako Yesu nfũ, ni baatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ akpanko nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lamufũ nwɔ kɔɔnɛɛ aakpaa nwɔ aadieko di okpoo ntɛɛ.
Ni aafiɛ nwɔ sita di anu, aayɔ nnɛɛ aatika nwɔ di anu, aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Fɔɔnya lɛsaa lewo?” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu latakatɛsa anu aanyu osi aabuɛ alɛ, “Yii kɔnya batii, kafɔɔ bate fɛɛ awoso.
Bakyɛ bookyi.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aakpanko osuɔtɔ nwu anu nɛ.
Di obe nyɔɔfa wɔ mmle kamɛ, osuɔtɔ nwu latikiti anu nwaa aanyu, diakpa nwɔ aakyako asaa ɔnya klekle.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki nwɔ osuku alɛ atɔɔkyɛ leyo nɔɔ, kafɔɔ ataasinkple aalaafe diɛ okpoo nwu kamɛ.
Petro Ladiki Aatuo Otii Wɔ Okle Di Yesu Nle Nii.
Nni kamaa Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ladie ninfa baasifi nkpayotũ be niɛkaako ni Kaesarea di Filipi.
Baakyɛ ni diɛ osuku, Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔkɔ mi ɔmɛntiikle baatii kobuɛ alɛ nle?” Baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Batii bawo kobuɛ alɛ, Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane fale.
Bawo kafɔɔ kobuɛ alɛ Elia fale.
Bawo kafɔɔ kobuɛ alɛ Yaa Ɔlaabuɛtɛtɛ onwii lɛma fale.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ni aye mɔ?
Owe biefũ bienu bilɛ nle?” Petro latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakpee ma kufiofa alɛ batantɔkɔ kuonwi ɔlaa wɔ mmle baye beekyeko nwɔ ni suoto.
Yesu Lakakatɛ Ankyeko Dibuo Nɔɔ Ku Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Ni di Yesu lakyako basaateketetɛ nɔɔ asaa otuo nɛ.
Aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Dikpe nii Otii Obi lefe diibuo kpinwu kamɛ diɛ okpoo banɔɔfo ku Yaa olebatatɛ ku kufiofa batuotɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ mansĩ nwɔ.
Babalo nwɔ, kafɔɔ, di dii tiɛfa, abakple ansɛnkɛ.” Aatɔkɔ ma sɛlaa se mmle klekle aaloo nii, ninfɛ di Petro lakpaa Yesu aasifiko ɔlɔɔkɔ ni aalaasĩ ɔlaa nwu aatɔɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ di Yesu lamunikĩi aanyu ni basaateketetɛ nɔɔ, aasĩ ɔlaa nwu aata Petro alɛ, “Abonsam kyɛ mi di ɔlɔɔkɔ!” Ni aakple aabuɛ alɛ, “Disibu lɛfɔ nwu diekye Yaa nfũ kafɔɔ otii nfũ diekye!” Nioso Yesu lalɛɛ batii dikudi nwu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nse otii owo komiɛ alɛ awa abatikankoe, ni dikpe nii ansĩ suoto nɔɔ, an-yɔ aatoo nɔɔ, antikankoe.
Diekye otii lele nialɛ ɔɔta nkpa nɔɔ, abayu mi, kafɔɔ otii lele nieyu nkpa nɔɔ diisi nii ta ɔlaa nii biene oso, abawɛ nkpa.
Lɛmɛntota dibiene di otii mawɛ nse ɛɛwɛ kayi ka mmle asaa amuu eeyu nkpa nɔɔ?
Ee obelɛsaa di otii kayɔ ankyɛlɛnsa anfũ nkpa nwaa nwu?
Nse otii owo lenunsɔ mi ku ɔlaa nii di Yaa ɔtanyɛkɛ di ayi kpile ya mmle kamɛ, ni ami, Otii Obi nwu, kafɔɔ manunsɔ nwɔ, nse lekple lɛwa di Teemi leklekle kamɛ ku Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ klekle.”
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, batii bawo kaamɛ lee dilɔbakpi, diediki bitɔɔnya bilɛ Yaa sɛka ole ntɔɔwa ku osie fiɛ.” Yaa Ladiki Yesu Leklekle Aatuo.
Ayi akuɔ sɛmaa, Yesu lakpaa Petro ku Yakobo ku Yohane baakyɛ kobokote takale kunwii osi.
Lete lɛma niawɛ ninfa.
Obe wɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoonyu nii, kakyi kanwii lawa di Yesu suoto.
Awu nɔɔ lapu fututu osie kanya aatoosese di anu aalenke mmle diɛ otii kafoto lɛsaa nindie ni nintu.
Ninfɛ diɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ batiɛ nwu lanya Yaa Ɔlaa Babuɛtɛtɛ Mose ku Elia lakyɔɔ baatɔɔkakatɛko Yesu.
-Lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ Petro ku bawo nɔɔ diata alɛ, batatofo be baatoobuɛ.
Ninfɛ di Petro latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, nfũ loo lɛwa lɛtɛ dilɛ.
Diki wo osuku buɔpɛ akpaayo atiɛ.
Anwii alefɔ, anwii Mose, anwii kafɔɔ Elia.” Ninfɛ di dituntũ ninwii labatĩi ma ku kunyĩi nɔɔ, ninfɛ sɛɛlɔ sinwii ladie di dituntũ nwu kamɛ diabuɛ alɛ, “Nnya obi nii bɔmbɔtɛ ninle nwɔ nɛ.
Bikyɔɔ nwɔ atoko bienu nwɔ ɔlaa!” Nfanwu baanyunyu nii, batasinya kuonwii dilenkee Yesu lete niayila ma diɛ ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Baakye kobokote osi boosoo manwa nii, Yesu lakpee ma kufiofa alɛ, “Bitantɔkɔ kuonwii lɛsaa le biɛnya ni ninfũ, diɛlase diɛ obe wɔ di ami, Otii Obi nwu, mataka nkye ni bakpi kamɛ.” Baakyɔɔ ɔlaa nwu atoko, kafɔɔ se nima nima basi, mantɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Ɔtaka Baakpi kamɛ kasɔ mɔ?” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Lɛ oso di kufiofa batuotɛ labuɛ alɛ Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Elia kakasa Kristo ɔwa?” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako baabuɛ Elia maka Kristo katũ ole amalolaa asaa antɛ.
Kafɔɔ bɛɛkpana Kɔɔkpana Klekle kamɛ alɛ Otii Obi nwu mafe diibuo kpinwu kamɛ.
Babasĩ nwɔ kafɔɔ.
Lɛ oso bienyu bilɛ baabuɛ nkpo?
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Elia ntɔɔwa ɛɛbafe kofokofoko.
Kafɔɔ batii ditafũ nwɔ, baabla nwɔ nle ninlɛ ma nii, fɛ mmle baakpana baatɛ ni di suoto nɔɔ.” Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔbi Onwii Ninwuna Kpile Lasiɛ Ni Kaamɛ Ofiɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ batiɛ ba mmle lakple baawa ni bawo lɛma kamɛ, baanya alɛ batii kpinwu lamana ma baakyi, baatɔɔnanfi sɛlaa ku kufiofa batuotɛ bawo.
Obe wɔ baatii nwu lanya alɛ Yesu nfɛ kɔwa nii, diabala ma ɔkpɛ, ninfɛ baatoso baalaakyakako nwɔ baasɛɛsa nwɔ nɛ.
Yesu lakaalɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Obe sɛlaa biyɛ biɔnanfi?” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ onwii di batii nwu kamɛ latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, lɛkpaa obi nii lɛwako ɔkyɛ lɛfɔ, ta niwuna kpile nsi nwɔ ni oso, oloofuo ɔkakatɛ.
Obe lele nse ninwuna nwu kɔkpɛko nwɔ, annɔɔ ampɛ kaasɔ, afuuta ntoodie nwɔ kaanya, antoowee anyɛɛ, eebensa suoto tii.
Ninfɛ lɛkpaa nwɔ lɛwako basaateketetɛ lɛfɔ nfũ nlɛ batososa ninwuna nwu di suoto nɔɔ, kafɔɔ baafuo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ee!
Miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle lee, ofũ onu lee diɛpɔ!
Sɛsɛ bilɛ nsiɛ ye kaamɛ fiɛ biefũ binu.
Ee lɛ ninkle ye naase fiɛ bibanu asaa kasɔ?
Bikpaa obisɔ nwu biwakoe!” Ninfɛ baakpaa nwɔ baawako Yesu nfũ nɛ.
Diɛ ninwuna kpile nwu lanya ɔnya Yesu, diawanyinsa obisɔ nwu, aanɔɔ aapɛ kaasɔ aakyako osisikiti, afuuta latoodie nwɔ kaanya.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ obisɔ nwu ote alɛ, “Diɛkyako nwɔ ni ɔbla mmle ditɔɔkɛlɛ?” Osuɔtɔ nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Sibisɔ nɔɔ ke diakyako nwɔ ɔbla.
Obe lele ninwuna le mmle komiɛ alɛ dilo nwɔ kokooko.
Se diɛwa nkpo, ninta alɛ antɔɔnɔɔ antoobuo di ɔtɔ ee ntu kamɛ.
Lekoto, nya wo nyaami faakyakaako wo, se lɛsaa le faafuo ni ɔbla dile!” Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛ oso fɔɔtɔkɔ mi falɛ se kafuo?
Lɛsalɛsaa nnaa otii wɔ niefũ mi eenu ni osie.” Nfanwu, obisɔ nwu ote labuɛ osie kanya alɛ, “Nkpe ofũ onu kafɔɔ kuɔpɔ.
Kyakaakoe ninwɛ ofũ onu nkyakaa!” Obe wɔ nfɛ di Yesu lanya alɛ batii kpinwu nfɛ kɔtɛɛtɛ nwɔ nii, ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ninwuna kpile nwu alɛ, “Afɔ ninwuna le ninanta batii lanu ni ku ɔtankakatɛ, kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ die di obisɔ nwu kamɛ, diidii kafɔɔ tamasimbuo nwɔ kaamɛ!” Ninfɛ ninwuna le mmle layiisa kudu osie kanya, diawanyinsa obisɔ nwu diatɛ kaasɔ fiɛ diadie diasifi.
Obisɔ wɔ late ninfa fɛ le okpi atookpi.
Batii ba niayila ni ninfa latoobuɛ alɛ, “Eekpi.” Kafɔɔ Yesu lamufũ obisɔ nwu kɔɔnɛɛ aatakatɛsa aase.
Sɛmaa obe wɔ di Yesu lalabuo ni leyo, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakyɛ baalaakaalɛ nwɔ buɛɛ alɛ, “Lɛ oso butafuo ninwuna kpile nwu otososa di obisɔ nwu kamɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Diediki otii kɔpɛ ɔlaa anta Yaa, annii kanya wlawla fiɛ abafuo ninwuna le mmle okle otososa odiki di otii kamɛ.” Yesu Lakple Aakakatɛ Di Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ladie ninfa baafe di Galilea kasɔ.
Yesu ditamiɛ alɛ otii kuonwii atofo nfũ akpe nii, diekye aatootuo basaateketetɛ nɔɔ asaa.
Aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii onwii madiki Otii Obi kálɔ anta batii alɛ balo nwɔ.
Ni kafɔɔ dii tiɛfa, abakple ansɛnkɛ ansiɛ nkpa.” Kafɔɔ batanu ɔlaa wɔ aatɔkɔ ma ni kasɔ, baayɛkɛ batakaalɛ nwɔ ɔlaa nwu kasɔ.
Yesu Latuo Otiikle Wɔ Ninlenke Nii.
Baalabuo ni Kapernaum, baalabuo leyo.
Nfa di Yesu lakaalɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Obe ɔlaa biɛtɔɔ nanfi ko bawo biɔwa ni?” Kafɔɔ batadiki kanya.
Diekye baatɔɔwa nii baatɔɔ nanfi alɛ bootofo otii wɔ nii lenke ni kaamɛ lɛma.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lasiɛ ni kaasɔ, aalɛɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi banyɔ nwu ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Olele nikomiɛ alɛ ale ɔkasale ni aabla suoto fɛ anaa kayilakɔ, aakyakaako bawo nɔɔ.” Ninfɛ aata obisɔ onwii lawa aabayila sĩitũ lɛma.
Aakpaa obisɔ wɔ aatika l'aatĩ nɔɔ ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii lele niefũ obisɔ fɛ nwɔ mmle okle ta ami oso, ami eefũ.
Otii lele niefũ mi, diele lete nii eefũ.
Kafɔɔ ku Teemi wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ eefũ.” Otii Lele Ninan-yɛ Wo Di Suoto, Ayɛ Wo Kamaa.
Ninfɛ di Yohane latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buɔnya osuɔtɔ onwii kotososa anwuna kpile baatii suoto leeyoto lɛfɔ kamɛ.
Buatɔkɔ nwɔ bulɛ adiɛ, diekye aasi wo kaamɛ.” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitantĩi nwɔ osuku, diekye otii wɔ ni kɔbla ni sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ di leeyooto nii kamɛ, di nni kamaa, ɔlɔbamunikĩi wla akple abuɛ ɔlaa kpile di suoto nii.
Diekye otii wɔ ninantaka ayila wo ni di suoto, awo ku nnwɔɔ, onwii bule.
“Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse otii lɛta ye ntu kakɔkwɛɛ kanwii bienyi ta ami Kristo bale bile ni oso, Yaa dilabasĩ nwɔ letota biene ɔta.
Bitanta Kuonwi Lakple Sɛmaa Di Ofũonu Suoto.
“Kafɔɔ se otii owo lɛta babisɔ ba mmle niefũ mi beenu nii, onwii lɛma lekple diɛ ofũ onu nɔɔ sɛmaa, otii nwu dibabuo nwɔ osie kanya!
Se bɛɛyɔ okũ beenii difuɔ dibinte bɛɛsaka nwɔ siimuu, beefuki nwɔ beekpee di leekpo kamɛ, dialɛ nwɔ ninlenkee.
-“Nioso se kɔnɛɛ lɛfɔ kunwii kɔlalaasa fɔ ofũ onu, nu kasɔ faabudi kũ fayu!
Dilɛ dilenke alɛ faayɔ kɔnɛɛ kunwii fambuo di nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo, alɛ faawɛ nnɛɛ nnyɔ, Yaa n-yɔ fɔ anfuki ankpee di ɔtɔ wɔ nikofiɛ kunaa ni kaloo kamɛ.
-Se loo kɔkpaa lɛfɔ kafɔɔ nikɔlalaasa fɔ ofũ onu, faabudi kũ fayu.
Se nkpaa nnyɔ ɔwɛ alɛ baafuki fɔ mankpee diɛ ɔtɔ wɔ ninnaa ni kaloo kamɛ oso, fakpe kɔkpaa kunwi fasi nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo, dilɛ dilenke.
Se loo ninu lɛfɔ ninwii kafɔɔ nikɔlalaasa fɔ ofũ onu, faadiki ni fayu.
Dibalɛfɔ ninlenkee alɛ faayɔ ninu ninwii fambuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ, alɛ faawɛ anu anyɔ alɛ baafuki fɔ mankpee di ɔtɔ kplɛ wɔ nikofiɛ kunaa ni kaloo kamɛ.
Nfa suoto beebuɛ alɛ, ‘Bakunnwɔɔ ba ninlalasa ni asaa ninfa, manankpi ni diidii!
Ɔtɔ wɔ kafɔɔ ninfiɛ ni asaa ninfa, diidii kunnii.’ Diekye babayɔ ɔtɔ mankleklesa batii bamuu suoto, fɛ mmle man-yɔ mba mankleklesa oleɔta kafɔɔ.
“Mba nlɛ.
Kafɔɔ nse ditooyu ɔmɛnɛfɛ ni mi, be baakple man-yɔ mankpee mi ɔmɛnɛfɛ?
Nioso bita mba ɔkpɛ biene disiɛ ye kaamɛ, biesiɛ ku bawo lee di atoko ɔkyɛ ole kamɛ.”
Yesu Latuo Asaa Aakyeko Ɔsa Ku Ɔsɔfɔ Kusĩ Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ladie ninfa, aasifi Yudea kasɔ, aataalɛ Yordan okle.
Batii kpinwu lakple baawa baabamana nwɔ baakyi ninfa, ninfɛ aatootuo ma Yaa ɔlaa fɛ mmle ambla ni ɔbla nɛ.
Farisi batii bawo lawa Yesu ɔkyɛ alɛ bɔɔkyɔɔ nwɔ okũ.
Baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Kufiofa loo lɛta osuku alɛ osuɔtɔ kasĩ ɔsɔfɔ?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kanya, aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe kufiofa diɛ Mose lɛta ye?” Ni baata ntale alɛ, “Mose lɛta osuku alɛ, osuɔtɔ wɔ nialɛ ansimbɔ ni ɔsɔfɔ, aakpana kukũ antɔɔ letofo fiɛ aasĩ nwɔ.” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Mose lakpana nle mmle aata ye di osuku wɔ mmle suoto diekye biesĩ bilɛ, baatantuo ye lɛsaa.
Diɛ kayi kasɔkakyekɔ, Yaa labla osuɔtɔ ku ɔsanko.
Nioso Kɔɔkpana klekle kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Nle mmle oso, osuɔtɔ madie di ote ku ɔya suoto ansifi manko ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ manaabla onwii, banyɔ lɛma mankple suoto sina sinwii.’ Di Yaa anu, otii onwii nfɛ bale.
Diele batii banyɔ.
Nioso batii ba di Yaa ntɔɔbla ni onwii kasɔ ka suoto, otii atamblasa ma ntɛɛ!” Sɛmaa obe wɔ baakyɛ ni leyo, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ ɔlaa wɔ aabuɛ aakyeko ni kufiofa nwu suoto.
Yesu ladiki kamɛ aata ma alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ niesĩ ni ɔsɔfɔ eekple ɛɛlayɔ ni ɔbamba, ntookpee asɔnɔ, ɛɛbla ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ nwu kofole okpile.
Nkpo nwu ke se ɔsanko lesĩ ɔsa ɛɛkyɛ asi ko osuɔtɔ bamba, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ atookpee asɔnɔ, ɛɛbla ɔsa nɔɔ nwu kofole okpile.” Yesu Lawii Babisɔ Lɛyɔɔ.
Di obe nwu kamɛ tutuutu, batii banwii lakpaa babi lɛma baawako Yesu ɔkyɛ alɛ atika ma nnɛɛ di suoto aakusɛkusɛ ma.
Kafɔɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lalɔnko ma.
Di Yesu lanya ni nkpo, ɔblɔ lafiɛ nwɔ, ni aatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bita babisɔ bawa ɔkyɛ nii, bitantĩi ma osuku.
Diekye batii fɛ babisɔ ba mmle okle kale ninle Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo.
Nwaa kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii wɔ ninanfũ ni Yaa sɛka kalekɔ fɛ mmle di obisɔ nwakosa ni suoto kasɔ dilabuo nfa diidii.” Ninfɛ aasiisa babisɔ ba niawɛ ni ninfa dikudi aatika ma nnɛɛ di suoto aata ma dikusɛkusɛ nɛ.
Saawɛntɛ Onwii Lakaalɛ Yesu Osuku Wɔ Baafe Manwɛ Ni Nkpa Nwaa.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lataka alɛ ooyefe ni osuku, osuɔtɔ onwii latoso aabadu nwɔ aapɛ akunkyi kaatũ nɔɔ, aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ Biene, be kabla fiɛ kawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo?” Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be oso fɔɔlɛɛ mi otii biene?
Otii kuonwii nnaa ale ni bienetɛ, diediki Yaa lete.
Faye Yaa afiofa amuu.
‘Tanlo otii, tankpee asɔnɔ, tan-yu, tanlaa faatika di otii suoto, tankyɔnkyɔ otii faafũ nwɔ asaa, bu teefɔ ku yaafɔ.’ ” Osuɔtɔ wɔ lakple aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, diɛyɔ ni di sibisɔ nii, diɛbase ni bia miɛ, kole afiofa ya mmle amuu.” Yesu lanyu nwɔ ku lɛbɔmbɔ ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛsaa ninwii ko niebu fɔ ɔbla.
Tɔɔkyɛ faalaayɔ asaa ya amuu niikpe fɔ ni fasunsũ, faayɔ koto nwu fata bapiitɛ, se fatookple saawɛntɛ di Yaa kafa.
Nni kamaa faabatikankoe nfɛ!” Obe wɔ di osuɔtɔ wɔ lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ, nnɛɛ lafee nwɔ aakyɛ aasifi ku sɛnyaami diekye asaa lawɛ nwɔ kpinwu.
Yesu lamunikĩi aanyu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Dibawɛ osie fiɛ diɛ basaawɛntɛ mafuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ obuo.” Ɔlaa wɔ lata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ disi obu.
Kafɔɔ Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Babi nii, binyu mmle dikpe osie diɛta ni basaawɛntɛ alɛ baawɛ osuku mambuo ni Yaa sɛka kalekɔ!
Nfa lɛma obuo mawɛ ma osie dilenke alɛ, kapupɔnkɔ kabuo di pandiɛ dituɛ anfe!” Aatɔkɔ ma ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, diata ma disibu osie kanya!
Ninfɛ baatɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Ni owe mɔ, nimawɛ didiki?” Ninfɛ di Yesu lanyu ma tuwĩi ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii kuonwii dilaafuo nle mmle ɔbla.
Kafɔɔ nnwɔɔ Yaa, abafuo lɛsaa lele ɔbla.” Ninfɛ di Petro lakakatɛ aabuɛ alɛ, “Ni awo mɔ?
Nyu, buodiɛ asaa loo amuu buɔtɛ buɔwa butikanko fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakakatɛ aabuɛ alɛ, “Nwaa kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ bibawɛ asaa ya ninlenkee ni n-ya biediɛ biɛtɛ nii.
Diekye otii lele niediɛ leyo nɔɔ ɛɛtɛ, ee babi lɛma, ee ɔya, ee ote, ee babi nɔɔ, ee kofe, ta ami ku ɔlaa biene nwu oso, aawɛ asaa nwu anlenkee kɔlafa nɔɔ kaasɔ ka suoto.
Abawɛ ayo ku babi lɛma ku baya ku babi ku afe.
Kafɔɔ, abawɛ atikanko.
Nni kamaa abawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo di kayi ka fɔle nimawa ni kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ batii kpinwu ba ninle ni katũ male bayɛntɛle.
Bayɛntɛle kafɔɔ male bakasale.” Yesu Lakple Aakakatɛ Dii Tiɛfa Di Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Di obe wɔ baakyɛ di osuku baatoofe ni Yerusalem okpoo, Yesu lale katũ fiɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latika.
Ditutukũ lamufũ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ, lɛyɛkɛ kafɔɔ lapɛ batii ba niatikanko ma nii.
Yesu lakple aalɛɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi banyɔ nwu di ɔlɔɔkɔ aalaatɔkɔ ma lɛsaa le nimawa nwɔ ni di suoto.
Aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Binu!
Buofe Yerusalem lɛba le babalaayɔ ami, Otii Obi, mankpee ni di Yaa olebatatɛ ku kufiofa batuotɛ nnɛɛ.
Babalo mi lɛpɔɔ manyɔ mi mankpee di batii ba ninanle ni Yuda batii nnɛɛ, mma kafɔɔ babakpee mi sinunsɔ, mantufa sita mankpete mi, mampɛ mi ku mpile, manloe.
Kafɔɔ di dii tiɛfa suoto, mataka nsiɛ nkpa.” Yesu Latuo Asaa Di Sɛlanle Ole Suoto.
Ni di Sebedeo babi dile ni Yakobo ku Yohane lawa Yesu nfũ baabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buomiɛ bulɛ bla lɛsaa ninwii fata wo.” Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be lɛsaa dile?” Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse fɛbasiɛ di lɛkakpomii lɛfɔ nwu di Yaa kafa leeklekle kamɛ, buomiɛ bulɛ faata wo mumasiɛ fɔ di ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Onwii loo di oletanɛɛkyɛ lɛfɔ, onwii kafɔɔ di ɔmɛntukyɛ lɛfɔ.” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bieye lɛsaa le biɔkaalɛ nii!
Biefũ bienu bilɛ bibafuo dibuo kakɔkɔɛ ka ntu manyi ni, onyi?
Bibafuo ntu okpeesa amanle ya makpe ni dibuo kamɛ kaasɔ ka mmle okpe?” Ni baatuna alɛ, “Bubafuo.” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ɛɛ, bibanyi kakɔkɔɛ ka ntu be manyi nii, ku ntu okpeesa amanle ya okle makpe nii.
Kafɔɔ nnaa osuku ndiki otii wɔ nimasiɛ ni di oletanɛɛkyɛ nii ee ɔmɛntukyɛ nii.
Teemi omu mayɔ anta batii ba atoololaa ɛɛtɛ ni kofokofoko.” Obe wɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi ba niabu ni lanu ni ɔlaa nwu, baanya ɔblɔ di Yakobo ku Yohane suoto.
Nioso Yesu lalɛɛ bamuu aasiisa aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye bamu biye bilɛ abaa banɔɔfotii ninanle ni Yuda batii, nkpe otumi di baatii bamuu kaasɔ suoto.
Banɔɔfotii nwu kafɔɔ kotuo suoto maakpee ma.
Kafɔɔ bitanta diate nkpo kaamɛ lee.
Nse onwii kaamɛ lee komiɛ alɛ ale ɔnɔɔfo kaamɛ lee yi, ni dikpe ni eele kpɛmblatɛ ɛɛta babule.
Se onwii kaamɛ lee komiɛ alɛ ale ɔkasale, ni aale ɔlanle ata batii bamuu.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ bia di Otii Obi nwu nkpo diɛwa alɛ batii katɔɔbla sɛkpɛ mantɔɔtɔɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nnwɔɔ ɛɛwa alɛ ɔɔbla sɛkpɛ anta batii alɛ aayɔ nkpa nɔɔ kafɔɔ antɛ kaasɔ andiki batii kpi.” Yesu Latikiti Bartimeo Numbiɛtɛ Anu.
Nle sɛmaa Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lalaabuo Yeriko.
Baatoodie ni di okpoo nwu kamɛ, batii kpinwu latikanko ma.
Obe wɔ baakyɛ ni di osuku, baafe numbiɛtɛ onwii bɔɔlɛɛ ni Bartimeo, Timeo obi aale.
Aasiɛ kaasɔ aatɔɔkaalɛ asaa di osukulɔɔkɔ.
Obe wɔ aanu alɛ Yesu Nasaret Otii nikofe nii, aayiisa kudu abuɛ alɛ, “Yesu!
Dawid leyo kamɛ obi!
Nyɛɛ nyaami!” Batii kpinwu ba niatoofe ni ninfa lasĩ ɔlaa baatɔɔ alɛ, adiɛ kudu oyiisa.
Kafɔɔ mia aatɛ aayiisa kudu alɛ, “Dawid leyo kamɛ obi ee!
Nyɛɛ nyaami kyu woo!” Di Yesu lanu nwɔ ni lɛlɛɛ, ni aayila, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Bilɛɛ nwɔ bitɛɛ.” Ninfɛ baalɛɛ numbiɛtɛ nwu baabuɛ alɛ, “Ta suoto siyɔɔ fɔ!
Taka pla, diekye ɔɔlɛɛ fɔ.” Kakuinwu, aafuki awu nɔɔ wua aayu aayefe aalaadu Yesu.
Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Obe foomiɛ falɛ mabla nta fɔ?” Numbiɛtɛ wɔ mmle latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, ta anu atikiti mi nintɔɔnya!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔɔkyɛ.
Ofũonu lɛfɔ ntoo diki fɔ.” Kakuinwu, anu nɔɔ latikiti aakyako asaa ɔnya.
Ninfɛ aatikanko Yesu, baasifi bamuu lɛma nɛ.
Baafũ Yesu Di Yerusalem Fɛ Ɔka.
Di obe wɔ baatɛɛtɛɛ ni Yerusalem baabadu ni Betfage ku Betania ntɛɛ nwu, baabadu kobokote ko bɔɔlɛ ni Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote.
Nfa di Yesu lakyesee basaateketetɛ nɔɔ banyɔ alɛ batɔɔsɔ.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Se biedu okpoo kasale wɔ bibabuo nii, bibanya bilɛ beekpee bɔkɛɛ wɔ ninte ni fɛ pɔnkɔ dibi okũ di otii kuonwii diisiɛ nwɔ ni di suoto.
Bidiki nwɔ di okũ, biɛkpaa ni biwakoe.
Se otii owo lɛkaalɛ ye alɛ, ‘Lɛ oso biɛkpaa ni?’ Bitɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ Saate komiɛ ni ɔkpɛ ɔbla ko, abakplesa anwako nunua.” Nioso batii ba mmle banyɔ lakyɛ baalaanya alɛ beekpee bɔkɛɛ wɔ ninte ni fɛ pɔnkɔ okũ beese di osuɔtɔ onwii kayoko di osukulɔɔkɔ.
Obe wɔ baatodiki ni ni di okũ, batii ba banwii niayila ni ninfa lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe biɔbla, be biodiki lɛpɔnkɔbi nwu mimblako?” Ni baabuɛ fɛ mmle di Yesu latɔkɔ ma ni nɛ.
Ni baasuɔtɔ nwu kafɔɔ ladiɛ ma baasifiko ni nɛ.
Obe wɔ baakpaa bɔkɛɛ nwu baawako ni Yesu, baadiki abula lɛma baatika di bɔkɛɛ nwu suoto, ninfɛ di Yesu layie aasiɛ nwɔ kaamaa nɛ.
Batii kpinwu lafukuti abula lɛma baatɛ di osuku, bawo kafɔɔ labudi afata di osukulɔɔkɔ baatɛ diɛ osuku nwu suoto alɛ anafu afe.
Batii ba niale ni katũ ku mba niatikanko ni sɛɛmaa latɔɔtaa siwidi alɛ, “Hosiana!
Di kusɛkusɛ ninle nwɔ nikɔwa ni di Saate leyooto kamɛ!
Bikusɛkusɛsa Ɔka Dawid sɛka kalekɔ ka nikɔwa ni!
Biɛtansa Yaa kaatoo!” Aabuo ni Yerusalem, Yesu lakyɛ Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ.
Aalaanyunyu asaa ya amuu niayila ni ninfa aafenko.
Kafɔɔ ta kale nfɛ latooloo ni oso, aadie aasifi Betania ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi banyɔ nwu baalaate nfa.
Yesu Lakpaani Kolewoso Kunwii.
Di obe wɔ kaale ntɔɔsɛ batoodie di Betania bɔɔwa nii, kɔka laklee Yesu.
Aanya kaakyonkɔ alɛ kolewoso kunwii n-yɛ ku afata kpinwu bɔɔlɛɛkũ ni figi kowoso.
Nioso aakyɛ aalaanyu nse kutika abi di osi.
Kafɔɔ obe wɔ aadu ni kowoso nwu kalɔ, aanya alɛ kuotika abi kuanwii.
Afata ko niatika.
Obe wɔ kubakple kunkpee ni diiwo saa.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ kowoso nwu alɛ, “Kuonwii dilaasinkpee lewosobi lɛfɔ kaanya diidii!” Basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lanu alɛ aabuɛ nkpo.
Yesu Lakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ.
Baakyɛ baalabuo ni Yerusalem, Yesu lakyɛ Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ ninfɛ aakyako mba niatoosunsu ni asaa ku mba niatɔɔya ni asaa ninfa ototososa odiki leeyo nwu kamɛ.
Aatutukusa koto babiɛtɛ siipunu aayu.
Aatukusa mba ninsi boosunsu ni ablonumaa kafɔɔ akpomii aayu.
Nioso atatuna alɛ otii kuonwi atuka lɛsalɛsaa afenko di Yaa Olekatakɔ anu ninfa.
Ninfɛ aatuo ma asaa aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bɛɛkpana di kɔkpana kelekele kukũ kamɛ alɛ, ‘Baalɛɛ mi leyo alɛ ɔlaa ɔpɛ katakɔ.’ Kafɔɔ aye, bitɔɔyɔ biɛbla bayu kawofakɔ!” Yaa olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ ba niawɛ ni ninfa lanu ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu labuɛ nii.
Nioso baatoomiɛ osuku wɔ baafe baalo nwɔ nii.
Kafɔɔ baatɔɔyɛkɛ ta mmle di asaa otuo nɔɔ labla ni ɔkpɛ oso.
Kɔɔtɔɔfɔ nkpaa lawo nii, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ladie diɛ okpoo nwu kamɛ.
Yesu Latuo Asaa Di Ɔlaa Ɔpɛ Ɔta Yaa Ku Ofũ Onu.
Kaleesɛ ku kuyitatũ, batooyefe osuku boosifi nii, baanya alɛ kolewoso nwu ntookpi ku sidu nɔɔ kuyɛ.
Petro lanyuma lɛsaa le niawa nii, ninfɛ aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, nyu kowoso ko faakpaani ni ntɔɔyɔɔ!” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bifũ Yaa binu.
Kɔtɛ nta ye letofo nlɛ otii lele niɛtɔkɔ kobokote ko alɛ kutaka kulabuo diɛ lekpo kamɛ, di otu nɔɔ dietĩi nwɔ osuku, eefũ eenu, dibawa kanya ninkpo nintɔɔ.
Nioso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse biɛpɛ ɔlaa biɛta Yaa, lɛsaa lele biɛkaalɛ nwɔ, biefũ bienu bilɛ bibawɛ, Yaa kafɔɔ mabla anta ye.
Se biɛwakosa asi kasɔ bilɛ biɔpɛ ɔlaa minta Yaa, biɛnya bilɛ otii owo lɛbla ye okpile, biyɔ bikyɛ nwɔ mmle diɛ Teeye kaatoo kafɔɔ kayɔ sikpile lee ankyɛ ye ni.
Kafɔɔ se biɛyɔ bikyɛ nwɔ, Teeye kaatoo kafɔɔ dilɔbayɔ sikpile lee akyɛ ye.” Batii Lakaalɛ Yesu Alɛ Fɛ Diɛ Otumi Nɔɔ Nwu Lekye.
Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakple baakyɛ Yerusalem.
Obe wɔ di Yesu nkyɛ ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ, Yaa olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo lakyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ.
Ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔmɛnsuku fakpe fɔɔbla asaa ya mmle?
Owe kafɔɔ niɛta fɔ osuku nwu nkpo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bitɛɛ nkaalɛ ye ɔlaa onwii, nse biediki kanya yi, ni amii matɔkɔ ye osuku wɔ nkpe fiɛ kɔbla ni asaa ya mmle nwu nkpo.
Bitɔkɔ mi, ɔfɛ di Yohane lawɛ osuku fiɛ aatookpeesa batii Yaa ntu?
Yaa nfũ kuakye ɛɛ, sɛɛ batii nfũ kuakye?” Ninfɛ baamumufũ ɔlaa nwu nimanima baanyu alɛ, “Be nfɛ buabuɛ?
Nse buobuɛ bulɛ Yaa nfũ kuokye yi, abakaalɛ wo alɛ, ‘Ni be oso bitafũ Yohane bianu mɔ?’ Kafɔɔ nse buobuɛ bulɛ ‘Otii nfũ kuokye’ yi!” Bɔɔyɛkɛ nwu kafɔɔ obuɛ diekye bamuu lɛma beefũ beenu alɛ Yohane yi, Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ aale.
Nioso baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Buoye.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di amii, namatɔkɔ ye otii wɔ niɛtɛɛ ni osuku fiɛ kɔbla ni asaa ya mmle nɛ.”
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Aakyeko Awosobi Ya Man-yɔ Mambla Ni Nta Kofe Banyutɛ Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa alɛ, “Obe onwii, osuɔtɔ onwii lakpɛ awosobi ya man-yɔ mambla ni nta kofe.
Aakpee kɔba aakyisa kofe nwu.
Aakutu dibiɔ di kasɔ nwu ntɛɛ di nfũ abatoodiki ni awosobi nwu nta.
Aatofo lɛba le niataka ni kle, baayila mantoonyu ni kofe nwu.
Ninfɛ aayɔ kofe nwu nkpo aakpee di bakpɛntɛ banwii nnɛɛ kamɛ alɛ batoonyu, ni aadie aasifi osuku nɛ.
Di obe lawo alɛ baatɛsɛ ni awosobi nwu, aakpee kpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ alɛ, akyɛ aalaafũ kalekɔ nɔɔ awako nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ kofe nwu banyuntɛ lamufũ kpɛmblatɛ nwu, baapɛ nwɔ, baatososɔɔ aasifi nnɛɛ fukiti.
Nni sɛmaa, kofe saate wɔ mmle lakple aakpee kpɛmblatɛ bamba.
Aakyɛ nii, kofe banyuntɛ ba mmle lapɛ nwɔ baapila nwɔ disi baakpee nwɔ sinunsɔ nwaa.
Osuɔtɔ wɔ lakple aakpee kpɛmblatɛ bamba, baalo nwɔ.
Aakple aakpee babamba.
Baapɛ bawo, baalo kafɔɔ babule.
“Otii wɔ niabu aakple ankpee nwɔ ni niale obi nɔɔ wɔ ambɔmbɔ nii.
Lɛyɛntɛle aakple aakpee obi nɔɔ nwu.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ suoto alɛ, ‘Lefũ lenu nlɛ babata obi nii nwu dibu.’ Kafɔɔ kofe nwu nkpo banyuntɛ latɔkɔ bawo alɛ, ‘Nnya kofe saate obi wɔ nimale ni atesaa ninle nwɔ mmle nɛ.
Biwa biɛta bulo nwɔ di atesaa nɔɔ nwu nkpo akple wo ale!’ Nioso baamufũ obi nwu, baalo nwɔ.
Baafuki nwɔ baayu diɛ kɔba nwu sɛmaa.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ batii nwu alɛ, “Lɛ bienyu bilɛ kofe saate nwu mabla?
Matɔkɔ ye!
Abakyɛ nfa aanaalo kofe banyuntɛ nwu an-yɔ kofe nɔɔ ankpee baatii bamba nnɛɛ.
N-ye nlɛ bitɔka di Kɔkpana Klekle kamɛ lɛba le beebuɛ alɛ, ‘Difuɔ le baayotofotɛ lesĩ nii, nni nintookple difuɔ le niemufũ leyokɔ dikle ni nɛ.
Saate niɛbla lɛsaa kplɛ le mmle.
Nioso diɛbla wo ɔkpɛ osie kanya.’ ” Obe wɔ baanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, Yuda batii batunletɛ lamiɛ osie kanya alɛ boomufũ Yesu.
Diekye baatofo alɛ mma oso aapɛ lɛkpa nwu.
Kafɔɔ baayɛkɛ batii dikudi le niayila ni ninfa.
Nioso baadiɛ nwɔ baasifi.
Baakaalɛ Yesu Ɔlaa Di Akpooto Ofũ Suoto.
Sɛmaa, baakyesee Farisi batii bawo ku Herodes batikankotɛ bawo baakyɛ Yesu nfũ alɛ, baalaawolaa nwɔ kaanya di sɛlaa ɔkaalɛ kamɛ.
Baadu nwɔ nii, baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buye bulɛ nwaako ɔlaa fambuɛ obe lele.
Fanyɛkɛ otii, nkpo kafɔɔ fanannyu otii di anu nɛ.
Kafɔɔ fantuo batii bamuu osuku wɔ ninkpaa otii kunsifiko ni Yaa nfũ.
Nioso tɔkɔ wo se dilɛ alɛ buata akpooto munta Roma Batii Ɔka Kplɛ Kaesare.
Buta ɛɛ, butanta?” Kafɔɔ Yesu lanya kakyɔnkyɔ osuku wɔ suoto baakyɛ nii, nioso aabuɛ alɛ, “Be oso biomiɛ bilɛ bikyɔɔ mi okũ?
Biyɔ koto nwu biwakoe ninnyu.” Baayɔ koto nwu kunwii baawako nwɔ.
Ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Owe disi ku leyooto nintika?” Ni baadiki kanya alɛ, “Kaesare nintika.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nioso biyɔ lɛsaa le ninle ni Kaesare lele bitɔɔ.
Biɛyɔ lɛsaa le ninle ni Yaa lele kafɔɔ bita Yaa.” Ta nni oso, kanya ditasimbɛ ma, diekye diabla ma ɔkpɛ.
Yaa Ninle Ɔka Di Batii Ba Nintookpi Ni Suoto.
Ni di Saduki batii ba nimbuɛ alɛ nse otii lekpi alaasintaka akye ni bakpi kamɛ lawa Yesu nfũ baabakaalɛ nwɔ ɔlaa nɛ.
Baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, Mose lakpana kufiofa ko mmle ɛɛtɛ wo alɛ, nse osuɔtɔ owo lekpi eediɛ ɔsɔfɔ ɛɛtɛ, manko nwɔ banaa obi, osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo obilɛma kayɔ kpisɔfɔ nwu nkpo manlofo babi.
Ni babi nwu nkpo, batii manya ma fɛ osuɔtɔ wɔ ninnaa ni babi.
Obe onwii, babilɛma suɔtɔbi bakuɛnsĩ banwii lawɛ.
Ɔkasale layɔ ɔsanko aakpi obe wɔ manayilofo ni babi.
Ɔnyɔɔfa kafɔɔ layɔ nwɔ, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aakpi diɛ obe wɔ manko ɔsanko nwu bayilofo ni obi kuonwii.
Obilɛma tiɛfa kafɔɔ labayɔ ɔsanko nwu, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aabafe aakpi di obe wɔ manayilofo ni obi.
Ta nkpo oso bakuɛnsĩ lɛma nwu layɔ ɔsanko wɔ onwii baaloo.
Bamuu lɛma baakpi di obe wɔ batalofo ni obi ku ɔsanko nwu.
Yɛntɛyɛntɛ, ɔsanko nwu kafɔɔ labakpi.
Nimɔ, di dii le baakpi makple mantaka nii, owe lɛma ɔsɔfɔ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo male di obe wɔ baakuɛnsĩ lɛma nwu layɔ nwɔ ni?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Diele nkpo dibate saa.
Lɛnya nlɛ bienu ɔlaa wɔ mmle kasɔ, diekye bieye sɛlaa se ninsi ni diɛ Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ, ee Yaa osie.
Obe wɔ di bakpi mataka nii, babate fɛ Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ di osi, nioso sɛsa ku sɛsɔfɔ dilabasinwɛ.
Kafɔɔ fɛ bakpi okple ɔtaka ɔlaa, Mose lakpana lɛsaa di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ aakyeko dibuu le niatoofiɛ ni suoto.
Sɛɛ biloonyuma?
Nfa aakpana alɛ, Yaa latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Ami ninle Abraham Yaa, ku Isak Yaa, ku Yakob Yaa nɛ.’ Nle mmle kotuo alɛ, nnwɔɔ ninle batii ba ninkpe ni nkpa Yaa, diele bakpi Yaa ale.
Katɔkɔ ye nii, aye biɛtɛ bieyu!” Kɔmɛnfiofa Ninle Kufinle?
Ni diɛ kufiofa tuotɛ onwii layila ninfa aanu ɔlaa wɔ baatoobuɛ nii.
Ni aanu alɛ Yesu lalolaa ɔlaa nwu kanya aadiki nwaa.
Ninfɛ aatɛɛtɛ Yesu aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔmɛnfiofa ninle kufinle di afiofa nwu amuu kamɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kufiofa ko niefĩ kulenke ni amuu ninle, ‘O Israel batii, bilolaa binu!
Saate Yaa onwii ko ale, lete nɔɔ kafɔɔ ko ninkpe nɛ.
Nioso dikpe nii fɛɛbɔmbɔ Saate lɛfɔ Yaa, ku otu lɛfɔ omuu, ku ninwuna lɛfɔ nimuu, ku disibu lɛfɔ nimmuu, ku osie lɛfɔ omuu.’ Kufiofa ko niekple kutikanko ni nko ninle alɛ, ‘Bɔmbɔ owo lɛfɔ fɛ mmle okle fambɔmbɔ ni suoto.’ Kufiofa kukunwii nsinnaa kulenke ni n-ya mmle.” Ninfɛ di kufiofa tuotɛ nwu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, fɛɛkakatɛ nwaa!
Nwaa dile fɛ mmle feebuɛ ni alɛ, Saate lete ninle Yaa, ni Yaa bamba kuonwii nsinnaa dilenkee ni nnwɔɔ.
Nioso dikpe ni otii lɛbɔmbɔ Yaa ku otu nɔɔ omuu ku disibu nɔɔ nimuu ku osie nɔɔ omuu.
Dikpe ni kafɔɔ, ambɔmbɔ owo nɔɔ fɛ mmle okle ambɔmbɔ ni suoto nɔɔ.
Dilɛ alɛ otii katikanko afiofa ya mmle anlenkee alɛ ɔɔyɔ babɔkɛɛ ku oleɔta alɛ ɔɔta Yaa.” Diɛ Yesu lanya osuku biene wɔ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle ladiki ni kanya, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Faakyo di Yaa kafa nwu saa.” Nni kamaa, kuonwii ditasinkpee otu aakaalɛ Yesu ɔlaa kuonwii.
Owe Ninle Otii Wɔ Bɛɛpɛ Ni Ɔfɔɔ?
Obe wɔ di Yesu latootuo ni ɔlaa biene nwu di Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ, aakaalɛ ɔlaa alɛ, “Lɛ diawa fiɛ kuufiofa batuotɛ labuɛ alɛ Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ, Dawid leyo kamɛ obi ale?
Dawid nwu omu, Ninwuna Klekle niakpaa nwɔ ni abuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa latɔkɔ Saate nii alɛ, “Siɛ di oletanɛɛkyɛ nii, dilaase di, obe wɔ fabatakatɛsa nkpaa fantika ni di balo lɛfɔ suoto.” ’ Obe wɔ di Dawid omu lalɛɛ Kristo nwɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ alɛ Saate nii, lɛ nfɛ di Kristo nwu, makple anle nwɔ obi?” Batii kpinwu layila ninfa ku suoto lɛyɔɔ baatoonu sɛlaa se di Yesu layila aatoobuɛ nii.
Yesu Lasĩ Ɔlaa Aata Kufiofa Batuotɛ.
Di Yesu latootuo ni batii nwu asaa, aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu di kufiofa batuotɛ suoto.
Manklee asaa kplɛ mantookyikyii akpaka mmle baatii kasɛɛsa ma ni ku dibu.
Mammiɛ alɛ boosiɛ diɛ banɔɔfotii nsiɛkɔ di bawokalɛɛkɔ ku asaa kalekɔ di siipunu kplɛ ntũ.
Mantafaa bakpisɔfɔ kafɔɔ manfũ ma asaa amuu ninnɛɛ.
Mambla fɛ balɛ baatii anu, manklɛsa ɔlaa ɔpɛ ɔta Yaa di akpaka.
Letoko nanfi lɛma mapɔ ninlenkee batii bamuu ale!” Kpisɔfɔ Piitɛ Onwii Lata Lɛsaa.
Yesu lakyɛ aalaasiɛ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu ninfũ manta ni asaa, aatoonyu mmle di batii kofe mankpee ni ato di asaa ɔta lekpeesa kamɛ.
Basaawɛntɛ kpinwu lata ato kplɛ alɛ bootuo suoto.
Kafɔɔ kpisɔfɔ piitɛ onwii labafe aalaakpee mplɛ nnyɔ.
Ni di Yesu lalɛɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ aasiisa aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɛ ntɔkɔ ye nlɛ, kpisɔfɔ piitɛ wɔ mmle niɛta koto alenke di batii ba bamuu niɛta ni koto kamɛ.
Diekye batii ba bamuu niɛta ni asaa, di lɛsaawɛ lɛma kamɛ nle ninlɛ ma ni bɛɛyɔ bɛɛbata.
Kafɔɔ ɔsanko wɔ mmle di dipii nɔɔ kamɛ, lɛsaa le ninkpe nwɔ aale ansiɛ ni nkpa nimuu ɛɛyɔ ɛɛbata nɛ.”
Yesu Lakakatɛ Aakyeko Yaa Leyo Nwu Obiɛ Suoto Di Yerusalem.
Obe wɔ di Yesu ladie ni di Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ oosifi nii, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ onwii latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, nyu afuɔ nwaa ya bɛɛyɔ beetofo ni ayo ya kplɛ ku mmle beetofo nya ni.
Diɔlɛ onyu lo!” Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Lolaa ayo biene ya mmle fanyu nwaa, diekye afuɔ ya mmle kuninwii dilɔɔbabu ditika leewo suoto alɛ blɔbabiɛ nya bakpakpaa bawii!” Yesu Latɔkɔ Batikankotɛ Nɔɔ Alɛ Babawɛ Amiina Ku Dibuo.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu lasifi aalaasiɛ ni di Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote suoto yi, nfa aanyu Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu di osuku kakyɛ nyɔɔfa.
Ninfɛ di Petro ku Yakobo ku Yohane ku Andrea lawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ buɛɛ baabakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, tɔkɔ wo, ɔmɛmbe di nle mmle mawa?
Be nimale dituosaa le bubayɔ muntofo bulɛ, obe nwu ntoowo ni?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu nwaa alɛ otii kuonwii lakyɔnkyɔ ye.
Batii kpinwu mayɔ leyooto nii manwa ɔkyɛ lee, mamatɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Ami dile,’ man-yɔ mankyɔnkyɔ batii kpinwu.
Bitanta diabla ye ɔkpɛ se bienu kakpɛ kudu di ɔlɔɔkɔ lee ee kakyonkɔ.
Dikpe ni asaa ya mmle okle lɛwa.
Kafɔɔ dietuo alɛ kayi kalookɔ ntoowo.
Nnle mataka baawo suoto, sɛka nlekɔ kafɔɔ mataka baawo suoto.
Nsɔ matũkũ di aba aba.
Aka siene kafɔɔ makpɛ di aba aba.
Asaa ya mmle nte fɛ mmle lɛɛmɛ nkye kasɔ nintoonu ni mɛlakatɛ nintɔɔtɛ nii.
“Dikpe nii, bielolaa bienyu.
Babamufũ ye mansifiko nkankɔ.
Babapɛ ye di Yuda batii bawo nsiisakɔ.
Ta ami oso, bibayila di baka ku batunletɛ anu, mintɔkɔ ma Yaa ɔlaa biene nwu nkpo.
Kafɔɔ fiɛ di kayi kaloo mawa nii, dikpe nii beebuɛ Yaa ɔlaa biene nwu bɛɛtɔkɔ batii bamuu kaayi.
Di obe wɔ babamufũ ye mansifiko ni kakankɔ, bitambu diisi di ɔlaa wɔ biofe ni obuɛ olesakatũ.
Se obe nwu lewo, biebuɛ ɔlaa lele di Yaa Ninwuna Klekle mata ye ni.
Diekye diele aye bamu ɔlaa bibabuɛ.
Ninwuna Klekle nimata ye ɔlaa wɔ bibabuɛ nii.
“Batii mayɔ babilɛma manta alɛ balo.
Balofotɛ kafɔɔ mabla nkpo di babi lɛma suoto.
Babi mataka di balofotɛ lɛma suoto alɛ balo ma.
Batii bamuu makyidi ye ta ami oso.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ niekpee otu ɛɛlaase ni kaayɛntɛlekɔ, kamawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Yesu Lakple Aabuɛ Alɛ, Dibuo Mawa Diɛ Obe Nwu Kamɛ Di Aye Ba Nintikankoe Ni Suoto.
“Binu ɔlaa wɔ matɔkɔye ni nwaa obebe biɛnya abusufɔɔsaa yɛkɛle n-yɛ di lɛba le ninankaatɛ alɛ aayila nii, ni biɛta batii ba ninkpe ni di Yudia batoso basifi abokote osi balaawofa.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ nintika ni di leyo nɔɔ osi, atantɔkɔ alɛ oosoo anwa amayɔ lɛsalɛsa nɔɔ leeyo kamɛ ansifiko.
Otii wɔ ninkpe ni koofe, atasinkple aatɔkɔ alɛ ooyie ammayɔ akleesaa nɔɔ leeyo.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, dibatɛ ninwɛ osie ninta basanko ba ninlaka ni amɛ ku mba nikɔta babi nyɛɛfu nii.
Bipɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa bilɛ, obe nwu kutanwa di lɛwɔɔfɔ obe!
Diekye dibuo le nimawa ni diɛ obe nwu kamɛ malenkee nle okle nintɔwa diɛbafe ni di obe wɔ kaayi lakye ni kasɔ diɛbase ni diɛ miɛ dii le mmle.
Dibuo le mmle okle kafɔɔ dilabasinwa diidii.
Kafɔɔ Saate lɛkɔkɔlɛ ayi nwu nkpo.
Se diele nkpo ɛɛbla se otii kuonwii dilababu.
Kafɔɔ ta batii nɔɔ ba eediki ɛɛta ni suoto oso, ɛɛkɔkɔlɛ ayi nwu.
“Nioso se otii owo lɛtɔkɔ fɔ alɛ, ‘Nyu!
Nnya Kristo ninfũ!’ ee ‘Nyɔɔ ninfa!’, tanfũ nwɔ faanu!
Diekye batii mataka manlaa mambuɛ alɛ mma ninle Kristo nwu nkpo, bawo kafɔɔ mabuɛ alɛ Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ bale.
Bababla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni sɛkpɛ ku atuosaa ate ate mantuo alɛ, nse dialɛ yi, baayɔ mankyɔnkyɔ bia batii ba di Yaa lediki eese ni lete.
Nioso bilolaa binyu!
Nkpo oso ntoole katũ lɛtɔkɔ ye sɛlaa se mmle simuu fiɛ di obe nwu mawo nɛ.
Otii Obi Nwu Makple Anwa.
“Ayi ya nimawa ni diibuo nwu sɛmaa, ‘Kufĩ mata ditunu, kɔwɛntɛ kafɔɔ dilabapu.
Awɛntlɛbi kafɔɔ makpa ankye osi, osi asaa kafɔɔ matididi di aba ya atika nii.’ “Nni kamaa batii manya Otii Obi nwu makyɔɔ di alokonkyɛ kamɛ ɔɔwa ku osie kplɛ di leklekle kamɛ.
Abakyesee Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ kaayi ka mmle nkyakakɔ nwu nkpo nna, mansiisa batii nɔɔ ba eediki ni mankyeko kaasɔ disi le diɛlase ni diisi le.
Lɛsaa Tekete Di Kolewoso Suoto.
“Bitekete lɛsaa bikyeko kolewoso suoto.
Nse kuodie sɛlamii fɔle kuodie atoto kuokpee afata fɔle kamaa, bietofo bilɛ kanto ɔnɔɔ bee nfɛ kowo.
Nkpo kafɔɔ se nfɛ diɛwa alɛ asaa ya lɛtɔkɔ ye ni nfɛ kɔkyɔɔ, ni bietofo bilɛ ni kayi kalookɔ nfɛ kɔtɛɛtɛɛ katoodu ni kayokontũ lɛfɔ tintĩ!
Nwaa kɔta ye mintofo nlɛ asaa ya mmle amuu mawa fiɛ di kale lee batii bamuu maloo okpi.
Osi ku kasɔ kamuu mafe, kafɔɔ ɔlaa nii nnwu, kulabafe diidii.
“Otii kuonwii dieye dii nwu nkpo ku obe wɔ kamɛ dibale nii.
Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ ba ninkpe ni di osi dieye.
Bia Obi nwu nkpo omu dieye, Ote lete ninnye.
Bilolaa binyu, biɛta anu lee ate kesekese, ta bieye dii le diɛ obe nwu mawo nii.
Ote di bate fɛ mmle diɛ otii ndie ni di okpoo nɔɔ alɛ ɔɔkyɛ ni osuku, andiɛ ni bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ leeyo.
Aata obiala ɔkpɛ wɔ abatɔɔbla nii.
Nni kamaa, aatɔkɔ otii wɔ nikonyu nwɔ ni ayo kayoko kplɛ alɛ alolaa kayoko anyu nwaa.
“Ta nninkpo oso ayee bilolaa suoto.
Diekye bieye obe wɔ diɛ Saate lee mawa ammabuo nii.
Diafuo ole alɛ kakũ, ee nkyɛntɛɛ, ee obe wɔ diɛ bakɔɔkɔ mbo nii, ee oyita.
Se loo eefua ɛɛwa, mmle ninamate alɛ ɛɛbatũ ye bisi biɔkyɔsĩi nii.
Lɛsaa le kɔtɔkɔ ye ni ninfũ, nni nwu ko nkle kɔtɔkɔ batii bamuu nɛ.
Nni oso kafɔɔ bialolaa suoto nɛ.”
Yuda Batii Ku Yaa Olebatatɛ Lakpee Asi Baawo Alɛ Boolo Yesu.
Ditoobu ayi anyɔ fiɛ di Yuda batii male ni ayi lɛma ya manlɛɛ ni Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ku Bloblo wɔ Ninantaka Ni Olebee, man-yɔ mannyuma ni odie lɛma di Egipte.
Olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ lawɛ ninfa baatoomiɛ osuku wɔ baawofa mamufũ Yesu manlo nii.
Ni baabuɛ baatɔkɔ bawo alɛ, “Ditanwa alɛ buɔbla lɛsaa le mmle di ayi ya buole ni kamɛ.
Se diele nkpo, batii manya ɔblɔ mantaka wo di suoto.” Ɔsanko Onwii Lafifia Yesu Nnɔnyi Kɔnɔkɔnɔ Diisi Diɛ Betania.
Yesu lawɛ di Betania okpoo diɛ Simon wɔ niafiɛ ni ofiɛ sɛɛle leyo.
Ɔbe wɔ di Yesu lasiɛ aatoole ni alesaa, ɔsanko onwii lawa nfa.
Aaklee difuɔ kylɔkylɔ lebo ninwii di nnɔnyi kɔnɔkɔnɔ be niefũ ni kɔya osie kanya lasiɛ ni kaamɛ.
Ɔsanko wɔ mmle latikiti lebo nwu aanyɛɛnɛ nnɔnyi nwu aakpete di Yesu disi.
Lɛsaa nwu lafiɛ batii ba niayila ni ninfa bawo ɔblɔ diata baabuɛ alɛ, “Be lɛsaa oso ɛɛlalaasa nnɔnyi be mmle, nkpo okle?
Aafuo ɔyɔ osunsũ anwɛ lɛlɛɛ nɔɔ ɔkpɛ koto an-yɔ anta bapiitɛ.” Ta nnle mmle oso, baasĩ ɔlaa baatɔɔ ninfa osie kanya.
Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bidiɛ nwɔ!
Be oso biokpee ɔsanko wɔ mmle kubuɛ?
Lɛsaa biene ninle nle mmle ɛɛbla ɛɛtɛɛ nii nɛ.
Bapiitɛ nsi ye kaamɛ obe lele.
Obe lele mimbɔ biafuo ma ɔkyakaako.
Kafɔɔ ami, diele obe lele kamawɛ ye kaamɛ.
Ɔsanko wɔ lɛbla lɛsaa le aafuo ni ɔbla.
Ɛɛyɔ nnɔnyi kɔnɔkɔnɔ be mmle eekpete mi, oololaa mi anta okookaa bee nii.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, kakɔ lele beeyie ɔlaa biene wɔ mmle lɛkya di kayi ka mmle kamɛ yi, lɛsaa le di ɔsanko wɔ mmle lɛbla nii, bababuɛ nwu man-yɔ mannyuma nwɔ.” Yuda Latuna Alɛ Oodiki Yesu Anta.
Ninfɛ di Yuda Iskariot, dile ni Yesu basaateketetɛ onwii lɛma, lakyɛ olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nfũ aalaatɔkɔ ma alɛ abadiki Yesu anta ma nɛ.
Suoto layɔɔ ma nwaa diɛ ɔlaa wɔ aabatɔkɔ ma ni oso, mma kafɔɔ baabuɛ alɛ babatɔɔ koto.
Nioso Yuda nfɛ lawɛ ninfa aatoomiɛ osuku wɔ suoto abafe andiki Yesu anta ma nii.
Yesu Ku Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Lale Okpi Diisi Ofe Alesaa Lɛyɛntɛle.
Diɛ Bloblo wɔ Ninantaka ni Dii ole kamɛ, di dii kasale le suoto manlo ni Okpi Diisi Ofe lefosobi, Yesu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔfɛ foomiɛ falɛ bulaawa Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole alesaa nwu buta fɔ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki banyɔ kaamɛ lɛma aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bikyɛ okpoo, osuɔtɔ onwii mawa amakyakako ye atuka ntu dibukii.
Bitikanko nwɔ biɛlaabuo leyo le kamɛ ababuo ni.
Biɛkaalɛ leyo nwu saate bilɛ, ‘Saatuotɛ alɛ bukaalɛ fɔ nii, lɛmɛnyo kamɛ di ami ku basaateketetɛ nii, bubasiɛ munle Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa?’ Abatuo ye leyo dibinte ninwii beetofo beetika ni di osi, nfũ beelolaa, beese ni asiɛsaa.
Biwa mmiɛ dii nwu alesaa ninfa bita wo.” Basaateketetɛ ba ladie baasifi okpoo nwu, baalaanya lɛsaa biala fɛ mmle di Yesu latɔkɔ ma ni.
Ni baawa Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa nwu ninfa baase nɛ.
Obe wɔ di kɔtɔɔfɔ lawo nii, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu lefosi banyɔ lasifi baalaabuo nfa.
Obe wɔ nfɛ baasiɛ baatoole ni alesaa di opunu katũ, Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii onwii kaamɛ lee madiki mi anta, nũ busi buole alesaa mmle.” Ɔlaa nwu lata ma disibu, ninfɛ baatɔɔkaalɛ nwɔ onwii onwii alɛ, “Nwaa, n-ye nlɛ diele ami falaka, sɛɛ ami dile?” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Onwii leefosi banyɔ lee kamɛ dile.
Munko nwɔ niekpee kɔnɛɛ kaasɛfɛ ninfũ nɛ.
Ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, makpi fɛ mmle okle di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ labuɛ nii.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimadiki ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, anta nii, ayɔɔsa.
Nse bia batanlofo nwɔ, nse dilɛ nwɔ dilenke!” Saate Loo Opunu Katũ Alesaa Nyɛntɛle Ole.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nsi boole ni alesaa yi, ni aayɔ bloblo nɛ.
Ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, aafee nwɔ, aayɔ aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ, aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bifũ bile.
Nle mmle ninle suoto nii sina nɛ.” Ninfɛ aayɔ opũ, ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, aayɔ aata bamuu lɛma baanyi.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nle mmle ninle ntɔ nii be bɛɛyɔ beese ni kaanya di Yaa kanya ninii le eenii ni ku batii nɛ.
Beewii mi kaasɔ di batii kpinwu disi.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, noosinwa nta be mmle onyi diɛlase di dii le makple nyi ni nta fɔle diɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ.” Ninfɛ baasa onu onwii baatansa Yaa, ni baadie baasifi Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote suoto nɛ.
Yesu Labuɛ Aatɛ Alɛ Petro Mabɛ Ɔnyasie Di Suoto Nɔɔ Alɛ Aaye Nwɔ.
Nfa di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bamuu lee bibatoso mindiɛ mi.
Diekye Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ labuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa malo bafosokpatɛ nwu nkpo se bafoso nwu bamuu ntɔɔsamii.’ Kafɔɔ nse beekple bɛɛsɛnkɛsɛɛ bɛɛwako nkpa kamɛ yi, male ye katũ nsifi Galilea.” Ninfɛ di Petro latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Mintɛ bawo nii bamuu matoso mandiɛ fɔ yi, ami diidii namatoso ndiɛ fɔ!” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ Petro alɛ, “Kɔta fɔ fantofo nwaa nlɛ miɛ kakyɛ fiɛ di kɔɔkɔ mabo ni sɛnyɔ afɔ omu fababuɛ sitiɛ simu falɛ faaye mi.” Petro lakple aatɔkɔ nwɔ osie kanya aalenkee lɛkasale alɛ, “Nse bia olo alɛ booloe munko fɔ yi, diidii namabuɛ nlɛ ninye fɔ.” Basaateketetɛ bule bamuu kafɔɔ labuɛ nkpo.
Yesu Lapɛ Ɔlaa Aata Yaa Di Lɛba Le Bɔɔlɛɛ Ni Getsemane.
Nni kamaa baalaadu lɛba le bɔɔlɛɛ ni Getsemane.
Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bisiɛ ninfũ ninaapɛ ɔlaa nta Yaa.” Ni aakpaa Petro ku Yakobo ku Yohane aasifiko nɛ.
Otu latɔɔpɛ nwɔ, aakyako otũtũkũ kpakpa.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Konu dibuo di otu nii kamɛ osie kanya fɛle kukpi ninkle mi.
Aye bisiɛ ninfũ bietoonyu.” Aakyɛ ni sitũ kɛɛkɛ, aapɛ akunkyi, ni aafuusa anu kaasɔ aatikiti Ote lekoto alɛ, “Se dialɛ, ni, dibuo obe wɔ mmle dife mi.” Ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Teete nii!
Fanfuo asaa amuu ɔbla.
Se feetuna, faatekete dibuo opũ wɔ mmle di suoto nii.
Kafɔɔ tambla nle ninlɛ mi nii, bla dibiesaa lɛfɔ.” Ninfɛ aakple aawa basaateketetɛ nɔɔ batiɛ nwu nfũ, aabatũ ma bɔɔkyɔsĩi.
Ni aatɔkɔ Petro alɛ, “Simon, sɛkyɔsĩ bikle?
Ni bilaafuo osiɛ otoonyunkoe lebombo ninwii pɛ?” Ni aakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bita anu lee ate kesekese biɛpɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa mmle minaabuo ni diɛ ɔsɔ onyu kamɛ.
Ninwuna komiɛ ɔbla, kafɔɔ suoto sina nnaa osie.” Aakple aasifi aalaapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa fɛ mmle aabuɛ ni lɛkasale.
Obe wɔ aakple aawa ni basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo nfũ, aabanya ma baatɔɔkyɔsĩi, batafuo bia anu otikiti.
Nioso batafuo ɔlaa kuonwii obuɛ ɔtɔkɔ Yesu.
Aakple aawa ni ditiɛfa, aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Sɛkyɔsĩ biɔkyɔsĩi mintɛ ɔnyɛɛ nkpo nɛ?
Nfɛ dilɛ!
Obe ntoowo!
Batɔɔyɔ ami, Otii Obi nwu, beekpee diɛ bakpileblatɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Binyu, nfɛ bakyɛ diɛ osuku bɔɔwa.
Bitaka buɔlaakyakako ma.
Binyu!
Otii wɔ niediki mi ɛɛta ni nleko ma katũ.” Baamufũ Yesu.
Yesu lakple aayila aatɔɔkakatɛ ko ma fiɛ di Yuda wɔ ninle ni lefosi batii banyɔ nwu nkpo onwii lɛma lawa.
Batii dikudi le di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo ladiki ni latikanko nwɔ baatɔɔwa.
Baaklee nwosoku ku mpamii.
Otii wɔ niadiki Yesu aata ni latɔkɔ ma aatɛ alɛ, “Otii wɔ kamaminiko mbla ni atuu yi, nnwɔɔ ninle nwɔ biowolaa ni nɛ.
Biemufũ nwɔ, biɛkpaa nwɔ bisifiko, biɛta anu lee atika nwɔ di suoto.” Obe wɔ diɛ Yuda labadu ni nfa, ni aakpukuti aatɛɛtɛ Yesu, aalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ!” Ni aaminiko nwɔ aabla nwɔ aatuu nɛ.
Ninfɛ baamufũ Yesu nɛ, baakle nwɔ kpinkpĩ.
Kafɔɔ batii ba niayila ni di Yesu ɔlɔɔkɔ onwii lɛma ladiki kapamii nɔɔ aasafɔ Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo kpɛmblatɛ onwii kotoko aakpa nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Be oso di mpamii ku nwosoku bikle biɛwa mi omufũ fɛle kpileblatɛ nɔɔfo nle?
Lasiɛ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo dii biala latootuo batii asaa, kafɔɔ bitatɔkɔ bilɛ biomufũ mi.
Kafɔɔ fɛ mmle di Yaa Kɔkpana Klekle lebuɛ nii, dikpe nii, ninwa kaanya.” Ninfɛ diɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ bamuu latoso baadiɛ nwɔ nɛ.
Di obe wɔ mmle kamɛ, okosopo onwii lakpa kabulɛɛ fututu lete aatikanko Yesu aatoonyu ɔsaabla nwu omuu.
Basaanyuntɛ nwu lamiɛ alɛ boomufũ okosopo nwu.
Kafɔɔ kabulɛɛ fututu nɔɔ nwu ko baafuo ɔwɛ.
Diekye aasikitisa suoto, aadie ma ninnɛɛ.
Ninfɛ aatoso aasifi ku lɛkyɔtɔ nɛ.
Aadiɛko ma kabulɛɛ nɔɔ nwu.
Yesu Layila Diɛ Yuda Batii Banɔɔfo Anu Kaakankɔ.
Ninfɛ baakpaa Yesu baasifiko Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo leyo nɛ.
Nfa diɛ Yaa olebatatɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ lasi nɛ.
Petro latikanko nwɔ sɛɛmaa fanfa aalaabuo Yaa Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo nwu leyo kaflɔnkɔ di bawo kalɛɛkɔ.
Aalaasiɛ di asaa banyuntɛ ɔlɔɔkɔ, aatɔɔwɔfɔ ɔtɔ.
