Olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku bakantɛ nwu nkpo niawɛ ni ninfa bamuu lamiɛ alɛ boobudi kanya mantika di Yesu suoto mmle baafuo nwɔ ni olo.
Kafɔɔ batawɛ ɔlaa kuonwii di suoto nɔɔ.
Batii kpinwu lababuɛ sɛlaa baatika nwɔ di suoto kafɔɔ nnya lɛma ditabla kanwii.
Batii bawo kafɔɔ labayila baalaa sɛlaa kuafunu baatika di Yesu suoto alɛ, “Buanu aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Mabiɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ ka mmle bɛɛyɔ nnɛɛ beetofo nii.
Diɛ ayi atiɛ kamaa, makple ntofo lɛbamba ninanle batii nietofo nii.’ ” Batii ba mmle kafɔɔ, nnya lɛma ditabla kanwii di sɛlaa se baabuɛ ni di suoto nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo lataka aayila siitũ lɛma aakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Feenu ɔlaa wɔ beebuɛ ni di suoto lɛfɔ?
Ɔmɛnlaa ninkpe fɔ fambuɛ?” Kafɔɔ Yesu lamaasa kanya atabuɛ ɔlaa kuonwii.
Yaa Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo nwu lakple aakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Kristo nwu di Yaa lɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ ale ni Yaa Klekle Obi nɛ?” Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ami nɛ.
Diɛyɔ di nua diesifi nii, bibanya Otii Obi nwu nkpo nsi di Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni oletanɛɛkyɛ.
Bibanyɔɔ kafɔɔ eekye osi ɔɔwa di alokonkyɛ kamɛ!” Ninfa nwu, Yaa Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo niabɛ awu nɔɔ ku ɔblɔ aabuɛ alɛ, “Falɛ obee ye?
Diesinfĩ alɛ otii kuonwii kayila ɔlaa owo kamaa!
Bienu mbusuo ɔlaa wɔ eebuɛ ni di Yaa suoto?
Ɔmɛnlaa ninkpe ye mimbuɛ?” Ni bamuu lɛma baabuɛ alɛ, eekpi lɛpɔɔ, dikpe nii beelo nwɔ.
Batii bawo kaamɛ lɛma lakyako sita otufa okpete Yesu.
Baanii nwɔ anu, baakyako nwɔ ɔpɛ ku nnɛɛ lɛma.
Ni baatɔɔtɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Faye ni lɛsaa biala, tɔkɔ wo otii wɔ niɛpɛ fɔ ni!” Ninfɛ di basaanyuntɛ nwu kafɔɔ lakpaa nwɔ baalaapɛ nɛ.
Petro Lasĩ Alɛ Aaye Yesu.
Di obe nwu kamɛ Petro lakple aawɛ di bawo kalɛɛkɔ nwu fiɛ di Yaa Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo kpɛmblatɛ sankobi nɔɔ onwii lawa nfa.
Obe wɔ aanya alɛ Petro nsi ɔɔwɔfɔ ni ɔtɔ, ni aakyako nwɔ onyu tuwĩi aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔɔ faatikanko Yesu Nasaret Otii nwu!” Ninfɛ di Petro labɛ ɔnyasie aabuɛ alɛ, “Obeeye?
Ami noonu ɔlaa wɔ foobuɛ ni ninfũ kasɔ!” Ninfɛ aataka aadie di kayoko nɛ.
Nfanwu aadu ni kayoko, kɔɔkɔ niabo.
Okpeele wɔ mmle lakple aabanya Petro ninfa, ni aakple aatɔɔtɔkɔ batii ba niayila ni ninfa alɛ, “Onwii lɛma ale!” Kafɔɔ Petro lakple abe ɔnyasie.
Ditale obe fiɛ diɛ batii ba niayila ni ninfa latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Flafuo ɔnyasie obe falɛ diele onwii lɛma fale diekye afɔɔ Galilea kasɔ feekye.” Ninfɛ di Petro labuɛ alɛ, “Lɛka nlɛ nwaako kobuɛ!
Yaa ananfi mi kootoko nse ɔlaa kɔlaa!
Ninye osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle ɔlaa biobuɛ nii!” Nfanwu kɔɔkɔ niabo lɛnyɔɔfa, ninfɛ di Petro lanyuma mmle di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Fiɛ di kɔɔkɔ mabo ni sɛnyɔ, fababuɛ sitiɛ falɛ faaye mi.” Obe wɔ diabudi nwɔ nii, aawi kaku.
Baakpaa Yesu Baasifi Ko Pilato Abaa Ɔnɔɔfo Ɔkyɛ.
Dii nwu kuyitatũ Yaa olebatatɛ lakyakako okpoo banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ kuɛ bakantɛ bamuu.
Obe wɔ batoosiɛ beebu ni ɔlaa nwu disi ku mmle baabla ko nwɔ ni ɔkpɛ, baanii Yesu baakpaa nwɔ baasifiko Roma abaa ɔnɔɔfo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Pilato ɔkyɛ.
Nfa diɛ Pilato lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Yuda batii Ɔka nwu nɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nnwu fatoobuɛ nɛ.” Yaa olebatatɛ nwu layɔ sɛlaa kpinwu baatika di Yesu suoto.
Nioso Pilato lakple aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Floobuɛ ɔlaa kuonwii?
Kyɔɔ atoko faanu sɛlaa se boobuɛ fɔ ni di suoto!” Kafɔɔ Yesu ditabɛ kanya, nioso diabla Pilato ɔkpɛ!
Baalo Yesu Lɛpɔɔ Alɛ Aakpi.
Di Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole biala yi, Pilato ndiɛ Yuda batii leyo batentɛ lele, baatii nwu lɛkaalɛ ni anta ma.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, baamufũ osuɔtɔ onwii bɔɔlɛɛ ni Baraba baalaatɛ leeyo ku batii nɔɔ.
Ta kudu lɛma okpee ku batii olo di obe wɔ baataka baayila ni di Roma batii ɔka suoto.
Obe wɔ baatii labasi nii, baanyumasa Pilato leyo batentɛ ba andiɛ antɔɔta ma ni obe lele di dii nwu ole kamɛ.
Ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Biomiɛ bilɛ ndiɛ Yuda Batii Ɔka nwu nta ye?” Pilato lakaalɛ ma nkpo ta aatofo alɛ onunsɛɛ kanya oso di Yaa olebatatɛ nwu lakpaa Yesu baawako nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ Yaa olebatatɛ nwu lamunikĩisa batii dikudi nwu disibu mmle diɛ Pilato kadiɛ Baraba bonwu anta ma nii.
Pilato lakple aakaalɛ batii dikudi nwu alɛ, “Obe biomiɛ bilɛ mbla otii wɔ biɔlɛɛ ni Yuda batii Ɔka nwu ninfũ?” Ninfɛ baayiisa kudu baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Pɛ nwɔ sibuɛ fakaasa koowoso suoto!” Kafɔɔ Pilato lakple aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ɔmɛnkpile ɛɛbla fiɛ?” Kafɔɔ mia nfɛ baakple baatɔɔfaa osie kanya baatoobuɛ alɛ, “Pɛ nwɔ sibuɛ fakaasa koowoso suoto!” Ta Pilato komiɛ alɛ suoto siyɔɔ ma ni oso, aadiɛ Baraba aata ma.
Ni aata baapɛ Yesu nwaa ku mpile, ni aayɔ nwɔ aakpee ma ninnɛɛ alɛ balaapɛ nwɔ sibuɛ bakaasa koowoso suoto nɛ.
Bakpɛtɛ Nwu Lakpee Yesu Sinunsɔ.
Bakpɛtɛ nwu lakpaa Yesu baasifiko Roma batii abaa banɔɔfo leyo diɛ bawo kalɛɛkɔ, ni baalɛɛ bakpɛtɛ bule alɛ bawa nɛ.
Ninfɛ baayɔ awu sɛɛle ya niefũ ni kɔya wua baakpa nwɔ fɛ ɔka, ni baabla sɛkansi lɛkakoto baatũkũsɔɔ nɛ.
Ni baayila baatookpee nwɔ sinunsɔ alɛ, “Yii yiiduu!
Yuda batii Ɔka, asiɛ nkpa aklɛ!” Baayɔ kawesee baatɔɔpɛ nwɔ diisi, baatufa sita baakpete nwɔ di suoto.
Ninfɛ baapɛ akunkyi kaatũ nɔɔ baawakosa asi kasɔ baatɔɔ.
Obe wɔ batooloo nwɔ ni ɔma, baadiki nwɔ awu sɛɛle nwu di suoto baakplesa awu nɔɔ baakpee nwɔ.
Ninfɛ baakpaa nwɔ baasifiko alɛ bɔɔlaapɛ nwɔ sibuɛ mankaasa koowoso suoto nɛ.
Baakaasa Yesu Koowoso Suoto.
Obe wɔ baatoofe nii, baakyakako osuɔtɔ onwii bɔɔlɛɛ ni Simon, aakye kakpayotũ kanwii ɔɔwa Yerusalem.
Ninfɛ di bakpɛtɛ nwu nkpo layila nwɔ di suoto alɛ afũ Yesu kowoso nwu nkpo atuka nɛ.
Simon nwu lakye Kireni kasɔ.
Babi nɔɔ kafɔɔ niale Aleksandro ku Rufo.
Ni baakpaa Yesu baalaadu lɛba le manlɛɛ ni Golgota lɛɛsɔdiki ninle ni alɛ Otii Disi Dikufi.
Nfa baayɔ nta be bɛɛkpɔtɔɔsa ni ku kɔfa lonle nimata alɛ ɔlɔbanu ni dibuo baatɔɔ alɛ anyi, kafɔɔ Yesu ditanyi.
Ninfɛ di bakpɛtɛ nwu nkpo lapɛ nwɔ sibuɛ baakaasa koowoso suoto nɛ.
Nni kamaa, baayɔ awu nɔɔ baasɛ bawo di obe wɔ baawii ni atrebi baatofo n-ya di obiala lɛma kayɔ nii.
Baapɛ Yesu sibuɛ baakaasa koowoso suoto ku oyita elomu ɛnaasĩ.
Baapɛ kataaboo kakyɛɛ sibuɛ baakaasa nwɔ diɛ lɛkantosi baakpana lɛsaa le oso baalo nwɔ nii alɛ, “Nnwɔɔ ninle Yuda Batii Ɔka nɛ.” Baapɛ bayu banyɔ kafɔɔ sibuɛ baakaasa di awoso suoto diɛ Yesu ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Onwii lakaa diɛ oletanɛɛkyɛ nɔɔ, onwii kafɔɔ lakaa diɛ ɔmɛntukyɛ.
Diawa ninkpo fɛle mmle baakpana ni diɛ Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, “Baalo nwɔ manko bakpileblatɛ.” Batii ba niatoofe ni ninfa bamuu latũkunsa asi, baatufa Yesu baabuɛ alɛ, “Ɛhɛɛ!
Afɔ niabuɛ falɛ fababiɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ ka mmle, fanse ni letofo di ayi atiɛ kamɛ nɛ!
Soo koowoso nwu fawa, faafũ suoto lɛfɔ nkpa buonyu!” Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ nwu nkpo lama nwɔ baatoobuɛ kaamɛ lɛma alɛ, “Aafũ batii bamba nkpa kafɔɔ oloofuo suoto nɔɔ odiki!
Se nwɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Yuda Batii Ɔka, dile ni Kristo wɔ di Yaa lɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ ale nwaako, aasoo di kowoso suoto awa buofũ nwu bunu!” Batii ba banyɔ baakaasa ni di awoso suoto ku nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ latufa nwɔ.
Yesu Lakpi.
Kakũ lefosi elomu ɛnyɔ lebe, kayi kamuu lawɔfɔ.
Dialaase di kɔtɔɔfɔ elomu etiɛ kamɛ.
Di kɔtɔɔfɔ elomu etiɛ kamɛ okle, Yesu lafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Eli, Eli, lama sabaktani?” Lɛsɔdiki ninle alɛ, “Yaa nii, Yaa nii, be oso feediɛ mi nnɛɛ nkpo?” Batii ba bawo niayila ni ninfa, baanu ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, “Bikyɔɔ atoko!
Ɔɔlɛɛ Elia.” Nfanwu onwii kaamɛ lɛma latoso aalaayɔ oleteku aanyɔ di nta nyankale kamɛ, aayɔ aatũ di owoso suoto, aamiɛ alɛ ɔɔyɔ ankyɔɔ nwɔ annyi.
Kafɔɔ batii bule labuɛ alɛ, “Bita buyila buonyu, nse Elia kamawa amadiki nwɔ di kowoso suoto!” Yesu lakple aafaa osie kanya ninfɛ aakpi nɛ.
Nfanwu, dibula le ninsaka ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ niabɛ di akyuu anyɔ diakye di osi dialaase kaasɔ.
Di bakpɛtɛ ɔnɔɔfo wɔ niayila ni di kowoso nwu katũ lanu mmle di Yesu lafaa fiɛ aakpi nii, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako, Yaa Obi ninle otii wɔ mmle!” Basanko bawo kafɔɔ layila kaakyonkɔ baatoonyu asaa ya niatɔɔwa nii.
Bawo niale Maria Magdalene ku Salome ku Maria wɔ babi ninle ni Yakobo bisɔ ku Yose.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu lawɛ ni di Galilea kasɔ, mma niatootikanko nwɔ baatɔɔ kyakaako nwɔ nɛ.
Basanko kpinwu ba latikanko nwɔ baakyɛ ni Yerusalem ke layila ninfa.
Baakookaa Yesu.
Asaa ya mmle amuu lawa fiɛ diadu Yuda batii Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi.
Nfɛ diofe ni kɔɔtɔɔfɔ, Yuda batii ɔnɔɔfotii onwii bɔɔlɛɛ ni Yosef eekye ni Arimatea, lakpee otu aakyɛ aalanya Roma batii ɔnɔɔfo Pilato.
Yosef wɔ mmle ninle otii wɔ niatookpee ni osie diɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɔwabee nɛ.
Obe wɔ aadu ni Pilato nfũ, aatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ atɔɔ osuku aalaayɔ Yesu kpi alaakookaa, fiɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi diwo.
Diabla Pilato ɔkpɛ obe wɔ aanu alɛ Yesu lawolaa ni okpi nkpo.
Nioso aalɛɛ bakpɛtɛ ɔnɔɔfo wɔ niayila ni kaanya ninfa aakaalɛ nwɔ aanu nkaakyonkɔse nwaa Yesu ntookpi.
Di ɔnɔɔfo nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ kute ni nkpo, Pilato lata Yosef osuku alɛ alaayɔ kpi nwu akookaa.
Ninfɛ di Yosef lasifi aalaayɔ Yesu kpi nwu nkpo, ni aayɔ dibula fɔle le aaya ni aamiminisa nwu di suoto nɛ.
Ni aayɔ aalaakookaa di ofuɔntuu kamɛ beekutu ni di kabokotee ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Ninfɛ aamunusa difuɔ aatĩi ofuɔntuu nwu kanya nɛ.
Obe nwu kamɛ, Maria Magdalene ku Maria dile ni Yosef ɔya layila baatonyu lɛba le baakookaa ni Yesu.
Yesu Lataka Aakye Baakpi Kamɛ.
Kaleesɛ dile ni Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi kɔtɔɔfɔ, Maria Magdalene ku Maria dile ni Yakobo ɔya ku Salome lakyɛ baalaaya kɔfa kɔnɔkɔnɔ alɛ babalaafifia di Yesu kpi suoto.
Nioso kaasɛ ni Kɔsida kolesɛtũ, baataka baakyɛ di ɔkya katũ.
-Baatoofe nii baatɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Owe bubawɛ abamunusa difuɔ le kplɛ di akya kanya anta wo?” Baakaalɛ bawo ta difuɔ nwu lamuɔ nwaa.
Kafɔɔ baadu ni nfa, baanya alɛ batoomunusa difuɔ nwu beekyisa.
Nioso baabuo ni di ɔkya nwu kamɛ, baanya alɛ okosopo onwii nsi diɛ oletanɛɛkyɛ.
Aaklee abula fututu!
Ɔfɔɔ lasifi ma.
Ninfɛ di okosopo nwu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitanyɛkɛ.
N-ye nlɛ Yesu Nasaret Otii wɔ baakasa ni koowoso suoto biowolaa.
Anaa ninfũ!
Atɔɔtaka, akpe nkpa!
Binyu!
Nnya nfũ baatɛ nwɔ ni.
Nioso bitɔɔkyɛ biɛlaa tɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ku Petro bilɛ, ‘Yesu ntoole ye katũ oofe Galilea kasɔ.
Nfa bibanyɔɔ nɛ, fɛ mmle aatɔkɔ ye aatɛ nii.’ ” Diabla basanko ba ɔkpɛ, ni baakyɛ di ɔkya nwu katũ ku lɛyɛkɛ baatoso baasifi nɛ.
Baakyɛ di osuku baatoosifi nii, batatɔkɔ otii ɔlaa kuonwii, ta lɛyɛkɛ lamufũ ma ni oso.
Yesu Ladiki Suoto Aatuo Maria Magdalene.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lataka aakye ni baakpi kamɛ di Kɔsida kolesɛtũ, Maria Magdalene aaka suoto odiki otuo, nwɔ kamɛ aatososa ni anwuna kpile akuɛnsĩ di obe onwii kamɛ.
Aakyɛ aalaatɔkɔ Yesu batikakotɛ nɔɔ alɛ, Yesu ntɔɔtaka di obe wɔ basi boowi kaku ta kukpi nɔɔ oso.
Obe wɔ di Maria latɔkɔ ma alɛ, Yesu ntɔɔtaka akpe nkpa ni ɛɛnyɔɔ nii, batafũ nwɔ baanu.
Yesu Ladiki Suoto Atuo Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Banyɔ.
Nni sɛmaa, Yesu ladiki suoto aatuo basaateketetɛ nɔɔ banyɔ, obe wɔ baakye Yerusalem boofe ni sekpoo nwu.
Batatofo nwɔ di kasɔ kakyekɔ.
Kafɔɔ sɛmaa baabatofo nii, baakple baasifi baalaatɔkɔ babule.
Kafɔɔ batafũ ma baanu.
Yesu Ladiki Suoto Aatuo Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Lefosi Onwii.
Lɛyɛntɛle, Yesu ladiki suoto aatuo basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi onwii di obe wɔ basi boole ni alesaa.
Aananfiko ma ɔlaa ta banaa ni ofũ onu oso, bakpe kafɔɔ otokopĩ kpã ta batafũ batii ba nianyɔɔ nii baanu di obe wɔ atɔɔtaka, akpe ni nkpa.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ kayi kamuu biɛlaayie Yaa ɔlaa biene nwu lɛkya diɛ batii bamuu kamɛ.
Otii wɔ nimafũ ɔlaa biene nwu annu nii, eefũ ni Yaa ntu okpeesa, Yaa madiki nwɔ di sikpile letokonanfi kamɛ.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ ninaanfũ anu nii, Yaa malo nwɔ lɛpɔɔ.
Yaa mata bafũbanutɛ osie mambla ablasaa ya niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ kpinwu.
Babatososa anwuna kpile di leyooto nɔɔ kanya.
Bababuɛ sele ate ate.
Se beemufũ asaanwu ee beenyi kɔfa kpile, dilababla ma lɛsalɛsaa.
Se beetika nnɛɛ lɛma di bafiɛtɛ suoto, babawɛ osie.” Yaa Lakpaa Yesu Aasifiko Yaa Kafa.
Di Saate Yesu lakakatɛ aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ aaloo ni sɛmaa, Yaa lakpaa nwɔ aasifiko osi, ni aasiɛ di oletanɛɛkyɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Batikankotɛ nɔɔ kafɔɔ lakyi kakɔ biala baabuɛ ɔlaa biene nwu.
Saate lɛma lasiɛ ma kaamɛ aadiki atuo alɛ ɔlaa nɔɔ nwu ɔlaa biene kule di ablasaa ate ate ya baatɔɔbla ni di otumi nɔɔ kanya.
Obiloo Tiofilo, batii kpinwu lekpee ɔnyɛɛ bɛɛbla mmle baafuo nii, bɛɛkpana lɛsaa biala niawa ni kaamɛ loo bɛɛtɛ.
Baakpana nya baatɛ fɛ mmle baatii ba nianya ni asaa ya mmle ku anu lɛma kaasɔ kakyekɔ latɔkɔ wo nii, ku mba kafɔɔ nia buɛ nwu nii.
Nkpo oso, bienetɛ Tiofilo, ta nntoobuo di asaa ya mmle kamɛ nwaa lɛnyu ni diɛyɔ ni kaasɔ kakyekɔ oso, ntɔɔbla disibu nlɛ, dilɛ alɛ kakpana nya fɛ mmle diawa ni klekle nta fɔ.
Kɔbla nle mmle ta mmle faatofo ni onukware omuu wɔ ninsi ni di asaa ya baatootuo fɔ ni suoto.
Baayie Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Olofobee Lɛkya Baatɛ.
Di obe wɔ kamɛ di Herode latoole ni sɛka di Yudea kasɔ suoto, Yaa oletatɛ onwii lawɛ baatɔɔlɛɛ nwɔ ni Sakaria.
Aakye olebatatɛ dikudi le manlɛɛ ni Abia kamɛ.
Sakaria wɔ mmle ɔsɔfɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ Elisabet nɛ.
Nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aakye Yaa oletatɛ wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Aaron kafaabi kamɛ.
Ɔsa ku ɔsɔfɔ wɔ mmle, baasiɛ nkpa biene di Yaa anu.
Baale kafɔɔ Saate afiofa nwu amuu, baakyɛ di sisuku nɔɔ suoto.
Batii ba mmle ditawɛ obi kuonwii, diekye Elisabet ɔlɛma aale.
Banyɔ lɛma kafɔɔ batoobe beefũ alɛɛ kpinwu.
Dii ninwii, Sakaria latɔɔbla ɔkpɛ nɔɔ fɛ oletatɛ di Yuda batii Olekatakɔ, diekye dikudi lɛma suoto nfɛ diadu.
Diekye, di olebatatɛ ɔsaabla kanya, baawii atrebi baadiki Sakaria alɛ akyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ aalaafiɛ odufii di Yaa oleɔta akyikye suoto.
Obe wɔ aawɛ ni ninfa aatoofiɛ ni odufii nwu, batii dikudi bule kafɔɔ lawɛ kaayi baatɔɔpɛ ɔlaa baatɔɔta Yaa.
Ninfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ onwii lakyɔɔ di oleɔta akyikye oletanɛɛkyɛ, aadiki suoto aatuo nwɔ di obe wɔ ayɛ ofiɛ ni olufii nwu.
Di Sakaria lanyɔɔ nii, aabla tro, lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ nwɔ osie kanya.
Kafɔɔ Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Sakaria, tanyɛkɛ!
Yaa ntoonu fɔ ɔlaa ɔpɛ, ɔsɔfɔ lɛfɔ Elisabet malofo obi suɔtɔbi anta fɔ.
Faatika nwɔ leyooto falɛ Yohane.
Suoto mayɔɔ fɔ osie kanya se beelofo nwɔ.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di suoto mayɔɔ batii kpinwu nɛ.
Aba le otii finle di Yaa anu.
Atannyi wanyi ee nta siene kunwii.
Ni dibayɔ ni di olofobee nɔɔ, Ninwuna Klekle mayii nwɔ kamɛ pɔ.
Nnwɔɔ nimakplesa Israel batii kpinwu anwako Saate Yaa lɛma nfũ nɛ.
Abale Saate katũ anwa di osie ku sɛkambi kamɛ fɛ mmle di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Elia late nii.
Di lɛwa nɔɔ kamɛ abalolaa babi ku bate ntɛɛ.
Abata batokopĩtɛ disibu nkyi mambu disi fɛ batii klekle.
Abalolaa kafɔɔ Saate batii nɔɔ mansiɛ mansoko nwɔ.” Ninfɛ di Sakaria lakaalɛ Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu alɛ, “Be nimata nfũ ɔlaa wɔ mmle nnu?
Diekye ntoobe kofokofoko, ɔsɔfɔ nii kafɔɔ ntoobe laakpa nwu.” Ninfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ami ninle Gabriel wɔ ninyila ni di Yaa anu nɛ.
Nnwɔɔ niekpee mi alɛ, matɔkɔ fɔ ɔlaa biene wɔ mmle nɛ.
Kafɔɔ faafũ mi ɔlaa wɔ mmle nimawa ni kaanya di obe biene kamɛ fanu.
Ta nkpo oso fabakple omumu flabasinfuo ɔkakatɛ, diɛlase di obe wɔ kamɛ di ɔlaa wɔ mmle kɔtɔkɔ fɔ ni lɛwa ni kaanya.” Di obe wɔ kamɛ diɛ asaa ya mmle amuu latɔwa nii, diabla batii ba niayila ni kaayi baasoko ni Sakaria ɔkpɛ.
Diekye batatofo lɛsaa le oso aatɔɔklɛ ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo.
Obe wɔ nfɛ di Sakaria ladie ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu, atafuo ma ɔkakatɛko.
Nioso nnɛɛ nfɛ aatoowiwii aayɔ aatɔɔkakatɛko ma.
Nioso batatofo alɛ, odiki otuo aanya.
Obe wɔ di Sakaria ɔkpɛ ɔbla ntooloo ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu, aadie ninfa aasifi leyo.
Ni di obe owo kamɛ, ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ Elisabet labalaka lɛmɛ, aawofasa suoto awɛntɛ anɔɔ amu, atadie kayi.
Ninfɛ di Elisabet labuɛ alɛ, “Nunua, Yaa ntoole mi sibualɛ, atootekete mi sinunsɔ di suoto di batii anu.” Baayie Yesu Olofobee Lɛkya Baatɛ.
Di awɛntɛ akuɔ kamɛ nfɛ di Elisabet nlaka ni lɛmɛ, Yaa lakpee tɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ Gabriel alɛ akyɛ okpoo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Nasaret, di Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ wɔ mmle layɔ kanya aakyɛnko kakpeelebitɛ ka baakaalɛ baata ni osuɔtɔ wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Yosef, aakye ni ɔka Dawid kɔna kamɛ.
Kakpeelebitɛ nwu leyooto niale Maria nɛ.
Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu lawa Maria nfũ aabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔsɛɛsa fɔ!
Saate nwu nsiko fɔ, eekusɛkusɛsa fɔ kafɔɔ.” Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ wɔ mmle ɔlaa wɔ aatɔkɔ ni Maria latɔɔ disibu, diekye atanu ɔlaa nwu kasɔ.
Ninfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Maria, tanyɛkɛ, diekye Yaa ntoole fɔ sibualɛ.
Fabalaka lɛmɛ, fanlofo obi suɔtɔbi, fantika nwɔ leyooto falɛ Yesu.
Abale otii kplɛ, babalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni petee Obi.
Saate nɔɔ Yaa mase nwɔ sɛka fɛ mmle aase ni ɔwa nɔɔ Dawid.
Abale sɛka di Yakob kɔna kamɛ obe lele.
Diidii sɛka kalekɔ nɔɔ nnaa kaloo.” Nfa nfɛ di Maria lakaalɛ Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu alɛ, “Lɛ nfɛ di nle mmle mawa kaanya, ninanye ni osuɔtɔ?” Nfa nfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ninwuna Klekle mawafɔ di suoto, Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni osie kafɔɔ matikafɔ di suoto.
Ta nkpo oso Obi Klekle nwu fɔɔwa ni ɔbalofo, baalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ, Yaa omu Obi.
Nunua, komiɛ nlɛ fatofo falɛ, leyo lee kamɛ ɔsanko wɔ ninle ni Elisabet bɔɔlɛɛ ni ɔlɛma, nfɛ alaka lɛmɛ, nu atoobe nkpo.
Kɔwɛntɛ kuɔnle nɔɔ nfɛ asi ni nɛ.
Diekye lɛsalɛsaa nnaa Yaa osie ku ɔbla.” Ninfɛ di Maria latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nyu lo, Saate kpɛmblatɛ nle.
Abla aatɛɛ fɛ mmle okle feebuɛ ni.” Ninfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu lasifi aadiɛ nwɔ nɛ.
Maria Lakyɛ Elisabet Nfũ.
-Di ayi nwu kamɛ Maria lataka aapɛsɛwa aalolaa suoto, aakyɛ okpoo onwii di Yudea kasɔ di kabokoee suoto, aalaabuo Sakaria leyo, aasɛɛsa Elisabet.
Diawa alɛ obe wɔ di Elisabet lanu ni Maria lɛsɛɛsa, obi wɔ ninsi nwɔ ni kaafutu kamɛ lakpɛ.
Nfanwu Ninwuna Klekle niayii Elisabet kamɛ pɔ.
Ninfɛ aakakatɛ aabuɛ osie kanya alɛ, “Beekusɛkusɛsa fɔ di basanko bamuu kamɛ, beekusɛkusɛsa kafutu lɛfɔ kamɛ obi kafɔɔ!
Sɛmɛmbualɛ ninle nse, alɛ, Saate nii ɔya kawa amasɛɛsɛɛ?
Di obe wɔ kamɛ fɛɛkyako mi ni ɔsɛɛsa, nfanwu obi wɔ ninsi mi ni kaafutu kamɛ niɛkyako ɔkpɛ ku suoto lɛyɔɔ.
Suoto siyɔɔ fɔ osie kanya, diekye feefũ feenu falɛ ɔlaa wɔ di Yaa lɛkakatɛ eekyeko ni suoto lɛfɔ mawa kaanya.” Maria Lasa Katansa Onu.
Maria lataka aabuɛ alɛ, “Otu nii kɔtansa Saate nwu.
Suoto kɔyɔɔ ninwuna nii di Yaa wɔ ninle mi ni Dikitɛ suoto, diekye eenyuma mi, ami wɔ ninle nwɔ ni kpɛmblatɛ ninandie ni lɛsalɛsaa.
Nioso diɛyɔ ni di nua diesifi nii, ana ya nikɔwa ni sɛɛmaa, mawa mamalɛɛ mi suoto lɛyɔɔ otii, Diekye di lɛsaa le di Yaa wɔ ninklenke nii, lɛbla ɛɛtɛɛ ni oso.
Leyooto nɔɔ ninle klekle nɛ.
Nyaami nɔɔ ɔnya nte diɛta mba ninyɛkɛ nwɔ nii, diɛyɔ ni kɔɔna diesfi ni kɔɔna, Eediki osie nɔɔ kayi, ɛɛsamiisa batii ba nintakatɛsa ni suoto lɛma katoo ku disibu lɛma nimuu, Ɛɛtakatɛsa baka siene laakpomii lɛma suoto, ni ɛɛtakatɛsa mba niɛwakosa ni suoto lɛma kasɔ katoo nɛ.
Ɛɛta batii ba di aka nkle ni lele alesaa biene beemiɛ, kafɔɔ ɛɛta basaawɛntɛ lesifi ku kɔka.
Eenyuma ntam nɔɔ be aaka aata ni bawa loo, ni atɔɔwa alɛ ɔɔbadiki bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ Israel nɛ.
Atoonyuma alɛ ootuo nyaami nɔɔ ɔnya di Abraham suoto ku banantii nɔɔ diesifi ni, dinnaa ni kaloo.” Maria lasiɛ di Elisabet nfũ fɛ awɛntɛ atiɛ fiɛ aakple aasifi leyo nɔɔ.
Yohane Ntu Kpeesatɛ Lelofo.
Di obe lawo alɛ Elisabet kalofo nii, ni aalofo obi suɔtɔbi nɛ.
Ni di Elisabet bawo nɔɔ ku banatii nɔɔ lanu mmle okle di Yaa lele nwɔ ni sibualɛ, ni baamuu lɛma lanyako nwɔ suoto lɛyɔɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di obi nwu nkpo lafũ ni ayi anɛ, baawa alɛ bɔɔbabudi nwɔ lɛsɔkɔsɔkɔ, ni baamiɛ alɛ bɔɔyɔ ote Sakaria leyooto mantika nwɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ ɔya ditatunako ma, ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Batika nwɔ leyooto bilɛ, Yohane.” Ninfɛ baananfiko nwɔ ɔlaa baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔnantii lee kuonwii diloole leyooto le mmle okle fiɛ de?” Nioso, baawiwii nnɛɛ baakaalɛ obisɔ nwu ote alɛ, lɛmɛnyooto omiɛ alɛ bayɔ batika obi nɔɔ nwu.
Ninfɛ di Sakaria lakaalɛ alɛ batɔɔ lɛkpanafuɔ, ni aakpana aatika alɛ, “Leyooto nɔɔ ninle Yohane.” Diabla bamuu lɛma ɔkpɛ osie kanya.
Nfanwu, Sakaria lakple aakyako ɔkakatɛ, ni aakyako Yaa ɔtansa nɛ.
Lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ manko mba ninsi bakaako ni bawo.
Batii labuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle baakyakasa sekpoo se simuu ninkpe ni di Yudea kobokotee kamɛ.
Batii ba bamu nianu ni sɛlaa se mmle latoobu diisi baatɔɔkaalɛ alɛ, “Ɔmɛntiikle di obisɔ wɔ mmle kɔwa ɔbale?” Diekye diakpa kɔmɛ alɛ, Yaa otumi ntika nwɔ di suoto.
Sakaria Ladiki Yaa Ɔlaa Aabuɛ.
Diawa alɛ Yaa Ninwuna Klekle layii Yohane ote Sakaria kamɛ, ni aabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa alɛ, “Bita butansa Saate, Israel Yaa nwu diekye atɔɔwa kale nɔɔ ɔkyakaako, ɛɛwa ma kafɔɔ odiki.
Atɔɔta wo Dikitɛ wɔ ninkpe ni osie nwɔ niekye ni kpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ Dawid kɔna kamɛ.
Yaa labuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle aatɛ kofokofoko diefe ni di ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nɔɔ suoto alɛ, abadiki wo ankyeko bakpileblatɛ ku batii ba niekyidi wo ni bamuu nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Aabuɛ alɛ abanya bawa loo nyaami abanyuma kafɔɔ kanya ninii klekle le aanii ni ku mma.
Aaka ntam aata ɔwa loo Abram osie kanya alɛ, abadiki wo ankyeko bakyiditɛ loo nnɛɛ kamɛ, abata mambla nwɔ ɔkpɛ kafɔɔ di ɔtanyɛkɛ kamɛ.
Alɛ ababla wo klekle, munte tinini di anu nɔɔ di nkpa loo mmuu disiɛbi kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ, afɔ obi nii, babalɛɛfɔ alɛ Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ.
Fabale Saate nwu katũ, fanlolaa osuku fantɛ fanta ɔwabee nɔɔ.
Fabata batii nɔɔ kafɔɔ ntofo alɛ babawɛ didiki, ku sikpile lɛma se babayɔ mankyɛ ma ni oso.
Yaa loo lɛyɔɔ buɛɛ, annya nyaami.
Abakyesee wo dikitɛ wɔ ninkpa ni fɛ mmle kuufĩ nkpa nii.
Abata lɛkpa le mmle nwa di batii ba ninsi ni di ditunu kamɛ di kukpi lɛyɛkɛ nkle ma nii alɛ, abakpaa wo anfenko di atoko ɔkyɛ ole osuku suoto.” Nioso obisɔ nwu lamuɔ di suoto sina kamɛ ku Yaa Ninwuna kamɛ osie kanya.
Aasiɛ di ɔfaafuu di lɛba le baatii diesi ni diaalase di obe wɔ aadiki ni suoto kayi di Israel kafaabi anu.
Yesu Lelofo.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, Ɔka Kplɛ Kaesare Augusto lata otumi alɛ baka batii bamuu ba ninkpe ni di Roma sɛka kalekɔ kamɛ.
Di batii ɔka kasale wɔ mmle kamɛ, abaa ɔnɔɔfo wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Kirenio niatoole sɛka di Siria kasɔ suoto.
Nkpo oso otii biala lasifi okpoo nɔɔ alɛ balaaka nwɔ.
Nioso Yosef kafɔɔ ladie di Nasaret okpoo di Galilea kasɔ aasifi Betlehem di Yudea kasɔ suoto, nfũ baalofo ni ɔka Dawid.
Yosef lasifi nfa diekye Dawid ɔnantii aale.
Manko Maria wɔ baakaalɛ baatɔɔ ni niasifi nfa alɛ balaaka ma.
Aalaka lɛmɛ kafɔɔ.
Obe wɔ baawɛ ni di Betlehem, Maria obe lawo alɛ aalofo.
Ni aalofo obi suɔtɔbi nɔɔ kasale nɛ.
Ni aayɔ sikplakpi aamiminisa nwɔ, aayɔ nwɔ aatensa di lɛsaa le mankpee ni babɔkɛɛ alesaa kamɛ nɛ.
Diekye batawɛ leyo di bafɔɔ kafunkɔ.
Yaa Batɔkyɛntɛ Layɔ Ɔlaa Biene Baawako Bafoso Bakpatɛ.
Diawa alɛ bafoso bakpatɛ banwii lawɛ nintɛɛ nwu kasɔ suoto, baatoonyu bafoso lɛma ku kakyɛ.
Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ onwii ladiki suoto aatuo ma, ni di Saate leklekle lakpa diakpete ma di suoto nɛ.
Ta nkpo oso baayɛkɛ osie kanya, kafɔɔ Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitanyɛkɛ, ɔlaa biene nkyɛnko, nwɔ nimata ye ni suoto lɛyɔɔ osie kanya ku batii bamuu.
Di miɛ dii le mmle suoto, batoolofo Saate wɔ ninle ni Kristo bɛɛtaye di ɔka Dawid okpoo kamɛ.
Lɛsaa le bibanya mintɛ ni nsũ, diotuo alɛ kute ni nkpo ninle alɛ, bibanya beemiminisa obifɔɔle nwu ku sikplakpi, bɛɛyɔ nwɔ beetensa di bafoso lɛsaa le manle ni alesaa kamɛ.” Nfanwu, Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ dikudi kplɛ ninwii niakye osi baakyɔɔ babakyakaa di nwɔ nkpo suoto baatɔɔtansa Yaa alɛ, “Leklekle baata Yaa di osi fanfan, di suoto lɛyɔɔ diwa di batii ba suoto di Yaa mbɔmbɔ ni kaayi!” Di obe wɔ di Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ nwu lakple baasifi ni osi baadiɛ ma ni, bafoso bakpatɛ nwu labuɛ baatɔkɔ suoto lɛma alɛ, “Bita bukyɛ Betlehem buɔlaanyu lɛsaa le niɛwa ni, di Saate nwu ntɔɔtɔkɔ wo ni.” Nioso baapɛsɛwa baakyɛ baalanya Maria ku Yosef ku obifɔɔle nwu niate ni di babɔkɛɛ alesaa lekpeesaa nwu kamɛ.
Nioso obe wɔ baanyɔɔ ni nkpo, baabuɛ lɛsaa biala di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu latɔkɔ ma aakyeko ni obisɔ nwu suoto.
Batii ba bamuu nianu ni bafoso bakpatɛ ba mmle ɔlaa wɔ baabuɛ nii, diabla ma ɔkpɛ.
Maria lamufũ sɛlaa se mmle simuu aakpee diisi, aatoobusĩ disi osie kanya.
Ninfɛ baafoso bakpatɛ ba mmle lakple baasifi, ni baatɔɔtansa Yaa di asaa ya amuu baanu, baanya ni suoto nɛ.
Diekye diawa kaanya tutuutu fɛ mmle di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu latɔkɔ ma nii.
Baatika Yesu Obifɔɔle Nwu Leyooto.
Di ayi anɛ kamaa, obe wɔ di obe lawo alɛ baabudi ni obisɔ nwu lɛsɔkɔsɔkɔ, ni baatika nwɔ leyooto alɛ Yesu, fɛ mmle di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ nwu labuɛ aatɛ ni fiɛ baalaka nwɔ ni lɛmɛ.
Baakpaa Yesu Baakyɛnko Yuda Batii Yaa Olekatakɔ.
Obe wɔ di obe lawo alɛ Yosef ku Maria kabla suoto okleklesa amanle fɛ mmle di Mose kufiofa letuo nii.
Ni baakpaa obifɔɔle nwu nkpo kafɔɔ baasifiko Yerusalem alɛ, bɔɔyɔ nwɔ manakpee di Saate nnɛɛ kamɛ nɛ.
Fɛ mmle bɛɛkpana beekpee ni di Yaa kufiofa kukũ kamɛ alɛ, “Obi suɔtɔbi kasale lele beelofo, baadiki nwɔ lete base bata Saate nwu.” Nioso baakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaayɔ Abronuma anyɔ ee alaapɔɔ anyɔ manta Yaa ole, fɛ mmle di Saate nwu kufiofa lebuɛ nii.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, osuɔtɔ onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Simeon lawɛ di Yerusalem.
Aale otii biene wɔ ninyɛkɛ ni Yaa, aasiɛ aatoonyu osuku aatɔɔta Israel didiki.
Yaa Ninwuna Klekle lasiɛko nwɔ, ni diatɔɔ aatoofo alɛ ɔlabakpi, diediki diɛlase di obe wɔ atɔɔnya ni Saate Dikitɛ nwu baabuɛ alɛ babalofo nii.
Yaa Ninwuna Klekle lakpaa Simeon diasifiko Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu.
Obe wɔ baalofotɛ ba mmle lakpaa obifɔɔle nwu baawako alɛ bɔɔbla fɛ mmle kuufiofa nwu lebuiɛ ni mantɔɔ nii, ninfɛ di Simeon lafũ obifɔɔle nwu aaklee ninnɛɛ, ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa alɛ, “Saate, nunua, fatɔɔnya fɛɛbla di ntam be faaka ni kanya oso, diki ami, kpɛmblatɛ lɛfɔ, osuku aatɔɔkyɛ di atoko ɔkyɛ ole kamɛ.
Ami omu, ntoodiki anu nii lɛnya Dikitɛ lɛfɔ nwu, nwɔ fɛɛta falɛ awa ni di nnle batii anu.
Nnwɔɔ ninle lɛkpa le nimadiki dibiesaa lɛfɔ kayi anta ni batii ba ninanle ni Yuda batii nɛ.
Annanfi dibu kafɔɔ anwako ni Israel batii lɛfɔ kale kamɛ nɛ.” Sɛlaa se di Simeon labuɛ ni di obifɔɔle nwu suoto labla Yosef ku Maria ɔkpɛ.
Ni di Simeon lakusɛkusɛsa ma, aatɔkɔ ɔya Maria alɛ, “Obisɔ wɔ mmle Yaa niekyesee nwɔ ale didiki ku kawɔɔ ɛɛta batii kpinwu di Israel.
Ale nsũ be niekye ni Yaa nfũ baatii kpinwu mataka manyila nwɔ ni di suoto.
Alɛ abadiki batii disi kamɛ sɛwofalaa kayi antuo.
Afɔ kafɔɔ, diefe ni di nle mmle kamɛ oso, fabanu otu kamɛ dibuo fɛ kapamii kobe piɔ̃piɔ̃ bakle bootofo fɔ di otu kamɛ.” -Ɔsanko onwii lawɛ aale ni Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ, nnwɔɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ Hana nɛ.
Ɔsanko nwu ote niale Fanuel, aakye Aser kafaabi kamɛ.
Alɛɛ akuɛnsĩ ko manko ɔsa baayɔ bawo fiɛ aakpi aadiɛ nwɔ.
Ni kamaa aale kpisɔfɔ alɛɛ afosi anɛ alɛɛ ana.
Obe lele ankyɛ Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ kakũ ku kakyɛ anaatɔɔtansa Yaa, annii kanya, antɔɔpɛ ɔlaa antɔɔta Yaa.
Di obe nwu kamɛ tutuutu, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aawa aabapɛ Yaa sɛfa, ni aakakatɛ aakyeko obisɔ nwu nkpo suoto aata batii ba bamuu ninsi boonyu osuku manta ni Yerusalem didiki nɛ.
Baakple Baasifi Nasaret.
Di obe wɔ di Yosef ku Maria ntooloo ni amanle nwu ɔbla fɛ mmle di Yaa kufiofa kukũ letuo nii, baakple baasifi okpoo lɛma di Nasaret, di Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Obisɔ nwu lamuɔ, aawɛ suoto osie, aawɛ kafɔɔ ninumbe osie kanya.
Yaa sibualɛ latika nwɔ di suoto.
Yesu Lakyɛ Yuda Batii Yaa Olekatakɔ.
Lɛlɛɛ biala, Yesu balofotɛ nkyɛ Yerusalem manaale dii le manlɛɛ ni alɛ, Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii.
Nioso obe wɔ di Yesu lafũ ni lefosi alɛɛ anyɔ baakpaa nwɔ baakyɛ dii nwu kalekɔ di Yerusalem, fɛ mmle mambla ni saa.
Di obe wɔ batooloo ni dii nwu nkpo ole, baakple baatoosifi okpoo lɛma, kafɔɔ Yesu lakple aasiɛ di Yerusalem.
Balofotɛ nɔɔ ditatofo.
Baanyu alɛ asi baatii nwu kamɛ, nkpo oso baakyɛ dii kufĩ osuku fiɛ baakyako nwɔ owolaa di basiɛwo nɔɔ ku batii nɔɔ kamɛ.
Obe wɔ batanyɔɔ nii, baakple baasifi Yerusalem baalaatoowolaa nwɔ.
Di dii tiɛfa kamɛ, ni baakyɛ baalaanyɔɔ di Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ nɛ.
Aasiɛ ku Yuda batii basaatuotɛ bawo aatoonu ma, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aatɔɔkaalɛ ma sɛlaa.
Batii ba bamuu nianu nwɔ ni sɛlaa, diabla ma kpo, diekye di lɛɛsɔnu kplɛ le aayɔ aatoodiki ni sɛlaa se baatɔɔkaalɛ nwɔ ni kasɔ oso.
Obe wɔ di Yesu balofotɛ lanyɔɔ nii, diabla ma yaaa.
Ni di ɔya lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Obi, obe oso fɛɛbla wo nkpo?
Ami ku Teefɔ ditɔɔbla wo ninunsɛɛ buokyi munwolaa fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Be oso biokyi minwolaa mi?
Bieye bilɛ Teemi leyo dikpe ni lesiɛ?” Kafɔɔ batanu ɔlaa wɔ aatɔkɔ ma ni kasɔ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latikanko ma baasifi Nasaret nɛ.
Aawakosa suoto kasɔ aata ma.
Ɔya lamufũ sɛlaa se mmle aakpee diisi aatoobu sĩ disi osie kanya.
Yesu lalolaa aamuɔ aawɛ suoto osie.
Aawɛ kafɔɔ ninumbe.
Aabuo batii ku Yaa anu osie kanya.
Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane Layie Ɔlaa Biene Nwu Lɛkya.
-Di lefosi alɛɛ anɔɔ ya kamɛ di ɔka nɔɔfo Kaesare Tiberio latoole ni sɛka, Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛ Yohane wɔ ninle ni Sakaria obi lafũ ɔlaa aakyeko Yaa nfũ di obe wɔ aasiɛ ni di ɔfaafuu kamɛ.
Ni di Pontio Pilato lale Abaa ɔnɔɔfo di Yudea kasɔ suoto nɛ.
Herode kafɔɔ latoole sɛka di Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Di obe nwu kamɛ tutuutu, Herode obilɛma Filipo kafɔɔ latoole sɛka di kasɔ ka bɔɔlɛɛ ni Iturea ku Trakoniti ntɛɛ nwu suoto.
Ni di ɔka Lisania kafɔɔ latoole sɛka di Abilene kasɔ suoto nɛ.
Di obe wɔ mmle kamɛ kafɔɔ, ni di Hana ku Kaiafa lale Yaa olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yohane lakyɛ aakyi Yordan okle sɛmaa ku ntɛɛ nwu mmuu aatoobuɛ Yaa ɔlaa alɛ, “Bikyi siikpile lee kamɛ biefũ Yaa ntu okpeesa, di Yaa ayɔ sikpile lee akyɛ ye.” Fɛ mmle bɛɛkpana bɛɛtɛ ni di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yesaia kukũ kamɛ alɛ, “Otii onwii kɔfaa di ɔfaafuu kamɛ ambuɛ alɛ, ‘Bilolaa osuku bitɛ Saate nwu ɔwabee.
Biɛkyɛkyɛsa abaya abafe ni bitɛ nwɔ.
Bietĩi abaya amuu niekyofo ni.
Biebiɛ kafɔɔ abokote ku kobokotee amuu bitɛ kaasɔ.
Bieyilasa sisuku se niɛkɔnkɔ ni.
Biɛkylɔkylɔsa abaya kafɔɔ niekukyukukyu ni.
Kayi batii bamuu manya Yaa Didiki!’ ” Batii kpinwu ladie baawa alɛ Yohane akpeesa ma Yaa ntu.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye kɔsaanwu kɔna!
Owe niɛka ye alɛ biatoso di Yaa lɛkanko le nikɔwa ni kamɛ?
Bibla asaa ya nimatuo alɛ bitookyi ni siikpile lee kamɛ.
Biediɛ obuɛ ɔtɔkɔ suoto lee bilɛ Abraham banantii bile.
Diekye kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Yaa mafuo afuɔ ya mmle ɔyɔ ɔbla banantii anta Abraham.
Nunua bia yi, batɔɔyɔ kafɛ beese di awoso sidu suoto kofokofoko.
Kowoso lele ninantika abi biene yi, bababudi kũ, man-yɔ kũ mankpee di ɔtɔ kamɛ.” Ninfɛ baatii nwu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni be nfɛ buabla nunua?” Ninfɛ aadiki kanya, aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii lele nikpe osi awu anyɔ, ayɔ anwii ata otii wɔ ninnaa ni kuanwii.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ nikpe ni alesaa, asɛko owo nɔɔ wɔ di alesaa nnaa ni.” Akpooto bafuntɛ bawo kafɔɔ lawa alɛ, bakpeesa ma Yaa ntu.
Ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, be dikpe ni buɔbla?” Ninfɛ di Yohane latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitanfũ akpooto bialenkeesa n-ya bɛɛta ye alɛ biafũ nii.” Bakpɛtɛ bawo kafɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni awo mɔ?
Be dikpe ni buɔbla?” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitan-yɔ suoto osie biafũ koto di otii kuonwii nnɛɛ, ee bitambudi otii kuonwii kanya di osuku kpile suoto.
Bita ato lee ya biofũ ni sɛɛkpɛ mmɛ abuoye anu.” Batii osuku onyu lakyako katoo ɔtaka, ni baatoobu alɛ, loo Yohane ninle Kristo wɔ boonyu ni osuku alɛ abawa ni nɛ.
Nioso Yohane latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ami, ntu kɔyɔ nkpeesa ye.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nikɔwa ni sɛɛmaa nii nlenkee mi.
Otii wɔ ninansiɛko alɛ bia kadiki nwɔ ni ntokota.
Nnwɔɔ, abayɔ Ninwuna Klekle ku ɔtɔ ankpeesa ye.
Akle kɔfɛɛ nɔɔ di nnɛɛ kamɛ, abafɛɛlɛ ni kamɔɔ andiki ni kufuo kaamɛ, an-yɔ kamɔɔ abi ankpete di owu kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ kufuo nkũ, abafiɛ kũ di ɔtɔ wɔ ninaanii ni diidii kamɛ.” Yohane latɔkɔ batii nwu Yaa ɔlaa biene nwu di sisuku ate ate suoto, ni aaka ma alɛ, bakyisa nkpa, di nkpa lɛma disiɛbi kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yohane lasĩ ɔlaa aata Herode wɔ niale ni abaa ɔnɔɔfo, diekye aafũ obilɛma ɔsɔfɔ wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Herodia aayɔ, ku sikpile bamba se kpinwu aabla ni oso.
Nioso okpile wɔ ninlenke ni di Herode lakple aabla ni, ninle alɛ, aamufũ Yohane aatɛ leeyo.
Yohane Lakpeesa Yesu Yaa Ntu.
Obe wɔ di Yohane ntooloo ni batii Yaa ntu okpeesa, aakpeesa Yesu kafɔɔ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu latɔɔpɛ ɔlaa aatɔɔta ni Yaa, kolo lasɛkɛtɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yaa Ninwuna Klekle lasoo nwɔ di suoto fɛ mmle di lɛlaapɔɔ nsoo ni nɛ.
Ninfɛ baanu sɛlɔ lakye osi siabuɛ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle obi nii wɔ suoto ninantuna ni nɛ.
Foobuo mi anu nwaa.” Yesu Banantii Ninle Mba Mmle Nɛ.
Yesu lafũ fɛ alɛɛ afosi atiɛ di obe wɔ aakye ni ɔkpɛ nɔɔ kasɔ.
Batii lanyu alɛ Yosef obi ale.
Yosef ote niale Eli.
Eli ote niale Mattat, Mattat ote niale Lewi, Lewi ote niale Melki, Melki ote niale Yanai, Yanai ote niale ni Yosef.
Yosef ote niale Matatia, Matatia ote niale Amos, Amos ote niale Nahaum, Nahaum ote niale ni Esli, Esli ote niale Nagai.
Nagai ote niale Mahat, Mahat ote niale ni Matatia, Matatia ote niale Semein, Semein ote niale Yosef, Yosef ote niale ni Yuda.
Yuda ote niale Yohanan, Yohanan ote niale Resa, Resa ote niale Sorobabel, Sorobabel ote niale Sealtiel, Sealtiel ote kafɔɔ niale Neri.
Neri ote niale Melki, Melki ote niale Adi, Adi ote niale Kosam, Kosam ote niale Elmadam, Elmadam ote niale Er.
Er ote niale Yosua, Yosua ote niale Elieser, Elieser ote niale Yorim, Yorim ote niale Matat, Matat ote niale Lewi.
Lewi ote niale Simeon, Simeon ote niale Yuda, Yuda ote niale Yosef, Yosef ote niale Yonam, Yonam ote niale Eliakim.
Eliakim ote niale Melea, Malea ote niale Mena, Mena ote niale Matata, Matata ote niale Natan, Natan ote niale Dawid.
Dawid ote niale Yisai, Yisai ote niale Obed, Obed ote niale Boas, Boas ote niale Salomo, Salomo ote niale Nahason.
Nahason ote niale Aminadab, Aminadab ote niale Adimin, Adimin ote niale Arni, Arni ote niale Hesron, Hesron ote niale Peres, Peres ote niale Yuda.
Yuda ote niale Yakob, Yakob ote niale Isak, Isak ote niale Abraham, Abraham ote niale Tera, Tera ote niale Nahor, Nahor ote niale Serug, Serug ote niale Regu, Regu ote niale Peleg, Peleg ote niale Eber, Eber ote niale Sala.
Sala ote niale Kainan, Kainan ote niale Arfaksad, Arfaksad ote niale Sem, Sem ote niale Noa, Noa ote niale Lamek.
Lamek ote niale Metusala, Metusala ote niale Henok, Henok ote niale Yared, Yared ote niale Mahalaleel, Mahalaleel ote niale Kainan.
Kainan ote niale Enos, Enos ote niale Set, Set ote niale Adam, Adam ote kafɔɔ niale Yaa nɛ.
Abonsam Lasɔ Yesu Aanyu.
Obe wɔ di Yesu ladie ni di Yordan okle nwu kamɛ, aayii pɔ ku Ninwuna Klekle.
Ni di Ninwuna nwu lakpaa nwɔ aasifiko ɔfaafuu kamɛ, lɛɛba le di Abonsam lasɔ nwɔ aanyu ni ayi afosi ana amu.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, Yesu ditale lɛsalɛsaa, nioso kɔka lakle nwɔ osie kanya di ayi nwu kayɛntɛkɔ.
Ninfɛ di Abonsam latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse Yaa obi fale, ni tɔkɔ difuɔ le mmle falɛ dikple alesaa.” Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Diele alesaa lete suoto di otii nsiɛ nkpa.’ ” Nni kamaa, Abonsam lakpaa nwɔ aalaase di lɛba le niataka ni suoto.
Ni aatuo nwɔ kayi asaa ku sɛka nlekɔ mmuu di onumpoo lɛpɛ kamɛ nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kamayɔ kayi kamuu otumi wɔ mmle ku kamɛ lɛsaawɛ nta fɔ, diekye ami bɛɛyɔ bɛɛta, otii lele kafɔɔ ninlɛ mi kafuo nwɔ ɔyɔ ɔta.
Nioso asaa ya amuu makple fɔ ale nse fabase katũ kasɔ fantɛɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Saate Yaa lɛfɔ lete faase katũ kaasɔ fanta.
Lete nɔɔ kafɔɔ faatansa.’ ” Nni kamaa, Abonsam lakpaa Yesu aasifiko Yerusalem aalaatika nwɔ di Yuda batii Yaa Olekatakɔ lɛkya kapiɔ̃piɔ̃kɔ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse Yaa obi fale, faayefe fakye ninfũ fasifi kasɔ.
Diekye Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa mata batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ nyila mannyu fɔ.’ ‘Babaklee fɔ di nnɛɛ lɛma kamɛ di osi alɛ, bia falaatuula diifuɔ kuninwii suoto.’ ” Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Tansɔ Saate Yaa lɛfɔ faanyu.’ ” Obe wɔ di Abonsam lasɔ Yesu di sisuku se mmle suoto aaloo nii, aayidiɛ nwɔ kɛɛkɛ aasifi.
Yesu Lakye Ɔkpɛ Nɔɔ Kasɔ Di Galilea.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aasifi Galilea nɛ.
Yaa Ninwuna Klekle otumi lasiɛ nwɔ kaamɛ.
Ni di suoto nɔɔ ɔlaa lakyaka ntɛɛ nwu nɛ.
Aatuo asaa di Yuda batii nsiisakɔ, obiala latansa asaa nɔɔ otuo.
Baasĩ Yesu Di Nasaret.
Nni kamaa, Yesu lakyɛ Nasaret ninle ni okpoo wɔ baaklee nwɔ aamuɔ nii.
Ni di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto, aakyɛ Yuda batii kasiisakɔ fɛ mmle ambɔmbɔ ni ɔbla.
Ni aataka aayila alɛ ɔɔka asaa di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ nɛ.
Ninfɛ baayɔ Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yesaia kukũ baatɔɔ nɛ.
Ni aatikiti kukũ nwu aanya lɛba le bɛɛkpana ni alɛ, “Saate Ninwuna ntika mi di suoto, diekye eediki mi alɛ, kayɔ ɔlaa biene nwu nwako bapiitɛ.
Eekyesee mi kafɔɔ alɛ kayie lɛkya nta batii ba beemufũ bɛɛpɛ ni akpo alɛ baawɛ difukiti.
Ku mba di anu lebiɛ nii, alɛ baanya.
Ku batii ba beenyinka bɛɛtɛ ni kaasɔ ku dibuo alɛ, baawɛ ɔnyɛɛ ɔtɛ.
Alɛ kata mantofo kafɔɔ alɛ obe ntoowo di Saate madiki ni batii nɔɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latĩi kukũ nwu nkpo, aakplesa aata tɔkyɛntɛ nwu, ni aasiɛ kaasɔ nɛ.
Batii ba bamuu niawɛ ni di kasiisakɔ nwu lakyako nwɔ onyu tuwĩi.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lɛba le mmle biene lɛka ni ninfũ, nintɔɔwa kaanya miɛ dii le mmle nɛ.” Sɛlaa nɔɔ se aabuɛ ni lamufũ di batii nwu situ osie kanya, ku mmle aablako ni ɔkplalomii nɔɔ ɔkpɛ, diabla batii nwu ɔkpɛ.
Ni baakaalɛ alɛ, “Diele nnwɔɔ ninle Yosef obi nwu nkpo nɛ?” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “N-ye nlɛ bibapɛ mi lɛkpa le mmle bilɛ, ‘Fablatɛ, bla suoto kɔfa.’ Bibakple mintɔkɔ mi kafɔɔ bilɛ, ‘Asaa ya okle bianu bilɛ labla ni di Kapernaum, mbla nya kafɔɔ di okpoo nii.’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, mánfũ Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ di nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ okpoo.
Binu!
Nwaako diale alɛ bakpisɔfɔ kpinwu lawɛ di Israel kasɔ suoto di obe wɔ di Elia lawɛ nii.
Di kanto ladiɛ ni ɔnɔɔ alɛɛ atiɛ ku ɔfã, di kɔka kplɛ lawa ni kaasɔ nwu kamuu suoto.
Kafɔɔ, Yaa ditakyesee Elia alɛ akyɛ kuonwii lɛma nfũ.
Kafɔɔ aakyesee nwɔ aakyɛ bakpisɔfɔ nfũ di Sarep okpoo kamɛ di Sidon kasɔ suoto.
Nkpo nwu kafɔɔ baatii kpinwu latoofiɛ ofiɛ sɛɛle di Israel kasɔ di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Elia obe kamɛ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ kuonwii ditawɛ difiɛyɔɔ kaamɛ lɛma, dilenkee Naeman wɔ niakye ni Siria kasɔ lete niawɛ difiɛyɔɔ.” Obe wɔ baatii ba niawɛ ni di kasiisakɔ nwu lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, ɔblɔ lafiɛ ma osie kanya di Yesu suoto.
Ni baataka, baananfi Yesu baadieko di okpoo nwu baasifiko kobokote ko suoto baabudi ni okpoo nwu kobembe, alɛ bootukusɔɔ mankpee di kɔwɛ kamɛ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu lafe ma nintɛɛ aasifi.
Yesu Latososa Ninwuna Kpile Aadiki Di Osuɔtɔ Onwii Kamɛ.
Nni nkpo kamaa, Yesu lasifi Kapernaum okpoo kamɛ di Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Ni di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto aalaakya ko batii asaa otuo nɛ.
Asaa nɔɔ otuo labla ma ɔkpɛ, diekye aatuo nya ku otumi.
Otii onwii lawɛ di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ nwu niinwuna kpile lasiɛ nii.
Ni aafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Oo!
Be foomiɛ di ɔkyɛ loo, afɔ Yesu Nasaret Otii?
Ɔwɔɔsa fɛɛwa wo?
N-ye otii wɔ fale nii!
Afɔ ninle Otii Klekle wɔ di Yaa lekyesee ni nɛ!” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakpee ninwuna nwu kufiofa alɛ, “Lo kanana!
Faadie nwɔ kaamɛ!” Ninfɛ di ninwuna kpile nwu lanwanyisa nwɔ aatɛ kaasɔ di batii nwu anu nɛ.
Ni aadie nwɔ kaamɛ aasifi nɛ, kafɔɔ lɛsalɛsaa ditabla osuɔtɔ nwu.
Diabla batii nwu bamuu yaaa, ni baakaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Ɔmɛnlaa ninle nwɔ?
Otii wɔ mmle lɛyɔ otumi ku osie kplɛ antososa anwuna kpile andiki di batii suoto.” Nioso Yesu leyooto lakyaka ntɛɛ nwu sekpoo simuu kamɛ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Batii Kpinwu Sifiɛ.
Yesu ladie di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ, ni aasifi Simon leyo nɛ.
Simon ɔmaato late aatoofiɛ kɔbɔ ofiɛ osie kanya.
Ninfɛ baata Yesu latofo nɛ.
Ninfɛ aakyɛ aalaayila diɛ atensaa nɔɔ ɔlɔɔkɔ ni aasĩ ɔlaa aata ofiɛ nwu nɛ.
Nfanwu, ofiɛ nwu layɔɔ nwɔ, ni aataka aanyu ma kanya nɛ.
Obe wɔ kuufĩ ntɔɔmɛɛ nii, batii ba bamuu baafiɛtɛ ate ate nkpe ni lakpaa ma baawako Yesu nfũ.
Ni aatika ma nnɛɛ di suoto aayɔɔsa bamuu lɛma sifiɛ nɛ.
Anwuna kpile kpinwu kafɔɔ ladie baatii kamɛ baatooyiisa kudu alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Yaa obi nwu nɛ!” Kafɔɔ Yesu ditata anwuna kpile nwu osuku alɛ abuɛ ɔlaa kuonwii, diekye baatofo alɛ nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ nɛ.
Yesu Labuɛ Yaa Ɔlaa Di Yuda Batii Kasiisakɔ.
Kaale lasɛ nii, Yesu ladie di okpoo nwu aasifi lɛba le nialo nii, batii nwu lakyako nwɔ owolaa.
Obe wɔ baanyɔɔ nii, baamiɛ alɛ se atansifi aadiɛ ma fiɛ.
Kafɔɔ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Dikpe nii lɛkyɛ lɛlaabuɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɔlaa biene nwu di sekpoo bamba kamɛ, diekye nni oso di Yaa lekyesee mi nɛ.” Nkpo oso aabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa di Yuda batii nsiisakɔ nwu mmuu di kasɔ nwu suoto.
Yesu Lalɛɛ Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Kasale.
Dii ninwii, Yesu layila di lekpo le bɔɔlɛɛ ni alɛ Genesaret kotoko.
Ni baatii dikudi nwu latoosisikiti alɛ bɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ nwɔ mmle baanu ni Yaa ɔlaa wɔ ababuɛ nii.
Yesu lanya ekolo ɛnyɔ n-yɛ di lekpo nwu kotoko ninfa, kɔkpaku badikitɛ ladiɛ sĩ bɛɛkyɛ boofoto asawu lɛma.
Ninfɛ di Yesu layie aabuo di oklo onwii kamɛ, nwɔ ninle ni Simon ole.
Ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ atukusa oklo nwu kuɔkyɛ ntu kamɛ kɛkɛɛ.
Oklo nwu kamɛ di Yesu lasiɛ aatuo batii dikudi nwu asaa nɛ.
Obe wɔ aatuo ma asaa aaloo nii, Yesu latɔkɔ Simon alɛ, “Tukusa oklo nwu fakyɛnko sitũ nintu nwu kamɛ lɛɛba le niekyofo ni, di afɔ ku basiɛwo lɛfɔ biɛtaa asawu bidiki kɔkpaku.” Ni di Simon labuɛ alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, kakyɛ ka kpe buɔbla ɔkpɛ ku ninunsɛɛ, kafɔɔ butadiki lɛsalɛsaa.
Kafɔɔ bubataa asawu nwu fɛ mmle feebuɛ nii.” Baataa asawu nwu, ni baadiki kɔkpaku kpinwu diata alɛ asawu lɛma lakyako ɔbɛbɛɛ.
Nioso, baawii nnɛɛ baalɛɛ basiɛwo lɛma diɛ oklo nyɔɔfa kamɛ alɛ bawa babakyakaako ma.
Baawa babadiki kɔkpaku baayiisa eklo ɛnyɔ be mmle kamɛ pɔ alɛ kɛkɛɛ niabu di eklo nwu kamɛɛ ni nintu kamɛ.
Obe wɔ di Simon Petro lanya lɛsaa le niawa nii, ni aapɛ akunkyi di Yesu katũ, aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, tantɛɛtɛɛ mi, diekye kpileblatɛ nnle!” Kɔkpaku ko kpinwu baadiki ni ninfa oso, dibla nnwɔɔ ku basiɛwo nɔɔ ɔkpɛ osie kanya.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ diabla Simon basiɛwo ba ninle Sebedeo babi, Yakobo ku Yohane ɔkpɛ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ Simon alɛ, “Tanyɛkɛ.
Diɛyɔ ni di nua diesifi nii, batii dikitɛ nfɛ fabale.” Nni kamaa, baananfi seklo nwu baase di lekpo kotoko, ni baadiɛ lɛsaa biala baatɛ, baasifi baalaatikanko Yesu nɛ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Niatoofiɛ Ni Ofiɛ Sɛɛle Ofiɛ.
Obe onwii, Yesu lakyɛ okpoo onwii kamɛ, nfũ di osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ aatoofiɛ ni ofiɛ sɛɛle.
Obe wɔ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lanya ni Yesu, ni aapɛ akunkyi di Yesu katũ aatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, “Saate!
Nse dilɛ fɔ, faafuo ɔta suoto nii mbla klekle.” Yesu ladiki kɔnɛɛ aakpanko nwɔ, aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Letuna, suoto lɛfɔ siklekle!” Nfanwu, ni di ɔfiɛ nwu layɔɔ nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakpee nwɔ kufiofa alɛ, “Tantɔkɔ otii kuonwii.
Kafɔɔ tɔɔkyɛ falaayɔ suoto lɛfɔ fatuo Yaa oletatɛ, faata ole di mmle di Mose lekpee kufiofa ɛɛtɛ ni di suoto okleklesa suoto, diatuo alɛ ɔfiɛ nwu ntɔɔyɔɔ fɔ ni.” Kafɔɔ Yesu leyooto lakyaka kayi osie kanya.
Diata alɛ batii kpinwu latɔɔwa alɛ bɔbatoonu nwɔ asaa otuo anyɔɔsa ma sifiɛ.
Kafɔɔ obe obe, andie ankyɛ lɛba le nielo ni anaatɔɔpɛ ɔlaa antɔɔta Yaa.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Niafefe Aate Ni Ofiɛ.
Dii ninwii obe wɔ di Yesu latotuo ni asaa, Yuda batii dikudi le bɔɔlɛɛ ni Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ bawo lakye Galilea ku Yudea ku Yerusalem kasɔ aba aba baawa nfa.
Ni di Yaa Ninwuna lasiɛ di Yesu kamɛ alɛ ɔɔyɔɔsa batii sifiɛ nɛ.
Nfanwu, batii banwii niakpaa osuɔtɔ onwii niafefee aate ni di ɔkla suoto baawako.
Baatoomiɛ osuku wɔ baayɔ nwɔ mambuoko ni leyo le di Yesu lawɛ nii, man-yɔ osuɔtɔ nwu mantɛ ni di anu nɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ batii lɛpɔ nwu oso, batafuo osuku ɔwɛ.
Nle mmle oso, baatuka nwɔ baalaayie lɛkya osi.
Ni baadufu kutuɛ di lɛkya nwu suoto baasoosa fiɛtɛ nwu ku ɔkla nɔɔ wɔ suoto aate nii, baatɛ di Yesu anu di batii nwu ntɛɛ nɛ.
Di Yesu lanya ni ofũ onu lɛma oso, ni aatɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu alɛ, “Siɛwo nii, ntɔɔyɔ sikpile lɛfɔ lɛkyɛ fɔ!” Ninfɛ di Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ lakyako bawo ɔkaalɛ alɛ, “Owe ninle nwɔ mmle nikobuɛ ni mbusuo ɔlaa wɔ mmle?
Yaa lete nikafuo sikpile ɔyɔ ɔkyɛ!” Obe wɔ di Yesu latofo ni disibu lɛma, ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be oso biobu sɛlaa se mmle okle disi?
Lɛmɛnle niɛyɔɔ dilenke di sɛlaa se mmle obuɛ kamɛ, ‘Bɛɛyɔ sikpile lɛfɔ bɛɛkyɛ fɔ’ ɛɛ sɛɛ baabuɛ alɛ, ‘Taka faakyɛ’?
Kamadiki ntuo ye nlɛ ami, Otii Obi nkpe, otumi kaasɔ ka mmle suoto n-yɔ okpile nkyɛ.” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ otii wɔ niekpi ni kakyɛkakyɛ alɛ, “Kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, taka faayɔ ɔkla lɛfɔ faatɔɔkyɛ leyo!” Nfanwu, osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo niataka aayila baati nwu anu, aayɔ atensaa nɔɔ ya suoto aate nii, aasifi leyo, aakyako Yaa ɔtansa.
Lɛsaa le mmle labla batii nwu bamuu ɔkpɛ!
Nioso lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ bamuu lɛma, ni baatansa Yaa, baabuɛ alɛ, “Be mɔ lɛsaa kplɛ buɔnya miɛ nkpo?” Yesu Lalɛɛ Lewi.
Nni kamaa, Yesu ladie leeyo nwu kamɛ, ni aanya akpooto funtɛ onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Lewi, aasiɛ di akpooto kafunkɔ.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tikankoe!” Nfanwu, Lewi ladiɛ lɛsaa biala aatɛ, ni aataka aatikanko nwɔ nɛ.
Lewi lata baawa alesaa biene leeyo nɔɔ, aatũ opunu kplɛ aata Yesu.
Baakyakako akpooto bafuntɛ kpinwu ku batii bamba kafɔɔ.
Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ ba niawɛ ni di alesaa nwu kalekɔ lakye kasɔ baatɔɔnanfiko Yesu basaateketetɛ ɔlaa alɛ, “Be oso biole minwee ku akpooto bafuntɛ ku bakpileblatɛ bamba ba mmle?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Fablatɛ diefĩ batii ba ninoofiɛ nii, bafiɛtɛ di fablatɛ lefĩ.
Ninwa babienetɛ ɔlɛɛ, bakpiletɛ oso lɛwa.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Di Kanya Onii Suoto.
Batii bawo lakaalɛ alɛ, “Lɛ diɛwa fiɛ di Yohane basaateketetɛ nnii kanya mampɛ ɔlaa manta Yaa wlawla, Farisi batii basaateketetɛ kafɔɔ mbla nkpo, kafɔɔ bale fɔ mma obe lele manle manyi?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Biefũ bienu bilɛ batii ba bɛɛkyakako bɛɛwako ni ɔsanko kayɔkɔ kaanii kanya di obe wɔ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo ɔsa nkpe ma ni di ɔkyɛ?
Oowo!
Diidii dilaafuo ɔwa nkpo!
Kafɔɔ, dii lewo kɔwa, babakpaa ɔsanko nwu ɔsa di ɔkyɛ lɛma mansifiko nii.
Nfa nfɛ babakyako kanya onii nɛ.” Nni kamaa, Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa le mmle alɛ, “Otii konwii nimbɛ dibula fɔle aakaa aatĩi lekofole kabɛkɔ.
Nse otii owo lɛbla nkpo, abalalaasa dibula fɔle nwu.
Ni kafɔɔ, lekofole nwu nkpo ku lɛfɔle nwu nkpo dilabakaatɛɛ bia.
Nkpo kafɔɔ kuonwii nin-yɔ nta fɔle aakpete di bɔkɛɛ kukũ kotofo kofole kamɛ nɛ.
Diekye nse diɛwa nkpo, nta fɔle nwu nkpo mafuu ninta alɛ, kɔbɔkɛɛkũ kotofo nwu nkpo mbɛ, nta nwu nkpo kafɔɔ nwii nyinlalaa.
Nioso dikaatɛ alɛ baayɔ nta fɔle mankpete di kɔbɔkɛɛkũ fɔle kamɛ.
Diɛkyakaa nii, otii kuonwii ninyi nta kofole, nfɛ oosiɛ nii aakple aakaalɛ nfɔle.
Nse diele nkpo ɔlaa wɔ ababuɛ ni ko ninle alɛ, ‘Nkofole nwu nlɛ dilɛnke nfɔle!’ ”
Yesu Ku Farisi Batii Lananfi Ɔlaa Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi Suoto.
Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi ninwii suoto, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoofe di atita kofe kunwii kamɛ.
Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu lakyako atita nwu ofee, baafini nya baakyako owee nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Farisi batii bawo lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be oso biɔbla lɛsaa le di kufiofa loo diɛta ni osuku alɛ babla ni di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Biika lɛsaa le di Dawid labla ni ku bawo nɔɔ di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ binya, di obe wɔ kɔɔka laklee ma ni?
Dawid lakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ kamɛ aalaayɔ alesaa ya baata ni Yaa ole, aale ni.
Aayɔ awo kafɔɔ aata bawo nɔɔ lale ni.
Nu kuufiofa loo diɛta osuku alɛ otii bamba kale ni alesaa nwu nkpo.
Diediki Yaa oletatɛ lete pɛ nikale ni.” Ninfɛ di Yesu labuɛ aanyɛntɛ alɛ, “Ami, Otii Obi, ninle Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi Saate.” Yesu Layɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Kɔnɛɛ Nɔɔ Kunwii Lakatu Nii Ofiɛ.
Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi bamba suoto Yesu lakyɛ Yuda batii kasiisakɔ, aalaatuo asaa.
Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ ninfa di koletanɛɛ nɔɔ lakatu nii.
Kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii bawo lawɛ ninfa baatoomiɛ osuku wɔ baafe man-yɔ ni ɔlaa di Yesu suoto oso, baadiki anu baase nwɔ baatoonyu, nse, abayɔɔsa ofiɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi nwu suoto.
Di Yesu latofo ma ni disibu nwu oso, ni aatɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu kɔɔnɛɛ lɛkatu ni alɛ, “Taka, fawa sitũ ninfũ.” Ni di osuɔtɔ nwu lataka aakyɛ aalaayila ma diɛ anu nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be di kufiofa loo lɛta osuku alɛ buabla di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto?
Dilɛ alɛ buabla dibiene di lɛnyɛɛtɔyi suoto ɛɛ, buabla dikpile?
Ee dilɛ alɛ buafũ batii nkpa ɛɛ, sɛɛ buawɔɔsa mi?” Yesu lanyu batii nwu bamuu aafenko, ni aatɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu alɛ, “Yilasa kɔnɛɛ lɛfɔ.” Ni aayilasa kũ nɛ, nfanwu kɔnɛɛ nɔɔ nwu lakple kualɛ.
Ɔblɔ lafiɛ batii nwu bamuu ni baakyako disi obu di lɛsaa le babafuo ni Yesu ɔbla.
Yesu Ladiki Batɔkyɛntɛ Lefosi Banyɔ.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, Yesu lasifi kabokotee kanwii osi, alɛ ɔɔlaa pɛ ɔlaa anta Yaa.
Aawɛ ninfa kakyɛ kamuu, aatɔɔpɛ ɔlaa aatɔɔta Yaa.
Obe wɔ kaale lasɛ nii, aalɛɛ basaatekete nɔɔ bamuu aasiisa, ni aadiki lefosi batii banyɔ kaamɛ lɛma, aata ma leyooto alɛ, batɔkyɛntɛ.
Mma ninle, Simon wɔ aata ni leyooto alɛ, Petro ku obilɛma suɔtɔbi Andrea ku Yakobo ku Yohane ku Filipo ku Bartolomeo, ku Mateo ku Toma ku Yakobo wɔ ninle ni Alfeo obi ku Simon wɔ manlɛɛ ni alɛ otii wɔ nimbɔmbɔ ni okpoo nɔɔ.
Ku Yakobo obi Yuda ku Yuda Iskariot wɔ niabakple ni otii dikitatɛ.
Yesu Latuo Asaa, Aayɔɔsa Batii Sifiɛ.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ku batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ lasosoo baakye ni kabokotee nwu osi, baabayila lɛɛba le ninte ni yaaa.
Ni di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kpinwu bawo lawɛ ninfa ku batii dikudi kplɛ ninwii le niakye ni Tiro ku Sidon.
Baawa alɛ, bɔɔbanu asaa ya di Yesu kotuo nii, anyɔɔsa ma sifiɛ ate ate se boofiɛ nii.
Batii ba di anwuna kpile latɔɔhaa ni kafɔɔ lawa aayɔɔsa bamuu lɛma sifiɛ.
Batii ba mmle bamuu lakpee ɔnyɛɛ baakpanko nwɔ, mmle siifiɛ lɛma kayɔɔ ma nii.
Diekye osie owo latoodie di Yesu suoto kamɛ diatɔɔyɔɔsa batii bamuu sifiɛ.
Suoto Mayɔɔ Batii Bawo, Bawo Kafɔɔ Mawɛ Dibuo.
Yesu latakatɛsa anu aanyu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ, ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Suoto siyɔɔ aye bapiitɛ, dikye Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ninle ye kale!
Suoto siyɔɔ aye ba kɔɔka nkle ni nunua diekye aye nimamiɛ nɛ!
Suoto siyɔɔ aye ba nikowi ni nunua, diekye aye nimama nɛ!
Suoto siyɔɔ ye nse batii lekyidi ye, beesĩ ye, beetufa ye, beebuɛ kafɔɔ alɛ batii kpile bile ta ami, Otii Obi, oso!
“Binya suoto lɛyɔɔ nse n-ya mmle amuu kɔwa, bietũ ku suoto lɛyɔɔ, diekye Yaa mata ye letota kplɛ di Yaa kafa.
Diekye asaa ya mmle okle di bawa lɛma layɔ baabla Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nɛ.
Aye ba ninle ni basaawɛntɛ biyɔɔsa, diekye bitɔɔwɛ suoto lɛyɔɔ lee ninfũ!
Aye ba nintoole biemiɛ ni nunua biyɔɔsa, diekye kɔka kɔwa ye ɔbaklee!
Aye ba nikɔma ni miɛ, biyɔɔsa diekye biɔwa sɛnyaami obuo ku kaku owi!
Biyɔɔsa, aye ba baatii kɔtansa ni miɛ, diekye nkpo okle kafɔɔ di bawa lɛma latansa balaatɛ Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nɛ.
Bɔmbɔ Balo Lɛfɔ.
“Kafɔɔ aye ba nikonu mi ni ɔlaa, kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bibɔmbɔ balo lee, biɛbla dibiene bita ma.
Batii ba ninkpaani ye nii, bikaalɛ dikusɛkusɛ bita ma.
Batii ba kafɔɔ nikɔbla ye ni amumu, bipɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa diisi lɛma.
Nse otii owo kafɔɔ lɛpɛ fɔ kɔnɛɛ kootokosi, faamunikĩisa kɔnyɔɔfa kafɔɔ fatɔɔ apɛ.
Nse otii owo lefũ fɔ osi awu kplɛ, faadiɛko nwɔ kalɔ ale kafɔɔ.
Otii lele niɛkaalɛ fɔ lɛsaa, faatɔɔ.
Nse otii owo lɛyɔ fɔ lɛsaa, tambuɛ falɛ dikpe ni eekplesa ni ɛɛwako.
Lɛsaa le biomiɛ bilɛ batii babla bata ye nii, nni okle biɛɛbla bita ma nɛ.
“Nse mimbɔmbɔ batii ba nimbɔmbɔ ye ni lete, ni lɛmɛnkusɛkusɛ bibawɛ?
Bia bakpileblatɛ mbɔmbɔ batii ba nimbɔmbɔ ma nii.
Ni nse batii ba nimbla ye ni dibiene lete mimbla dibiene minta, sɛmɛnfa babapɛ ye?
Bia bakpileblatɛ mbla nkpo.
Ni nse minfɛnsa asaa minta batii ba lete biye bilɛ babakplesa manwako ye nii, lɛmɛnkusɛkusɛ bibawɛ?
Bia bakpileblatɛ nfɛnsa asaa manta bawo alɛ baakplesa manwako ma!
Kafɔɔ, bibɔmbɔ balo lee, biɛbla dibiene bita ma.
Bifɛnsa ma asaa, kafɔɔ bitantika anu bilɛ babakplesa manwako ye kokooko.
Nse biɛbla nkpo, bibawɛ letota kplɛ.
Ni babalɛɛ ye alɛ Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni babi.
Diekye Yaa nkpe sifutulɛ ɛɛta batii ba di asaa nimbuo ni anu ku basiensietɛ.
Binya nyaami fɛ mmle okle di Teeye nnya ni nyaami.
Yesu Latuo Asaa Aakyeko Bawo Ɔkanko Suoto.
“Bitankanko bawo lee, ni Yaa kafɔɔ dilɔbakanko ye.
Bitanlo bawo lee lɛpɔɔ, ni Yaa kafɔɔ dilɔbalo ye lɛpɔɔ.
Biyɔ bikyɛ bawo lee, ni Yaa kafɔɔ mayɔ ankyɛ ye.
Bita batii asaa, ni Yaa kafɔɔ mata ye asaa.
Nwaako, Yaa mata siwu lee nyii pɔ di sifutulɛ nɔɔ kanya.
Diekye leklapoosaa le biɛyɔ biɛklapoosa biɛta ni bawo lee, nninwu okle di Yaa mayɔ anklapoosa anta ye nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa alɛ, “Numbiɛtɛ dilɔbafuo numbiɛtɛ wo nɔɔ katũ oleko, se diele nkpo, ni banyɔ lɛma babakpa mambuo diibiɔ kamɛ.
Saateketetɛ kuonwii ninlenkee saatuotɛ nɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ nse saateketetɛ ntooloo asaa nɔɔ otekete, ote ante fɛ mmle di saatuotɛ nɔɔ nte nii.
“Lɛ diɛbla fɔɔnya diku biibii le ninsi ni di owo lɛfɔ ninu, kafɔɔ fɔlɔɔnya kawosoku ka ninsi fɔ ni leele kamɛ?
Lɛ dibawa alɛ faatɔkɔ owo lɛfɔ falɛ, ‘Lekoto, owo nii, tɛɛ ndiki fɔ diku niinu.’ Kafɔɔ fɔlɔɔnya kawosoku ka ninsi fɔ ni niinu kamɛ?
Afɔ laatɛ!
Lekatũ fadiki kawosoku ka ninsi ni niinu lɛfɔ kamɛ fiɛ, ni fabafuo ɔnya nwaa, fandiki diku biibii le ninsi ni di obilee ninu kamɛ.
Kowoso Biala Ku Abi Ni Kũ.
“Kowoso biene níntika abi lalaale, kowoso lalaale kafɔɔ níntika abi biene.
Kowoso biala, abi ya ootika ni man-yɔ mantofo kũ.
Mántɛsɛ akpaloo abi di kukutuwoso suoto, nkpo kafɔ manantɛsɛ akutu di akpaloo dikũmii suoto nɛ.
Otii biene yi, asaa biene ya eekookaa ni di otu nɔɔ kamɛ andiki asaa biene kayi ankyeko.
Kafɔɔ otii kpile nnwɔɔ, asaa kpile ya eekookaa ni di otu nɔɔ kamɛ andiki asaa kpile ankyeko.
Diekye asaa ya nintooyii ni otii otu kamɛ, nnya ambuɛ nɛ.
Kyɔɔ Yesu Ɔlaa Atoko Faabla Ninnwu Suoto.
“Be lɛsaa oso biɔlɛɛ mi Saate, kafɔɔ mimbla di lɛsaa le kɔtɔkɔ ye ni suoto?
Otii lele niɛwa ɔkyɛ nii, annu mi ɔlaa, ambla nwu di suoto, matuo ye otii wɔ ale nii.
Ate fɛ otii wɔ nikotofo ni leyo, eekutu ni kasɔ diekyofo nii, ese ni lɛsɔse nɔɔ di afuɔ suoto.
Nse okle leyii, kuobiɛ kuɔbasa di seyoyiɛ nwu suoto, leyo nwu nimbla lɛsalɛsaa, diekye diɛwɛ lɛba biene diyɛ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ ninnu mi ni ɔlaa anaamufũ nwu aaklee nii, ate fɛ otii wɔ nietofo ni leyo di kɔtɛ suoto lɛɛsɔse nɔɔ nnaa ni osie.
Nioso nse okle leyii kuobiɛ kuɔbasa leyo nwu, nimbiɛ osie kanya wududu ninkaa kaasɔ!”
Yesu Layɔɔsa Roma Batii Bakpɛtɛ Nɔɔfo Kpɛmblatɛ Nɔɔ Onwii Ofiɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu latɔkɔ batii sɛlaa se mmle simuu aaloo nii, ni aasifi Kapernaum nɛ.
Roma batii bakpɛtɛ nɔɔfo onwii lawɛ ninfa, aawɛ kpɛmblatɛ onwii ambɔmbɔ ni osie kanya.
Kpɛmblatɛ wɔ mmle latoofiɛ osie kanya diabu kɛɛkɛɛ aakpi nii.
Nioso obe wɔ aanu ni Yesu lɛkpanko, aakpee Yuda batii banɔɔfo bawo alɛ bakyɛ baalaatɔkɔ nwɔ aawa abayɔɔsa kpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ nwu ofiɛ atɔɔ.
Obe wɔ baatii ba mmle lawa ni Yesu nfũ, baatikiti nwɔ lekoto osie kanya alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lesiɛko alɛ faatɔɔ lɛkyakaako, diekye ambɔmbɔ kale loo.
Nnwɔɔ nietofo Yuda batii kasiisakɔ ɛɛta wo nɛ.” Nioso Yesu lataka aatikanko ma.
Obe wɔ di Yesu nfɛ kɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni bakpɛtɛ nɔɔfo nwu leyo, ni aakpee basiɛwo nɔɔ alɛ bakyɛ baalaatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, tankpee suoto dibuo.
Diekye ami, ninsiɛko alɛ, faawa mi leyo.
Nkpo kafɔɔ ninasiɛko alɛ kawa fɔ anu nɛ.
Nkpo oso afɔ buɛ ɔlaa onwii pɛ, kpɛmblatɛ nii mawɛ osie.
Diekye ami kafɔɔ nsi di ɔnɔɔfo wɔ ninlenke mi ni kalɔ.
Ni baakpɛtɛ nsi mi kaalɔ.
Nse lɛtɔkɔ onwii nlɛ, ‘Akyɛ nfũ,’ ni ankyɛ nɛ.
Nse lɛtɔkɔ ɔbamba nlɛ, ‘Awa ninfũ,’ ni anwa nɛ.
Nse lɛtɔkɔ kpɛmblatɛ nii nlɛ, ‘Bla nle,’ ni ambla nɛ.” Obe wɔ di Yesu lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ aabuɛ nii, diabla nwɔ ɔkpɛ.
Ninfɛ aamunikĩi aatɔkɔ batii dikudi le niatikanko nwɔ ni alɛ, “Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, diidii ninnya ofũ onu wɔ mmle okle di Israel batii kamɛ nnya!” Obe wɔ baatii ba baakpee ni kɔtɔ lakple baalaabuo ni leyo, baanya alɛ kpɛmblatɛ nwu sitoosie nwɔ.
Yesu Lasɛnkɛsa Kpisɔfɔ Onwii Obisuɔtɔbi.
Ninkpo kamaa, Yesu lakyɛ okpoo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Nain kamɛ.
Basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ku batii dikudi kpinwu latikanko nwɔ.
Obe wɔ aadu ni okpoo nwu kasũkunya, aakyakako batii kodie bakle kpi boofenko kakookaakɔ.
Otii wɔ niakpi nii, obisuɔtɔbi onwii nwu pɛ aale aata kpisɔfɔ nwu nɛ.
Batii dikudi kpinwu di okpoo nwu kamɛ lawɛ di kpisɔfɔ nwu ɔkyɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lanya ni ɔsanko wɔ mmle, aakpɛ nwɔ nyaamii.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Diɛ owi.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lafe kaamɛ lɛma aalaakpanko kpi alakaa nwu nɛ.
Ninfɛ baatii ba niatuka ni kpi nwu nkpo layila nɛ.
Ni di Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Okosopo!
Kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ taka!” Nfanwu kpi nwu nkpo niataka aasiɛ, aakyako ɔkakatɛ.
Ni di Yesu lakpaa nwɔ aata ɔya nɛ.
Lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ batii nwu bamuu osie kanya, ni baatansa Yaa nɛ.
Ta nkpo oso baabuɛ alɛ, “Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ kplɛ nintɔɔwa wo kamɛ!
Yaa ntoosoo ɛwa batii nɔɔ odiki!” Yesu suoto ɔlaa wɔ mmle lakpɛ kuakyaka Yuda kasɔ nwu suoto ku aba bule amuu.
Batɔkyɛntɛ Lakye Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Nfũ Baakyɛ Yesu Nfũ.
Obe wɔ di Yohane basaateketetɛ latɔkɔ ni Yohane sɛlaa se mmle, nfanwu aalɛɛ batii banyɔ kaamɛ lɛma.
Ni aakpee ma Saate nwu nfũ alɛ balaakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle otii wɔ alɛ abawa ni ɛɛ, sɛɛ buatoonyu osuku muntɔɔta otii bamba?” Nioso obe wɔ baawa ni Yesu nfũ, baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ntu kpeesatɛ Yohane lekpee wo alɛ buwa buɔbakaalɛ fɔ alɛ, ‘Afɔ ninle otii wɔ aabuɛ alɛ abawa ni ɛɛ, sɛɛ buanyu osuku munta otii bamba?’ ” Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yesu ntɔɔyɔɔsa batii kpinwu sifiɛ, ate ate, eetososa anwuna kpile baatii suoto, eetikiti kafɔɔ banumbiɛtɛ kpinwu anu.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ Yohane basaateketetɛ nwu alɛ, “Bikple biɛlaatɔkɔ Yohane asaa ya biɛnya ni ku n-ya bienu ni bilɛ, banumbiɛtɛ nfɛ kɔnya asaa, abafa nfɛ kɔtaka ankyɛ, batii ba nikofiɛ ni sifiɛ sɛɛle suoto ntɔɔkpa, batokotĩitɛ nfɛ konu, bakpi kɔtaka mansiɛ nkpa, bapiitɛ kafɔɔ nfɛ konu ɔlaa biene nwu nkpo.
Suoto mayɔɔ batii ba ninanya ni ɔlaa kpile kuonwii di suoto nii.” Obe wɔ di Yohane basaateketetɛ ntoosifi beeloo nii, Yesu lakye kasɔ aatɔɔkakatɛ aatɔɔta batii dikudi nwu nkpo di Yohane suoto alɛ, “Obe wɔ biadie biakyɛ ni Yohane nfũ di ɔfaafuu kamɛ, be biatoonyu osuku bilɛ bianya?
Lɛkpɛnyi le di kɔfɛɛfɔ latɔɔfɛ ni?
Be lɛsaa biadie biakyɛ bialaanya?
Otii wɔ niakpe ntu aasiɛ ni di asaa biene kamɛ?
Batii ba ninlolaa suoto mansiɛ ni di suoto lɛyɔɔ kamɛ yi, baka ayo mansiɛ.
Aye bitɔkɔ mi, be biakyɛ bialaanya?
Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ?
Nwaako katɔkɔ ye nii, otii wɔ biakyɛ bialaanya ni nlenke bia Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ.
Diekye Yohane ninle otii wɔ di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Makyesee tɔkyɛntɛ nii anlefɔ katũ, analolaa osuku antɛ fɔ.’ ” Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Yohane nlenke Otii biala beelofo ni kaayi ka mmle kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ ninle ni ɔyɛntɛle di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ, nlenke Yohane.” Batii nwu nkpo bamuu lanu Yohane ɔlaa biene wɔ aabuɛ nii, kyenkye akpooto bafuntɛ lafũ Yaa dibiesaa baanu, ninfɛ aakpeesa ma Yaa ntu nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ lasĩ Yaa dibiesaa, nioso Yohane ditakpeesa ma Yaa ntu.
Yesu lakple aabuɛ aakyakaa alɛ, “Nunua, be lɛsaa kayɔ miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle nkaatɛɛsa ko?
Nkpo bate fɛ babisɔ ba ninsi bookpee ni kɔkyɔ di asaa kasunsukɔ nɛ.
Bɔɔtɔkɔ dikudi bamba alɛ, ‘Buasa sɛkafɔɔnu buata ye, kafɔɔ biasĩ otũ.
Buakpee sikunu buata ye, kafɔɔ biasĩ kaku owi.’ Ntu kpeesatɛ Yohane lawa, aanii kanya, atanyi nta kafɔɔ diidii, biatɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ, ‘Ninwuna kpile ninsi nwɔ!’ Ni di ami, Otii Obi, kafɔɔ lɛwa, lele, lenyi.
Ni biobuɛ bilɛ, ‘Banyu lenyatɛ ku tanyintɛ nwu lo!
Ale akpooto bafuntɛ ku bakpileblatɛ siɛwo!’ Kafɔɔ batii ba bamuu nintikanko ni Yaa ninumbe nkpaamaa, batoodiki beetuo alɛ ninumbe nwaa dile.” Yesu Lakyɛ Simon Wɔ Niale Ni Farisi Otii Leyo.
Farisi otii onwii lalɛɛ Yesu alɛ awa abale ko nwɔ alesaa.
Nioso Yesu lakyɛ leyo nɔɔ aalaasiɛ alɛ ooleko nwɔ alesaa.
Ɔsanko onwii lawɛ di okpoo nwu kamɛ, aale sɔnɔkpeetɛ.
Nioso obe wɔ aanu alɛ Yesu lɛwa akpe ni di Farisi otii nwu leyo oole ni alesaa, aayɔ lebo kylɔkylɔ ninwii di nnɔnyi kɔnɔkɔnɔ layii ni aawako.
Aabayila di Yesu ɔlɔɔkɔ, aatoowi kaku aatookpete di Yesu nkpaatũ.
Ni di ɔsanko nwu nkpo layɔ disi nɔɔ sinwini aatoosunsũ nnumɛɛ be niakpete ni di Yesu nkpaa nɛ.
Aafĩfĩɔ nwɔ nkpaatũ, ni aanyɛɛnɛ nnɔnyi kɔnɔkɔnɔ nwu kafɔɔ aakpete nwɔ ninkpaatũ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di Farisi otii wɔ niakyakako ni Yesu lanya ni nle mmle, aabuɛ di disi nɔɔ kamɛ alɛ, “Nse otii wɔ mmle Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ ale nwaako, se dikpeni antofo ɔsanko wɔ mmle otiikle wɔ ale ni fiɛ ɛɛwa ɔɔkpanko nwɔ nii!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Simon, nkpe ɔlaa komiɛ nlɛ ntɔkɔfɔ nii.” Ninfɛ di Simon labuɛ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, tɔkɔ mi ɔlaa wɔ kule ni.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakye kasɔ aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Otii onwii lawɛ aatɔɔfɛnsa ato, aatɔɔta batii, ni baatii banyɔ banwii lasiɛko nwɔ koto nɛ.
Onwii lasiɛko koto ko nikawo ni fɛ otii kɔwɛntɛto.
Ɔnyɔɔfa kafɔɔ lasiɛko fɛ awɛntɛ lefosi kɔkpɛnto.
Batii ba mmle banyɔ kuonwii dilɔbafuo koto nwu nkpo ɔta.
Nkpo oso, ato fɛnsatɛ nwu layɔ ato ya baasiɛko nwɔ ni aakyɛ ma.
Baatii ba mmle kamɛ, ɔmɛnle lɛma feenyu falɛ ababɔmbɔ ato fɛnsatɛ nwu anlenkee?” Ninfɛ di Simon labuɛ alɛ, “Lefũ lenu nlɛ otii wɔ koto nimpɔ kulenke nii.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Feelolaa feebuɛ, nkpo kute nɛ.” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu lamunikĩi aanyu ɔsanko nwu, ni aatɔkɔ Simon alɛ, “Fɔɔnya ɔsanko wɔ mmle?
Obe wɔ lɛwa ni leyo lɛfɔ, faatɛɛ ntu nfoto nkpaa, kafɔɔ ɔsanko wɔ mmle lɛyɔ nnumɛɛ nɔɔ eefoto mi nkpaa ɛɛyɔ disi sinwini nɔɔ eesunsũ mi.
Faafũ mi fabla mi atuu ku suoto lɛyɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ diɛyɔ ni di obe wɔ lɛbabuo ni nfũ, ayidiɛ mi nkpaatũ ofĩfĩɔ.
Faatɛɛ nnɔnyi falɛ nkpee diisi.
Kafɔɔ ɔsanko wɔ mmle lɛyɔ nnɔnyi kɔnɔkɔnɔ eekpeete mi ninkpaatũ.
Nkpo oso kɔtɔkɔfɔ nlɛ, di lɛbɔmbɔ kplɛ le eediki eetuo mi ni oso, diotuo alɛ batɔɔyɔ sikpile nɔɔ se kpinwu ɛɛbla ni bɛɛkyɛ nwɔ.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ bɛɛyɔ sikpile kɛɛkɛɛ bɛɛkyɛ nii, lɛbɔmbɔ nɔɔ kafɔɔ kɛɛkɛɛ ninle.” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ɔsanko nwu alɛ, “Batɔɔyɔ sikpile lɛfɔ bɛɛkyɛ fɔ.” Obe wɔ baatii ba niasiɛ ni di alesaa kalekɔ nwu ninfa lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu labuɛ nii, baakaalɛ suoto alɛ, “Owe ninle nwɔ ninfũ oofuo bia batii sikpile ɔyɔ ɔkyɛ ma ni?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ɔsanko nwu alɛ, “Ofũ onu lɛfɔ ntoodiki fɔ, nioso tɔɔkyɛ ku atoko ɔkyɛ ole.”
Basanko Bawo Latikanko Yesu.
Obe owo kamaa, Yesu lakyɛ aatookyi sekpoo ku nkpayotũ kamɛ, aatoobuɛ ɔlaa biene nwu di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ suoto.
Lefosi batii banyɔ ba kafɔɔ aadiki ni latikanko nwɔ.
Basanko ba di Yesu layɔɔsa ni sifiɛ ate ate ku mba aatososa ni anwuna kpile aadiki ni kaamɛ lɛma kafɔɔ latikanko nwɔ.
Di kamɛ lɛma onwii lasiɛ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Maria Magdalene, nwɔ kamɛ di Yesu latososa ni anwuna kpile akuɛnsĩ.
Ɔsanko bamba kafɔɔ kaamɛ lɛma niale nwɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Yohana, ɔsa baatɔɔlɛɛ Kusa, aale ni Herode kakankɔ asaa nyuntɛ nɔɔfo nɛ.
Basanko bamba kpinwu ku nwɔ kafɔɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Susana latikanko Yesu, baatɔɔyɔ mma bamu asaa ya baatɔɔwɛ nii baatɔɔkyakaako Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ.
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Aakyeko Alesaa Kubi Santɛ Onwii Suoto.
Batii kpinwu lakye sekpoo ate ate baatɔɔwa Yesu nfũ.
Ni di obe wɔ baatii kpinwu ntɔɔbasi nii, Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa le mmle alɛ, “Alesaa kubi santɛ onwii lakyɛ aalaasa alesaa kubi.
Obe wɔ ɔɔsa ni kubi nwu koofe kamɛ, kowo lakpete di osuku suoto batii lananafu kũ, bakansiɛ kafɔɔ labasɛsɛɛ kũ baale.
Kowo kafɔɔ lakpete di afuɔ kasɔ.
Di obe wɔ kuakɔntɔ nii, kutawɛ ntu ku kasɔ nwaa kuayila.
Nkpo oso kuayɔɔ kuakpi.
Alesaa kubi nwu kowo lakpete di siwuu sɛfa kamɛ.
Ni siiwuu sɛfa nwu lamuɔ siafukiti siatĩi alesaa kubi nwu kumuu nɛ.
Alesaa kubi nwu kowo kafɔɔ lakpete di kasɔ biene suoto.
Kuakɔntɔ kuamuɔ kuatika abi alafa alafa.” Di Yesu latoobuɛ ni sɛlaa se mmle, aanyɛntɛ alɛ, “Otii wɔ kuunutoko nkpe nii yi, aanu!” Lɛsaa Le Oso Di Yesu Lapɛ Ni Lɛkpa Nwu.
Yesu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ lɛkpa nwu nkpo kasɔ.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye beediki lɛsaatofo le niewofa ni di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ beetuo.
Kafɔɔ batii bule akpa kamɛ bɛyɔ bɛɛta ma alɛ, ‘Babanya asaa, kafɔɔ blɔbanya batɛ nsũ.
Babanu kafɔɔ, blɔbanu kasɔ.’ Yesu Ladiki Lɛkpa Nwu Kasɔ.
“Lɛkpa nwu lɛsɔdiki ninle nle mmle nɛ.
Alesaa kubi nwu nkpo baasa ni ninle Yaa ɔlaa nɛ.
Alesaa kubi nwu nkpo niakpete ni di osuku suoto ninle batii ba, nse beenu ɔlaa nwu nkpo, Abonsam nwa amadiki nwu di situ lɛma kamɛ, mmle manaafũ banu alɛ Yaa kadiki ma anta ma ni nkpa.
Nko kafɔɔ niakpete ni di afuɔ kasɔ suoto, ninle batii ba nse beenu ɔlaa nwu nkpo, manfũ nwu ku suoto lɛyɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ kumbuo ma kaamɛ nwaa.
Manfũ nwu manu di obe kakuii kamɛ.
Nkpo oso nse ɔsɔ onyu lɛwa ma di suoto, mankple nkpaamaa.
Alesaa kubi ko kafɔɔ niakpete ni di siwuu sɛfa kamɛ ninle, batii ba nienu ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo, kafɔɔ kayika mmle nimiina ku lɛsaawɛ ku kayi suoto omɛnɛfɛ okpee nfukiti nintĩi ma, mámmuɔ baatika abi.
Alesaa kubi ko niakpete ni di kasɔ biene suoto, ninle batii ba nse beenu ɔlaa biene nwu nkpo, mammufũ nwu manklee ku situ biene.
Manwakosa suoto kasɔ mankpee okyiini ninaadu obe wɔ beetika ni abi.
Ta Kandiɛ Lɛfɔ Akpa Ata Batii.
“Otii kuonwii ninsɔ kandiɛ, aayɔ lɛsaa aatĩi nwɔ.
Ee aayɔ ase di mpa kalɔ.
Kafɔɔ antakatɛsa kandiɛ nwu antika lɛɛba le niɛtaka nii, alɛ aakpa anta batii ba nikɔwa ni leyo nwu kamɛ.
Lɛsaa lele niewofa kaakɔ lele, babadiki ni kayi.
Lelele kafɔɔ beetĩi bɛɛtɛ diitunu kamɛ, babanya ni mandiki ni manwako lɛkpa kamɛ.
“Bilolaa atoko bikyɔɔ di sɛlaa se bianu ni suoto.
Otii wɔ nienu, eenu ni kasɔ, abakple annu kasɔ anlenkee bia.
Otii wɔ ninankyɔɔ ni atoko, kɛɛkɛɛ wɔ eenyu alɛ eenu nii bia, babakle manfũ nwɔ ninnɛɛ mansifiko.” Owe Ninle Yesu Ɔya Ku Babilɛma?
Yesu ɔya ku Yesu basuɔtɔbi lɛma lawa nwɔ ɔnya, kafɔɔ batafuo nwɔ ɔnya, ta batii dikudi nwu oso.
Ninfɛ baatii bawo lakyɛ baalaatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Yaafɔ ku babilee suɔtɔbi n-yɛ kaayi boomiɛ alɛ banya fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ bamuu lɛma alɛ, “Yaami ku babiloo suɔtɔbi ninle batii ba nikonu ni Yaa ɔlaa bɔɔbla nwu ni di suoto nɛ.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Aata Kɔfɛɛfɔ Kuadiɛ Ɔfɛ.
Dii ninwii, Yesu labuo di oklo kamɛ ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bita butaalɛ busifi lekpo le mmle sɛmaa.” Nkpo oso baayefe osuku baakyako osifi.
Obe wɔ batika ni di ntu osi bɔɔkyɛ nii, Yesu lakyɔsĩi.
Nfanwu, kɔfɛɛfɔ siene kunwii niakyako ɔfɛ di ntu nwu osi, ntu lakyako ɔpɛ obuo di oklo nwu kamɛ.
Nioso diata alɛ baasiɛ di kukpi ku nkpa ntɛɛ.
Nioso basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo lakyɛ baalaasɛnkɛsa Yesu, baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, ɔnɔɔfo!
Nfɛ buokpi lo!” Ninfɛ di Yesu lataka aayila aamuɛ kɔfɛɛfɔ ku ntu nwu nikɔkpɛ ni suoto, ni diate kloklo dialo kanana nɛ.
Ni aakaalɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Fɛ di ofũ onu lee nkpe?” Kafɔɔ oyila ko baayila baatoonyu yaaa, lɛyɛkɛ kafɔɔ lapɛ ma.
Ni baatɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Ɔmɛntii okle ninle nwɔ?
Ankakatɛ anta kɔfɛɛfɔ ku ntu be nikɔkpɛ ni alɛ ankyɔɔ nwɔ atoko!” Yesu Latososa Ninwuna Kpile Ninwii Aadiki Di Osuɔtɔ Onwii Kamɛ.
Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lataalɛ baalaadu Galilea lekpo kotoko kakyɛ nyɔɔfa di Gadara kasɔ suoto.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lasoo ni di oklo, osuɔtɔ onwii di anwuna kpile nsi ni ladie aakye okpoo nwu kamɛ abakyakako nwɔ.
Ditɔɔklɛ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle disinkpee ni awu, ánsiɛ kafɔɔ leeyo.
Sɛkya kamɛ ko ansiɛ.
Di obe wɔ aanya ni Yesu, aayiisa kudu osie kanya aapɛ akunkyi di Yesu katũ.
Ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Yesu, Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni Obi!
Ɔmɛnlaa ninsi munkofɔ ntɛɛ?
Kotikiti fɔ lekoto, tannanfi mi kootoko.” Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle labuɛ nkpo, diekye Yesu lamuɛ ninwuna kpile nwu ninsi nwɔ ni kaamɛ alɛ, “Didie nwɔ kaamɛ!” Obe kpinwu kamɛ ninwuna kpile nwu mmufũ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo, nse beekpee nwɔ nkɔkyɔ ninnɛɛ ku nkpaa, anfefee mi kafɔɔ.
Ninwuna nwu nkpaa nwɔ ninsifiko ɔfaafuu kamɛ.
Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛ manlɛɛ fɔ?” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Ami manlɛɛ dikudi nɛ.” Aabuɛ nkpo diekye anwuna kpile nwu nsi nwɔ kaamɛ apɔ.
Ninfɛ di anwuna nwu nkpo latikiti Yesu lekoto alɛ, atantososa ma aakpee di lɛba le manfuki anwuna kpile mankpee ni di dibiɔ le ninaani kase, diibuo nsi ni kaamɛ.
Aplakuo ɔlambu kplɛ onwii latoole alesaa di kabokotee nkpaa ninfa.
Ni di anwuna kpile nwu latikiti Yesu lekoto alɛ, ata ma balaabuo di aplakuo nwu kamɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lata ma osuku nɛ.
Nfanwu anwuna kpile nwu ladie di osuɔtɔ nwu kamɛ aalaabuo di aplakuo nwu kamɛ.
Ni di aplakuo ɔlambu nwu latoso kitikiti aakye kabokotee nwu nkpaa aalaakpa aabuo diɛ lekpo kamɛ aamɛmɛɛ ntu aakpi nɛ.
Obe wɔ baatii ba niatɔɔkpa ni aplakuo nwu lanya lɛsaa le niawa nii, baatoso baasifi sekpoo simuu ku afe kamɛ baalaabuɛ ɔlaa nwu baakyakasa.
Nioso batii ladie baakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaanyu lɛsaa le niawa nii.
Di obe wɔ babadu ni Yesu nfũ, baanya osuɔtɔ wɔ di Yesu latososa ni anwuna kpile nwu aadiki ni kaamɛ nsi di Yesu nkpaatũ.
Ditɔɔkpa nwɔ eekpee awu asi kloklo.
Bamuu lɛma, lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ ma.
Batii ba nianya mmle okle diawa nii, latɔkɔ batii bule mmle okle diabla fiɛ diakpa ni osuɔtɔ wɔ kamɛ diɛ anwuna kpile lasiɛ nii.
Nkpo oso ntɛɛ nwu batii bamuu di Gadara kasɔ lawa babatikiti Yesu lekoto alɛ, adie ma kaasɔ suoto asifi, diekye baayɛkɛ.
Nkpo oso Yesu labuo di oklo kamɛ aasifi.
Osuɔtɔ wɔ kamɛ di Yesu latososa anwuna kpile nwu aadiki ni kaamɛ, latikiti Yesu lekoto alɛ, “Tɛɛ ntikanko fɔ.” Kafɔɔ Yesu ditatuna ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔɔkyɛ leyo, faalaabuɛ lɛsaa le di Yaa lɛbla ɛɛta fɔ ni.” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lakple aasifi okpoo nwu kamɛ aalaatoobuɛ lɛsaa le di Yesu labla atɔɔ ni nɛ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Yairo Obi Sankobi Ku Ɔsanko Onwii Ofiɛ.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu lakple aataalɛ lekpo nwu aasifi nii, batii nwu nkpo lafũ nwɔ osie kanya, diekye bamuu lɛma baatoonyu nwɔ osuku.
Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Yairo, ale ni Yuda batii kasiisakɔ ɔnɔɔfo lawa abapɛ akunkyi di Yesu nkpaatũ aatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, awa baakyɛ leyo nɔɔ, diekye obi nɔɔ sankobi onwii wɔ ninkpe nwɔ ni, atoofũ ni fɛ lefosi alɛɛ anyɔ, latookpi.
Obe wɔ di Yesu layefe osuku oofe nii, batii kpinwu latikanko nwɔ baamana nwɔ kpinkpĩ baakyi.
Baatii nwu nkpo kamɛ, ɔsanko onwii diɛ asaa latoowii ni osie kanya fɛ lefosi alɛɛ anyɔ lasiɛ kaamɛ.
Ɔsanko wɔ mmle ntɔɔlalaasa koto nɔɔ kumuu di bafatɛ sɛkyɛ alɛ diayɔɔ nwɔ, kafɔɔ kuonwii ditafuo nwɔ kɔfa ɔbla.
Nioso aafe di Yesu sɛmaa di batii nwu kamɛ, aalaakpanko nwɔ awu kotokosi.
Nfanwu, asaa owii nwu niabudi.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ alɛ, “Owe niɛkpankoe?” Kafɔɔ kuonwii ditabuɛ alɛ nnwɔɔ niɛkpanko nwɔ.
Ninfɛ di Petro lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, nyu mmle okle baatii nwu lɛmana fɔ kpinkpĩ beekyi ni!” Kafɔɔ Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “N-ye nlɛ otii lɛkpankoe, diekye osie owo ledie mi kaamɛ.” Obe wɔ di ɔsanko nwu lanya alɛ Yesu ntootofo lɛsaa le aabla nii, atafuo suoto owofasa.
Aadie aawa aabapɛ akunkyi di Yesu katũ ku ditũtũkũ di batii nwu anu.
Ninfɛ aadiki aabuɛ lɛsaa le oso aakpanko nwɔ nii, ku mmle di ofiɛ nwu layɔɔ nwɔ ni ninfanwu nɛ.
Nkpo oso Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Obi nii sankobi, ofũ onu lɛfɔ ntɔɔyɔɔsa fɔ ofiɛ.
Tɔɔkyɛ di atoko ɔkyɛ ole kamɛ.” Di obe wɔ di Yesu lekple akle ɔlaa nwu oobuɛ nii, tɔkyɛntɛ onwii niakye Yuda batii kasiisakɔ ɔnɔɔfo Yairo leyo aawa lɛba nwu.
Ni aabatɔkɔ nwɔ kanya alɛ, “Obi lɛfɔ sankobi nwu ntookpi kofokofoko.
Nioso taansinkpɛnsa saatuotɛ ninwuna odiki!” Kafɔɔ di Yesu lanu ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo, aatɔkɔ Yairo alɛ, “Tanyɛkɛ.
Afɔ fũ fanu falɛ obi lɛfɔ nwu dibayɔɔ nwɔ.” Obe wɔ di Yesu labuo ni Yairo leyo yi, atata osuku alɛ otii kuonwii abuo leyo nwu kamɛ ku nnwɔɔ, diediki Petro ku Yakobo ku ɔsankobi nwu ote ku ɔya lete aata osuku baabuo.
Batii bamuu ninfa layila baatoowi kaku ta obisɔ nwu oso.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitansinwi kaku, obisɔ nwu diekpi ɔkyɔsĩi ɔɔkyɔsĩi.” Ninfɛ baatii nwu bamuu lama nwɔ nɛ, diekye baye alɛ atookpi.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lamufũ nwɔ di kanɛɛtũ, ni aalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Obi nii, taka!” Nfanwu ɔsankobi nwu ninwuna niakple diabuo, aasɛnkɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, bamiɛ lɛsaa batɔɔ ale.
Lɛsaa le mmle labla ɔsankobi nwu balofotɛ ɔkpɛ, kafɔɔ Yesu lakpee ma kufiofa alɛ, batantɔkɔ otii kuonwii lɛsaa le niɛwa nii.
Yesu Lakpee Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Lefosi Banyɔ Nwu Kɔtɔ.
Nni kamaa, Yesu lalɛɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi banyɔ nwu asiisa, ni aadiki ma osuku aata ma kafɔɔ otumi alɛ baayɔ mantososa anwuna kpile amuu, manyɔɔsa sifiɛ ate ate kafɔɔ.
Ninfɛ aakpee ma alɛ batɔɔkyɛ baalaabuɛ Yaa sɛka kalɛkɔ sɛlaa bata batii, baayɔɔsa bafiɛtɛ sifiɛ.
Fiɛ nfɛ babasifi nii, Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitan-yɔ lɛsalɛsaa biaklee di osuku nwu biofe ni kamɛ.
Bitanklee ɔkyɛnwoso, ee asaa ɔkaalɛ kotofo ee alesaa ee koto.
Bitanklee bia osi awo nyɔɔfa.
Kakɔ lele beefũ ye, biesiɛ leeyo nwu nkpo dilaase di dii le bibadie ni di okpoo nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Nse baafũ ye di okpoo owo kamɛ, nfɛ biodie ninfa minsifi, biɛfɛntɛ nkpaasɔ lee kɔtɛ bitɛ ma.
Nni nimatuo alɛ baasĩ ye ofũ nɛ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lasifi, baakyɛ baalaakyi nkpayotũ mmuu kamɛ, baabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa biene nwu baayɔɔsa kafɔɔ batii sifiɛ kaakɔ biala.
Herode Lakpɔkpɔtɔ Diisibu Kamɛ Ta Yesu Oso.
Obe wɔ di Herode wɔ niatoole ni sɛka di Galilea kasɔ lanu ni asaa ya niatɔɔwa nii, aakpɔkpɔtɔ.
Diekye batii bawo latoobuɛ alɛ, Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane nintookple ɛɛtaka eekye bakpi kamɛ ɛɛwa.
Batii bamba kafɔɔ latoobuɛ alɛ, Elia ntookple ɛɛwa.
Ni baawo kafɔɔ latoobuɛ alɛ Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ owo nintookple ɛɛtaka ɛɛwa ninkpa.
Ni di Herode labuɛ alɛ, “Ami niata baabudi Yohane disi, ni owe ninle otii wɔ mmle suoto konu sɛlaa se mmle nkyeko ni?” Nkpo oso Herode latoomiɛ osuku wɔ abafe annya ni Yesu.
Yesu Lata Basuɔtɔ Nkpe Nnɔɔ Alesaa Baale Baamiɛ.
Obe wɔ baasaateketetɛ nwu nkpo lakple baawa nii, baatɔkɔ Yesu asaa ya amuu baabla nii.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakpaa lete lama aasifiko okpoo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Betsaida nɛ.
Obe wɔ baatii kpinwu lanu nii, ni baatikanko nwɔ baakyɛ nfa nɛ.
Yesu kafɔɔ lafũ ma, ni aakakatɛ aata ma di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ suoto nɛ.
Ni aayɔɔsa mba niatoofiɛ ni kaamɛ lɛma sifiɛ nɛ.
Obe wɔ kuufĩ nfɛ kofe ni ɔmɛɛ, ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lefosi banyɔ nwu nkpo lawa Yesu nfũ baabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ta batii nwu nkpo batɔɔkyɛ nkpayotũ ku afe ya baatii nte ni, ɛɛtɛtɛɛ wo ni kamɛ, baalaamiɛ alesaa ku ntenkɔ.
Diekye lɛba le bukpe nii ayo nnaa ninfũ.” Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye bamu bimiɛ alesaa bita ma bale.” Nfa nfɛ baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Alesaa ya bukle ni ninfũ ninle bloblo akudi anɔɔ ku kɔkpaku kɔnyɔ, sɛɛ foomiɛ falɛ bukyɛ buɔlaaya alesaa buwako banankpantii ba?” Basuɔtɔ ba niawɛ ni ninfa kabla fɛ nkpe nnɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu alɛ, “Bita batii nwu nkpo basiɛ kaasɔ akudi akudi.
Diikudi ninwii dibla fɛ batii afosi anɔɔ.” Di basaateketetɛ nwu labla nkpo baalo nii, ninfɛ di Yesu layɔ bloblo akudi anɔɔ ku kɔkpaku kɔnyɔ nwu nkpo, ni aatakatɛsa anu aanyu osi nɛ.
Ninfɛ aapɛ Yaa sɛfa diisi lɛnya nɛ.
Ninfɛ abɛbɛɛ nya aayɔ aata basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ basɛ bata batii nwu nɛ.
Bamuu lɛma baale baamiɛ, ni basaateketetɛ nwu lasiisa kɔkyɛɛ kɔkyɛɛ ko niabu ni nɛ.
Kuayii lefosi nkyikyɛ nnyɔ.
Petro Labuɛ Alɛ Yesu Ninle Otii Wɔ Beediki Ni Nɛ.
Dii ninwii obe wɔ di Yesu lete latɔɔpɛ ɔlaa aatɔɔta ni Yaa, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ.
Ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Owe baatii kobuɛ alɛ nnle?” Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Batii bawo kobuɛ alɛ Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane fale.
Bawo kafɔɔ kobuɛ alɛ, Elia fale.
Fiɛ baawo kafɔɔ kobuɛ alɛ, aaa Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ onwii nintookple ɛɛtaka ɛɛwa ninkpa.” Ninfɛ aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ni aye mɔ, owe biobuɛ bilɛ nnle?” Ninfɛ di Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ nɛ.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Aakyeko Dibuo Nɔɔ Ku Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu laakpee ma kufiofa osie kanya alɛ, batantɔkɔ otii kuonwii ɔlaa wɔ mmle.
Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Dikpe ni, ami, Otii Obi nwu, lefe di dibuo kamɛ di okpoo banɔɔfo ku olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ, beesĩ mi, beelo mi.
Kafɔɔ di dii tiɛfa kamɛ, Yaa makple ansɛnkɛsɛɛ ankyeko bakpi kamɛ anwako nkpa.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ bamuu lɛma alɛ, “Nse otii owo komiɛ alɛ awa abatikankoe, ni dikpe nii ansĩ suoto nɔɔ, an-yɔ aatoo nɔɔ, antikankoe dii biala.
Diekye otii lele nikomiɛ alɛ ata nkpa nɔɔ, abayu mi.
Kafɔɔ otii lele nieyu nkpa nɔɔ ta ami otikanko oso, nwaako, abawɛ nkpa.
Lɛmɛntota biene di otii mawɛ nse ɛɛwɛ kayi ka mmle asa amuu eeyu nkpa nɔɔ?
Nse ami ku asaatuo nii ya kotuo ni amuu lɛkpɛ otii owo sinunsɔ, otii nwu kafɔɔ makpɛ, ami, Otii Obi nwu, sinunsɔ di obe wɔ mawa ni lɛɛkpa nii kamɛ ku Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ klekle bamuu lɛkpa kamɛ.
Nwaako, kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ batii bawo nsi kaamɛ lee ninfũ, bɔlɔɔwa ɔbakpi diɛlase di obe wɔ di Yaa lediki sɛka nɔɔ kalekɔ eetuo ma nii.” Yesu Letembi Lakyi Di Kobokote Osi.
Fɛ nanwɔkyĩ sɛmaa di Yesu labuɛ ni sɛlaa se mmle, aakpaa Petro ku Yohane ku Yakobo aasifiko kabokotee kanwii osi alɛ, bɔɔlaapɛ ɔlaa manta Yaa.
Obe wɔ ɔɔpɛ ɔlaa anta ni Yaa, anu nɔɔ lakyi.
Awu nɔɔ kafɔɔ lapu fututu aatoosese di anu.
Nfanwu, ni baasuɔtɔ banyɔ banwii labayila baatɔɔkakatɛ ko nwɔ nɛ.
Basuɔtɔ nwu niale Mose ku Elia nɛ.
Baakyɔɔ di Yaa kafɔɔ leklekle kamɛ, ni bakakatɛko Yesu di osuku wɔ suoto abafe anyɛntɛ lɛsaa le di Yaa komiɛ ni kuukpi nɔɔ kamɛ di Yerusalem nɛ.
Petro ku bawo nɔɔ labuo sɛɛkyɔsi kamɛ osie kanya, kafɔɔ baasɛnkɛ baanya leklekle le kamɛ di Yesu lasiɛ nii ku batii banyɔ ba niayila nwɔ ni di ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Obe wɔ baatii nwu nkpo latoosifi nii, Petro latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, nwaako nfũ mmle loo ɔwa lɛtɛ dilɛ!
Ta bupɛ akpanta atiɛ ninfũ.
Anwii alefɔ, anwii Mose ale, anwii kafɔɔ Elia ale.” Atatɛ aatofo bia ɔlaa wɔ aatoobuɛ nii.
Di obe wɔ eekple ayɛ ɔɔkakatɛ nii, dituntũ ninwii lasoo diawa, diablɛfɛ diatĩi ma suoto.
Basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo layɛkɛ obe wɔ diituntũ le mmle lakyɔɔ ma ni di suoto.
Ninfɛ di sɛlɔ ladie di dituntũ nwu kamɛ siabuɛ alɛ, “Nnya Obi nii ninle nnwɔ nɛ.
Nnwɔ lediki nii bikyɔɔ nwɔ atoko!” Obe wɔ sɛɛlɔ nwu laloo ni ɔkakatɛ, baanya nii, Yesu lete nfɛ niabu aayila.
Basaateketetɛ nwu layɔ asaa ya baanya ni ninfa baakookaa, batabɛ kanya baatɔkɔ otii kuonwii di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Yesu Latososa Ninwuna Kpile Aadiki Di Osuɔtɔbi Onwii Kamɛ.
Kaleesɛ, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu batiɛ lasoo baakye kabokotee nwu nkpo osi baawa.
Ninfɛ baatii kpinwu lawa babakyaka ko nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ onwii lafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ!
Kotikiti fɔ lekoto, nyu obi nii!
Obi nwu onwii Pɛ!
Ninwuna kpile ninwii nkpɛko nwɔ, ninta alɛ nfanwu, anyiisa kudu osie kanya.
Ambensa suoto anfuki nwɔ anlaasa kaasɔ, afuuta ntoodie nwɔ kaanya.
Nse diɔkpɛko nwɔ nkpo ninwɛ osie fiɛ niinwuna nwu ndiɛ nwɔ.
Letikiti basaateketetɛ lɛfɔ lekoto nlɛ batososa ninwuna kpile nwu batɛɛ, kafɔɔ baafuo ni otososa.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye, miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle, be oso biloofũ mi binu, biɔbla otokopĩ nkpo?
Ɔmɛmbe okle biomiɛ bilɛ nsiɛko ye naase?
Ɔmɛmbe okle kakpee otu nnanfi ye nnaase?” Ni aatɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu alɛ, “Kpaa obi lɛfɔ nwu fawako ninfũ.” Obe wɔ di ote kɔkpaa nwɔ aanwako nii, nfanwu, ninwuna kpile nwu niapɛ nwɔ diatɛ kaasɔ aakyako ɔnananfi tii.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lamuɛ ninwuna nwu aadiki di obisɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ, aayɔɔsɔɔ ofiɛ, aakpaa nwɔ aata ote nɛ.
Diabla batii nwu bamuu ɔkpɛ di Yaa otumi kplɛ wɔ mmle suoto.
Yesu Lakple Aakakatɛ Di Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Obe wɔ di asaa ya amuu di Yesu labla ni latɔɔbla ni batii nwu ɔkpɛ oso, Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bitanyee lɛsaa le lakye kasɔ latɔɔtɔkɔ ye nii!
Babayɔ ami, Otii Obi nwu, mankpee di batii nnɛɛ kamɛ.” Kafɔɔ basaateketetɛ ba mmle ditanu ɔlaa wɔ mmle kasɔ.
Dile lɛsaa le baayɔ baawofasa ma nii, kafɔɔ baayɛkɛ nwɔ ɔlaa ɔkaalɛ di ɔlaa nwu suoto.
Yesu Ladiki Otii Wɔ Ninlenke Ni Aatuo.
Kananfi kanwii labuo di basateketetɛ nwu ntɛɛ alɛ, owe niefũ kɔya kaamɛ lɛma alenke.
Di Yesu latofo lɛsaa le disi baatoobu ni oso aayɔ obisɔ onwii aase diɛ anu lɛma di katũ nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Otii wɔ niefũ obisɔ wɔ mmle leeyooto nii kamɛ, ami eefũ.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ niefũ mi nii, eefũ otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ.
Diekye otii wɔ niɛwakosa ni suoto kasɔ nnwɔɔ niefũ kɔya alenke bamuu nɛ.” Otii Wɔ Ninantaka Ayila Ye Ni Di Suoto, Ayɛ Ye Kamaa.
Ninfɛ di Yohane latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, buanya osuɔtɔ onwii kotososa anwuna kpile baatii suoto leeyoto lɛfɔ kamɛ, ni buatɔkɔ nwɔ bulɛ adiɛ, diekye aasi wo kaamɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bitantĩi nwɔ osuku.
Diekye otii wɔ ninantaka ayila wo ni di suoto, bitofo bilɛ, ni ayɛ wo kamaa.” Baasĩ Yesu Ofũ Di Samaria Kakpayotũ Kanwii Kamɛ.
Di obe ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ alɛ Yaa kakpaa Yesu ansifiko ni osi, aabla disibu, aadie aayefe osuku aatoofe Yerusalem.
Aakyesee batɔkyɛntɛ bawo alɛ balekatũ basɔ kakpayotũ kanwii kamɛ di Samaria, balaalolaa asaa batɛ bata ɔwa nɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ di okpoo nwu batii latofo alɛ ɔwaalɛ ɔɔwalɛ anfe ni Yerusalem oso, batatuna alɛ boofũ nwɔ.
Di obe wɔ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ba ninle ni Yohane ku Yakobo latofo nii, baalɛɛ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, foomiɛ falɛ bulɛɛ ɔtɔ kuookye osi kuwa kubawɔɔsa ma?” Ninfɛ di Yesu lamunikĩi aasĩ ɔlaa aata ma nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lawaalɛ baasifi kakpayotũ bamba nɛ.
Batii Bawo Lamiɛ Alɛ Bootikanko Yesu Nkpaamaa.
Obe wɔ bakyɛ di osuku boofe nii, osuɔtɔ onwii lawa aabatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, kakɔ lele fabakyɛ, matikanko fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nkpikiti nkpe atuɛ ya kamɛ mansiɛ nii, bakansiɛ nkpe ayo mante nii.
Kafɔɔ ami Otii Obi, nnaa lɛba katɛ ni disi.” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ otii bamba alɛ, “Tikankoe.” Kafɔɔ otii nwu labuɛ alɛ, “Saate, tɛɛnkyɛ ninakookaa teemi fiɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ “Ta batii ba ninte ni fɛ bakpi bakookaa mma bamu bakpi lɛma.
Kafɔɔ afɔ yi, tɔɔkyɛ falaabuɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɔlaa nwu.” Otii bamba kafɔɔ latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, matikanko fɔ.
Kafɔɔ tɛɛ osuku ninkyɛ naata batii nii bamu letofo fiɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Otii wɔ nfɛ ninkle ni lɛnwa ayɛ ni katũ, ookple annyu ni sɛmaa, diesiɛko ata Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu ɔkpɛ.”
Yesu Lakpee Batikankotɛ Afosi Akuɛnsĩ Batii Banyɔ Kɔtɔ.
Nle mmle sɛmaa, Saate nwu ladiki basuɔtɔ afosi akuɛnsĩ basuɔtɔ banyɔ bamba, aakpee ma banyɔ banyɔ alɛ bakyɛ sekpoo ku nkpayotũ be kamɛ ɔɔwa ni ɔbakyɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ofiɛlɛ nwu mpɔ, kafɔɔ bafiɛlɛtɛ diɛpɔ.
Nkpo oso bipɛ ɔlaa bita Saate nwu nimba ni ofiɛlɛ nwu nkpo bilɛ, aakyesee bafiɛlɛtɛ mamakyakaako di ofiɛlɛ nwu nkpo kamɛ mansiisa.” Bitɔɔkyɛ!
Kokyesee ye fɛ afosobi di bakplɛle kamɛ.
Bitanklee koto lekpeesa ee asaa ɔkaalɛ kotofo ee ntokota.
Bitanyila di osuku kafɔɔ bilɛ biɔsɛɛsa otii kuonwii.
“Leyo lele kamɛ biebuo, bile katũ bisɛɛsa ma bilɛ, ‘Atoko ɔkyɛ ole disiɛko leyo le mmle batii.’ Kafɔɔ nse otii wɔ nimbɔmbɔ ni atoko ɔkyɛ ole owo nkpe ninfa, ni biɛta atoko ɔkyɛ ole lee ditikanko nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ nse kuonwii nnaa yi, ni biɛta atoko ɔkyɛ ole lee dikple diwa ye ɔkyɛ.
Bikple bisiɛ di leyo le kamɛ beefũ ye ni.
Bile, bienyi lɛsaa lele bɛɛta ye, diekye kpɛmblatɛ ninfũ koto.
Bitandie leeyo lewo kamɛ, biasifi lɛbamba kamɛ.
“Okpoo lele kamɛ biɛkyɛ, beefũ ye yi, biele lɛsaa lele bɛɛta ye.
Biɛyɔɔsa bafiɛtɛ ba ninkpe ni di okpoo nwu kamɛ sifiɛ.
Biɛtɔkɔ okpoo nwu batii bilɛ, ‘Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ ye.’ Kafɔɔ nse biɛkyɛ okpoo owo kamɛ, di okpoo nwu batii diefũ ye, biɛkyɛ okpoo nwu lɛkpaka biebuɛ bilɛ, ‘Okpoo lee kɔtɛ ko ninka wo ni di nkpaasɔ, buɔfɛntɛ muntɛ ye.
