Kafɔɔ binyuma bilɛ Yaa sɛka ole bee ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ!’ Nioso kɔtɔkɔ ye ntikiti nlɛ di lɛkankoyi suoto, Yaa manya Sodom okpoo nyaami, anlenkee okpoo nwu!
Sɛkpoo Sewo Ditafũ Yesu Ɔlaa.
“Korasin okpoo batii, biyɔɔsa!
Betsaida okpoo batii, ayee biyɔɔsa!
Nse Tiro ku Sidon sekpoo kpile nwu kamɛ nimbla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ ntuo, nse batoosiɛ kaasɔ kofokofoko, beenyukũ sikplakpi, beefifia ntɔ di suoto beetuo alɛ batookyi di sikpile lɛma!
Yaa manya Tiro ku Sidon sekpoo nyaami anlenkee ye di lɛkankoyi suoto.
Ni afɔ Kapernaum, foonyu falɛ babatakatɛsa fɔ katoo mansifiko osi?
Babawakosa fɔ kasɔ mankpee fɔ di kawɔɔ kamɛ!” Ninfe di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Otii lele niɛkyɔɔ ye atoko, ami ɛɛkyɔɔ atoko.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niesĩ ye, ami eesĩ.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niesĩ mi, eesĩ otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ.” Batii Afosi Akuɛnsĩ Batii Banyɔ Nwu Lakple Baawa Yesu Nfũ.
Batii afosi akuɛnsĩ batii banyɔ nwu lakple baawa ku suoto lɛyɔɔ kplɛ.
Ni baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, bia anwuna kpile lanu wo ɔlaa aadie, buatososa nya ni di leyooto lɛfɔ kamɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Lanya Satana kɔkpa ankye osi fɛ mmle di ɔplalaa mmunaa nii.
Bikyɔɔ atoko bienu nwaa!
Ntɔɔta ye otumi nlɛ biafuo ɔkyɛ di asaanwu ku nnkpakana suoto, ku lo nwu situmi nɔɔ simuu suoto alɛ lɛsalɛsa dilaabla ye.
Kafɔɔ, bitanta suoto layɔɔ ye alɛ anwuna kpile lɛkyɔɔ ye ni atoko oso.
Kafɔɔ suoto siyɔɔ ye alɛ Yaa ntɔɔkpana ye ayooto ɛɛtɛ di Yaa kafa.” Yesu Latansa Yaa.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, Yaa Ninwuna lakpee Yesu suoto lɛyɔɔ ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Teete, osi ku kasɔ Saate, kɔpɛ fɔ sɛfa.
Diekye asaa ya fɛɛyɔ feekookaa ni bakũyentɛ ku banumbentɛ, nnya fatoodiki feetuo batii ba ninanye ni akũ nɛ.
Nwaako, Teete, nkpo okle foomiɛ falɛ dite nɛ.” Ninfɛ aakple aabuɛ alɛ, “Teemi lɛyɔ asaa amuu eekpee mi ninnɛɛ kamɛ.
Kuonwii dieye otii wɔ ninle ni Obi nwu, diediki Ote lete.
Otii kuonwii kafɔɔ dieye Ote nwu diediki Obi lete ku batii ba di Obi nwu nkpo komiɛ alɛ adiki atuo nii.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lamunikĩi aatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo buɛɛ alɛ, “Aye leleye nlɛ alɛ biɔnya asaa ya biɔnya ni lo!
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ kpinwu ku baka lamiɛ alɛ bɔɔnya lɛsaa le biɔnya nii, kafɔɔ batanya.
Baamiɛ kafɔɔ alɛ boonu lɛsaa le bionu nii, kafɔɔ batanu.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Samaria Otii Futulɛtɛ Onwii Suoto.
Kufiofa tuotɛ onwii lawa ku disibu alɛ ɔɔbasɔ Yesu annyu.
Ni aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, be kabla fiɛ kawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛ Kɔɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ fiɛ?
Lɛ feenu ɔlaa nwu nkpo kafɔɔ kasɔ?” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bɔmbɔ Saate Yaa lɛfɔ ku otu lɛfɔ omuu, ku ninwuna lɛfɔ nimuu ku osie lɛfɔ omuu ku disibu lɛfɔ nimuu, ni faabɔmbɔ owo lɛfɔ kafɔɔ fɛ mmle fambɔmbɔ ni suoto.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Mmle feebuɛ nii, nkpo kute nɛ.
Ni bla nkpo fabawɛ nkpa.” Kafɔɔ kufiofa tuotɛ nwu nkpo lamiɛ alɛ ɔɔta suoto lɛbɛ, nioso aakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Owe ninle mi owo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Obe onwii, osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ, aakye Yerusalem aatoofe Yeriko okpoo, ni baayu lamufũ nwɔ di osuku nɛ.
Baapɛ nwɔ, baadiki nwɔ asaa di suoto, ni baadiɛ nwɔ baatɛ ninfa, ooloo okpi.
Ni diabawa alɛ Yaa oletatɛ onwii labafe di osuku nwu suoto.
Kafɔɔ obe wɔ aanya ni osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo di osukulɔɔkɔ, aawaalɛ nwɔ aafe kaakyɛ nyɔɔfa aasifi.
Nkpo okle di oletatɛ kyakaakotɛ onwii kafɔɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Lewi labatoofe nɛ.
Obe wɔ aanya ni osuɔtɔ nwu, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aawaalɛ nwɔ aafe di osuku kakyɛ nyɔɔfa aasifi.
Kafɔɔ Samaria otii onwii latoofe osuku, aakyɛ di osuku nwu nkpo suoto, abakyakako osuɔtɔ nwu.
Obe wɔ aanyɔɔ nii, kafutu lanyinyii nwɔ.
Ninfɛ aakyɛ aalaadu nwɔ, ninfɛ aayɔ nnɔnyi ku nta aakpete nwɔ di nkɔ nwu suoto, ninfɛ aaninii nwɔ nkɔ nwu mmuu nɛ.
Ni aakɛnkɛ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo aatika di nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ bɔkɛɛ wɔ suoto aasiɛ nii.
Ni aakpaa nwɔ aasifiko bafɔɔ kafunkɔ, aalaanyu nwɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ kale lasɛ nii, Samaria otii nwu layɔ koto kowo aata bafɔɔ kafunkɔ nyuntɛ, aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Toonyu fiɛtɛ nwu.
Nse kokple mmafe, lɛsaa lele feekple fɛɛlalaasa di suoto nɔɔ, kamata nta fɔ.’ ” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ kufiofa tuotɛ nwu alɛ, “Afɔ fɔɔnya nii, di batii ba mmle batiɛ kamɛ, owe lɛma ninle osuɔtɔ wɔ niabuo ni baayu nnɛɛ kamɛ siɛwo?” Ninfɛ di kufiofa tuotɛ ladiki kanya alɛ, “Otii wɔ nianyɔɔ ni nyaami.” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔɔ yi, tɔɔkyɛ falaabla nkpo.” Yesu Lakyɛ Marta Ku Maria Nfũ.
Dii ninwii Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoofe osuku, ni baalaadu okpoo onwii nɛ.
Nfa di ɔsanko onwii bɔɔlɛɛ ni Marta lafũ nwɔ kɔfɔɔ di leyo nɔɔ nɛ.
Marta wɔ mmle lawɛ obilɛma sankobi onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Maria.
Ɔsanko wɔ mmle lalasiɛ di Yesu nkpaatũ aatoonu nwɔ asaa otuo.
Leyo ɔsaabla latika di Marta lete suoto, nioso diatoobuo nwɔ suoto.
Ni aakyɛ aalaatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, ni faayɔ nwu ole falɛ obiloo ntoodiɛ leyo sɛkpɛ eetika mi di suoto?
Tɔkɔ nwɔ aawa abakyakaakoe!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Marta!
Nyu mmle fookpee ni suoto kubuɛ di asaa kpinwu suoto lo.
Lɛsaa ninwii pɛ niefĩ.
Nni ninle dibiene le di Maria ntoodiki ni nɛ.
Kuonwii kafɔɔ dilabafũ nwɔ ninnɛɛ.”
Yesu Latuo Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Mmle Baapɛ Ɔlaa Manta Ni Yaa.
Dii ninwii, Yesu lawɛ lɛɛba ninwii aatɔɔpɛ ɔlaa aatɔɔta Yaa.
Obe wɔ aaloo nii, Saateketetɛ nɔɔ onwii lawa nwɔ ɔkyɛ abatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, tuo wo mmle mampɛ ɔlaa manta ni Yaa, fɛ mmle di Yohane latuo ni basaateketetɛ nɔɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nse biɔpɛ ɔlaa minta Yaa yi, biebuɛ bilɛ, ‘Teete, ta balɛɛ leyooto lɛfɔ klekle nwu ku dibu.
Sɛka kalekɔ lɛfɔ diwa wo kaamɛ.
Ta wo dii alesaa ya buale ni obe lele.
Faayɔ sikpile loo fakyɛ wo, diekye awo kafɔɔ mun-yɔ munkyɛ otii lele niɛbla wo okpile.
Tankpaa wo faakpee di ɔsɔ onyu kamɛ.’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Nse diɛwa alɛ onwii kamɛ lee lɛkyɛ siɛwo nɔɔ nfũ di nkyɛntɛɛ ɛɛlaatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Siɛwo, fɛnsa mi bloblo akudi atiɛ awo, diekye siɛwo nii onwii lekye osuku ɛɛwa ɛbasoosa di ɔkyɛ nii nunua.
Lelesaa kuninwii diete mi kamayɔ ntɔɔ anle nii!’ “Di siɛwo lɛfɔ nwu lɛtɔkɔfɔ alɛ, ‘Tandiki mi ninwuna!
Munko babi nii nfɛ bute, butɔɔsɛɛ leyo kafɔɔ kofokofoko.
Namasinfuo kafɔɔ okple ɔtaka mayɔ lɛsalɛsaa kuninwii nta fɔ.’ Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, se kuntɛ ɔlɔbataka ayɔ bloblo nwu nkpo aatɔɔ ta siɛwo nɔɔ ale ni oso, abataka an-yɔ lɛsaa lele niefĩ nwɔ antɔɔ, nse sinunsɔ diɛkpɛ nwɔ eekpee okyiini ayɛ ɔɔkaalɛ, ɔkaalɛ.
“Nkpo oso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ bikaalɛ Yaa asaa, abayɔ anta ye.
Biwolaa asaa, abata ye minnya.
Bipɛ nwɔ kokloo kɔnɛɛ, abasɛkɛtɛ anta ye.
Diekye otii lele niɛkaalɛ Yaa asaa, an-yɔ antɔɔ.
Otii lele niewolaa, antɔɔ anya.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niɛpɛ Yaa kokloo kɔnɛɛ, ansɛkɛtɛ antɔɔ.
“Aye ba ninle ni babi bate, nse obi lee lɛkaalɛ ye kakpaku, min-yɔ kɔsaanwu mintɔɔ?
Ee min-yɔ kakpakana mintɔɔ nse ɛɛkaalɛ ye lɛkɔɔkɔfuɔ?
Bia aye ba ninle ni bakpileblatɛ yi, biye mmle okle biayɔ asaa biene minta ni babi lee.
Ni lɛ oso nfɛ di Teeye wɔ ninkpe ni di osi ate ni klekle dilaayɔ Ninwuna Klekle ata batii ba niɛkaalɛ nwɔ ni alenkee!” Batii Bawo Lananfi Ɔlaa Di Yesu Ku Beelsebul Otumi Suoto.
Di obe onwii, Yesu latootososa ninwuna kpile ninwii ninanfuo ni ɔkakatɛ di otii onwii kamɛ.
Obe wɔ di ninwuna nwu ladie ni di otii nwu kamɛ, aakyako ɔkakatɛ.
Lɛsaa le mmle labla batii ba niayila ni ninfa ɔkpɛ.
Kafɔɔ batii bawo labuɛ alɛ, “Anwuna kpile ɔka wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Beelsebul niɛtɔɔ otumi nwu nkpo ootososa nya andiki.” Batii bawo kafɔɔ lamiɛ alɛ bɔɔkyɔɔ Yesu okũ, nioso baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, abla lɛsaa le niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ, diatuo alɛ Yaa nfũ eekye ni.
Kafɔɔ Yesu latofo lɛsaa le bakle ni di disibu lɛma kamɛ.
Nkpo oso aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kale ka niɛsɛ ni suoto akudi akudi kɔɔkpɛko ni suoto, ninyila diidii.
Leyo le kafɔɔ niɛsɛ suoto bɛɛtaka bayɛ ni baawo suoto mbiɛ.
Nkpo oso nse Satana sɛka kalekɔ lɛsɛ suoto akudi akudi bɔɔkpɛko bawo, lɛ sɛɛka kalekɔ lɛma nwu mayila?
Biobuɛ bilɛ kotososa anwuna kpile diekye Beelsebul niɛtɛɛ otumi fiɛ kɔbla nkpo.
Ni nse Beelsebul suoto kofe ntososa nya, ni owe suoto baatikankotɛ lee mma, baafe baatososa anwuna kpile baadiki baatii kamɛ?
Aye bamu batikankotɛ lee kodiki mantuo alɛ ole ye nnaa.
Oowo!
Kafɔɔ Yaa otumi kamɛ kotososa anwuna kpile ndiki.
Nle mmle kotuo kafɔɔ klekle alɛ, Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ntɔɔwa ye kamɛ kofokofoko.
“Nse sientɛ owo lɛyɔ akpɛsaa nɔɔ amuu ɛɛkpakũ ayɛ oonyu leyo nɔɔ yi, lɛsalɛsaa nɔɔ kuninwii nin-yu.
Kafɔɔ nse otii wɔ ninkpe ni osie alenke nwɔ ni lɛbakpɛ ko nwɔ eelenkee nwɔ, anklee akpɛsaa nɔɔ ya suoto eetika ni disi anfũ di nnɛɛ nɔɔ, lenkeetɛ nwu n-yɔ asaa ya beefũ nii mansɛ ku bawo nɔɔ.
“Otii lele ninan-yɛ mi kamaa, nwaako ɛɛtaka ayɛ mi di suoto.
Otii lele kafɔɔ ninankyakaakoe busiisa kamaa, ɔsamiisa ansamiisa.
Ninwuna Kpile Okple Ɔwa.
“Nse ninwuna kpile ledie di otii kamɛ, ninaakyɛ ninkyi aba ya niekoso nii ninmiɛ lɛba le diasiɛ nii.
Nse diɛwɛ lɛba kuninwii, ninmbuɛ alɛ, ‘Makple nsifi leyo nii le kamɛ ladie nii.’ Nkpo oso ninkple ninwa, ninmanya alɛ batoofiɛ leyo nwu kamɛ nimuu, bɛɛbla ni klekle.
Ta nkpo oso, ninkple ninsifi ninaakpaa anwuna kpile akuɛnsĩ ya ninkpe osie alenke nwɔ nii, manwa, mamayie mansiɛ di otii nwu kamɛ.
Di kayɛntɛkɔ, otii nwu nkpo nkpa be nfɛ ansiɛ ni, nlalaa ninlenkee nkpa kasale be aasiɛ nii.” Yesu Latuo Asaa Aakyeko Otii Wɔ Ninkpe Ni Suoto Lɛyɔɔ Nwaa Suoto.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu ntoobuɛ sɛlaa se mmle eeloo ni sɛmaa, ɔsanko onwii lafaa osie kanya baatii nwu kamɛ aabuɛ alɛ, “Suoto siyɔɔ ɔsanko wɔ nialakafɔ ni lɛmɛ aata fɔ lɛnyɛɛ, faanyɛɛfu ni!” Ninfɛ di Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Kafɔɔ batii ba nikonu ni Yaa ɔlaa, bɔɔbla nwu ni di suoto, di suoto siyɔɔ!” Yesu Lasĩ Alɛ Ɔlɔbabla Dituosaa Kuninwii Atuo.
Obe wɔ baatii dikudi labasi ni di Yesu ɔkyɛ, ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle ntɔɔlalaa lo!
Sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ bomiɛ alɛ banya, kafɔɔ blɔbanya dituosaa kuninwii dilenkee Yona lele le okle.
Fɛ mmle ke di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yona lale ni ɔtɛ onyu aata ni Niniwe batii, nkpo kafɔɔ di Otii Obi nwu male ɔtɛ onyu anta miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle nɛ.
Di lɛkankoyi suoto, ɔka sanko wɔ niakye ni kala kasɔ, mataka anyila ankanko miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle anlo ye lɛpɔɔ diekye aakye okpoo nɔɔ fanfa aawa alɛ ɔɔbanu Ɔka Salomo ninumbe asaa otuo.
Kafɔɔ kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii wɔ ninlenke ni Salomo nkpe ninfũ.
Niniwe batii mataka manyila di lɛkankoyi nwu kamɛ mankanko ye manlo ye lɛpɔɔ.
Diekye di obe wɔ di Yona latɔkɔ ma ni Yaa ɔlaa, baakyisa nkpa, baadiɛ sikpile lɛma ɔbla.
Kafɔɔ nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, otii onwii nsi ye kaamɛ ninfũ alenke ni Yona!
Yesu Ladiki Asaa Ya Ninta Ni Otii Lɛkpa Aatuo.
“Otii kuonwii ninsɔ kandiɛ ayɔ akookaa ee ayɔ lɛsaa atĩi nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ an-yɔ antika lɛsaa suoto, lɛɛba le dibakpa ninta ni batii ba nikobuo ni leyo.
Anu lɛfɔ nte fɛ kandiɛ diɛta suoto lɛfɔ simuu.
Nse anu lɛfɔ nlɛ, ni afɔ otii omuu fankpa, kafɔɔ nse anu lɛfɔ diɛlɛ, afɔ otii omuu fansiɛ di ditunu kamɛ.
Nkpo oso lolaa fanyu falɛ lɛkpa le ninsi fɔ ni kaamɛ dilaakple ditunu.
Nse lɛkpa leyii fɔ kamɛ, di lɛba lɛfɔ kuninwii diesi di ditunu kamɛ, ni afɔ otii omuu fabakpa fante klekle, fɛ mmle di kandiɛ nkpa ankpete ni di lɛsaa suoto ninkpa nii.” Yesu Lalo Farisi Batii Ku Kufiofa Batuotɛ Lɛpɔɔ.
Di obe wɔ di Yesu laloo ni lɛkakatɛ, Farisi otii onwii lalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ awa abaleko nwɔ alesaa leeyo.
Nioso aakyɛ alɛ ɔɔlaaleko nwɔ alesaa.
Diabla Farisi otii nwu ɔkpɛ obe wɔ aanya alɛ Yesu ditafoto kɔnɛɛ, di amanle lɛma kanya fiɛ aakyako ni alesaa ole.
Nkpo oso Saate nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Aye Farisi batii, minfoto sĩpũ ku abɛsibii lee kayi, kafɔɔ kamɛ lee leyii pɔ ku kayu kuɛ asaakuu ɔbla.
Biébe anu!
Diele Yaa wɔ niɛbla ni asaa nwu amuu kayi niɛbla kamɛ kafɔɔ?
Biyɔ lɛsaa biala ninsi di abɛsibii ku nkɔkɔɛ lee kamɛ bita bapiitɛ, ni lɛsaa lee biala makpa di afiofa lee kanya.
“Biyɔɔsa, aye Farisi batii!
Diekye min-yɔ alesaa lee lefosi le ku kɔba lee kamɛ sɛfa se nimpɛ ni ɔkɔnɔ nwaa ate ate minta Yaa.
Kafɔɔ biesĩ lɛbɛ ɔta di osuku kanya ku Yaa lɛbɔmbɔ.
Nle mmle dikpe ni biɛbla biɛkyakaa di n-ya biɔbla ni kofokofoko nɛ, dinaa alɛ biediɛ kuninwii biɛtɛ.
“Biyɔɔsa, aye Farisi batii!
Diekye mimbɔmbɔ nsiɛkɔ kplɛ osiɛ di nsiisakɔ lee, mimmiɛ kafɔɔ bilɛ batii batɔɔsɛɛsa ye ku dibu di akpaka.
“Biyɔɔsa, diekye bite fɛ sɛkya se mɔnɔɔnya nii, baatii nkyɛ sĩ ni di suoto, ta mananye ni oso.” Ninfɛ di kufiofa batuotɛ onwii lɛma latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, nse foobuɛ nkpo, ni footufa awo kafɔɔ nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Biyɔɔsa aye basaatuotɛ kafɔɔ.
Atoo ya baatii dilabafuo ni otuka, nnya minkpee min-yɔ mintukasa ma nɛ.
Minsunko ma nnɛɛ kafɔɔ bilɛ biɔkyakaako ma mantuka atoo nwu nkpo.
“Biyɔɔsa, diekye mimbla sɛkya biene minta Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yaa ɔlaa bauɛtɛtɛ ba mmle bawa lee nialo ma.
Aye bamu bitoofũ biekpee bilɛ, bieetuna di lɛsaa le baawa lee labla nii.
Diekye baalo Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nwu.
Ni di ayee bielolaa sɛkya lɛma nwu nɛ.
Nle mmle oso di Yaa ninumbe labuɛ alɛ, ‘Makyesee Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ ku batɔkyɛntɛ kaamɛ lɛma, kafɔɔ babalo bawo, mantikanko bayɛntɛle.’ Nkpo oso Yaa mananfi miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle bamuu laatoko di Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ ba bamuu batoolo ni diɛyɔ ni di kayi ka mmle kasɔ kakyekɔ.
Diayɔ ni di obe wɔ baalo Abel diɛlase ni di Sakaria wɔ baalo ni di oleɔta akyikye ku kakleklekɔ obo.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Yaa mananfi miɛ akyɛnfɔɔle laatoko, ta ɔsaabla wɔ mmle fɛɛ oso.
“Biyɔɔsa, aye kufiofa batuotɛ!
Diekye leyo le kamɛ ninumbe nte nii, biɛsɛɛ kayoko nɔɔ biediki saafĩi.
Diekye aye bamu biesĩ bilɛ biloobuo nii, biotĩi batii ba kafɔɔ nikomiɛ alɛ babuo ni osuku.” Obe wɔ di Yesu ladie ni ninfa, Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ lakyako Yesu suoto ɔlaa obuɛ ku ɔblɔ, Baakaalɛ nwɔ sɛlaa kpinwu di asaa ate ate suoto.
Diekye baatoomiɛ osuku wɔ suoto baafe mantika nwɔ ni ɔlaa di suoto alɛ ɛɛbla ni okpile.
Yesu Lasĩ Ɔlaa Aata Batii Ba Ninnyu Ni Batii Di Anu Mambla Ni Asaa.
Obe wɔ baatii nkpe nkpe bawo labasi ni dikudi, baakyako ni bia bawo ɔnanafũ, Yesu lakye kasɔ aatɔɔtɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu di Farisi batii mmɔle nyankale le suoto, dile ni sɛlaa kuafunu ɔsaabla lɛma.
Lɛsaa lele baatii lɛbla beekookaa, dibadie kayi klekle.
Ee owofalaa kuonwii nnaa alɛ blɔbanu ni diidii.
Nkpo oso ɔlaa lele biebuɛ diitunu kamɛ, kubadie kayi kakũ kpanamantãa.
Ɔlaa lele kafɔɔ biebuɛ sɛɛwɛɛwɛɛ leeyo kamɛ, kubadie kayi manyie nwu lɛkya lɛɛkpaka.
Biyɛkɛ Yaa, Diele Otii.
“Basiɛwo, kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bitanyɛkɛ batii ba ninlo ni suoto sina, ninni kamaa, lɛsalɛsaa nsinnaa ma babakple manfuo ni ɔbla.
Kamatuo ye otii wɔ biayɛkɛ nii, biyɛkɛ Yaa wɔ nse atoolo eeloo, eekple akpe ni osie an-yɔ anfuki ankpee ni di ɔtɔ wɔ nikofiɛ ni kunaa ni kaloo kamɛ.
Nwaako kɔtɔ ye nlɛ, nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ biayɛkɛ ni nɛ.
Diele mplɛ nnyɔ pɛ man-ya kutĩitĩi kɔnɔɔ?
Kafɔɔ Yaa ninyee kukanwii.
Bia disi lee sinwini yi, Yaa n-ye sĩ lɛpɔɔ.
Nkpo oso yi, bitanyɛkɛ.
Diekye biefũ kɔya bilenke kutĩitĩi.
Biyila Yesu Kamaa Fɛ Kafaabi Nɔɔ.
“Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, otii lele nimadiki ambuɛ baatii anu alɛ ole mi ale ami, Otii Obi nwu, kafɔɔ madiki mbuɛ di Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ anu nlɛ ole mi ale.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimasĩ mi ni di batii anu, ami, Otii Obi, kafɔɔ mansĩ nwɔ di Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ anu.
Otii lele nimabuɛ ɔlaa kpile owo anyila di Otii Obi nwu suoto, Yaa mayɔ ankyɛ nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimabuɛ ni ɔlaa kpile diɛ Ninwuna Klekle suoto, Yaa dilabayɔ akyɛ nwɔ.
“Nse bɛɛkpaa ye bɛɛkyɛnko Yuda batii nsiisakɔ ee banɔɔfo ku baka anu alɛ bɔɔkanko ye yi, bitambu diisi di ɔlaa wɔ bibabuɛ mindiki ni suoto kanya.
Diekye Yaa Ninwuna Klekle nimatuo ye ɔlaa wɔ biabuɛ ni di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Saawɛntɛ Buutɛ Onwii Suoto.
Osuɔtɔ onwii lasiɛ baatii dikudi nwu kamɛ, ni aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, tɔkɔ obiloo aasɛ atesaa ya di teewo lediɛ ɛɛtɛ ni aatɛɛ ale mi.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ, owe niɛtɛɛ osuku kakanko ee kasɛ atesaa lee nta batii lee banyɔ?” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ bamuu lɛma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu, di onumbɛbɛɛ lele suoto, diekye otii nkpa nwaa diesi di lɛsaawɛ le ninkpe nwɔ ni lɛɛpɔ kanya.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa le mmle alɛ, “Fekpɛntɛ saawɛntɛ onwii lawɛ, kaasɔ nɔɔ lalɛ ni alesaa osie kanya.
Nioso aabu diisi aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Lɛ mabla?
Diekye nnaa lɛba le mayɔ alesaa ya mmle ntɛ nii.
“ ‘Ninfɛ aabuɛ aatɔkɔ suoto alɛ, lɛsaa le kamabla ni ninle alɛ, kama biɛ alesaa katɛkɔ kofole nwu.
Nintofo lɛfɔle le niemuɔ dilenke nii.
Nfa matɛ alesaa ya lɛwɛ ni ku asaa bamba nɛ.
Ni kamatɔkɔ suoto nlɛ, disi nlɛ fɔ!
Fakpe asaa biene ya mmle amuu alɛɛ kpinwu.
Nioso tɛ ɔnyɛɛ, faale, faanyi, faale nkpa.’ “Kafɔɔ Yaa latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Afɔ buutɛ!
Miɛ kakyɛ ka mmle babafũ fɔ nkpa ninnɛɛ.
Ni owe nfɛ nimale asaa ya mmle fesiisa fɛɛtɛ fɛɛta ni suoto?’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɛntɛ alɛ, “Nkpo dibate ninta batii ba niesiisa asaa bɛɛta ni suoto kaasɔ ka mmle suoto nɛ, kafɔɔ banaa ni lɛsalɛsaa di Yaa anu nɛ.” Yaa Nnyu Babi Nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Nkpo oso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bitankpɛ sikitii di nle biale minsiɛ ni nkpa suoto ee nle biakpee ee minklee ni suoto.
Nkpa lefũ kɔya dilenke alesaa, nkpo kafɔɔ di suoto lefũ kɔya silenke akleesaa nɛ.
Binyu bakwakwalobi.
Mankpɛ kofe, manfiɛlɛ kafɔɔ.
Banaa alesaa katɛkɔ ee siwu, kafɔɔ Yaa nta ma alesaa!
Aye yi, biefũ kɔya bilenke bakansiɛ fanfanfa!
Owe nimafuo dii ninwii ɔyɔ ɔkyakaa ninkpa nɔɔ suoto, nse eebu nkpa nɔɔ disi osie kanya?
Ni, di obe wɔ minoofuo ni asaa pitipiti ɔbla, be oso biodiki suoto ninwuna di asaa bamba suoto?
“Binyu mmle okle di atoto leepoo kamɛ mmuɔ anlɛ ni onyu.
Ántaa oleteku ee aloso awu ata suoto.
Kafɔɔ kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ Ɔka Salomo omu, di lɛsaawɛ nɔɔ nimuu kamɛ, atakpee awu alɛ onyu awo lepoo kamɛ atoto kpeele ya mmle kaamɛ lɛma onwii.
Ni nse Yaa lekpee sɛfa se mmle okle ninkpe ni nkpa sekpeele miɛ, kɔɔsɛɛ babayɔ mankpee ni di ɔtɔ kamɛ sinfiɛ nii.
Ni Yaa nwu nkpo dilaanyuma ye ata ye akleesaa lee alenkee sɛfa nwu nkpo?
Ofũ onu lee diɛpɔ.
Nkpo oso bitankpɛ sikitii di nle bibale ku nle bibanyi ni suoto.
Bitambu kafɔɔ disi sikitii.
Diekye n-ya mmle di kayi batii bamuu ntikanko obe lele nɛ.
Teeye n-ye alɛ asaa ya mmle amuu lefĩ ye.
Kafɔɔ, biwolaa Yaa sɛka kalekɔ, ni abayɔ asaa ya mmle amuu anta ye.
Bitika Anu Di Yaa Kafa Lɛsaawɛ Suoto.
“Bafoso nii dikudi biibii, bitanyɛkɛ!
Diekye dilɛ Teeye alɛ ɔɔyɔ sɛka kalekɔ nɔɔ anta ye.
Biyɔ suoto lee asaa bisunsũ, biɛyɔ koto nwu bita bapiitɛ.
Biemiɛ kotontofo ko ninamalalaa ni bita suoto, biekookaa lɛsaawɛ lee di Yaa kafa ninfũ abate anta ye ni.
Diekye yu kuonwii dilabafuo ɔkyɛ ɔlaayɔ, bakunsũ kafɔɔ dilabafuo ɔkyɛ ɔlawee.
Diekye nfũ di lɛsaawɛ lɛfɔ nte nii, nfa kafɔɔ di otu lɛfɔ nwɛ nɛ.
Yesu Latɔkɔ Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Alɛ Basiɛ Batoonyu Osuku.
“Bilolaa suoto bita lɛsaa lele nimawa, biɛta bakandiɛ lee batɔɔkpa.
Bite fɛ batii ba nikonyu osuku manta ni saate lɛma alɛ, abakye ɔsanko kayɔkɔ anwa ni.
Nse ɛɛwa ɛbapɛ kokoloo kɔnɛɛ, nfanwu, baasɛkɛtɛ nwɔ.
Suoto mayɔɔ bakpɛmblatɛ ba di saate lɛma manya ma basi boonyu ni osuku nse eekple ɛɛwa!
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, abadiki awu antɛ ampɛ lɛtapo d iɔtɔ, antɔkɔ ma alɛ basiɛ kaasɔ, nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ anse ma opunu anta ma alesaa manle.
Nse nkyɛntɛɛ ee kolesɛtũ di saate nwu lɛwa, ɛɛbatũ ma basi boonyu osuku, suoto matɛ sinyɔɔ ma lo!
Biye bilɛ nse leyo saate matofo obe wɔ kamɛ di yu mawa amayu nwɔ nii, see atabatɔɔ osuku abiɛ nwɔ leyo abuo.
Nkpo oso ayee bisiɛ bitoonyu osuku, diekye ami, Otii Obi nwu, mawa di obe wɔ minoonyu osuku bitɛɛ nii.” Dikpe Nii Kpɛmblatɛ Nle Otii Wɔ Ninnu Ni Ɔlaa.
Ninfɛ di Petro lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, lɛkpa le mmle lete loo falaka ɛɛ, sɛɛ ku batii bamuu falaka?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Kpɛmblatɛ wɔ nimbla ni lɛsaa di osuku kanya, nnwɔɔ di saate nɔɔ n-yɔ anse di bakpɛmblatɛ bule kanya nɛ.
Nnwɔɔ nimata bakpɛmblatɛ bule alesaa fɛ mmle diesiɛko ni di obe biene kamɛ.
Babakusɛkusɛsa kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo nse saate nɔɔ lɛwa ɛba nyɔɔ ɔbla ɔkpɛ wɔ eekpee nwɔ ni ninnɛɛ!
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, saate nwu nkpo mayɔ kpɛmblatɛ nwu anse di asaa nɔɔ amuu kanya.
“Kafɔɔ nse kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Saate nii maklɛ di osuku nwu fiɛ abawa.’ Nkpo oso ɛɛkyako bakpɛmblatɛ bule ɔpɛ dile ni basanko ku basuɔtɔ, ɛɛkyako suoto lɛyɔɔ ɔnya, anle, anwee, annyi nta ansiɛ, saate nɔɔ nwu mawa di dii le ku obe wɔ kamɛ onoonyu osuku atɔɔ nii.
Saate nɔɔ nwu mananfi nwɔ kootoko osie kanya, antɔɔ kasiɛkɔ di batokopĩtɛ kamɛ.
“Kpɛmblatɛ wɔ ninye lɛsaa le di saate nɔɔ komiɛ alɛ abla atɔɔ ni fiɛ eesĩ ni ɔbla, ta áalolaa suoto alɛ ɔɔbla ni oso, lɛpɛ le mampɛ nwɔ ni mpɔ.
Kafɔɔ kpɛmblatɛ wɔ ninanye lɛsaa le di saate nɔɔ komiɛ alɛ abla nii, kafɔɔ ɛɛbla lɛsaa le baananfi nwɔ ni kootoko, letokonanfi nɔɔ kɛɛkɛɛ ninle.
Otii wɔ bɛɛta ni asaa kpinwu, nkpo okle kafɔɔ mamiɛ asaa kpinwu mankyeko ɔkyɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ beekple bɛɛta balenke nii, nkpo okle babafũ manlenkeesa di ɔkyɛ nɔɔ nɛ.
Batii Masɛ Suoto Ta Yesu Oso.
“Ɔtɔ lɛwa okpee kaasɔ ka mmle suoto, komiɛ kafɔɔ nlɛ kuakɛsɛɛ wla.
Yaa ntu okpeesa onwii nkpe babakpeesɛɛ nii.
Nioso ninwɛ onwu nwuna diɛlase di obe wɔ beekpeesɛɛ mi nii.
Bienyu bilɛ atoko ɔkyɛ ole lɛwako kayi ka mmle?
Oowo!
Diele atoko ɔkyɛ ole, kafɔɔ kasɛ.
Diɛyɔ ni nua diesifi nii, batii banɔɔ leeyo ninwii kamɛ ntɛɛ masɛ.
Batii batiɛ mataka manyila baanyɔ suoto, banyɔ bule kafɔɔ mataka manyila baatiɛ suoto.
Obi ote mataka anyila di obi suɔtɔbi suoto, obi suɔtɔbi kafɔɔ mataka anyila di ote suoto.
Obi ɔya mataka anyila di obi sankobi suoto, obi sankobi kafɔɔ mataka anyila di ɔya suoto.
Ɔmaato mataka anyila di obisɔfɔ suoto, obisɔfɔ kafɔɔ mataka anyila di ɔmaato suoto.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Aata Batii Mmle Baatofo Ni Obe Wɔ Kamɛ Basi Nii.
Yesu latɔkɔ batii nwu nkpo kafɔɔ alɛ, “Nse biɛnya alokonkyɛ di kufĩ kamɛɛkɔ, bilɛ kanto manɔɔ.
Ninwa kafɔɔ kanya.
Nse biɛnya kɔfɛɛfɔ kɔfɛ kunkye kala kasɔ, mimbuɛ bilɛ difila nfɛ kɔwa.
Ninwa kafɔɔ kaanya.
Aye balaatɛ!
Minfuo osi ku kasɔ onyu mintofo lɛsaa le nimawa ni mimbuɛ, ni be oso minoonu obe wɔ mmle kasɔ?
Yesu Latuo Mmle Okle Baatii Kalolaa Ni Bawo Ntɛɛ.
“Be oso minaabuo sɛɛla kamɛ bitofo lɛsaa biene le dikpe ni biɛbla ni?
Nse otii owo lɛlɛɛfɔ lɛka di bakantɛ nfũ, fe di osuku biala suoto bilolaa ɔlaa nwu bita baawo fiɛ biɛlaadu kakankɔ.
Nse diele nkpo, abayɔ fɔ ankpee di kantɛ nnɛɛ, kantɛ nwu n-yɔ fɔ ankpee di bamufũtɛ nnɛɛ mantɛfɔ leeyo.
Kɔta fɔ fantofo nlɛ, nfa fɔɔwa ɔbasiɛ yiɛlaase di obe wɔ fatɔɔta ni letokonanfi lɛfɔ koto yɛntɛle nɛ.”
Nse Biékyi Di Situ Kamɛ, Biɔwa Ɔbakpi Siikpile Letembi Nwu Kamɛ.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, batii bawo lawɛ ninfa latɔkɔ Yesu mmle di Pilato lalo ni Galilea batii bawo di obe wɔ baatɔɔta ole baatɔɔta ni Yaa.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Bienyu bilɛ mmle okle beelo ni Galilea batii ba mmle oso, mma ninle bakpileblatɛ balenke Galilea batii bamuu bule?
Oowo, diele nkpo kute!
Nioso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse biékyi di sikpile lee ɔbla kamɛ, nkpo okle di aye kafɔɔ biɔwa ɔbakpi nɛ.
Ni lefosi batii banɛ ba di Siloa leyo kplɛ nwu labiɛ diapɛ, baakpi ni mɔ?
Bienyu bilɛ, nle mmle oso, mma ninle bakpileblatɛ balenke batii ba bamuu ninkpe ni di Yerusalem?
Oowo, diele nkpo kute!
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse biékyi di sikpile lee suoto, nkpo kafɔɔ di bamuu lee biɔwa ɔbakpi nɛ.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Aakyeko Kolewoso Ko Ninootika Ni Abi Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lapɛ lɛkpa le mmle aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Obe onwii kamɛ, osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ, aasɔ kolewoso kunwii di kofe nɔɔ kamɛ.
Dii ninwii aakyɛ alɛ ɔɔlamiɛ kowoso nwu nkpo dibi, kafɔɔ, atawɛ kuninwii.
Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu latɔkɔ kofe nɔɔ nyuntɛ alɛ, ‘Nyu!
Alɛɛ atiɛ amu nkyɛ ni nfũ komiɛ ni kowoso ko mmle dibi nlɛ kɔtɛsɛ, kafɔɔ ninwɛ kuninwii.
Budi kũ fayu!
Diekye nɔɔnya lɛsaa le oso kuyɛ ni kaasɔ ka mmle suoto.’ “Kafɔɔ kofe nwu nkpo nyuntɛ labuɛ alɛ, ‘Saate, ta kukple kuyila lɛlɛɛ ninwii buonyu.
Kamakutu kũ kalɔ nkpete asaa ya nimata lɛba le kuyɛ ni n-yɔɔ ninsiɛ lɛla munnyu.
Ni nse lɛlɛɛ lekyi kuofuo abi otika kpinwu, ni kulɛ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nse kúofuo abi otika, ni faafuo kũ obudi oyu nfɛ.’ ” Yesu Layɔɔsa Ɔsanko Onwii Ninkpaa Lakpi Ni Ofiɛ Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi Suoto.
Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi ninwii suoto, Yesu latotuo asaa di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ kanwii kamɛ.
Ɔsanko onwii lawɛ ninfa di ninwuna kpile ninwii latɔkpɛko ni lefosi alɛɛ anɛ amu.
Ninwuna nwu nkpo lata alɛ, obe lele ɔsanko nwu nkpo lebo, ánfuo suoto oyilasa.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lanyɔɔ nii, aalɛɛ nwɔ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔsanko, ofiɛ lɛfɔ nwu ntɔɔyɔɔfɔ!” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɔ kɔnɛɛ aatika di ɔsanko nwu suoto nɛ.
Nfanwu, ɔsanko wɔ mmle niataka aayila wlɔlɔ, aakyako Yaa ɔtansa nɛ.
Yuda batii kasiisakɔ nwu nkpo ɔnɔɔfo lanya ɔblɔ osie kanya di mmle di Yesu layɔɔsa ni ofiɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi nwu oso.
Nkpo oso aatɔkɔ batii nwu nkpo alɛ, “Ayi akuɔ ninkpe wo mumbla ni sɛkpɛ.
Nkpo oso biwa di ayi nwu nkpo kamɛ baayɔɔsa ye sifiɛ, diele di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto!” Ninfɛ di Saate ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Aye balaatɛ!
Mindiki banankyue ku bapɔnkɔ lee di sikũ minkpama minkyɛnko ntu kanyinkɔ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto.
Binyu ɔsanko wɔ mmle ninle ni Abraham ɔnantii di Satana lenii ni lefosi alɛɛ anɛ amu.
Diɛlɛ alɛ baafukuti nwɔ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto?” Yesu sɛlaa se aabuɛ ni lata sinunsɔ lakpɛ balo nɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ batii bule lanya suoto lɛyɔɔ di sɛkpɛ kplɛ se simuu aabla ni oso.
Yesu Layɔ Yaa Sɛka Kalekɔ Aakaatɛɛsa Di Lewosobi Biibii Ninwii.
Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be lɛsaa di Yaa kafa nwu nkpo ledie?
Ote dite fɛ, otii niɛyɔ lewosobi biibii ninwii ɛɛpɛ di kofe nɔɔ.
Diakɔntɔ nii, diamuɔ, diɛbakple kowoso dibinte kunwii di bakansiɛ lɛbla ni ayo lɛma di sɛla nɔɔ suoto.” Yesu Layɔ Yaa Kafa Aakaatɛɛsa Di Lɛnyankasaa Suoto.
Yesu lakple aakaalɛ alɛ, “Be lɛsaa suoto mayɔ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkaatɛsa?
Ote dite fɛ ɔsanko onwii niɛyɔ lɛnyakasaa eekpee di bloblo nnaafũ kotofo kunwii bɛɛnwɔtɔ ni kamɛ diɛlase di obe wɔ di nnafũ nwu bɛɛnwɔtɔ ni lɛtaka nii.” Yesu Labuɛ Alɛ Nkpa Kayoko Nte Biibii.
Yesu lafe di sekpoo ku nkpayotũ kamɛ aatootuo batii asaa di obe wɔ aatoofe ni Yerusalem.
Nfanwu otii onwii lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Teete, batii ba nimawɛ ni didiki, basɛɛ babale ɛɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?” “Kpee okyiini faafe di kayoko biibii nwu kamɛ fabuo.
Diekye batii kpinwu mamiɛ alɛ boobuo osie kanya, kafɔɔ bɔlɔbafuo obuo.
Diekye obe kɔwa di leyo saate masɛɛ ni kayoko nwu nkpo.
Bibaka kaayi minkyako kokloo kɔnɛɛ ɔpɛ mimbuɛ bilɛ, ‘Teete, sɛkɛtɛ wo!’ “Kafɔɔ abatɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Ninye ye nfũ biekye nii!’ “Nfa nfɛ bibakyako obuɛ bilɛ, ‘Awo ku afɔ niale, buanyi, faatuo wo kafɔɔ asaa di okpoo loo le!’ “Kafɔɔ abakple antɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Ninye ye nfũ biekye nii!
Bikyɛ mi di ɔlɔɔkɔ bisifi, aye bakpileblatɛ!’ “Nfa nfɛ bibawi nku, minwee anyɛɛ, di obe wɔ bibanya Abraham ku Isak ku Yakob ku Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ bamuu nsi ni di Yaa kafa.
Kafɔɔ aye, babafuki ye man-yu kaayi alɛ bitambuo.
Batii makye kufĩ katunkɔ ku kamɛɛkɔ manwa.
Bawo nkye katoo ku kala kasɔ manwa mamasi di opunu katũ di Yaa kafa, manle, manyi.
Nioso batii ba ninle ni bayɛntɛle, mawa mamale bakasale.
Mba kafɔɔ ninle ni bakasale mawa mamale bayɛntɛle.” Yesu Lawɛ Lɛbɔmbɔ Aata Yerusalem.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ kafɔɔ, Farisi batii bawo lawa Yesu nfũ babatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Pɛsɛwa fadie ninfũ fasifi kakɔ bamba, diekye ɔka Herode komiɛ alɛ alo fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bikyɛ biɛlatɔkɔ ahia nwu nkpo bilɛ, ‘Miɛ, matososa anwuna kpile, kɔsɛɛ nnyɔɔsa bafiɛtɛ sifiɛ.
Di dii tiɛfa suoto, maloo ɔkpɛ nii.’ Kafɔɔ dikpe nii lɛkyɛ osuku miɛ ku kɔsɛɛ ku sakale.
Diekye diɛkaatɛ alɛ baalo Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ di lɛba bamba kuninwii ninanle ni Yerusalem okpoo kamɛ.
“O Yerusalem, Yerusalem, afɔ nialo Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ, faasafɔ batii ba kafɔɔ di Yaa lakpeefɔ ni ɔkyɛ aafuɔ faalo!
Obe kpinwu ntoomiɛ nlɛ kosiisa babi lɛfɔ di afoko nii kalɔ fɛ mmle okle di kɔɔkɔɔbiɔya nkpaa abi ankpee ni di afoko nɔɔ kalɔ, kafɔɔ floonu kasɔ.
Ta nle mmle oso, Yaa madiki okpoo wɔ mmle atoko manwɔɔsa nwu.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, biloosinwa mi ɔbanya diediki diɛlaase di obe wɔ biebuɛ bilɛ, ‘Yaa lekusɛkusɛsa otii wɔ nikɔwa ni di Saate leyooto kamɛ!’ ”
Yesu Lakple Aayɔɔsa Osuɔtɔ Onwii Ofiɛ Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi Suoto.
Di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi ninwii suoto, Yesu lakyɛ Farisi batii ɔnɔɔfo onwii leyo ninfũ baalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ abale ni alesaa.
Batii lawɛ ninfa baatɔɔtɛtɛɛ nwɔ osie kanya.
Osuɔtɔ onwii di nnɛɛ ku nkpaa lafufu ni lawa Yesu nfũ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ kufiofa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii alɛ, “Kufiofa loo lɛta wo osuku alɛ buayɔɔsa otii ofiɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto ɛɛ, sɛɛ kuɔta wo osuku?” Kafɔɔ batafuo kanya ɔbɛ obuɛ ɔlaa kuonwii.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lamufũ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo aayɔɔsa nwɔ ofiɛ, ni aatɔɔ aasifi nɛ.
Ninfɛ aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Nse onwii lee obi ee bɔkɛɛ nɔɔ lɛkpa eebuo di dibiɔ kamɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto, bilɔbadiki nwɔ dii nwu nkpo?” Kafɔɔ batafuo nwɔ ɔlaa nwu kanya odiki.
Yesu Labuɛ Mmle Baawakosa Ni Suoto Kasɔ Ku Mmle Baafũ Ni Bafɔɔ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lanya mmle di batii ba baakyakako ni latoodiki ni nsiɛkɔ kplɛ, ninfɛ aapɛ ma lɛkpa ninwii alɛ, “Nse otii owo lɛkyakako fɔ ɛɛwako ɔsanko nɔɔ kayɔkɔ yi, tansiɛ di kasiɛkɔ kplɛ.
Diekye dibafuo ɔwa alɛ bɛɛkyakako otii wɔ niɛtaka katoo alenke fɔ ni ninfa.
Ni otii wɔ niɛkyakako ni batii lee banyɔ mawa amatɔkɔ fɔ alɛ, ‘Taka faata otii wɔ mmle abasiɛ ninfa.’ Nioso fabataka fanaasiɛ di lɛba yɛntɛle ku sinunsɔ.
Nkpo oso nse bɛɛkyakako fɔ bɛɛwako lɛba yi, kyɛ faalaasiɛ di kasiɛkɔ yɛntɛle.
Nse otii wɔ niɛkyakako fɔ ni lɛwa yi, ni abatɔkɔ fɔ alɛ, ‘Siɛwo nii, taka ninfa, fabasiɛ di kasiɛkɔ kplɛ’ Nle mmle matakatɛsa fɔ katoo di batii ba bamuu bɛɛkyakako bɛɛwako ni ninfa anu.
Diekye otii lele niɛtakatɛsa suoto katoo, Yaa mawakosa nwɔ kasɔ.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niɛwakosa suoto kasɔ, Yaa matakatɛsa nwɔ katoo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ otii wɔ niakyakako nwɔ alɛ abale ni alesaa alɛ, “Nse fɔɔkyakako batii falɛ bawa babale alesaa yi, tanlɛɛ basiɛwo ee babilee ee banantii lɛfɔ ee basaawɛntɛ wo lɛfɔ lete.
Ta mmle di mma kafɔɔ baalɛɛ fɔ alɛ wa fabaleko ma ni oso.
Ni se dite nkpo, ni tofo falɛ lɛsaa le fɛɛbla fɛɛta ni koto nfɛ bɔɔta manta fɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nse foole dii le mmle okle yi, faalɛɛ bapiitɛ, ku batii ba ninoofuo ni ɔkyɛ nwaa, ku abafa ku banumbiɛtɛ.
Nle mmle mata alɛ Yaa mawii fɔ lɛyɔɔ.
Diekye batii ba mmle okle dilɔbafuo fɔ lɛsalɛsaa ɔbla ɔta.
Yaa nimata fɔ koto di dii le baatii biene makple mantaka mankye ni bakpi kamɛ.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Yaa Kafa Opunu Kplɛ Suoto.
Obe wɔ baatii ba niasiɛ ni di opunu katũ onwii lɛma lanu ni sɛlaa se mmle, aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Suoto matɛ sinyɔɔ batii ba nimale ni alesaa di Yaa kafa nwu nkpo osie kanya.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Di obe onwii kamɛ, osuɔtɔ onwii latũ opunu kplɛ, ni aakyakako batii kpinwu aawako alesaa nwu kalekɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di alesaa nwu olebee ntoowo nii, aakpee batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ alɛ balaatɔkɔ batii ba aakyakako ni alɛ bawa.
Diekye lɛsaa biala ntoosi!
“Kafɔɔ bamuu lɛma baakyako osuku ɔkaalɛ onwii onwii.
Otii kasale latɔkɔ tɔkyɛntɛ nwu alɛ, ‘Lɛya kasɔ kanwii, nioso kɔkyɛ nnaanyu ka.’ Nkpo oso laatɔkɔ nwɔ falɛ, ‘Lekoto, namafuo ɔwa.’ “Ɔbamba kafɔɔ alɛ, ‘Lɛya banankyue banyɔ banyɔ akyuu anɔɔ.
Osuku nfɛ n-yɛ kafɔɔ kofe ma ɔsɔ onyu nse balɛ nɛ.
Nle mmle oso, laatɔkɔ nwɔ falɛ, “Lekoto, namafuo ɔwa.” ’ “Ɔbamba kafɔɔ alɛ, ‘Nunua wɔ mmle ntɔɔyɔ ɔsanko nɛ, nkposo namafuo ɔwa.’ “Tɔkyɛntɛ nwu nkpo lakple aakyɛ aalaatɔkɔ saate nɔɔ sɛlaa se mmle simuu.
Saate nɔɔ nwu lanya ɔblɔ osie kanya ni aatɔkɔ tɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ alɛ, ‘Pɛsɛwa fatɔɔkyɛ okpoo sisuku ku akpaka faalaalɛɛ bapiitɛ ku batii ba ninoofuo ni ɔkyɛ nwaa ku banumbiɛtɛ ku abafa fawako.’ “Ditaklɛ tɔkyɛntɛ nwu nkpo lakyɛ aakple aabatɔkɔ saate nɔɔ alɛ ntɔlaabla nkpo, kafɔɔ kasiɛkɔ lekple keebu.
Nkpo oso saate nwu latɔkɔ tɔkyɛntɛ nwu alɛ, ‘Tɔɔkyɛ sekpoo kplɛ sisuku ku sibiibii suoto faakpee batii bamuu osie faakpaa ma fawako alɛ leyo nii kamɛ kayii.
Kɔtɔkɔ ye ntikiti nlɛ batii ba bamuu lɛlɛɛ ni fiɛ beesĩ ni ɔwa, kuonwii lɛma dilabatu alesaa nii ya mmle anyu!’ ” Fabawɛ Dibuo Nse Fale Yesu Saateketetɛ.
Di obe onwii kamɛ baatii dikudi ninwii ku Yesu latɔɔkyɛ nii, ni aamunikĩi aatɔkɔ ma lɛ, “Otii lele niɛwa ɔkyɛ nii, anambɔmbɔ mi alenkee ote ku ɔya, ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ ku babi, babilɛma sankobi ku basuɔtɔbi ku nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ suoto yi, ɔlɔbafuo mi saateketetɛ ole.
Otii lele ninan-yɔ atoo nɔɔ atuka atikankoe di nkpaamaa, ɔlɔbafuo mi saateketetɛ ole.
“Nse otii lee owo komiɛ alɛ atofo leyo kplɛ lewo, lɛkasale ansiɛ kaasɔ ambu asaa ya nimafĩ ni leeyo nwu otofo kamɛ.
Ambu koto ko ninte nwɔ nii, nse kubawo antofo fiɛ ankye kasɔ.
Nse aabla nkpo, fiɛ ɛɛlaase lɛsɔse, ɔlɔbafuo leyo nwu otofo oloo.
Batii ba bamuu nimanya ni leyo nwu siyiɛkuu mananloo ni otofo makyako leyo tofotɛ nwu ɔma alɛ, ‘Otii wɔ mmle lekye leyo kasɔ, kafɔɔ aaloo otofo.’ “Nse ɔka owo nkle bakpɛtɛ nkpe lefosi oofe ɔka wo nɔɔ wɔ ninkle ni bakpɛtɛ nkpe afosi anyɔ ɔkpɛ ko, abasiɛ ambu diisi nse osie wɔ ninkpe nwɔ ni, abafuo ɔka nwu ɔkpɛ ko.
Ni nse ɛɛnya alɛ ɔlɔbafuo ɔkɔ nwu osie oyilako, abakyesee batii, manaakyakako ɔka nwu nkpo, di obe wɔ anayitɛɛtɛɛ ma nii, mantikiti nwɔ lekoto, mankaalɛ onwii ɔbla.” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu layɛntɛ ɔlaa nɔɔ obuɛ ɔtɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nkpo okle di aye kafɔɔ bilaafuo mi basaateketetɛ ole, diediki biediɛ lɛsaa biala biɛtɛ nɛ.
Mba Be Ninnaa Ni Ɔmɛnɛfɛ, Man-yɔ Mi Manwii.
“Mba nlɛ.
Kafɔɔ nse ditooyu ɔmɛnɛfɛ ni mi, lɛsalɛsa nsinnaa baakple man-yɔ mankpee mi ni ɔmɛnɛfɛ.
Diesinlɛ dita bia kasɔ, ee bia lefleku, owii nfɛ man-yɔ manwii.
“Nkpo oso aye ba kuunutoko nkpɛ nii binu!”
Baanya Lefosobi Le Niayu Nii.
Dii ninwii akpooto bafuntɛ ku bakpileblatɛ lawa Yesu nfũ babanu nwɔ ɔlaa.
Ninfa, Farisi batii ku kufiofa batuotɛ lakye kasɔ baatɔɔkakatɛ nwɔ di suoto alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lefũ bakpileblatɛ, anle bia alesaa ku mma!” Nkpo oso Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa alɛ, “Nse diɛwa alɛ onwii lee nkpe bafoso kɔlafa, di onwii leyu kaamɛ, ɔlɔbadiɛ bafoso afosi anaasĩ banaasĩ nwu nkpo di alesaa kalekɔ alaawolaa onwii wɔ nieyu ni, diɛlaase di obe wɔ ɛɛnyɔɔ ni?
Ni nse ɛɛnyɔɔ, suoto dilabayɔɔ nwɔ osie kanya akɛnkɛ nwɔ atika di nimuusi.
Akpaa nwɔ awako leyo.
Abalɛɛ basiɛwo nɔɔ ku leyo nɔɔ batii ansiisa antɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Suoto kɔtɛ sinyɔɔ mi osie kanya, diekye ntɔɔnya foso nii nwu niayu nii.
Biwa biɛbanyakoe suoto lɛyɔɔ!’ Nioso kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ nkpo kafɔɔ di suoto lɛyɔɔ kplɛ mawɛ di Yaa kafa, nse kpileblatɛ onwii lekyi, ninlenkee babienetɛ afosi anaasĩ batii banaasĩ ba kaakyi diefĩ ni nɛ.
Baanya Koto Fututu Ko Niayu Nii “Ee nse koto fututu lefosi nkpe ɔsanko owo, eeyu kunwii, lɛ ambla?
Ansɔ kandiɛ anse, anfiɛ leyo nɔɔ kamɛ anwolaa kũ nwaa ninaase di obe wɔ ɛɛnya kũ nii.
Nse ɛɛnya kũ, anlɛɛ bawo nɔɔ ku leyo nɔɔ batii ansiisa, antɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Suoto kɔtɛ sinyɔɔ mi osie kanya, diekye ntɔɔnya koto nii nwu niayu nii, bibanyakoe suoto lɛyɔɔ.’ Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nkpo okle kafɔɔ di Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ nnya suoto lɛyɔɔ di kpileblatɛ onwii wɔ niekyi ni suoto nɛ.” Obi Wɔ Niayu Ni Lakple Aawa Ote Nfũ.
Yesu lakple abuɛ akyakaa alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ, aawa babi suɔtɔbi banyɔ banwii.
Ninfɛ di obisɔnle latɔkɔ ote alɛ, ‘Teete, yɔ kalekɔ nii ka fabatɛɛ ni di asaa lɛfɔ kamɛ fatɛɛ ninua.’ Nkpo oso osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo layɔ asaa nɔɔ aasɛ aata babi nwu nkpo banyɔ.
“Di ayi awo kamaa, obisɔnle nwu nkpo layɔ asaa nɔɔ nwu amuu aasunsũ aafũ koto aadie leeyo, aasifi kale bamba fanfanfa.
Aalaasiɛ nkpa lɛlaale, aalalaasa koto nɔɔ nwu kumuu.
Obe wɔ aale koto nɔɔ nwu kumuu kualoo nii, ditaklɛ, kɔka kplɛ kunwii labakpɛ kaasɔ nwu nkpo suoto.
Aabakple piitɛ, nle aale ni lawɛ nwɔ osie.
Nioso aayɔ suoto aalaakpee awoba di osuɔtɔ onwii nfũ di kasɔ nwu suoto.
Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu lakpaa nwɔ aasifiko kakpayotũ nɔɔ alɛ, alaatoonyu nwɔ aplakuo nɛ.
Kɔka oso, aamiɛ alɛ se aatoole aplakuo nwu alesaa awo, kafɔɔ kuonwii ditatɔɔ osuku alɛ ale.
“Nioso, osuɔtɔbi nwu lababuo di suoto nɔɔ kamɛ aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Batii ba di teemi lefũ bɔɔbla sɛkpɛ mantɔɔ nii, alesaa diefĩ ma, boole mammiɛ.
Ni di mi nsi ninfũ kɔka kolo mi nɛ!
Makple nsifi teemi nfũ nnaatɔkɔ nwɔ nlɛ, “Teete, lɛbla okpile leyila di Yaa ku afɔ suoto.
Ninsinsiɛko alɛ faalɛɛ mi alɛ obi lɛfɔ.
Kafɔɔ yɔ mi fabla fɛle bakpɛmblatɛ lɛfɔ onwii lɛma feefũ ni.” ’ Nfanwu ni aataka aayɔ asaa aayefe osuku aatoofe ote nfũ nɛ.
“Obe wɔ akyɛ di osuku fanfa ɔɔwa nii, ni di ote lanyɔɔ nɛ.
Ɔlaa nɔɔ lakpɛ ote nyaami.
Ni aatoso aakyɛ aalaaminiko nwɔ ku suoto lɛyɔɔ nɛ.
“Ninfɛ di obi labuɛ alɛ, ‘Teete, lɛbla okpile leyila di Yaa ku afɔ suoto.
Ninsinsiɛko alɛ faalɛɛ mi falɛ obi lɛfɔ!’ “Kafɔɔ, ote latɔkɔ bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ alɛ, ‘Bipɛsɛwa!
Biɛyɔ awu biene anwii bibakpee nwɔ.
Biɛyɔ lɛkɔnii ku ntokota biene bibakpee nwɔ.
Nle mmle kamaa, biɛkyɛ bilaamufũ nankyue wɔ ninsi ni lɛla bilo biɛwa alesaa, buɔnya suoto lɛyɔɔ.
Diekye obi nii wɔ mmle, buɔyɔ fɛ aakpi.
Kafɔɔ atookple ɛɛsɛnkɛ.
Aayu, kafɔɔ butookple buɔnyɔɔ.’ Nioso, baakyako suoto lɛyɔɔ ɔnya.
“Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, obi nɔɔ nɔɔfo lafe kofe.
Obe wɔ atookye kofe ɔɔwa nfɛ ɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni leyo, aanu sinu ku katũ kanya osie kanya.
Nioso, aalɛɛ kpɛmblatɛ onwii, ni aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Be ninkpe leeyo?’ Ninfɛ di kpɛmblatɛ nwu ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Obilee nintookple ɛɛwa, ni di teefɔ lɛta beelo nankyue wɔ ninsi ni lɛla nɛ, diekye atookple ɛɛwa buɛɛ okpile kuonwii dietũ nwɔ.’ “Nkpo oso obi nɔɔfole nwu lanya ɔblɔ osie kanya alɛ, oloosinkyɛ leyo.
Ta nkpo oso, ote ladie aakyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ aalaatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ awa baasifi leyo.
Kafɔɔ obi nwu lamunikĩi aakaalɛ ote alɛ, ‘Nyu lo!
Ntɔɔbla ɔkpɛ lɛta fɔ alɛɛ ya kpe fɛ ɔlanle.
Diidii kafɔɔ ninsĩ fɔ ɔlaa onu.
Obe fatɔɔbla fɛɛtɛɛ ami?
Diidii bia tie, fayitɛɛ falɛ nnya suoto lɛyɔɔ ku bawo nii.
Kafɔɔ obi lɛfɔ wɔ mmle nintɔɔlalaasa fɔ ni asaa ku basanko basɔnɔkpeetɛ lekple ɛɛwa nii, fatoolo nankyue wɔ ninsi ni lɛla fɛɛtɔɔ nnwɔɔ!’ “Ninfɛ di ote latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Obi nii, munkofɔ ninsi ninfũ obe lele, lɛsaa lele kafɔɔ ninkpe mi, lele fɔ dile.
Kafɔɔ, dikpe nii munya suoto lɛyɔɔ, mumpɔ.
Diekye buɔyɔ bulɛ okpi di obilee lakpi, ni eekple ɛɛsɛnkɛ nɛ.
Oyu aayu ni buokple buɔnyɔɔ nɛ.’ ”
Asaa Nyuntɛ Onwii Ditatɔɔbla Asaa Di Osuku Kanya.
Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ, aale saawɛntɛ.
Aawɛ kpɛmblatɛ onwii niatoonyu nwɔ ni asaa.
Ni baabatɔkɔ saawɛntɛ nwu nkpo alɛ, asaa nyuntɛ nɔɔ kole nwɔ kote.
Nkpo oso saawɛntɛ wɔ mmle lalɛɛ saanyuntɛ nwu nkpo aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Be lɛsaa ninle nle konu nkyeko ni suoto lɛfɔ nkpo?
Babla nkuntaa di asaa nii ya amuu foonyu ni suoto fatɛɛ.
Diekye flabasinfuo mi asaa nyuntɛ ole.’ “Ninfɛ di kpɛmblatɛ nwu latɔkɔ suoto alɛ, ‘Saate nii nfɛ madiɛ mi di ɔkpɛ kamɛ.
Lɛ nfɛ mabla?
Nnaa osie kafɔɔ makpɛ ni kofe.
Asaa ɔkaalɛ kafɔɔ nkpɛ mi sinunsɔ.
Ahaa!
Nfɛ n-ye lɛsaa le mabla nii!
Ni nse ɔkpɛ nii lɛba die mi di nnɛɛ, baasiɛwo nii matoofũ mi ni laayo lɛma, mantoonyu mi ni kanya.’ “Nkpo oso aalɛɛ batii ba ninsiko ni saate nɔɔ koto onwii onwii.
Ni aakaalɛ ɔkasale alɛ, ‘Lɛ fasiko saate nii?’ “Ninfɛ di totɛ nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Nsiko nwɔ nnɔfɔ ataase kɔlafa.’ “Ni di saanyuntɛ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Nya koto lɛfɔ kukũ ninfũ.
Siɛ kaasɔ, faakpana falɛ afosi anɔɔ pɛ niebu.’ “Ninfɛ aakaalɛ ɔnyɔɔfa alɛ, ‘Ni afɔ mɔ?
Lɛ koto fasiko?’ “Ninfɛ di nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Diɛbla atitabi atofo kɔlafa.’ “Ninfɛ di saanyuntɛ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Nya kukũ lɛfɔ ninfũ.
Kpana afosi anɛ.’ “Nle mmle oso, saate nwu nkpo latansa saanyuntɛ nwu ninambla ni asaa di osuku kanya alɛ eebe anu.
Nwaako, batii ba ninsi ni kaayi lebe anu di kayi asaa ɔbla suoto balenke batii ba ninsi ni di Yaa kafa lɛkpa kamɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aabuɛ aakyakaa alɛ, “Aye biyɔ kayi asaa ɔwɛ bikyakaako batii.
Nse nnya nkpo ntɔɔbafe yi, Yaa mafũ ye di kafa nɔɔ ka ninnaa ni kaloo.
“Otii lele nielolaa asaa ya ninle ni abiibii eenyu di osuku kanya, abafuo akplɛ kafɔɔ onyu di osuku kanya.
Otii lele ninanlolaa asaa ya ninle ni abiibii anyu di osuku kanya, ɔlɔbafuo n-ya ninle kplɛ kafɔɔ onyu di osuku kanya.
Ni nse biloofuo kayi ka mmle asaa ololaa oklee di osuku kanya, ni lɛ nfɛ di otii mafuo ye ofũ onu alɛ biafuo ninwuna kamɛ asaa ya di Yaa lɛta ye ni oklee di osuku kanya?
Ni nse biloofuo otii bamba lɛsaa onyu di osuku kanya, ni lɛ nfɛ dibabla fiɛ baayɔ nle ninle ye ni lele manta ye?
“Kpɛmblatɛ kuonwii dilaafuo basaate banyɔ sɛkpɛ ɔbla.
Diekye abasĩ onwii ambɔmbɔ onwii.
Ee abakyɔɔ onwii ɔlaa kotoko, ansĩ onwii kotoko ɔkyɔɔ.
Flɔbafuo Yaa ku lɛsaawɛ ɔkpɛ ɔbla ɔkpɔtɔɔsa.” Yesu Latuo Asaa Bamba Kafɔɔ.
Obe wɔ di Farisi batii lanu ni sɛlaa se di Yesu labuɛ nii, baama nwɔ diekye baabɔmbɔ koto osie kanya.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye ninle mba ninta ni suoto lɛbɛ di batii anu nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yaa n-ye ye situ kamɛ.
Diekye asaa ya niefũ ni kɔya di batii anu yi, diedie lɛsalɛsaa di Yaa anu.
“Mose kufiofa ku Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ asaa ya bɛɛkpana bɛɛtɛ nii, labla ɔkpɛ dialaase di Ntu Kpeesatɛ Yohane obe.
Diɛyɔ ni di obe nwu kamɛ, ni bɛɛkyako Yaa sɛka kalekɔ ɔlaa biene nwu obuɛ nɛ.
Otii biala kɔkpɛ ku okyiini ambuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ, diɛtɛ diɛyɔɔ alɛ osi ku kasɔ kafe, ninlenkee alɛ Mose kufiofa kabɛfɛɛ kadie kaamɛ alɛ baabla.
“Osuɔtɔ lele niesĩ ɔsɔfɔ ɛɛlaayɔ ɔsanko bamba, ntookpee asɔnɔ.
Osuɔtɔ wɔ kafɔɔ nimayɔ ni ɔsanko wɔ beesĩ ni, ntookpee asɔnɔ.
Yesu Labuɛ Saawɛntɛ Onwii Ku Lasaro Suoto Ɔlaa.
“Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ, aale saawɛntɛ.
Obe lele ankpee asaa ya niefũ ni kɔya.
Aasiɛ nkpa obe lele di suoto lɛyɔɔ kamɛ.
Piitɛ onwii kafɔɔ lawɛ baatɔɔlɛɛ nwɔ ni Lasaro.
Nkɔ latitika nwɔ di suoto kpinwu.
Nioso mankpaa nwɔ manasiɛsa di saawɛntɛ nwu koyokontũ.
Antoonyu osuku alɛ nse saawɛntɛ nwu nkpo kole alesaa yi, kɔbɛfɛɛ ko nikɔkpa kumpɛ ni kaasɔ aayɔ anle.
Baweewee bia ninwa mamatɔɔya nwɔ nkɔ.
“Piitɛ nwu nkpo labakpi, Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ labakpaa nwɔ baasifiko Abraham nkpaatũ di Yaa kafa baatɔɔnya suoto lɛyɔɔ.
Saawɛntɛ nwu kafɔɔ labakpi baakookaa nwɔ.
Di bakpi kamɛ ninfa, obe wɔ asi ni diibuo kamɛ, aatakatɛsa anu aanyu osi.
Ni aanya Abraham fanfanfa di osi nɛ.
Lasaro lasiɛ nwɔ di nkpaatũ.
Nfanwu saawɛntɛ nwu lalɛɛ osie kanya alɛ, ‘Teete Abraham!
Nyɛɛ nyaami, faata Lasaro ayɔ lɛnɛɛ nɔɔ alaanyɔ nintu nwo kamɛ abalɛsɛsa di ɔkplalomii nii suoto diɛyɔɔ mi kɛɛkɛ.
Diekye kofiɛ di ɔtɔ wɔ mmle kamɛ!’ “Kafɔɔ Abraham latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Obi nii, nyuma falɛ di nkpa lɛfɔ kamɛ, asaa biene lete faafũ.
Lasaro nnwɔɔ yi, asaa kpile lete aafũ.
Kafɔɔ nunua yi, nfɛ ɔɔnya suoto lɛyɔɔ ninfũ, kafɔɔ afɔ fasi diibuo kamɛ.
Diɛkyakaa nii kafɔɔ yi, dibiɔ kplɛ ninwii nte di awo ku afɔ ntɛɛ.
Nse otii owo komiɛ alɛ ataalɛ awa nfa, ɔlɔbafuo.
Nkpo kafɔɔ di otii kuonwii dilɔbafuo okye ninfa ɔtaalɛ ɔwa ɔkyɛ loo nɛ.’ “Nfa nfɛ di saawɛntɛ latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Teete Abraham, kotikiti fɔ lekoto nlɛ kpee Lasaro aakyɛ teemi leyo.
Nkpe babilɛma suɔtɔbi, banɔɔ ninfa.
Aalaakpee ma kufiofa osie kanya alɛ balaawa lɛba le mmle di dibuo nkpe ni.’ “Ninfɛ di Abraham latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Mose ku Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ nkpe di babilee suɔtɔbi nfũ.
Dikpe ni mankyɔɔ ma ɔlaa wɔ boobuɛ ni atoko.’ “Kafɔɔ saawɛntɛ nwu lakple aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Teete Abraham, blɔbanu ma ɔlaa!
Kafɔɔ nse otii owo lɛtaka eekye bakpi kamɛ, ɛɛkyɛ ɛɛlaatɔkɔ ma yi, babanu nwɔ ɔlaa mankyi siikpile lɛma kamɛ.’ “Kafɔɔ Abraham lakple aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Nse blɔbanu Mose ku Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ ɔlaa kamaa, nse otii lɛtaka eekye bakpi kamɛ kafɔɔ ɛɛkyɛ ɔkyɛ lɛma yi, blɔbanu nwɔ ɔlaa!’ ”
Bitanta Otii Labla Okpile Ta Aye Oso.
Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Asaa ya nimakpaa otii ankpee ni di okpile kamɛ mawa kokooko.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ suoto abafe anwa nii, ayɔɔsa!
Nse bɛɛyɔ kukuɔ beenii bɛɛsakasa nwɔ siimu, bɛɛyɔ nwɔ beefuki beekpee di lekpo kamɛ, ditabalɛ nwɔ ninleenkee alɛ aata babisɔ ba mmle onwii lɛma mbla okpile.
“Nse obilee lɛbla okpile yi, faasĩ ɔlaa fatɔɔ.
Nse eekyi di otu kamɛ, eetikiti lekoto, faayɔ fakyɛ nwɔ.
Nkpo oso bilolaa binyu nwaa di lɛsaa lele biɔɔbla.
Nse ɛɛbla fɔ okpile sikuɛnsĩ, di dii ninwii kamɛ, eekple ɛɛwafɔ ɔkyɛ di sikuɛnsĩ nwu nkpo kamɛ, ɛɛbatikiti fɔ lekoto, faayɔ fakyɛ nwɔ.” Baatikiti Yesu Lekoto Alɛ Ata Ofũ Onu Lɛma Kupɔ.
Yesu batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ latikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, “Saate, ta ofũ onu loo kupɔ.” Ninfɛ di Saate nwu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nse bikpe ofũ onu fɛ sɛfá dibi, biafuo kowoso ko mmle ɔtɔkɔ bilɛ sifi suoto ninfũ mmle, ‘Falaasɔ suoto di lekpo kamɛ,’ ku babla ninkpo.
Yesu Labuɛ Mmle Okle Di Kpɛmblatɛ Biene Mbla Ni Ɔkpɛ.
“Biyɔ bilɛ onwii lee nkpe kpɛmblatɛ wɔ nikɔkpɛ nwɔ ni kofe, ee oonyu nwɔ ni bafoso.
Nse eeyie koofe, bibatɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ, pɛsɛwa fabasiɛ kaasɔ faale alesaa lɛfɔ?
Oowo!
Kafɔɔ bibatɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ, ‘Lolaa suoto faakpee awu, faawa alesaa, faatɛɛ ale mi nle, ninyi nloo fiɛ faalaale, ale fɔ.’ Nse kpɛmblatɛ nwu lɛkyɔɔ saate nɔɔ kotoko, kyinkyinaa dile alɛ saate nwu lɛpɛ kpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ nwu sɛfa?
Nkpo kafɔɔ ayee, nse bitooloo sɛkpɛ lee se bɛɛta ye alɛ biabla nii, biabuɛ bilɛ, ‘Awo, bakpɛmblatɛ ba ninandie ni lɛsalɛsaa ko bule.
Lɛsaa le dikpe ni buɔbla nii, nni butɔɔbla nɛ.’ ” Yesu Layɔɔsa Basuɔtɔ Lefosi Bawo Ofiɛ Sɛɛle.
Obe wɔ di Yesu latoofe ni Yerusalem, aafe di Samaria ku Galilea kɔmɛ suoto.
Aatoofe kaakpaayotũ kanwii kamɛ, ni aakyakako basuɔtɔ lefosi bawo niatoofiɛ ni ofiɛ sɛɛle nɛ.
Baayila fanfa.
Ni baafaa osie kanya baabuɛ alɛ, “Teete Yesu!
Nya wo nyaami!” Yesu lanya ma ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ biɛlaayɔ suoto bituo Yaa oletatɛ aanyunyu ye nwaa.” Obe wɔ bakyɛ ni di osuku boofe nii, ni di ofiɛ nwu layɔɔ ma nɛ.
Nioso obe wɔ di onwii lɛma lanya alɛ ofiɛ nwu ntɔɔyɔɔ nwɔ nii, aapɛ aakple aatɔɔtansa Yaa ku kudu osie kanya.
Ninfɛ aakyɛ aawa aabapɛ akunkyi di Yesu nkpaatũ, aapɛ nwɔ sɛfa nɛ.
Osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo Samaria otii aale.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ alɛ, “Diele basuɔtɔ lefosi lɛyɔɔsa ofiɛ?
Ni fɛ baanaasĩ bule nkpe?
Lɛ diɛwa fiɛ di otii wɔ ninanle ni Yuda otii niɛpɛ eekple ɛɛwa ɔɔpɛ Yaa sɛfa?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Taka, faatɔɔkyɛ.
Ofũ onu lɛfɔ ntɔɔyɔɔsa fɔ ofiɛ.” Yesu Labuɛ Mmle Di Yaa Sɛka Kalekɔ Nwu Mate Nii.
Diawa alɛ Farisi batii bawo lakaalɛ Yesu obe wɔ di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu mawa nii.
Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu dilɔbawa di osuku wɔ batii manya nii.
Kuonwii dilɔbabuɛ alɛ, ‘Binyu lo!
Nyaka ninfũ,’ ee ‘Nyaka ninfa.’ Diekye Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo nfɛ nsi ye kaamɛ.” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Obe kɔwa bibamiɛ bilɛ biɔnya ni ami, Otii Obi nwu, ayi nii nwu lewo, kafɔɔ bilɔɔwa ɔbanya!
Batii bawo kamawa mamatɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Binyu nfa lo, akpe ninfa,’ ee ‘Binyu nfũ lo, akpe ninfũ!’ Kafɔɔ bitankyɛ bialaawolaa mi ninfa!
Diekye fɛ mmle di ɔplalaa mmunaa ni di osi, kunkye ni kakyɛ kanwii, kumafe ni kakyɛ bamba, kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ nkpo di ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, ɔwabee kamate nɛ.
Kafɔɔ lɛkasale, dikpe nii, lefe di dibuo kpinwu kamɛ, miɛ batii nsĩ mi.
“Fɛ mmle diawa ni di Noa obe kamɛ, nkpo okle kafɔɔ diɔwa ɔbawa di ami, Otii Obi nwu, ɔwabee kamɛ nɛ.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, batii latoole baatoonyi.
Basanko ku basuɔtɔ latoobuo di sɛsa ku sɛsɔfɔ kamɛ, baayɔ basankobi kafɔɔ baatɔɔta asa dialase di dii le di Noa labuo ni di oklo kplɛ nwu kamɛ.
Fiɛ nfɛ di kanto labanɔɔ ntu layii kasɔ kamuu, diawɔɔsa batii bamuu.
“Dibate fɛ mmle diawa ni di Lot obe kamɛ kafɔɔ.
Batii latoole baatoonyi, baatɔɔya asaa baatoosunsũ.
Bawo latɔɔkpɛ afe, bawo kafɔɔ latootofo ayo.
Dii le di Lot ladie ni di Sodom, ni di ɔtɔ ku ɔtɔ afuɔ lakye osi kuabakpete di okpoo nwu kamɛ, kuawɔɔsa bamuu lɛma nɛ.
“Nkpo okle kafɔɔ diɔwa ɔbate di dii le di ami, Otii Obi nwu, kamadie nkyɔɔ ni nɛ.
Di dii nwu nkpo suoto, Otii wɔ kafɔɔ nintika ni di leyo nɔɔ osi, atantɔkɔ alɛ oosoo anwa amayɔ lɛsalɛsa nɔɔ leeyo kamɛ ansifiko.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di otii wɔ ninkpe ni koofe, atasinkple aatɔkɔ alɛ ooyie ammayɔ lɛsalɛsaa nɛ.
Binyuma lɛsaa le niawa ni di Lot ɔsɔfɔ suoto!
Otii lele niemiɛ alɛ ɔɔta nkpa nɔɔ, abayu mi.
Otii lele kafɔɔ nieyu nkpa nɔɔ, abakple anwɛ mi.
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ di dii nwu nkpo kakyɛ, batii banyɔ mate di atensaa anwii suoto, Yaa makpaa onwii ansifiko, andiɛ ɔnyɔɔfa nnte.
Basanko banyɔ matookuɔ nnaafũ di kukuɔ suoto, kafɔɔ Yaa makpaa onwii ansifiko andiɛ ɔnyɔɔfa di kukuɔ katũ.
Basuɔtɔ banyɔ mayila koofe mantɔɔkpɛ, Yaa makpaa onwii ansifiko andiɛ ɔnyɔɔfa antɔɔkpɛ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate di ɔfɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Lɛba le lɛɛsaa lekpi dite nii, nfa di alente nsi nɛ.”
Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Kpisɔfɔ Onwii Ku Kantɛ Kpile Onwii Suoto.
Yesu Lapɛ lɛkpa aatuo basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lɛsaa alɛ, dikpe nii, obe lele, bɛɛtɔɔpɛ ɔlaa bɛɛtɔɔta Yaa di nnɛɛ ɔtanfeesa kamɛ.
Aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kantɛ onwii lawɛ di okpoo onwii kamɛ, ananyɛkɛ ni Yaa ee otii.
Kpisɔfɔ onwii kafɔɔ lawɛ di okpoo nwu nkpo kamɛ, aatɔɔkyɛ kantɛ nwu nkpo nfũ wlawla aalaatootikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, ‘Kyakaakoe ta balo nii oso.’ “Diaklɛ, kantɛ nwu nkpo ditatookpee ɔlaa nwu kanya.
Kafɔɔ sɛmaa aabatɔkɔ suoto alɛ, ‘Kuntɛ ninyɛkɛ Yaa ee labu otii yi, ta kubuɛ ko di kpisɔfɔ wɔ mmle kokpee mi ni oso, manyu nlɛ lɛtɔɔ lɛbɛ.
Se diele nkpo, obe lele abatɔɔwa nfũ amatoodiki mi ninwuna.’ ” Ninfɛ di Saate nwu lakple aabuɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Binu ɔlaa wɔ di kantɛ wɔ mmle kpile labuɛ ni.
Ni, Yaa dilɔbatuna ata batii nɔɔ ba bamuu ninpɛ ɔlaa mantɔɔ ni kakũ ku kakyɛ?
Sɛɛ bienyu bilɛ ɔlɔbapɛsɛwa akyakaako ma?
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ Yaa matuna ma wla.
Kafɔɔ nse Otii Obi nwu lɛwa, abanya batii ba niefũ beenu ni kaasɔ ka mmle?” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Ninwii Di Farisi Batii Ku Akpooto Bafuntɛ Suoto.
Yesu lakple aapɛ lɛkpa ninwii di batii ba ninnyu alɛ bate ni tinini, mannyu ni batii bamba alɛ baate ni fɛ mma.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Obe onwii kamɛ, batii banyɔ banwii lakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ alɛ bɔɔlaapɛ ɔlaa manta Yaa.
Onwii lale Farisi otii, ɔnyɔɔfa kafɔɔ lale akpooto funtɛ.
Farisi otii nwu lablasa suoto aayila aapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa, kɔpɛ fɔ sɛfa, diekye nnaa koto onumbɛbɛɛ, ninle otii kpile, ninle sɔnɔkpeetɛ fɛ mmle baatii bamba mbla nii.
Kɔpɛ fɔ sɛfa kafɔɔ alɛ, ninte fɛ akpooto funtɛ nwu nkpo nin-yɛ ni ninfa.
Nnii kanya ayi anyɔ di osuku kaanya kamɛ.
N-yɔ kafɔɔ asaa ya amuu ninwɛ ni lefosile nwako fɔ.’ “Kafɔɔ akpooto funtɛ nwu nkpo layila fanfa, atakplesa bia anu aanyu osi.
Ni aayɔ kɔnɛɛ aatika nintɛɛ aabuɛ alɛ, ‘Yaa, kpileblatɛ nle, nyɛɛ nyaami!’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, akpooto funtɛ nwu nkpo lakple aasifi leyo, klekle di Yaa anu aalenkee Farisi otii nwu nkpo.
Diekye otii lele niɛtakatɛsa suoto katoo, Yaa mawakosa nwɔ kasɔ.
Kafɔɔ otii lele niɛwakosa suoto kasɔ, Yaa matakatɛsa nwɔ katoo.” Yesu Labɔmbɔ Babisɔ Ɔlaa Osie Kanya.
Batii bawo lakpaa babi lɛma baawako Yesu nfũ alɛ atika ma nnɛɛ di asi.
Obe wɔ di Yesu batɔkyɛntɛ lanya ni batii nwu nkpo, baasĩ ɔlaa baata ma ta lɛsaa nwu oso.
Kafɔɔ Yesu lalɛɛ babisɔ nwu nkpo aawako ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Bita babisɔ bawa ɔkyɛ nii, bitantĩi ma osuku.
Diekye batii fɛ babisɔ ba mmle okle kale ninle Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo nɛ.
Binyuma nle mmle, otii lele ninanfũ Yaa kafa nwu fɛ obisɔ, dilɔbabuo nfa diidii.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Di Basaawɛntɛ Ku Yaa Sɛka Kalekɔ Suoto.
Yuda batii tunletɛ onwii lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ biene, be kabla fiɛ kawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be oso fɔɔlɛɛ mi otii biene?
Otii kuonwii nnaa ale ni bienetɛ, diediki Yaa lete.
Faye Yaa afiofa amuu.
‘Tanlo otii, tankpee asɔnɔ, tan-yu, tanlaa faatika di otii suoto, bu teefɔ ku Yaafɔ.’ ” Ninfɛ di ɔnɔɔfo nwu labuɛ alɛ, “Diɛyɔ ni bia sibisɔ nii obe, lɛkyako afiofa ya mmle nwu nkpo ole.” Obe wɔ di Yesu lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Diebu fɔ lɛsaa ninwii dikpe ni fɛɛbla nii.
Laayɔ asaa lɛfɔ amuu fasunsũ, faayɔ koto nwu fata bapiitɛ, ni fabawɛ asaa di Yaa kafa.
Nni kamaa faawa fabatikankoe.” Kafɔɔ obe wɔ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lanu ni sɛlaa se mmle, suoto ditayɔɔ nwɔ, diekye saawɛntɛ aatɛ aale.
Yesu lanya alɛ suoto ditayɔɔ nwɔ, nioso aabuɛ alɛ, “Dikpe osie diɛta basaawɛntɛ fiɛ bababuo Yaa kafa!
Diɛbla lɛsaa le niɛyɔɔ diɛta ni kapupunkɔ alɛ aafe di paniɛ dituɛ, dilenke alɛ saawɛntɛ kabuo ni Yaa sɛka kalekɔ.” Batii ba nianu ni sɛlaa se mmle lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Ni owe nfɛ nimawɛ didiki?” Ninfɛ di Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Lɛsaa le di otii dilɔbafuo ni ɔbla diidii, Yaa nnwɔɔ abafuo ni ɔbla.” Ninfɛ di Petro latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Nyu!
Awo buodiɛ ayo loo buɔtɛ buɔwa butikanko fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako dile.
Kafɔɔ kɔta ye mintofo nlɛ otii lele niediɛ leyo nɔɔ ɛɛtɛ, ee ɔsɔfɔ nɔɔ ɛɛtɛ, ee babilɛma suɔtɔbi ɛɛtɛ, ee ote ku ɔya ɛɛtɛ, ee babi nɔɔ ɛɛtɛ, ta Yaa sɛka kalekɔ oso, abawɛ asaa nwu nkpo ampɔɔsa di nkpa be mmle kamɛ ku nkpa be nikɔwa dinnaa ni kaloo kafɔɔ kamɛ.” Yesu Lakple Aakakatɛ Ditiɛfa Di Kukpi Nɔɔ Suoto.
Yesu lalɛɛ batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ lefosi batii banyɔ nwu di ɔlɔɔkɔ ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Binu lo!
Nfɛ buofe Yerusalem, nfũ di asaa ya di Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ lɛkpana bɛɛtɛ ni di ami, Otii Obi nwu, suoto mawa ni kaanya.
Batii mayɔ mi mankpee di batii ba ninanle ni Yuda batii nnɛɛ kamɛ, babama mi, mantufa mi, mantufa sita kafɔɔ mankpete mi di suoto.
Babapɛ mi, manlo mi, kafɔɔ dii tiɛfa kamaa, makple ntaka nkye bakpi kamɛ.” Kafɔɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ditanu sɛlaa se mmle kuonwii kasɔ.
Sɛlaa se mmle lɛsɔnu lawofa ma.
Nioso batanu ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu latoobuɛ ni kasɔ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Numbiɛtɛ Onwii Niale Ni Asaakaalɛtɛ Ofiɛ.
Obe wɔ nfɛ di Yesu latɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni Yeriko, numbiɛtɛ onwii lasiɛ di osukulɔɔkɔ aatɔɔkaalɛ asaa.
Obe wɔ aanu batii kpinwu kofe nii, aakaalɛ alɛ, “Ɔmɛnlaa kule?” Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Yesu Nasaret Otii nikofe.” Ninfɛ aafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Yesu, Ɔka Dawid Obi ee!
Nyɛɛ nyaami!” Nioso batii ba niale ni katũ lamuɛ nwɔ alɛ, alo kanana.
Kafɔɔ mianfɛ aakple aafaa osie kanya aakyakaa alɛ, “Dawid Obi ee!
Nyɛɛ nyaami!” Nkpo oso Yesu layila, ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, bakpaa numbiɛtɛ nwu nkpo bawako nwɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di numbiɛtɛ nwu ladu ni Yesu nfũ, ninfɛ aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be foomiɛ falɛ mbla nta fɔ?” Ninfɛ di numbiɛtɛ nwu labuɛ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, ta anu atikiti mi nintɔɔnya!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni nyaɛ!
Ofũonu lɛfɔ ntoodiki fɔ.” Nfanwu, osuɔtɔ nwu lakyako ɔnya, ninfɛ aatikanko Yesu sɛɛmaa aatɔɔtansa Yaa nɛ.
Obe wɔ baatii dikudi nwu nkpo kafɔɔ lanya ni nle mmle, bamuu lɛma baatansa Yaa.
Yesu Lakakatɛko Sakeo.
Yesu labuo Yeriko okpoo kamɛ ɔɔwaalɛ anfe.
Akpooto funtɛ ɔnɔɔfo onwii lawɛ ninfa baatɔɔlɛɛ nwɔ ni Sakeo, koto late nwɔ osie kanya.
Aamiɛ alɛ ɔɔnya otii wɔ di Yesu nle nii, kafɔɔ atafuo nwɔ ɔnya ta batii lɛpɔ oso, diekye otii kunkudu aale.
Nkpo oso aatoso aale batii nwu katũ, aalaayie kowoso kunwii alɛ, ɔɔnya Yesu.
Diekye aatofo alɛ Yesu mafe ninfa.
Obe wɔ di Yesu labadu ni kowoso nwu kalɔ, aatakatɛsa anu aanyu osi ni aatɔkɔ Sakeo alɛ, “Sakeo, pɛsɛwa fasoo fawa, diekye leyo lɛfɔ masoosa miɛ.” Nioso Sakeo lapɛsɛwa aasoo aawa, aabafũ Yesu ku suoto lɛyɔɔ kplɛ.
Batii nwu nkpo bamuu nianya ni lakye kasɔ baatoonwununuu di Yesu suoto alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle kofe kpileblatɛ wɔ mmle nfũ osoosa.” Sakeo lataka aayila, ni aabuɛ aatɔkɔ Saate alɛ, “Teete!
Nyu lo!
Mayɔ asaa ya ninkpe mi ni kakyɛ kanwii nta bapiitɛ.
Otii lele kafɔɔ ntoyitafaa mata lɛsaa nwu ntɔɔ, nkyakaa nwɔ di akyuu ana kamɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Miɛ nkpa ɔwɛ ntɔɔwa leyo le mmle kamɛ.
Diekye osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle kafɔɔ Abraham ɔnantii ale.
Ami, Otii Obi, ɔwa lɛwa nlɛ, kɔmawolaa ndiki mba nintooyu nii.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Di Koto Sɛɛle Suoto.
Obe wɔ batii nwu nkpo konu ni sɛlaa se mmle, Yesu lakple aapɛ ma lɛkpa ninwii.
Diekye obe nwu nfɛ ɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ Yerusalem.
Baanyu alɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nfɛ makyɔɔ.
Nioso aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Obe onwii, osuɔtɔ finle onwii lawɛ, aatoofe kale kanwii fanfa alɛ bɔɔlaase nwɔ sɛka ankple anwa okpoo nɔɔ.
Fiɛ abasifi nii, aalɛɛ bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ lefosi aasiisa.
Ni aata obiala lɛma koto sɛɛle kunwii kunwii nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, ‘Biyɔ koto nwu bitɔɔblako ɔkpɛ dilaase di obe wɔ kamawa ni.’ “Kafɔɔ osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle okpoo nɔɔ batii nimbɔmbɔ nwɔ, nkpo oso baakpee batii sɛɛmaa nɔɔ alɛ, ‘Buloomiɛ osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle bulɛ ale wo ɔka.’ “Kafɔɔ baase osuɔtɔ nwu sɛka aakple aawa okpoo nɔɔ.
Nfanwu ni aakpee baalɛɛ bakpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ baatɔɔ alɛ, babatɔkɔ nwu mmle bɛɛblako ni koto ko aata ma ni ɔkpɛ, ku mmle bɛɛwɛ ni.
“Ninfɛ di kpɛmblatɛ kasale nɔɔ alɛ, ‘Teete, koto nwu, lɛwɛ lefosi lɛkyakaa di nko faatɛɛ ni suoto.’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nwu latansa nwɔ aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Lafe!
Feelolaa fɛɛbla!
Kpɛmblatɛ biene fale!
Di obe wɔ feelolaa lɛsaabii le mmle feeklee ni di osuku wɔ mmle suoto oso, mayɔ fɔ nse di eekpoo lefosi kanya.’ “Kpɛmblatɛ nyɔɔfa kafɔɔ lawa aabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Teete, di koto ko faatɛɛ nii, lɛwɛ anɔɔ lɛkyakaa di nkunkpo suoto!’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nwu nkpo latɔkɔ kpɛmblatɛ nwu nyɔɔfa alɛ, ‘Afɔ yi, mayɔ fɔ nse di eekpoo ɛnɔɔ kanya!’ “Kpɛmblatɛ bamba lawa aabatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Teete, nnya koto sɛɛle lɛfɔ nwu faatɛɛ ni.
Layɔ lakookaa di kadukufi kamɛ.
Latɔɔyɛkɛ fɔ diekye otii siene fale.
Fan-yɔ lɛsaa le ninanle fɔ ni lele.
Fanfiɛlɛ ninfũ kafɔɔ fanankpɛ nii.’ “Ninfɛ di Saate nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Afɔ kpɛmblatɛ kpile fale!
Afɔ omu kanya kamɛ sɛlaa mayɔ nlo fɔ lɛpɔɔ.
Faye falɛ otii siene nle.
N-yɔ lɛsaa le ninanle mi ni lele.
Nfiɛlɛ kafɔɔ ninfũ ninankpɛ nii.
Ni se faye nkpo mɔ, be oso fanan-yɔ koto nii nwu falaatɛ di koto katɛkɔ?
Alɛ nse lɛwa kamawɛ nfasũ nkyakaa.’ “Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ batii ba niayila ni ninfa alɛ, ‘Bifũ koto sɛɛle nwu di nnɛɛ nɔɔ biɛyɔ bita kpɛmblatɛ wɔ ninkpe ni koto sɛɛlɛ lefosi.’ “Kafɔɔ batii nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, ‘Teete, kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkle koto lefosi kofokofoko!’ “Ninfɛ di saate nwu ladiki kanya alɛ, ‘Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii wɔ lɛɛsaa nkpe nii, nnwɔɔ babakple mankyakaa nɛ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ lɛsalɛsaa nnaa nii, kɛɛkɛɛ wɔ ninkpe nwɔ nii, babaklee manfũ nwɔ ninnɛɛ.
Nunua yi, balo nii ba ninoomiɛ alɛ nle ma ni ɔka, bikpaa ma biwako nfũ biɛbalo ma di anu nii.’ ” Yesu Labuo Yerusalem Ku Katansa.
Obe wɔ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma ɔlaa wɔ mmle aaloo nii, aalekatũ aasifi Yerusalem.
Di obe wɔ nfɛ ɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni Betfage ku Betania di nnɔnyi kobokote ɔlɔɔkɔ, aakpee basaateketetɛ nɔɔ banyɔ alɛ bale katũ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ okpoo wɔ ninte ye ni siitũ ninfa.
Nse biebuo nwu kaamɛ, bibanya lɛpɔnkɔbi ninwii nsi di okũ, di otii kuonwii diisiɛ ni ni diidii.
Bidiki ni di okũ, biɛkpaa ni biwakoe.
Nse otii owo lɛkaalɛ ye alɛ be lɛsaa oso biodiki ni, biɛtɔkɔ nwɔ bilɛ, ‘Saate komiɛ ni.’ ” Batɔkyɛntɛ nwu lakyɛ baalaanya fɛ mmle okle di Yesu latɔkɔ ma nii.
Obe wɔ baatoodiki ni lɛpɔnkɔbi nwu, saate ni ni lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be lɛsaa oso biodiki ni?” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Saate nwu komiɛ alɛ ablako ni ɔpkɛ.” Ninfɛ baakpaa lɛpɔnkɔbi nwu baawako Yesu nɛ.
Ninfɛ baayɔ abula lɛma baatika di lɛpɔnkɔbi nwu kamaa, ni baakyakaako Yesu aayie aasiɛ ni kaamaa nɛ.
Obe wɔ nfɛ asi ni, ninni suoto bɔɔkyɛ nii, batii layɔ abula lɛma baatɛ di osuku suoto.
Obe wɔ di Yesu nfɛ kɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni Yerusalem, di lɛba le di osuku lesoo kuosifi ni Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ dikudi nwu lakyako Yaa sɛfa ɔpɛ baatɔɔtansa nwɔ kafɔɔ ku sɛlɔ siene di asaa kplɛ ya bɛɛnya ni oso.
Baatoobuɛ alɛ, “Yaa akusɛkusɛsa ɔka wɔ nikɔwa ni di Saate leyooto kamɛ!
Atoko ɔkyɛ ole diwɛ di Yaa kafa, Yaa lele ninle leklekle!” Ni di Farisi batii ba bawo niawɛ ni baatii dikudi nwu kamɛ latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, sĩ ɔlaa fata basaateketetɛ lɛfɔ, baadiɛ kudu oyiisa!” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse batii ba mmle lɛmaasa kanya, afuɔ amu makye kasɔ ankyako kudu oyiisa.” Yesu Lawi Di Yerusalem Disi.
Di Yesu nfɛ kɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni Yerusalem okpoo aanya nwu nii, aawi kaku diisi ninwu.
Ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Nse fɛ oye faye lɛsaa le niefĩ diɛta ni atoko ɔkyɛ ole miɛ!
Kafɔɔ nunua, flɔbafuo ɔnya!
Obe onwii kɔwa di balo lee mamana ye mankyi nii kaakɔ biala.
Babatĩi ye di aba amuu alɛ kuonwii dilɔbawɛ osuku adie ee abuo.
Babawɔɔsa okpoo wɔ mmle ku batii ba bamuu ninsi ni kaamɛ.
Blɔbadiɛ bia difuɔ kuninwii ditika leewo suoto.
Diekye bitatofo obe wɔ di Yaa lawa ye ni odiki!” Yesu Lakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ.
Yesu lakyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ, ni aakyako basaasunsutɛ otososa odiki nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bɛɛkpana di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, ‘Baalɛɛ mi leyo alɛ ɔlaa ɔpɛ katakɔ.’ Kafɔɔ aye, bitɔɔyɔ biɛbla bayu kawofakɔ!” Dii biala Yesu latuo asaa di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu ninfa.
Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ ku kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo lamiɛ alɛ boolo nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ batawɛ osuku wɔ suoto baafe manlo nwɔ nii.
Diekye batii bamuu latɔɔkyɔɔ nwɔ ɔlaa atoko osie kanya.
Batii Lananfiko Yesu Ɔlaa Di Osie Nɔɔ Suoto.
Dii ninwii obe wɔ di Yesu lawɛ ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ aatootuo ni batii asaa, aatɔɔtɔkɔ ma ni kafɔɔ ɔlaa biene nwu, Yaa olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ ku okpoo banɔɔfo lakyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ baabakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔkɔ wo, ɔmɛnsuku fakpe fɔɔbla asaa ya mmle?
Owe kafɔɔ niɛta fɔ osuku nwu nkpo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Amii bitɛɛ nkaalɛ ye ɔlaa onwii biɛtɔkɔ mi.
Ɔfɛ di Yohane lawɛ osuku fiɛ aatookpeesa batii Yaa ntu?
Yaa nfũ kuakye ɛɛ, sɛɛ batii nfũ kuakye?” Ninfɛ baamumufũ ɔlaa nwu nimanima baanyu alɛ, “Be nfɛ buabuɛ?
Nse buobuɛ bulɛ Yaa nfũ kuakye yi, abakaalɛ wo alɛ, ‘Ni be oso bitafũ Yohane bianu mɔ?’ Kafɔɔ nse buobuɛ bulɛ otii nfũ kuakye yi, batii ba mmle niesi ni ninfũ masafɔ wo afuɔ, diekye bamuu lɛma beefũ beenu alɛ Yohane yi, Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ aale.” Nioso baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Buoye nfũ kuakye nii.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di amii, namatɔkɔ ye otii wɔ niɛtɛɛ ni osuku fiɛ kɔbla ni asaa ya mmle nɛ.” Yesu Lapɛ Lɛkpa Aakyeko Kofe Nyuntɛ Kpile Onwii Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lapɛ lɛkpa le mmle aata batii nwu alɛ, “Obe onwii, osuɔtɔ onwii lakpɛ awosobi ya man-yɔ mambla ni nta kofe.
Ni aayɔ kofe nwu nkpo aakpee di bakpɛntɛ banwii nnɛɛ kamɛ alɛ, batoonyu batɔɔtɔɔ nɛ.
Ni aadie aasifi osuku, aalaasiɛ ninfa aaklɛ nɛ.
Di obe lawo alɛ baatɛsɛ ni awosobi nwu, aakpee kpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ onwii alɛ, akyɛ aalaafũ kalekɔ nɔɔ di kofe banyuntɛ nwu nfũ awako nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ kofe banyuntɛ nwu nkpo lapɛ kpɛmblatɛ nwu baatososɔɔ aasifi nnɛɛ fukuti.
Nioso, aakple aakpee kpɛmblatɛ bamba.
Kafɔɔ kofe banyuntɛ nwu nkpo lakple baapɛ nwɔ baakpee nwɔ sinunsɔ baatososɔɔ aasifi nnɛɛ fukuti.
Ni, aakple aakpee kpɛmblatɛ tiɛfa nɛ.
Kafɔɔ kofe banyuntɛ nwu lapɛ nwɔ baatika nwɔ nkɔ baatososɔɔ baadiki koofe nwu kamɛ ninfa.
“Ni koofe nwu saate lakaalɛ alɛ, ‘Be nfɛ kakple mbla?
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ suoto alɛ, kamakyesee obi nii bɔmbɔtɛ.
Loobia babata obi nii nwu dibu.’ “Kafɔɔ obe wɔ di kofe nwu nkpo banyuntɛ lanya ni obi nɔɔ nwu nkpo, ni baatɔkɔ bawo alɛ, ‘Nnya kofe saate obi wɔ nimale ni atesaa ninle nwɔ mmle nɛ.
Bita bulo nwɔ di atesaa nɔɔ nwu nkpo akple wo ale!’ Nioso baananfi obi nwu nkpo baadiki di kofe nwu kamɛ, ni baalo nwɔ nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be bienyu bilɛ kofe saate nwu mabla kofe banyuntɛ nwu?
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ abawa amalo kofe banyuntɛ nwu nkpo, an-yɔ kofe nwu ankpee koofe banyuntɛ bamba nnɛɛ kamɛ.” Obe wɔ baatii nwu nkpo lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle baabuɛ alɛ, “Oowo!
Dilɔbawa nkpo!” Yesu lanyu ma tuwĩi ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ni be di Kɔkpana Klekle ko mmle kotuo?
Nko niebuɛ alɛ, ‘Difuɔ le baayotofotɛ lesĩ alɛ diɛlɛ nii, nni bia nintoobakple difuɔ le nintoofũ kɔya dilenke ni di afuɔ amuu kamɛ nɛ.’ Otii lele niɛnɔɔ ɛɛpɛ diifuɔ le mmle, suoto nɔɔ mabibiɛ wɔkyɔwɔkyɔ.
Otii lele kafɔɔ diifuɔ le mmle lɛkpa diɛpɛ, suoto nɔɔ makuɔ muɛmuɛ.” Yesu Lakakatɛ Di Akpooto Ɔta Suoto.
Kufiofa batuotɛ ku ole batatɛ banɔɔfo lamiɛ alɛ boomufũ Yesu ninfa, diekye baatofo alɛ lɛkpa le di Yesu lapɛ nii mma aalaka.
Kafɔɔ baayɛkɛ batii nwu nkpo.
Ta nkpo oso, baamiɛ osuku bamba wɔ suoto baafe mammufũ nwɔ nii.
Nioso baata batii bawo asaa di lewofa kamɛ.
Ni baabla onwii baakyɛ Yesu ɔkyɛ fɛ batii biene bale.
Baakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaawolaa nwɔ kaanya ku sɛlaa kaalɛle sewo.
Mmle okle baawɛ osuku man-yɔ nwɔ mankpee ni di Roma abaa ɔnɔɔfo nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Nioso banyawolaatɛ ba mmle lakyɛ Yesu nfũ.
Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buye bulɛ lɛsaa lele feebuɛ, ee feetuo kute nkpo.
Buye kafɔɔ bulɛ fánnyu otii di anu faabla lɛsaa.
Kafɔɔ fantuo nwaako ɔlaa wɔ di Yaa komiɛ ni fanta batii.
Nioso buomiɛ bulɛ butofo, dilɛ alɛ buata akpooto munta Roma Batii Ɔka Kplɛ ɛɛ, sɛɛ diɛlɛ?” Kafɔɔ Yesu latofo kakyɔnkyɔ osuku wɔ suoto bakyɛ nii, nioso aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biyɔ koto fututu nwu biwakoe nnyu.
Obe wɔ baayɔ baakyɛnko nwɔ nii, aakaalɛ ma alɛ owɛ kunyii ku leyooto nintika?” Ninfɛ baadiki kanya alɛ, “Ɔka Kplɛ Kaesare lele dile.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ni biyɔ lɛsaa le ninle ni Ɔka Kplɛ lele, bita Ɔka Kplɛ.
Biɛyɔ lɛsaa lele ninle Yaa lele bita Yaa.” Batafuo ɔlaa kuonwii ɔwɛ, ɔyɔ omufũ nwɔ di batii nwu anu.
Nioso batasinfuo ɔlaa kuonwii obuɛ.
Diabla ma ɔkpɛ di ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu ladiki ni kanya oso.
Yesu Lakakatɛ Di Bakpi Okple Ɔtaka Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Saduki batii ba nimbuɛ alɛ bakpi dilɔbasintaka ni bawo lawa Yesu nfu babatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ.
“Saatuotɛ, Mose lakpana kufiofa ko mmle ɛɛtɛ wo alɛ, ‘Nse osuɔtɔ owo lekpi eediɛ ɔsɔfɔ, manko nwɔ banaa obi, osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo obilɛma osuɔtɔbi kayɔ kpisɔfɔ nwu nkpo manlofo babi.
Ni babi nwu nkpo, batii manya ma fɛ osuɔtɔ wɔ ninnaa ni babi.’ Obe onwii babilɛma suɔtɔbi bakuɛnsĩ banwii lawɛ.
Osuɔtɔbi nɔɔfole labayɔ ɔsanko, batalofo obi, aabafe aakpi.
Ni di obilɛma suɔtɔbi nyɔɔfa kafɔɔ labayɔ kpisɔfɔ nwu nɛ.
Otiɛfa kafɔɔ laakpanwu.
Lɛsaa le mmle lawa babilɛma suɔtɔbi nwu bakuɛnsĩ suoto.
Bamuu lɛma baakpi batalofo obi.
Yɛntɛyɛntɛ, ɔsanko nwu omu labakpi.
Nimɔ, di dii le baakpi makple mantaka nii, owe lɛma ɔsɔfɔ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo male di obe wɔ baakuɛnsĩ lɛma nwu layɔ nwɔ ni?” Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nkpa be mmle kamɛ lete di basuɔtɔ ku basanko kɔyɔ bawo.
Kafɔɔ basuɔtɔ ku basanko ba niesiɛko alɛ baataka mankye ni bakpi kamɛ mansiɛ ni nkpa be mmle yi, blosinwa sɛsa ku sɛsɔfɔ ɔbatoole.
Babate fɛ Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ, blosinwa ɔbakpi kafɔɔ.
Yaa babi nfɛ bale diekye batɔɔtaka beekye bakpi kamɛ.
Mose lɛkpasa kamɛ klekle di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ bakpi makple mantaka mansiɛ nkpa.
Diekye obe wɔ aayila ni di owuu dibuu le niatoofiɛ ni ɔlɔɔkɔ aabuɛ di Saate suoto alɛ, ‘Abraham Yaa, Isak Yaa ku Yakob Yaa.’ Nle mmle kotuo alɛ, nnwɔɔ ninle batii ba ninkpe ni nkpa Yaa, diele bakpi Yaa ale.
Diekye di anu nɔɔ bamuu lɛma bakpe nkpa.” Kufiofa batuotɛ bawo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nwaako, Saatuotɛ, feelolaa kanya feediki!” Di nni nkpo kamaa, kuonwii ditasinkpee otu aakaalɛ Yesu ɔlaa kuonwii.
Owe Obi Ninle Otii Wɔ Bɛɛpɛ Ni Ɔfɔɔ?
Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Lɛ diɛbla fiɛ baatii kobuɛ alɛ, Otii wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ Dawid ɔnantii ale?
Diekye Dawid omu labuɛ di sinu kukũ kamɛ alɛ, ‘Saate nwu latɔkɔ Saate nii alɛ, “Siɛ kaasɔ di oletanɛɛkyɛ nii diɛlase di obe wɔ mayɔ balo lɛfɔ nkpee ni di nkpaasɔ lɛfɔ kalɔ.” ’ Ni nse Dawid lalɛɛ nwɔ alɛ Saate, lɛ dibawa fiɛ di otii wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ male Dawid ɔnantii?” Yesu Lasĩ Ɔlaa Aata Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ Di Kufiofa Batuotɛ Suoto.
Obe wɔ baatii bamuu n-yɛ bɔɔkyɔɔ ni ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu latoobuɛ ni atoko, aatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bilolaa suoto binyu di kufiofa batuotɛ suoto.
Batii ba mmle mbɔmbɔ awu kplɛ okpee, mankyɛ mantookyi lɛkpaka alɛ batii katɔɔsɛɛsa ma ku suoto kasɔ ɔwakosa.
Mambɔmbɔ nisiɛkɔ kplɛ di Yuda batii nsiisakɔ ku dii nlekɔ.
Mankyɛ bakpisɔfɔ nfũ manatafaa ma manfũ ma asaa ninnɛɛ.
Mantakatɛsa suoto katoo baatii anu manklɛsa ɔlaa ɔpɛ ɔta Yaa.
Letoko nanfi lɛma mapɔ ninlenkee batii bamuu lele!”
Kpisɔfɔ Onwii Lata Koto Kplɛ.
Di Olekatakɔ ninfa, Yesu latakatɛsa anu ni aanya mmle di basaawɛntɛ layɔ asaa ɔta lɛma baatookpee ni di asaa ɔta lekpeesa kamɛ.
Ni aanya mmle kafɔɔ di kpisɔfɔ piitɛ onwii labafe aalaakpee ni mplɛ nnyɔ di asaa ɔta lekpeesaa nwu kamɛ nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, kpisɔfɔ piitɛ wɔ mmle niɛta koto alenke batii bule.
Diekye batii bule yi, di lɛsaawɛ lɛma kamɛ nle ninlɛ ma ni bɛɛyɔ bɛɛbata.
Kafɔɔ ɔsanko wɔ mmle di dipii nɔɔ kamɛ, lɛsaa le ninkpe nwɔ aale ansiɛ ni nkpa nimuu ɛɛyɔ ɛbata nɛ.” Yesu Labuɛ Obe Wɔ Batii Kɔwa Ni Yaa Olekatakɔ Nwu Obiɛ Ɔtɛ Kaasɔ.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, basaateketetɛ bawo latɔɔkakatɛ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo suoto.
Di mmle okle diɔlɛ ni onyu ku afuɔ ya bɛɛyɔ beetofo ni nii, ku asaa ɔta ya baayɔ baata ni Yaa.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Asaa ya amuu biɔnya ni ninfũ, obe owo kɔwa di difuɔ kuninwii dilababu ditika ni leewo suoto.
Bababiɛ amuu mantɛ kaasɔ.” Dibuo Ku Ditikanko Mawa.
Ninfɛ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, ɔmɛmbe di nle mmle mawa?
Be nimale dituosaa le bubayɔ muntofo bulɛ, obe nwu ntoowo ni?” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bilolaa binyu nwaa alɛ otii kuonwii diɛkyɔnkyɔ ye.
Batii kpinwu mayɔ leyooto nii manwa ɔkyɛ lee, mamatɔkɔ ye alɛ, ‘Ami dile,’ ni kafɔɔ, ‘Obe nwu ntoowo.’ Kafɔɔ bitantikanko ma di nkpaamaa.
Bitanyɛkɛ nse bienu kakpɛ kudu ku batii ɔtaka oyila baawo suoto.
Dikpe nii asaa ya mmle lɛkasa ɔwa, kafɔɔ dilootuo alɛ kayi kalookɔ ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ.” Yesu lakple aabuɛ aakyakaa alɛ, “Nnle mataka baawo suoto, sɛka nlekɔ kafɔɔ mataka baawo suoto.
Nsɔ matũkũ osie kanya.
Aka siene kafɔɔ makpɛ di aba aba.
Sifiɛ ate ate kafɔɔ mawa di aba aba kpi.
Ayɛkɛsaa ku atuosaa kafɔɔ matɔkyɔɔ di osi.
“Fiɛ di asaa ya mmle mawa nii, batii matikanko ye, mamufũ ye.
Batii mayɔ ye mankpee di bakantɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ, mankanko ye di Yuda batii nsiisakɔ mantɛ ye laayo.
Babakpaa ye manwako baka anu ku batunletɛ anu, ta ami oso.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, osuku kule kuɔsɛkɛtɛ kuɔta ye alɛ, biabuɛ Yaa ɔlaa biene nwu nkpo.
Bita disiɛ ye diisi alɛ, bilaabu ɔlaa wɔ bibabuɛ mindiki ni suoto kanya diisi bialesakatũ.
Diekye ami omu nimata ye lɛsaatofo ku ɔlaa wɔ bibabuɛ nii, alɛ balo lee dilabafuo oyila di ɔlaa lee nwu suoto, ee bayɔ nwu babudi ye kanya.
Balofotɛ ku babilee suɔtɔbi ku banantii lee ku basiɛwo lee madiki ye manta, manlo bawo kaamɛ lee.
Batii bamuu makyidi ye ta ami oso.
Kafɔɔ bia asi lee onwini onwii dilabayu.
Nse biekpee situ osie kanya, bibawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Yesu Labuɛ Obe Wɔ Baatii Mabiɛ Ni Yerusalem Okpoo.
“Nse obe lele biɛnya bakpɛtɛ lɛmana Yerusalem okpoo beekyi, ni bietofo bilɛ okpoo nwu obiɛ bee ntoowo.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, biɛta batii ba ninkpe ni di Yudia batoso basifi abokote osi balaawofa.
Mba kafɔɔ ninkpe ni di okpoo kamɛ, baadie.
Mba kafɔɔ ninkpe ni di nkpaayotũ ku afe, batasinkple baawa okpoo kamɛ.
Diekye obe nwu kamɛ ninle letokonanfi ayi ya bɛɛtɛ nii, alɛ sɛlaa se di Kɔkpana Klekle lebuɛ ni kawa kaanya.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, dibatɛ ninwɛ osie ninta basanko ba ninlaka ni amɛ ku mba nikɔta babi nyɛɛfu nii.
Dibuo dibinte mawa di kasɔ nwu suoto.
Diekye Yaa ɔblɔ mawa di batii ba mmle suoto.
Babalo bawo ku mpamii.
Babamufũ bawo kafɔɔ mansifiko nsɔ bamba suoto.
Batii ba ninanle ni Yuda batii male sɛka di Yerusalem suoto ninaase di obe wɔ di Yaa lɛtɛ ma nii.” Oti Obi Nwu Makple Anwa.
“Atuosaa madiki suoto kayi di kufĩ ku kɔwɛntɛ ku awɛntrɛbi suoto.
Di kasɔ ka mmle suoto, lɛyɛkɛ mapɛ batii di nnle mmuu kamɛ mankpɔkpɔtɔ mambla biɔɔ ta lekpo sɛlɔ ku mmle diɔkpɛ ni oso.
Batii matoloo ɔnyɛɛ ta lɛyɛkɛ, di obe wɔ basoko ni lɛsaa le nikɔwa ni kaayi kamuu suoto oso.
Diekye osi asaa kafɔɔ matididi di aba ya atika nii.
Di nni nkpo sɛmaa, batii manya Otii Obi nwu makyɔɔ di alokonkyɛ kamɛ ɔɔwa ku osie kplɛ di leklekle kamɛ.
Nse asaa ya mmle lɛkyako ɔwa bielolaa suoto bisiɛ ta bitoonyu osuku, diekye didiki lee obe ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ.” Bitekete Asaa Bikyeko Kolewoso Suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa ninwii alɛ, “Bibu disi di kolewoso ku awoso bamba suoto.
Nse biɛnya afata lɛnya koyie afɔle, mintofo bilɛ kanto ɔnɔɔbee nfɛ kɔtɛɛtɛɛ.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ nse biɛnya asaa ya mmle kɔwa, bietofo bilɛ Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nfɛ mawa.
“Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, asaa ya mmle amuu mawa fiɛ baatii ba ninkpe ni nkpa nunua bamuu makpi.
Osi ku kasɔ mafe, kafɔɔ ɔlaa nii nwu kulabafe diidii.
Dikpe Nii Biesiɛ Di Anu Kesekese Kamɛ.
“Bilolaa binyu nwaa bilɛ biɛyɔ obe lee bita alesaa ole ku nta onyi osiɛ bilenkeesa.
Ku kayi ka mmle asaa omiɛ kpinwu suoto.
Se diele nkpo, dii nwu nkpo mawa ninmafua ye.
Fɛ mmle di okũ ndiki ni bɔkɛɛ.
Diekye dibawa di batii bamuu suoto kaayi ka mmle kamɛ.
Nkpo oso bilolaa binyu, biɛtɔɔpɛ ɔlaa bitɔɔta Yaa alɛ biawɛ osie minfe di asaa ya mmle nimawa ni amuu kamɛ, alɛ biakyɔɔ di ami Otii Obi nwu anu di leklekle kamɛ di lɛkankoyi nwu suoto.” Di ayi nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yesu latuo batii asaa di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu kamɛ, kafɔɔ nse kɔtɔɔfɔ lewo, andie ansifi Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote suoto anaasiɛ kakyɛ.
Di kolesɛtũ biala batii nwu nkpo bamuu ntaka mankyɛ Yaa Olekatakɔ mananu nwɔ asaa otuo.
Yaa Oletatɛ Ku Banɔɔfo Lakpee Asi Baawo Alɛ Baalo Yesu.
Bloblo wɔ ninantaka ni, manlɛɛ ni Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole bee latɛɛtɛɛ.
Olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ latɔyɛkɛ ni batii nwu nkpo oso, baatoomiɛ osuku wɔ suoto baafe manlo ni Yesu di lewofa kamɛ.
Yuda Latuna Alɛ Abadiki Yesu Anta.
Ninfɛ di Abonsam labuo di Yuda wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Iskariot kamɛ nɛ.
Yesu basaateketetɛ lefosi batii banyɔ onwii lɛma aale.
Nkpo oso Yuda lasifi olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku Yaa Olekatakɔ banyuntɛ banɔɔfo nfũ.
Ni aalaakakatɛko ma di osuku wɔ suoto abafe andiki Yesu anta ma ni nɛ.
Suoto layɔɔ ma nwaa, ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ babatɔɔ koto nɛ.
Ni di Yuda latuna nɛ.
Nkpo oso aakye kasɔ aatoomiɛ osuku wɔ suoto abafe andiki Yesu anta ni baatii dilabatofo nii.
Yesu Lalolaa Suoto Aata Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii Alesaa.
Nni kama, dii le manlo ni lefosobi di Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii labawo di bloblo wɔ ninantaka ni ayi ole kamɛ.
Ni di Yesu lakpee Petro ku Yohane aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitɔɔkyɛ biɛlaawa Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa bitawo buɔbale.” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔfɛ foomiɛ falɛ bulaawa alesaa nwu buse?” Ninfɛ aadiki kanya alɛ, “Nse biebuo Yerusalem okpoo kamɛ, osuɔtɔ onwii mawa amakyakako ye atuka ntu dibukii.
Bitikanko nwɔ biɛlaabuo leyo le kamɛ ababuo ni.
Biɛkaalɛ leyo nwu saate bilɛ, ‘Saatuotɛ alɛ bukaalɛ fɔ nii, “Lɛmɛnyo kamɛ di ami ku basaateketetɛ nii, bubasiɛ munle Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa?” ’ Abatuo ye leyo dibinte ninwii beetofo beetika ni di osi, nfũ beelolaa, beese ni asiɛsaa.
Biwa miɛ dii nwu alesaa ninfa bita wo.” Baakyɛ baalaanya fɛ mmle di Yesu latɔkɔ ma nii.
Ni baawa Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa nwu ninfa baase nɛ.
Baale Saate Nwu Kɔtɔɔfɔ Alesaa.
Di obe nwu lawo nii, Yesu ku batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ lasiɛ kaasɔ di opunu katũ babale ni alesaa.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Dile mi dibiesaa alɛ kaleko ye Okpi Diisi Ofe alesaa ya mmle fiɛ kafe diibuo kamɛ.
Diekye kɔtɔkɔ ye ntikiti nlɛ, noosinwa nya ɔbale diɛlaase di obe wɔ di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu lɛwa nii.” Nni kamaa, ni di Yesu layɔ opũ ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa aabuɛ alɛ, “Bifũ nle mmle bienyi bita baawo.
Diekye kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ diɛyɔ ni nunua diesifi nii, noosinwa nta be mmle okle onyi diediki Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu lɛwa.” Ninfɛ aayɔ bloblo ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa nɛ.
Ni aafee, aayɔ aata ma, aabuɛ alɛ, “Nle mmle ninle suoto nii sina se bɛɛyɔ bɛɛta ni diisi lee nɛ.
Bibla nle mmle, biɛyɔ bitoonyuma mi.” Nkpo okle kafɔɔ, di alesaa nwu nkpo kamaa, aayɔ opũ nwu, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Opũ wɔ mmle ninle kanya ninii fɔle le di Yaa lɛyɔ ntɔ nii eese ni kaanya, beewii ni kaasɔ di disi lee nɛ.
Kafɔɔ binyu lo, otii wɔ nimadiki mi anta ni lekpee kɔnɛɛ kaasɛfɛ ninfũ oolekoe alesaa.
Ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo, makpi fɛ mmle di Yaa lɛtɛ nii.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimadiki mi anta nii, ayɔɔsa!” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu lakyako bawo ɔkaalɛ alɛ, owe mɔ kaamɛ lɛma nimabla lɛsaa le mmle okle.
Owe Ninlenke Di Basaateketetɛ Bamuu Kamɛ?
Kananfi kanwii lababuo di basaateketetɛ nwu kamɛ alɛ, owe lɛma boonyu alɛ alenke baamuu lɛma kamɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Batii ba ninanle ni Yuda batii, baka lɛma kole sɛsaate di batii lɛma suoto.
Batunletɛ ba mmle nkpe lɛyooto mammiɛ alɛ batii ba mmle katɔɔlɛɛ ma ni dile ni basiɛwo.
Kafɔɔ diele nkpo dikpe ni ninte kaamɛ lee.
Kafɔɔ nwɔ ninle ni ɔnɔɔfo kaamɛ lee dikpe nii ambla suoto fɛle obisɔ.
Nwɔ kafɔɔ ninle ni tunletɛ kabla suoto fɛle kpɛmblatɛ.
Owe ninle ɔnɔɔfo, nwɔ ninsiɛ ni kaasɔ anle ni alesaa ɛɛ, sɛɛ nwɔ ninse ni opunu?
Kamɛ lɛkpa klekle alɛ nwɔ ninsi oole ni alesaa ninle ɔnɔɔfo.
Kafɔɔ nsi ye kaamɛ fɛle kpɛmblatɛ.
Biakpee situ biatikankoe di abuo nii amuu kamɛ.
Nioso fɛ mmle di Teemi lɛtɛɛ otumi alɛ kale ni sɛka, nkpo okle kafɔɔ mata ye otumi nwu nɛ.
Bibale alesaa minnyi di alesaa nii kalekɔ di sɛka nii kalekɔ.
Bibasiɛ di akakpomii suoto minnle sɛka di Israel nfaabi lefosi nnyɔ nwu suoto.” Yesu Labuɛ Aatɛ Alɛ Petro Masĩ Nwɔ.
Yesu latɔkɔ Simon Petro alɛ, “Simon, Simon, Satana lɛkaalɛ osuku alɛ ɔɔsɔ ye annyu, ansɛ abiene andiki di alalaale kamɛ fɛ mmle di fekpɛntɛ nfɛɛlɛ kufuo andiki ni kaamɔɔ kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ ntɔɔpɛ ɔlaa lɛta Yaa diisi lɛfɔ Simon, alɛ ofũ onu lɛfɔ dilaayu.
Alɛ nse fɛɛpɛ feekple fɛɛwa ɔkyɛ nii, faakpee babilee suɔtɔbi osie.” Ninfɛ di Petro latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, lelolaa suoto nlɛ munko fɔ buate leeyo, nkpi ku afɔ!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Petro, kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, kakyɛ ka mmle fiɛ di kɔɔkɔ mabo nii, fababuɛ sitiɛ simu falɛ faaye mi.” Koto Katofoee Ku Kokpetetofo Ku Kapamii Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Obe onwii kamɛ lakpee ye ni kɔtɔ, bitaklee ni koto katofoe ku kokpetetofo ku ntokota, lɛsaa lewo lafĩ ye?” Ninfɛ baadiki kanya alɛ, “Lɛsalɛsaa ditafĩ wo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kafɔɔ nunua otii lele ninkpe koto katofoe kawo ee kokpetetofo kowo, aayɔ aklee.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ ninnaa ni kapamii, ayɔ awu nɔɔ asunsũ alaaya kapami kawo.
Diekye kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Kɔkpana Klekle ɔlaa wɔ kuobuɛ nii alɛ, ‘Bababu nwɔ mankpee di bakpileblatɛ kamɛ,’ dikpe nii diɛwa kaanya.
Diekye ɔlaa wɔ bɛɛkpana ni di suoto nii, nwaako nfɛ diɔɔwa kaanya.” Ni basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, nnya mpamii nnyɔ!” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Mminkpo mpɔ.” Yesu Lapɛ Ɔlaa Aata Yaa Di Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote Suoto.
Yesu ladie di okpoo aasifi Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote osi fɛ mmle ambla nii.
Ni baasaateketetɛ nɔɔ kafɔɔ latikanko nwɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ baadu ni lɛba nwu nkpo, Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bipɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa alɛ bilaabuo di ɔsɔ onyu kamɛ.” Ni aadiɛ ma aakyɛ sitũ kɛɛkɛ, ni aapɛ akunkyi aapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa nɛ.
Ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Teete, nse dilɛfɔ, ni faata dibuo opũ wɔ mmle kufe mi.
Kafɔɔ diele dibiesaa nii, ta dibiesaa lɛfɔ diwa kaanya.” Ninfɛ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ onwii lakyɔɔ aakye osi abakpee nwɔ osie nɛ.
Ni aakple aapɛ ɔlaa aata Yaa osie kanya ku dibuo di otu kamɛ.
Apipi ya niatoosoo aatookpete ni kaasɔ late fɛ ntɔ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu laloo ni ɔlaa ɔpɛ ɔta Yaa, aataka aawa basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nfũ, aabanya ma baatɔɔkyɔsĩi.
Ta lɛhaale niatika ma ni di suoto oso.
Ninfɛ aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Be lɛsaa oso biɔkyɔsĩi?
Bitaka biɛpɛ ɔlaa bita Yaa mmle minaabuo ni di ɔsɔ onyu kamɛ.” Ole Batatɛ Banɔɔfo Lata Baamufũ Yesu.
Obe wɔ di Yesu n-yɛ ɔɔkakatɛ nii, batii dikudi ninwii niakye baawa.
Yuda wɔ niale ni saateketetɛ di lefosi banyɔ nwu kamɛ nialeko ma katũ.
Ni aakyɛ Yesu nfũ alɛ ɔɔlaaminko nwɔ ambla nwɔ aatuu nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Yuda, atuu ɔbla fɔɔyɔ fandiki ami, Otii Obi nwu, fanta?” Obe wɔ di basateketetɛ nwu lanya lɛsaa le nimawa nii, baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, bublako mpamii loo ɔkpɛ?” Ninfɛ di saateketetɛ onwii layɔ kapamii aasafɔ Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo kpɛmblatɛ nɔɔ koletanɛɛ kotoko aakpa nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Oowo!
Tambla nkpo!” Ninfɛ di Yesu layɔ kɔnɛɛ aatika di kpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo kotoko, ni kuakple kuate fɛ mmle kuate ni nɛ.
Ni di Yesu lakaalɛ olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku Olekatakɔ banyuntɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo nwu niawa nwɔ ni omufũ alɛ, “Be oso di mpamii ku nwosoku bikle biɛwa mi omufũ fɛle kpileblatɛ nɔɔfo nle?
Lasiɛ di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo dii biala, kafɔɔ bitatɔkɔ bilɛ biomufũ mi.
Kafɔɔ Yaa niɛta ye osuku wɔ mmle.
Ni di Satana ditunu kamɛ otumi kole sɛka nunua nɛ.” Petro Lasĩ Yesu.
Baamufũ Yesu ni baakpaa nwɔ baasifiko Oletatɛ Nɔɔfo leyo nɛ.
Petro latikanko nwɔ sɛɛmaa fanfa.
Batii bawo lakutaa ɔtɔ di leyo nwu nkpo kaflɔnkɔ, ni di Petro kafɔɔ lakyɛ aalaasiɛ ma kaamɛ aatɔɔwɔfɔ ɔtɔ nwu nɛ.
Obe wɔ di ɔsanko kpɛmblatɛ onwii lanya Petro nsi ni di ɔtɔ nwu katũ, ni aanyu nwɔ tuwĩi aakyɔɔ nwɔ lɛnɛɛ aabuɛ alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle kafɔɔ Yesu tikankotɛ ale.” Kafɔɔ Petro lasĩ aabuɛ alɛ, “Ɔsanko, diidii ninye nwɔ!” Di obe kakuii sɛmaa, osuɔtɔ onwii kafɔɔ lanya Petro ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔɔ onwii lɛma fale!” Kafɔɔ Petro lakple aadiki kanya alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ, kpa woo!
Ninye nwɔ!” Diabla ni fɛ lebombo ninwii sɛmaa, osuɔtɔ bamba onwii lakple aabuɛ osie kanya aatika difuɔ alɛ, “Ɔlaa ɔnanfi kuonwii nnaa alɛ osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle diele Yesu tikankotɛ, diekye Galilea otii ale!” Kafɔɔ Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ, ninye ɔlaa wɔ foobuɛ nii!” Nfanwu ayɛ ɔɔkatatɛ nii, kɔɔkɔ niabo.
Nfanwu di Saate lamunikĩi aanyu Petro tuwĩi nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Petro lanyuma ɔlaa wɔ di Saate latɔkɔ nwɔ ni alɛ, “Fiɛ di kɔɔkɔ mabo ni ku kakyɛ ka, fababuɛ sitiɛ simu falɛ faaye mi.” Ni di Petro ladie aasifi kayi aalaawi kaku osie kanya nɛ.
Yuda Batii Asaa Banyuntɛ Lama Yesu Baapɛ Nwɔ.
Batii ba niatoonyu ni Yesu, baama nwɔ, baapɛ nwɔ kafɔɔ.
Baanii nwɔ anu baapɛ nwɔ, ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Owe niɛpɛ fɔ?
Tɔkɔ wo!” Ni baatufa nwɔ kafɔɔ di sisuku bamba kpinwu suoto nɛ.
Baakpaa Yesu Baawako Bakantɛ Nwu.
Obe wɔ kaale lasɛ nii, okpoo banɔɔfo ku olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku kufiofa batuotɛ labasi, ni baakpaa Yesu baawako bawokalɛɛkɔ nwu nkpo nɛ.
Di bawo kalɛɛkɔ nwu, ni baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Tɔkɔwo nsɛ afɔ ninle Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ.” Ninfɛ aadiki kanya alɛ, “Mintɛ lɛtɔkɔ ye, bilɔɔwa mi ɔbafũ onu.
Ni nse lɛkaalɛ ye ɔlaa owo kafɔɔ, bilɔɔwa mi kanya okpee.
Kafɔɔ diɛyɔ ni di nua diesifi nii, ami, Otii Obi nwu, masiɛ di Yaa wɔ ninlenke ni oletanɛɛkyɛ.” Ninfɛ bamuu lɛma baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Nioso afɔ ninle Yaa Obi nwu nɛ?” Ninfɛ aadiki kanya alɛ, “Aye bamu nikobuɛ bilɛ nnwɔɔ nle nɛ.” Ni baabuɛ alɛ, “Diesinfĩ alɛ otii kuonwii kayila ɔlaa owo kamaa!
Awo bamu butoonu ɔlaa wɔ eebuɛ nii!”
Baakpaa Yesu Baawako Pilato Nfũ Aakaalɛ Nwɔ Sɛlaa.
Nfanwu batii dikudi nwu lataka baakpaa Yesu baasifiko Pilato nfũ.
Nfa baakyako nwɔ kanya obudi alɛ, “Buomufũ osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle ɔɔkyɔnkyɔ batii loo anfenko di osuku lalaale suoto.
Ɔɔtɔkɔ ma alɛ batanta akpooto lɛma baata Roma Batii Ɔka Kplɛ, ni aatɔkɔ ma kafɔɔ alɛ nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ, ni ɔka ale.” Ni di Pilato lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Yuda batii Ɔka nwu nɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nnwu fatoobuɛ nɛ.” Ni di Pilato latɔkɔ olebatatɛ ku batii dikudi nwu nkpo alɛ, “Ninya okpile kuonwii di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle suoto baalo nwɔ ni lɛpɔɔ.” Kafɔɔ baayila osie kanya baabuɛ alɛ, “Asaa otuo nɔɔ kokpee kudu di Yuda batii kamɛ.
