Aakye kasɔ di Galilea, ni atɔɔwa ɛɛbadu nfũ kafɔɔ nɛ.” Baakpaa Yesu Baakyɛnko Herode Nfũ Aakaalɛ Nwɔ Sɛlaa.
Obe wɔ di Pilato lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, aakaalɛ alɛ, “Ni osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle Galilea otii ale?” Nkpo oso obe wɔ aatofo alɛ Yesu lekye ni Galilea kale kakyɛ ka di Herode kole ni sɛka, ni aakyesee nwɔ Herode nfũ nɛ.
Herode wɔ mmle lawɛ di Yerusalem di obe nwu kamɛ.
Suoto layɔɔ Herode di obe wɔ aanya ni Yesu.
Diekye atoonu nwɔ leyooto kofokofoko, aatoomiɛ kafɔɔ alɛ aanyɔɔ.
Aatoonyu osuku kafɔɔ alɛ aanya Yesu kɔbla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ.
Nkpo oso Herode lakaalɛ Yesu sɛlaa kpinwu, kafɔɔ Yesu ditadiki ɔlaa kuonwii kanya.
Nioso olebatatɛ ku kufiofa batuotɛ ladie baawa sitũ bababudi Yesu kanya, osie kanya.
Herode ku bakpɛtɛ nɔɔ lama Yesu osie kanya baatufa nwɔ.
Ni baayɔ awukyɔ biene biene anwii baakpee nwɔ, ni baakplesɔɔ baasifiko Pilato nfũ nɛ.
Dii nkpo kale, Herode ku Pilato lakple basiɛwo.
Diekye saa, bawo balo baale.
Pilato Lalo Yesu Lɛpɔɔ Alɛ Eesiɛko Kukpi.
Pilato lalɛɛ olebatatɛ, okpoo banɔɔfo ku batii bamuu aasiisa.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biɛkpaa osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle biɛwakoe bilɛ, ɔɔkyɔnkyɔ ye afenko di osuku lalaale suoto.
Ntoowolaa ɔlaa nwu kamɛ di anu lee.
Kafɔɔ ninnya okpile kuonwii di sɛlaa se biebuɛ bietika nwɔ ni di suoto.
Herode kafɔɔ diɛnya okpile kuonwi di suoto nɔɔ fiɛ ɛɛkplesa nwɔ eekyesee wo.
Otii wɔ mmle diɛbla okpile kuonwii baalo nwɔ lɛpɔɔ manta ni kukpi.
Nkpo oso mata mampɛ nwɔ, nindiɛ nwɔ ansifi.” Di Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole biala kamɛ, Pilato lɛblasaa dile andiɛ leyotentɛ onwii anta ma.
Nfa nfɛ baamuu lɛma baayiisa kudu osie kanya alɛ, “Lo nwɔ!
Faadiɛ Baraba fata wo!” Baraba wɔ mmle, baatɛ nwɔ leeyo di kudu kowo aakpee ni di okpoo kplɛ kamɛ aalo ni batii bawo oso.
Pilato lamiɛ alɛ oodiɛ ni Yesu oso, aakple aalaakakatɛ aata batii nwu nkpo.
Kafɔɔ baakple baayiisa kudu baalenkeesa kɔkasale alɛ, “Pɛ nwɔ sibuɛ fakaasa koowoso suoto!
Pɛ nwɔ sibuɛ fakaasa koowoso suoto!” Ninfɛ di Pilato lakple aakaalɛ ma ditiɛfa alɛ, “Ɔmɛnkpile ɛɛbla fiɛ?
Ninnya lɛsaa le ɛɛbla ni oso kalo nwɔ lɛpɔɔ alɛ aakpi nii!
Mata mampɛ nwɔ kowesee nindiɛ nwɔ ansifi.” Kafɔɔ mia nfɛ baakple baatɔɔfaa osie kanya baatoobuɛ alɛ, “Dikpe nii fɛɛta bɛɛpɛ Yesu sibuɛ bɛɛkaasa koowoso suoto.” Lɛyɛntɛle kudu lɛma nwu labalenkee Pilato nnɛɛ.
Nkpo oso Pilato lababudisa ɔlaa nwu nkpo fɛ mmle baatii nwu komiɛ nii.
Ni aadiɛ otii wɔ boomiɛ ni aata ma nɛ.
Nwɔ baatɛ ni leeyo ta kudu ko aakpee, aalo ni batii oso.
Ni aadiɛ Yesu aakpee ma ninnɛɛ kamɛ alɛ balaabla nwɔ fɛ mmle boomiɛ ni.
Bakpɛtɛ Lapɛ Yesu Sibuɛ Baakaasa Koowoso Suoto.
Bakpɛtɛ lakpaa Yesu baasifiko.
Ni di obe wɔ bakyɛ di osuku boofe nii, baakyakako Kirene otii onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Simon aakye kakpaayotũ ɔɔwa Yerusalem.
Ni baayilasa nwɔ, baanyinka nwɔ alɛ afũ Yesu kowoso nwu atuka.
Ni aafũ aatikanko Yesu nɛ.
Batii dikudi lewo latikanko Yesu di nkpaamaa, basanko bawo kafɔɔ lasiɛ ma kaamɛ baatoowi kaku baatɔɔtɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lamunikĩi aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Yerusalem basanko, bitanwi biatɛɛ, kafɔɔ biwi bita suoto ku babilee.
Diekye ayi awo kɔwa baatii mabuɛ alɛ, ‘Suoto siyɔɔ ɔlɛma ku olofofɔtɔ wɔ kamɛ di obi didie ni diidii ku lɛnyɛɛ le manayinyɛɛfu ni diidii!’ Obe nwu ninle obe wɔ batii matɔkɔ abokote alɛ, ‘Bibiɛ bikpete wo!’ Mantɔkɔ kobokotee kafɔɔ alɛ, ‘Biwofasa wo!’ Diekye nse kowoso kɔɔnle kofiɛ mmle okle mɔ, ni lɛ kookosole mafiɛ?” Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, bakpɛtɛ nwu lakpaa basuɔtɔ banyɔ banwii ninle ni bakpileblatɛ baakyakaa di Yesu, boofenko olo.
Obe wɔ baadu ni lɛba le bɔɔlɛɛ ni Otii Disi Dikufi, baapɛ Yesu sibuɛ baakaasa koowoso suoto ninfa, ku bakpileblatɛ banyɔ.
Baapɛ onwii baakaasa di Yesu oletanɛɛkyɛ, ɔnyɔɔfa kafɔɔ di ɔmɛntukyɛ.
Ni di Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Teete, yɔ fakyɛ ma, diekye baaye lɛsaa le bɔɔbla nii.” Nni kamaa, baayɔ awu nɔɔ baasɛ bawo di obe wɔ baawii ni atrebi baatofo n-ya di obiala lɛma kayɔ nii.
Batii dikudi nwu nkpo layila baatoonyu nwɔ.
Ni di Yuda batii batunletɛ nwu kafɔɔ layila baatɔɔma Yesu baatoobuɛ alɛ, “Aafũ batii bamba nkpa, bita afũ suoto nɔɔ kafɔɔ, nse nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo wɔ di Yaa lɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ!” Nkpo okle di bakpɛtɛ nwu kafɔɔ lama Yesu nɛ.
Baayɔ nta nyankale baakyɛnko nwɔ alɛ anyi.
Ni baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse afɔ ninle Yuda batii ɔka, faafũ suoto lɛfɔ nkpa buonyu!” Di lɛkantosi nɔɔ, baakpana sɛlaa se mmle alɛ, “Nnya Yuda Batii Ɔka ninle nwɔ nɛ.” Bakpileblatɛ banyɔ ba baapɛ baakasa ni koowoso suoto onwii lɛma latufa Yesu alɛ, “Diele afɔ ninle Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ?
Diki suoto faadiki wo kafɔɔ ɛɛ!” Kafɔɔ ɔnyɔɔfa lasĩ ɔlaa aatɔɔ aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Fɔlɔɔyɛkɛ Yaa?
Beelo fɔ lɛpɔɔ fɛ mmle okle beelo nwɔ ni lɛpɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ awo lɛpɔɔ le beelo wo nii, lesiɛko wo.
Diekye lɛsaa le buɔbla ni letokonanfi buofũ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nnwɔɔ aabla okpile kuonwii.” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Yesu, nyuma mi nse feebuo sɛka lɛfɔ ole kamɛ.” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, miɛ wɔ mmle, munko fɔ bubabuo Paradiso kamɛ.” Baalo Yesu.
Di obe wɔ diapɛ ni fɛ kakũ lefosi elomu ɛnyɔ, kufĩ ladiɛ ɔpɛ, kayi kamuu lawɔfɔ, dialaase di kɔtɔɔfɔ elomu etiɛ kamɛ.
Ni di dibula le niasaka ni di Yaa Olekatakɔ labɛ di nkyɛ nnyɔ nɛ.
Ni di Yesu lafaa osie kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Teete, leyɔ ninwuna nii, lekpee di nnɛɛ lɛfɔ kamɛ.” Obe wɔ aabuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle aaloo nii, ni aakpi nɛ.
Baakpɛtɛ ɔnɔɔfo nwu lanya lɛsaa le niawa nii, ni aatansa Yaa aabuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako otii wɔ mmle, otii biene ale.” Obe wɔ baatii ba niawa ni nfa alɛ bɔɔbaanyu lɛsaa le nikɔwa ni lanya ni lɛsaa le niawa nii, baakple baasifi ayo, baayɔ nnɛɛ baatika nintɛɛ ku sɛyaami.
Batii ba bamuu ninye ni Yesu ku basanko ba niatikanko nwɔ baakye ni Galilea layila kaakyonkɔ baatoonyu asaa.
Yosef Arimatea Otii Niakookaa Yesu.
Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Yosef.
Aakye Arimatea di Yudea kasɔ suoto.
Aale otii biene wɔ baatii mbu ni osie kanya.
Aasiɛ aatoonyu osuku obe wɔ di Yaa sɛka kalekɔ mawa nii.
Mintɛ aale Yuda batii Bakantɛ onwii lɛma yi, atatunako ma di disibu le baabla ni ku lɛsaa le baabla ni suoto.
Aakyɛ Pilato nfũ aalaafũ Yesu kpi.
Ni aasoosa kpi nwu nkpo di kowoso suoto aayɔ dibula fututu aamiminisa nwɔ di suoto.
Ni aayɔ nwɔ aalaakookaa di ofuɔnntuu ɔkya wɔ kamɛ manayikookaa ni otii kuonwii kaamɛ diidii nɛ.
Dii nwu nkpo Fiida diale, baatoololaa suoto baatɔɔta Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi kale ɔsɛ.
Basanko ba niatikanko Yesu baakye ni Galilea latikanko Yosef baakyɛ baalaanyu ɔkya nwu ku mmle baayɔ Yesu baakookaa ni kaamɛ.
Ni baakple baasifi leyo, baalaabla kɔfa kɔnɔkɔnɔ ku nnɔnyi be man-yɔ manfifia ni di kpi suoto baatɛ.
Ni baatɛ ɔnyɛɛ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto fɛ mmle di Yuda batii kufiofa nwu letuo ni nɛ.
Yesu Lataka Aakye Bakpi Kamɛ.
Di Kɔsida kolesɛtũ, basanko nwu lakyɛ ɔkya nwu katũ, baaklee kɔfa kɔnɔkɔnɔ ko baabla baase nii.
Ni baanya alɛ baamunusa difuɔ nwu di ɔkya kanya nɛ.
Nkpo oso baabuo di ɔkya nwu kamɛ, kafɔɔ batanya Saate Yesu kpi nwu.
Lɛsaa nwu labla ma yaaa.
Nfanwu batii banyɔ banwii niakyɔɔ baakpee asaa fututu ya nikosesee ni di anu.
Basanko nwu layɛkɛ osie kanya, ni baawakosa asi kasɔ baata batii nwu nɛ.
Ni baatii nwu lakaalɛ, ma alɛ, “Be oso biowolaa otii wɔ ninkpe ni nkpa baakpi kamɛ?
Anaa ninfũ.
Atɔɔtaka!
Binyuma ɔlaa wɔ aatɔkɔ ye ni, di obe wɔ aawɛ ni di Galilea alɛ, ‘Dikpe nii, bɛɛyɔ Otii Obi nwu beekpee di bakpileblatɛ nnɛɛ kamɛ.
Bɛɛpɛ nwɔ sibuɛ bɛɛkaasa koowoso suoto.
Ni ayi atiɛ kamaa, abakple antaka ankye bakpi kamɛ.’ ” Ni baasanko nwu lanyuma sɛlaa nɔɔ nwu nkpo nɛ.
Baakple ni di ɔkya nwu katũ, baabuɛ sɛlaa se mmle simuu baatɔkɔ batɔkyɛntɛ lefosi onwii nwu ku babule bamuu.
Basanko nwu niale Maria Magdalene ku Yohana ku Maria wɔ ninle ni Yakobo ɔya.
Mma ku basanko bamba niatɔkɔ batɔkyɛntɛ nwu sɛlaa se mmle nɛ.
Kafɔɔ batɔkyɛntɛ nwu lanyu alɛ, sɛlaa se baasanko nwu lebuɛ nii, sɛlaakuu sile batafũ sĩ baanu.
Kafɔɔ Petro lataka aatoso aakyɛ ɔkya nwu katũ.
Obe wɔ aadu ni nfa aakɛnsa aanyu ɔkya nwu kamɛ, kafɔɔ akookaabula lete aanya, atansinnya lɛsalɛsaa.
Ni aakple aasifi leyo, diabla nwɔ yaaa di lesaa le niawa ni suoto.
Batii Bawo Lanya Yesu Di Emaus Osuku.
Di dii nwu nkpo kale kafɔɔ, Yesu batikankotɛ banyɔ banwii latoofe kakpaayotũ kanwii manlɛɛ ni Emaus kamɛ.
Diawo fɛ akɔ akuɛnsĩ diedie ni di Yerusalem.
Baatɔɔkakatɛko bawo di lɛsaa biala niawa ni suoto.
Obe wɔ bakyɛ bɔɔkakatɛ mambuo ni sɛɛlaa nwu kamɛ yi, Yesu omu lakpukuti aatɛɛtɛɛ ma, baakyako ɔkyɛ.
Baanyɔɔ, kafɔɔ batatofo alɛ nnwɔɔ diale.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Ɔmɛnlaa bikyɛ biobuɛ di osuku?” Ni baayila baabla anu ku sɛnyaami.
Ni di onwii kaamɛ lɛma bɔɔlɛɛ ni Kleopa lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Lete lɛfɔ ninle ɔfɔɔ di Yerusalem, fananye asaa ya niɛwa ni ninfa di ayi asɛɛ ya mmle kamɛ?” Ni di Yesu lakaalɛ alɛ, “Be lɛsaa niawa?” Ni baadiki kanya alɛ, “Asaa ya niawa ni di Yesu Nasaret Otii suoto.
Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ aale.
Nnwɔɔ di Yaa ku batii bamuu lɛnya alɛ, nwaako akpe otumi di asaa nɔɔ ɔbla ku sɛlaa nɔɔ obuɛ kamɛ nɛ.
Yuda batii Yaa olebatatɛ banɔɔfo ku okpoo banɔɔfo loo layɔ nwɔ baakpee di Roma abaa ɔnɔɔfo nnɛɛ kamɛ, aalo nwɔ kukpi lɛpɔɔ baakaasɔɔ koowoso suoto baalo.
Nse nnwɔɔ buotika anu bulɛ ale otii wɔ nimadiki ni Israel batii bamuu nɛ.
Ni nni nkpo kamaa, miɛ ninle dii tiɛfa di sɛlaa se mmle lawa ni nɛ.
Basanko bawo kafɔɔ lɛbatɔkɔ wo ɔlaa wɔ niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ.
Diekye bɛɛkyɛ ɔkya nwu katũ miɛ ku kolesɛtũ ko mmle.
Kafɔɔ baanya kpi nɔɔ.
Beekple bɛɛwa bɛɛbatɔkɔ wo alɛ Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ bawo lediki suoto beetuo ma.
Ni bɛɛtɔkɔ ma alɛ, Yesu nkpe nkpa nɛ.
Batii bawo lɛkyɛ ɔkya nwu katũ bɛɛlaanya fɛ mmle baasanko nwu lɛbabuɛ nii, kafɔɔ baanyɔɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biébe anu!
Lɛ oso di ofũ onu lee lɛbla buɛɛ di asaa ya di Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ nwu latɔkɔ ye ni suoto?
Bieye bilɛ dikpe ni Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ kafe diibuo le mmle kamɛ fiɛ ababuo di sɛka nɔɔ klekle nwu kamɛ?” Ni di Yesu ladiki kɔsa aata ma di sɛlaa se beebuɛ ni di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ di suoto nɔɔ nɛ.
Diɛyɔ ni di Mose obe diɛlase ni di Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛ bamuu obe suoto.
Obe wɔ nfɛ bɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ ni kakpaayotũ ka boofe nii, Yesu labla fɛ ɔɔwaalɛ anfe sitũ.
Kafɔɔ baasĩ baatɔɔ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kufĩ nfɛ mamɛɛ ni oso, akple aate di ɔkyɛ lɛma.” Nkpo oso aatikanko ma alɛ ɔɔlaate di ɔkyɛ lɛma.
Aasiɛ kaasɔ alɛ oole alesaa ku mma.
Ni aayɔ bloblo aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, ni aafee aayɔ aata ma nɛ.
Nfanwu anu lɛma niasɛkɛtɛ baanya Yesu baatɛ nsũ, kafɔɔ aayu di anu lɛma.
Ni baatoobuɛ baatɔɔtɔkɔ bawo alɛ, “Obe wɔ ɛɛtɔɔkakatɛ kowo ni di osuku eetoodiki Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kasɔ ɛɛtɔɔta wo nii, suoto diɛtɔɔyɔɔ wo di otu kamɛ?” Nfanwu ni baataka baakple baasifi Yerusalem nɛ.
Ni baanya batɔkyɛntɛ batii lefosi onwii nwu ku batii bamba beesi basi nɛ.
Ni baatɔkɔ batii nwu banyɔ alɛ, “Nwaako Saate nwu ntɔɔtaka eekye bakpi kamɛ, atoodiki suoto eetuo Simon.” Ninfɛ di batii nwu banyɔ kafɔɔ latɔkɔ ma lɛsaa le niawa ni di osuku suoto ku mmle baanyɔɔ baatɛ ni nsũ di obe wɔ aafee bloblo aata ma nii.
Yesu Ladiki Suoto Aatuo Basaateketetɛ Nɔɔ.
Obe wɔ baatii nwu nkpo banyɔ nkle ɔlaa lɛma boobuɛ manayiloo nii, nfanwu Yesu niadie aayila ma kaamɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Atoko ɔkyɛ ole disiɛko ye.” Lɛyɛkɛ lapɛ ma osie kanya alɛ kpi bɔɔnya.
Kafɔɔ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Be oso diisibu lee kɔkpɔkpɔtɔ nkpo?
Be oso minofũ binu?
Binyu mi nnɛɛ ku nkpaa.
Biɛkpankoe kafɔɔ binyu, bietofo bilɛ ami dile.
Diekye kpi nnaa suoto sina ku akufi, fɛ mmle biɔnya bilɛ nkpe nii.” Aabuɛ nwu aaloo nii, ni aatuo ma nnɛɛ ku nkpaa nɔɔ nɛ.
Suoto latɔɔyɔɔ ma osie kanya, di lɛsaa nwu labla ma ni ɔkpɛ, batafuo ofũ onu.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Lelesaa lewo nkpe ye ninfũ?” Ni baayɔ kakpaku fiɛle kawo baatɔɔ nɛ.
Ni aafũ aawee di anu lɛma nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nle mmle ninle asaa ya latɔkɔ ye ni di obe wɔ lawɛ ni di ɔkyɛ lee nɛ.
Lɛsaa lele bɛɛkpana beekyeko suoto nii di Mose kufiofa kukũ kamɛ, Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ akũ kamɛ ku sinu akũ kamɛ ntɔɔwa kaanya.” Ni aasɛkɛtɛ ma disibu baanu Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kasɔ nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bɛɛkpana bɛɛtɛ alɛ Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ mafe diibuo kamɛ, abataka ankye bakpi kamɛ di dii tiɛfa suoto.
Ni leeyooto nɔɔ kamɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kayie lɛkya manta nnle mmuu alɛ baakyisa situ, alɛ Yaa kayɔ sikpile lɛma ankyɛ ma.
Lɛkya le mmle oyie makye kasɔ di Yerusalem.
Aye ninle sɛlaa se mmle kamaa bayilatɛ kaakɔ lele nɛ.
Ami omu mayɔ lɛsaa le di Teemi lebuɛ ɛɛtɛ alɛ abata ye ni nkyesee ye.
Kafɔɔ bisiɛ di Yerusalem okpoo kamɛ diɛlaase di obe wɔ di otumi makye osi kumabuo ye ni kaamɛ.” Yaa Lakpaa Yesu Aasifiko Osi.
Nni kamaa, Yesu lakpaa basateketetɛ nwu adieko di Yerusalem okpoo kamɛ aasifiko Betani ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Ni aakplesa nnɛɛ katoo aatama dikusɛkusɛ nɛ.
Di obe wɔ ɔɔta ma ni dikusɛkusɛ ninfa, ni baabla baawo suoto nɛ, ni di Yaa lakpaa nwɔ aasifiko osi nɛ.
Ninfɛ baapɛ akunkyi basumu nwɔ, ni baakple baasifi Yerusalem ku suoto lɛyɔɔ nimu nɛ.
Ni baatɔɔkyɛ Yaa Olekatakaɔ wlawla baalaatɔɔtansa Yaa nɛ.
Ɔlaa Wɔ Ninta Ni Nkpa.
Kaasɔ kakyeko fiɛ bababla ni kayi ka mmle yi, Ɔlaa nwu lawɛ.
Nnwu ku Yaa niawɛ.
Ɔlaa nwu nkpo kafɔɔ ninle Yaa nɛ.
Diayɔ ni kaasɔ kakyekɔ yi, Ɔlaa nwu ku Yaa niawɛ.
Ɔlaa nwu suoto di Yaa lafe aabla lɛsaa biala nɛ.
Lɛsalɛsaa kuninwii nnaa alɛ diele Ɔlaa nwu nkpo suoto beefe fiɛ bɛɛbla ni nii.
Ɔlaa nwu kamɛ di nkpa lɛtaa diekye nɛ.
Nkpa nwu nkpo kafɔɔ lɛyɔ lɛkpa diɛwako batii bamuu.
Lɛkpa le mmle kafɔɔ lɛkpa di ditunu kamɛ.
Ditunu kafɔɔ diefuo lɛkpa le mmle otĩi.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yaa lakyesee otii onwii.
Leyooto nɔɔ ninle Yohane nɛ.
Nnwɔɔ niawa aabakakatɛ aata batii di lɛkpa nwu nkpo suoto nɛ, alɛ batii bamuu kanu ɔlaa nɔɔ nwu alɛ, baafũ mannu.
Diele Yohane wɔ mmle ninle lɛkpa nwu nkpo.
Nnwɔɔ ɔwa ko aawa aabakakatɛ di lɛkpa nwu nkpo suoto.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, lɛkpa le nimu nimu ninkpa ninta ni batii bamuu nfɛ kɔwa kayi ka mmle kamɛ.
Ɔlaa nwu nkpo lawɛ kaayi ka mmle kamɛ, kafɔɔ kayi ka mmle ditatofo nwɔ, nu ninnwɔɔ suoto di Yaa lafe aabla kayi ka mmle.
Aawa nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ batii nfũ, kafɔɔ batii nɔɔ nwu nkpo ditafukuti nnɛɛ baafũ nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ batii ba bamuu niafũ nwɔ nii, baafũ nwɔ kafɔɔ baanu nii, ɛɛta ma osuku alɛ, baale Yaa babi.
Batalofo batii ba mmle fɛ mmle okle di osuɔtɔ ku ɔsanko nnya bawo fiɛ manlofo ni babi, ee otii dibiesaa kanya.
Kafɔɔ Yaa omu nfɛ nietuna alɛ baale nwɔ babi.
Ɔlaa nwu nkpo lɛbakple otii kuasiɛ wo kaamɛ, nwaako ole ku sibualɛ leyii nwɔ kamɛ pɔ.
Buanya kafɔɔ Lɛkpa nɔɔ.
Lɛkpa le aafũ aakyeko ni Ote nfũ ta Obi onwii ale nwɔ ni oso.
Yohane lakakatɛ aata batii aakyeko nwɔ suoto, aafaa aabuɛ alɛ, “Nnya otii wɔ mmle suoto labuɛ nlɛ, ‘Otii wɔ nikɔwa ni sɛɛmaa nii lɛtaka katoo alenke mi, diekye akpe kofokofoko fiɛ nfɛ bɛɛbabla mi.’ ” Ta sibualɛ ku nwaako ɔlaa nwu leyii nwɔ ni kamɛ oso, obe lele oowii wo lɛyɔɔ.
Lɛkasale, Yaa layɔ kufiofa nɔɔ nwu aafenko di Mose suoto aata wo.
Kafɔɔ eele wo sibualɛ ku nwaako ɔlaa nwu nkpo diefe ni di Yesu Kristo suoto.
Otii kuonwii diinya Yaa anya diidii.
Diediki Obi nwu nkpo onwii ninkyɛkyɛ ni ku Yaa, akpe ni di Ote nfũ, nnwɔɔ niediki nwɔ eetuo batii nɛ.
Yohane Lakakatɛ Aata Batii Alɛ Diele Nnwɔɔ Ninle Kristo Nwu Nkpo.
Yuda batii batunletɛ lakpee olebatatɛ ku Lewi batii bawo baakye Yerusalem alɛ, bakyɛ baalaakaalɛ Yohane alɛ, nnwɔɔ owe ale.
Yohane ditasĩ kanya odiki, ni aatɔkɔ ma aatikiti alɛ, “Diele ami ninle Kristo nwu nkpo.” Ninfɛ di olebatatɛ nwu lakple baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni owe fale mɔ?
Afɔ ninle Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Elia?” Ninfɛ di Yohane ladiki kanya alɛ, “Diele nnwɔɔ nle.” Ninfɛ baakple baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ wɔ baabuɛ baatɛ alɛ abawa ni nɛ?” Ninfɛ aadiki kanya alɛ, “Oowo.” Nkpo oso baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ni tɔkɔwo otii wɔ fale ni.
Diekye dikpe ni buɔkplesa kanya buɔkyɛnko batii ba niekpee wo ni kɔtɔ.
Ɔmɛnlaa fakpe fambuɛ di suoto lɛfɔ?” Ninfɛ di Yohane ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, fɛ mmle okle di Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ Yesaia lakpana aatɛ nii, “Ami ninle otii wɔ sɛlɔ nikɔfaa ni di ɔfaafuu kamɛ simbuɛ ni alɛ, bilolaa osuku bitɛ bita Saate nwu ɔwabee nɛ.” Ninfɛ di batii ba baakpee ni kɔtɔ baakye ni Farisi batii kamɛ, baakaalɛ Yohane alɛ, “Nni, nse faale Kristo, ee Elia, ee Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ nwu nkpo mɔ, ni lɛ oso fookpeesa batii Yaa ntu?” Ninfɛ di Yohane ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ami yi, kokpeesa batii Yaa ntu, kafɔɔ otii onwii n-yɛ kaamɛ lee minanye nwɔ nii.
Nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ nintikankoe ni sɛɛmaa abawa ni nɛ, otii wɔ ninansiɛko alɛ bia kadiki nwɔ ni ntokokata sikũ.” Asaa ya mmle amuu lawa di Betania okpoo diɛ Yordan okle sɛmaa.
Nfa di Yohane latokpeesa batii Yaa ntu nɛ.
Yesu Ninle Yaa Oleɔta Lefosobi Nwu Nkpo Nɛ.
Di kale lasɛ nii, Yohane lanya Yesu latɔɔwa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, ni aabuɛ aatɔkɔ batii ba niayila nwɔ ni di ɔlɔɔkɔ alɛ, “Nnya Yaa Oleɔta Lefosobi nwu nkpo niɛwa ni kayi ka mmle alɛ ɔbatekete ni batii sikpile di suoto lɛma!
Nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ suoto latɔɔkakatɛ ni di obe wɔ labuɛ nlɛ, ‘Otii onwii kɔwa sɛmaa nii, nnwɔɔ ɛɛtakakatoo aleneke mi, diekye, akpe kofokofoko fiɛ bia bɛɛbabla mi.’ Ami omu kafɔɔ ntatofo nlɛ nnwɔɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ lɛwa kokpeesa batii Yaa ntu alɛ kadiki nwu ntuo Israel batii bamuu.” Ninfɛ di Yohane lakple aabuɛ di suoto nɔɔ alɛ, “Lanya Yaa Ninwuna kosoo ninkye osi, fɛ mmle di lɛlaapɔɔ nsoo nii, diabasiɛ nwɔ di suoto.
Kaasɔ kakyekɔ yi, ntatofo nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ Yaa wɔ niekpee mi alɛ makpeesa ni batii nɔɔ ntu yi, aatɔkɔ mi alɛ, ‘Otii wɔ suoto fabanya Ninwuna nii lesoo diɛbasiɛ ni di suoto nɔɔ yi, nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ nimakpeesa ni batii ku Ninwuna Klekle nɛ.’ Nkpo oso amii ntɔɔnya.
Nioso nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye ntikiti nlɛ nnwɔɔ ninle Yaa Obi nwu nkpo nɛ.” Nnya Basaateketetɛ Kasale Ba Niatikanko Ni Yesu.
Kaleesɛ yi, Yohane ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ banyɔ lakple baayila ninfa.
Obe wɔ aanya Yesu latoofe ni yi, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Nnya Yaa Oleɔta Lefosobi nwu nkpo!” Obe wɔ di Yohane basaateketetɛ banyɔ nwu nkpo lanu aabuɛ ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo yi, ni baasifi baalaatikanko Yesu nɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lamunikĩi aanya alɛ batikanko nwɔ nii, ni aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe lɛsaa biowolaa?” Ni baadiki kanya, baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Rabi,” leyooto le mmle lɛsɔdiki ninle alɛ Saatuotɛ, “Lekoto, ɔfɛ fasi?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Biwa biɛbanyu.” Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ diabla fɛ kɔtɔɔfɔ abombo ana.
Nkpo oso baatikanko nwɔ baakyɛ baalaanyu nfũ asi nii, ninfɛ baayɛntɛ nwɔ osiɛko dii nwu nkpo kale nɛ.
Basaateketetɛ nwu nkpo nianu ni Yohane ɔlaa wɔ aabuɛ fiɛ baatikanko ni Yesu onwii lɛma niale Andrea wɔ niale ni Simon Petro obilɛma nɛ.
Nfanwu ni aanya obilɛma Simon nɛ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Butɔɔnya Mesia nwu nkpo.” Ɔlaa wɔ mmle kasɔ ninle alɛ Kristo wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ aakpaa Simon aakyɛnko Yesu nɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lanyu ni Simon, ni aabuɛ alɛ, “Afɔ ninle Simon, Yohane Obi nɛ.
Kafɔɔ nunua yi, babatɔɔlɛɛ fɔ alɛ Kefas,” ee Petro, ayooto ya mmle lɛsɔdiki ninle alɛ difuɔnkpaa nɛ.
Yesu Lalɛɛ Filipo Ku Natanael Alɛ Baatikanko Nwɔ.
Obe wɔ kaale lasɛ nii, Yesu labla disibu alɛ ɔɔkyɛ Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Ni aanya osuɔtɔ onwii manlɛɛ ni Filipo nɛ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Wa fabatikankoe.” Filipo wɔ mmle lakye Betsaida, okpoo wɔ di Andrea ku Petro kafɔɔ lakye nii.
Obe wɔ di Filipo lakyɛ aalaanya ni Natanael, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Butɔɔnya otii wɔ suoto di Mose ku Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ lakpana asaa baakyeko ni di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ.
Nnwɔɔ ninle Yesu wɔ niekye ni Nasaret nɛ.
Yosef obi ale.” Ninfɛ di Natanael lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛsaa biene lewo kafuo odie okye Nasaret fiɛ?” Ninfɛ di Fililpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ yi, wa fabanyu!” Obe wɔ di Yesu lanya Natanael kɔwa ni ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, ni aabuɛ aakyeko di suoto nɔɔ alɛ, “Nnya Israel obi omu omu ninle nwɔ mmle nɛ.
Kakyɔnkyɔ kukanwii diesi nwɔ kaamɛ.” Obe wɔ di Natanael lanu ni ɔlaa wɔ mmle, ni aakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Lɛ diɛbla fiɛ faye mi?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ntɔɔnya fɔ kofokofoko di kubue nwu nkpo kalɔ fiɛ di Filipo lalɛɛ fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Natanael ladiki kanya aabuɛ aatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, nwaako afɔ ninle Yaa Obi nwu nkpo nɛ.
Israel Batii Ɔka ninle afɔ!” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ta mmle lɛtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ lɛnya fɔ ni di kubue nwu nkpo kalɔ oso fatoofũ feenu?
Ni fabanya asaa kplɛ ya niɛtaka katoo alenke ni nle mmle.” Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, fabanya mmle okle di kolo masɛkɛtɛ nii, di Yaa batɔkyɛntɛ matooyie mantoosoo ni di ami, Otii Obi nwu, suoto.”
Baayɔ Ɔsanko Di Kana Okpoo Kamɛ.
Di ayi atiɛ sɛmaa, baayɔ ɔsanko di okpoo wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Kana di Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Yesu ɔya lakyɛ nfa.
Ni baakyakako Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kafɔɔ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo kayɔkɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di nta be baatɔɔblako ni ɔkpɛ laloo nii, ninfɛ di Yesu ɔya lakyɛ Yesu nfũ aalaatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nta be bɔɔblako ni ɔkpɛ ntooloo ma.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ɔya alɛ, “Mma, diele afɔ nimatɔkɔ mi lɛsaa le dikpe ni lɛbla nii.
Diekye obe wɔ dikaatɛ alɛ lɛta ni lɛkyakaako diiwo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ɔya lakyɛ aalaatɔkɔ bakpɛmblatɛ ba niatɔɔblako ni nta nwu nkpo ɔkpɛ alɛ, “Lɛsaa lele ɛɛtɔkɔ ye alɛ bibla yi, biɛbla.” Yuda batii ɔsaabla kuale alɛ baafoto suoto fiɛ baabuo ayo.
Nkpo oso baase afuɔ sɛpɔɔlɔ kplɛ akuɔ ninfa, di ntu adubukii fɛ ana ee anɔɔ nikayii ni ninwii kamɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ bakpɛmblatɛ nwu alɛ, “Bidu ntu biyiisa sɛpɔɔlɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ.” Nkpo oso baadu ntu baakpete sĩ kaamɛ siayii tɛkɛtɛkɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ bakpɛmblatɛ nwu alɛ, “Bikusii ntu nwu nwo bikyɛnko osuɔtɔ nwu nin-yɛ ni di ɔsaabla nwu kanya.” Ninfɛ baakusii mi baakyɛnko nwɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di ɔnɔɔfo nwu nin-yɛ ni di ɔsaabla nwu nkpo kanya latu ntu be nintookple ni nta aanyu nii, atatofo nfũ di nta nwu nkpo lakye nii.
Kafɔɔ bakpɛmblatɛ nwu nkpo niakusii mi nii, mma, baatofo.
Nkpo oso ɔnɔɔfo nwu nkpo lalɛɛ ɔsanko nwu nkpo ɔsa, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Otii biala n-yɔ nta biene anta batii manyi, nse nfɛ boosiɛ fiɛ nfɛ an-yɔ mbe ninanlɛ ni anwako ma manyi.
Kafɔɔ afɔ mianwu nfɛ fɛɛyɔ mbiene fɛɛwako nɛ.” Nle mmle di Yesu labla ni di Kana okpoo di Galilea kasɔ ninle ɔkpɛ wɔ niabla ni ɔkpɛ kasale aabla ni aayɔ aadiki ni lɛkpa nɔɔ aatuo ni nɛ.
Ni di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lafũ nwɔ baanu nɛ.
Di nle mmle sɛmaa, Yesu ku ɔya ku babilɛma suɔtɔbi ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasifi Kapernaum, baalaasiɛ ninfa ayi asɛɛ awo.
Yesu Latososa Basaasunsutɛ Aadiki Di Yaa Olekatakɔ.
Ditoobu ayi asɛɛ di Yuda batii Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii olebee nfɛ mawo nii, Yesu lakyɛ Yerusalem.
Obe wɔ aakyɛ ni Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ, aalaanya batii kosunsũ banankyue ku bafoso ku ablonumaa.
Aanya kafɔɔ batii ba nikobiɛ ni ato nsi di sipunu lɛma katũ.
Nkpo oso aayɔ sikũ aaloso mpile, ni aatososa batii nwu nkpo ninkosunsũ ni babɔkɛɛ nwu ku banankyue ku bafoso nwu nkpo aadiki di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu kamɛ nɛ.
Ni aatukusa koto babiɛtɛ sipunu nwu aayu, aasamiisa koto nwu nkpo kafɔɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ batii ba niatoosunsũ ni ablonumaa alɛ, “Bidieko ma ninfũ bisifiko!
Biediɛ Teemi leyo ɔyɔ ɔbla asaa kasunsukɔ!” Nfa nfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lanyuma ɔlaa wɔ bɛɛkpana ni Kɔɔkpana Klekle Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, “O Yaa, lɛbɔmbɔ nii di Leyo lɛfɔ suoto lɛta ninu lɛsɛɛ mi.” Ta nle mmle oso, Yuda batii batunletɛ lawa Yesu nfũ babakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛmɛntuosaa faafuo ɔbla otuo wo alɛ fakpe osuku fambla lɛsaa le mmle?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bibiɛ Yaa Leyo le mmle bitɛ kaasɔ, di ayi atiɛ kamɛ yi, makple nse ni letofo.” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Be foobuɛɛ?
Obe wɔ bɛɛyɔ alɛɛ afosi ana alɛɛ akuɔ beetofo ni Leyo le mmle, fabayɔ ayi atiɛ fanse ni letofo?” Batanu ɔlaa wɔ mmle kasɔ.
Diekye leyo le suoto di Yesu latɔɔkakatɛ ni niale suoto nɔɔ sina nɛ.
Nioso, sɛmaa, obe wɔ di Yaa lasɛnkɛsa Yesu aakyeko ni bakpi kamɛ fiɛ nfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lanyuma alɛ aabuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle.
Nkpo oso baafũ Kɔkpana Klekle kamɛ sɛlaa se bɛɛkpana ni ku ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu labuɛ ni baanu.
Yesu N-ye Otii Letembi Kaasɔ Ka Mmle Suoto Osie Kanya.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lawɛ ni di Yerusalem di Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii olebee nwu kamɛ yi, batii kpinwu lafũ nwɔ baanu, di obe wɔ baanya ni sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ ate ate se aabla ni oso.
Kafɔɔ Yesu omu ditadiɛ suoto nnɛɛ ata ma, diekye aatofo batii nwu bamuu.
Nkpo oso ditafĩ alɛ otii kuonwii katɔkɔ nwɔ batii ba okle bale nii, diekye nnwɔɔ omu aye otii letembi kaasɔ ka mmle suoto.
Yesu Latuo Nikodemo Asaa.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, Yuda batii tunletɛ onwii lawɛ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Nikodemo.
Aasiɛ di dikudi le baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Farisi batii kamɛ.
Dii ninwii kakyɛ, aamaa buɛɛ aawa Yesu nfũ, ni aabaakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buye bulɛ Yaa nfũ feekye.
Diekye otii kuonwii dilabafuo sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ, fɔɔbla ni ɔbla, nse Yaa diesiko nwɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, nse baase otii lelofo yi, ɔlɔbafuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ ɔnya.” Ninfɛ di Nikodemo lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be foobuɛɛ?
Lɛ nse otii ntoomuɔ baakple manse nwɔ lelofo, sɛɛ okple aakple ansifi ɔya kafutu kamɛ, mankple manse nwɔ lelofo lɛnyɔɔfa?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ, nse baase otii lelofo di ntu ku Yaa Ninwuna kamɛ, ɔlɔbafuo Yaa sɛka kalekɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ obuo.
Diekye otii wɔ beefe di suoto sina kamɛ beelofo ni yi, suoto sina kamɛ otii ale.
Kafɔɔ nwɔ beelofo ni di Yaa Ninwuna kamɛ yi, ninwuna kamɛ otii ale.
Nkpo oso tanta diabla fɔ ɔkpɛ alɛ lɛtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ dikpe nii beese ye lelofo.
Kɔfɛɛfɔ nfɛ kunfe nfũ ninlɛkũ nii.
Fannukũ diwi, kafɔɔ fántofo nfũ kuokye nii, ku nfũ kuofe nii.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ dite ku otii wɔ beelofo ni di Ninwuna kamɛ nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Nikodemo lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Lɛ ninle mmle kamafuo ɔwa kaanya?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ kplɛ fale di Israel batii kamɛ.
Ni be oso floonu asaa ya mmle kasɔ?
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ fɔ nlɛ munkakatɛ di asaa ya buye ni suoto, asaa ya butɔɔnya ni kafɔɔ mun-yɔ kanya loo mundiki mumbuɛ.
Kafɔɔ kuonwii lee dilootuna alɛ afũ ɔlaa wɔ lɛkya buoyie ni anu.
Nse lɛkakatɛ di kayi ka mmle asaa suoto lɛta fɔ fananfũ mi fanu mɔ, ni lɛ dibabla nse lekakatɛ lɛta fɔ di Yaa kafa asaa suoto fiɛ fabafũ mi fannu?
Otii kuonwii diikata akyɛ osi anya, dilenkee ami, Otii Obi nwu lete niakye osi aawa kasɔ ka mmle nwu suoto.
“Fɛ mmle okle di Mose latakatɛsa kɔsaanwu ko baayɔ lɛbɔɔsaa baabla ni aasaka ni koowoso suoto di ɔfaafuu kamɛ yi, nkpo okle kafɔɔ dikpe ni bɛɛtakatɛsa ami, Otii Obi nwu nkpo katoo nɛ, alɛ otii lele niefũ mi eenu, aawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
“Diekye Yaa ntɛ ambɔmbɔ kayi ka mmle osie kanya, ni ɛɛyɔ Obi nɔɔ onwii nwu ɛɛta alɛ, otii lele niefũ nwɔ eenu, alaawɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ, aawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Diekye Yaa diekyesee Obi nɔɔ nwu alɛ abakanko batii kaayi ka mmle alo ma lɛpɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ alɛ diefe ni di Obi nɔɔ nwu suoto, batii kawɛ didiki.
“Batii ba niefũ Yaa Obi nwu beenu nii, Yaa dilaakanko ma alo ma lɛpɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ batii ba ninanfũ nwɔ banu nii, batookpi lɛpɔɔ kofokofoko, diekye baafũ Yaa Obi nwu nkpo onwii banu.
Lɛsaa le oso baakanko ma manlo ma ni lɛpɔɔ ninle alɛ, lɛkpa ntookye osi diɛwa kayi ka mmle kafɔɔ batii kɔbɔmbɔ ditunu manlenkee lɛkpa nwu nkpo, diekye ɔsaabla lɛma lɛbla dikpile.
Diekye otii lele nimbla sikpile yi, ankyidi lɛkpa nwu, nioso ánwa lɛkpa nwu nkpo nfũ, diekye ɔɔyɛkɛ alɛ nse ɛɛwa lɛkpa nwu nkpo nfũ yi, babadiki ɔsaabla nɔɔ kayi.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimbla ni lɛsaa di osuku kanya yi, anwa lɛkpa nwu nkpo nfũ alɛ, lɛkpa nwu nkpo kadiki nintuo alɛ nwaako, ambla asaa di Yaa dibiesaa kanya.” Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ Nwu Latakatɛsa Yesu Katoo.
Di nle mmle sɛmaa, Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasifi Yudea ntɛɛ nwu baalaawɛ ninfa obe owo aatookpeesa batii Yaa ntu.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yohane kafɔɔ lawɛ di Aenon wɔ niatɛɛtɛɛ ni Salim aatookpeesa batii Yaa ntu, diekye ntu lawɛ ninfa diapɔ.
Nioso batii kpinwu latɔɔkyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ ninfa aatookpeesa ma Yaa ntu.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, bayimufũ Yohane batɛ leeyo.
Dii ninwii ɔlaa ɔnanfi labuo di Yohane basaateketetɛ bawo ku Yuda otii onwii ntɛɛ di suoto ofoto ɔsaabla suoto.
Nkpo oso baakyɛ Yohane nfũ baalaakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, foonyuma osuɔtɔ wɔ niawɛ ni di ɔkyɛ lɛfɔ, faadiki nwɔ faatuo wo ni di Yordan okle kakyɛ nyɔɔfa?
Nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ nfɛ ookpeesa batii Yaa ntu, batii bamuu nfɛ kosifi ɔkyɛ nɔɔ!” Ninfɛ di Yohane ladiki kanya alɛ, “Otii kuonwii dilabafuo lɛsalɛsaa kuninwii ɔwɛ, nse diele Yaa niɛtɔɔ.
Aye bamu bionyuma bilɛ latɔkɔ ye nlɛ, ‘Diele ami ninle Kristo nwu nkpo, kafɔɔ ami yi, okyesee ko di Yaa lekyesee mi alɛ kale nwɔ katũ.’ Ɔkafɔɔsa ole ninle ɔkafɔɔsɔfɔ.
Kafɔɔ nse ɔkafɔɔsa siɛwo wɔ nin-yɛ ni di ɔlɔɔkɔ eenu ɔkafɔɔsa sɛlɔ yi, suoto n-yɔɔ nwɔ osie kanya.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ di amii, ntoonu nwɔ ni sɛlɔ, suoto lɛyɔɔ nii ntɔɔbla nimu nɛ.
Nioso, dikpe nii nnwɔɔ ɛɛtaka katoo, amii dikpe nii lɛwa kasɔ.
Otii Wɔ Niekye Osi Ɛɛwa Ni Nlenke Bamuu.
“Otii wɔ niekye osi ɛɛwa ni lɛtaka katoo alenke bamuu.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ niekye ni kasɔ ka mmle suoto, kasɔ ka mmle otii ko ale, kasɔ ka mmle suoto asaa kafɔɔ suoto lete ankakatɛ.
Otii wɔ niekye osi ɛɛwa ni nlenke asaa amuu.
Oobuɛ lɛsaa le ɛɛnya ni ku nle eenu nii, kafɔɔ otii kuonwii diefũ nwɔ ɔlaa anu.
Batii ba niefũ nwɔ ɔlaa beenu nii, kodiki mantuo klekle alɛ Yaa ɔlaa nte nkpo.
Otii wɔ di Yaa lekyesee ni kodiki Yaa ɔlaa ambuɛ, diekye Yaa lɛyɔ Ninwuna nɔɔ eekpee nwɔ kaamɛ pɔ.
Yaa mbɔmbɔ Obi nwu nkpo, ni ɛɛyɔ lɛsaa biala eekpe nwɔ di nnɛɛ kamɛ nɛ.
“Otii lele niefũ Obi nwu eenu, akpe nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niesĩ Obi nwu atoko ɔkyɔɔ dilabawɛ nkpa, ni Yaa letokonanfi kafɔɔ matika nwɔ di suoto.”
Yesu Lakakatɛko Samaria Ɔsanko Onwii.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, Farisi batii lanu alɛ Yesu nfɛ kokpeesa batii Yaa ntu, basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kafɔɔ nfɛ latɔɔpɔ baatoolenkee Yohane bale.
Nwaako baabuɛ nii, Yesu omu ditakpeesa otii kuonwii Yaa ntu, kafɔɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ niatookpeesa batii.
Nioso obe wɔ di Yesu lanu ɔlaa wɔ baatoobuɛ nii, ninfɛ aadie di Yudea kasɔ suoto aakple aasifi Galilea nɛ.
Di osuku nɔɔ nwu nkpo ɔkyɛ kamɛ, dikpe nii eefe di Samaria kasɔ suoto.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lalaadu Sikar wɔ ninle ni Samaria okpoo onwii kamɛ nɛ.
Okpoo nwu lɛtɛɛtɛɛ kasɔ ka di ɔwa lɛma Yakob layɔ aata ni obi nɔɔ Yosef.
Ntu dibiɔ le di Yakob lakutu ni late ninfa.
Obe wɔ di Yesu labadu ni ntu dibiɔ nwu nkpo nfa, ditoobuo nwɔ ni di osuku nwu nkpo ɔkyɛ kamɛ, aasiɛ ni di ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Diabla fɛ kakũ lefosi abombo anyɔ kamɛ.
Di obe nwu kamɛ Samaria ɔsanko onwii lawa alɛ ɔɔbadu ntu.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɛɛ ntu nnyi.” Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yesu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lafe okpoo alɛ bɔɔlaaya alesaa manwako.
Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be oso di afɔ Yuda otii fɔɔkaalɛ ami Samaria otii ntu?” Aakaalɛ nwɔ ɔlaa nwu nkpo diekye Yuda batii ku Samaria batii nimbla asaa anwii.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nse fɛ oye faye lɛsaa le di Yaa nta ni ku otii wɔ nikɔkaalɛ fɔ alɛ tɔɔ ntu anyi nii, nse bia afɔ nitɔbakaalɛ nwɔ, anta fɔ ntu be ninta ni nkpa.” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo labuɛ alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, ntu didusaa nnaafɔ, dibiɔ le mmle kafɔɔ lekyofo, ni ɔfɛ fabawɛ ntu be ninta ni nkpa fankyeko?
Ɔwa loo Yakob niakutu dibiɔ le mmle aata wo, nnwɔɔ omu ku babi ku banankyue nɔɔ lanyi ntu di dibiɔ le mmle kamɛ.
Obuɛ foobuɛ falɛ fɛɛtakakatoo falenke nwɔ ɛɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Otii lele nienyi ntu di dibiɔ le mmle kamɛ yi, otukɔnsɔ makple kunklee nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ otii lele nienyi ntu be kamatɔɔ ni yi, otukɔnsɔ dilabasinklee otii nwu nkpo diidii.
Ntu nwu nkpo kamatɔɔ ni makple ntu kataakɔ di kamɛ nɔɔ nintɔɔ nkpa ntu, nintɔɔ kafɔɔ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, ni tɛɛ ntu nwu nkpo nnwo, mmle okle di otukɔnsɔ dilabasinklee mi ni diidii.
Ni namasinwa nfũ mmle kafɔɔ nlɛ kamadu ntu.” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔɔkyɛ faalaalɛɛ ɔsa lɛfɔ biɛwa.” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Nnaa kɔsa.” Ni di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kute nkpo nse feebuɛ falɛ fanaa kɔsa.
Nwaako feebuɛ.
Diekye fatɔɔyɔ basa banɔɔ diɛbafe.
Bia minko nwɔ ninsi ni nunua wɔ mmle aale fɔ kɔsa kumu kumu.” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, ntɔɔnya nlɛ Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ fale!
Awo Samaria batii yi, buye bulɛ kobokote ko mmle suoto di bawa loo latoosumu Yaa.
Kafɔɔ aye Yuda batii biobuɛ bilɛ Yerusalem lete dikpe nii, beesumu Yaa.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔsanko, fũ ɔlaa wɔ mmle kɔtɔkɔ fɔ ni fanu.
Obe kɔwa batii bamuu dilabasinwakosa asi kasɔ bata Yaa di kobokote ko mmle suoto, ee Yerusalem.
Aye Samaria batii yi, bieye lɛsaa le biosumu nii.
Kafɔɔ awo Yuda batii yi, buye otii wɔ buosumu nii.
Diekye, didiki yi, awo Yuda batii kamɛ diekye.
Kafɔɔ obe kɔwa, obe nwu nkpo kafɔɔ ntoowo di batii ba ninsumu ni Yaa di osuku kanya, kamasumu Teete nwu di Yaa Ninwuna kamɛ ku nwaako ole kamɛ.
Diekye batii ba mmle okle di Yaa komiɛ alɛ batansɔɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yaa nle ni Ninwuna oso, dikpe ni batii ba nikosumu nwɔ nii, basumu nwɔ di Ninwuna kamɛ ku nwaako ole kamɛ.” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “N-ye nlɛ otii wɔ bɛɛpɛ ni ɔfɔɔ manlɛɛ ni Kristo kamawa.
Nse ɛɛwa yi, abatɔkɔ wo lɛsaa biala.” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ami wɔ mmle nikɔkakatɛko fɔ ni ninfũ mmle yi, ami ninle otii nwu nkpo nɛ.” Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, Yesu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakple, nioso diabla ɔkpɛ alɛ ɔɔkakatɛko ɔsanko nwu nkpo.
Kafɔɔ kuonwii lɛma ditafuo ɔsanko nwu ɔkaalɛ alɛ, “Be foomiɛ” ee bakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Be oso fɔɔkakatɛ ko nwɔ?” Ɔsanko nwu ladiɛ ditubukii nɔɔ nwu nkpo ninfa, aakple aasifi okpoo aalaatɔkɔ batii alɛ, “Biwa biɛbanyu otii wɔ niɛtɔkɔ mi ni lɛsaa biala ntooyibla lɛnya ni!
Sɛɛ nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo nwu nkpo?” Nkpo oso batii nwu nkpo ladie di okpoo nwu nkpo kamɛ baakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaanyu Yesu.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ kafɔɔ, Yesu basaateketetɛ latootikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, bale alesaa!” Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nkpe alesaa male ni, minanye nii.” Nkpo oso basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakye kasɔ baatɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Sɛɛ otii owo ntɔɔwako nwɔ alesaa awo eele?” Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Alesaa nii ninle alɛ kabla otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ dibiesaa, alɛ kaloo ɔkpɛ wɔ eekpee mi alɛ mabla ni ɔbla.
Aye nimbuɛ bilɛ, ‘Awɛntɛ ana kamaa, se ofiɛlɛbee ntoowo.’ Kafɔɔ kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bitakatɛsa anu bienyu kofe nwu nkpo, alesaa nwu nkpo ntɔɔsɛɛ, dikpe nii nfɛ manfiɛlɛ nya nii.
Otii wɔ nikofiɛlɛ ni yi, nnwɔɔ di Yaa nta koto, ansiisa alesaa nwu nkpo kafɔɔ anta nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo nɛ.
Nkpo oso otii wɔ nimpɛ ni ku otii wɔ ninfiɛlɛ nii yi, akyuu lɛma anyɔ manya suoto lɛyɔɔ osie kanya.
Nkpo oso ɔlaa nwu nkpo mambuɛ alɛ, ‘Otii onwii mpɛ, ɔbamba kafɔɔ nfiɛlɛ ni yi, kute nkpo.’ Ami yi, lekpee ye nlɛ, biakyɛ minaafiɛlɛ alesaa di nfũ minankpɛ dibuo ye nii.
Batii bamba lɛbla ɔkpɛ ninfa diebuo ma.
Kafɔɔ aye yi, biɔwɛ kowee di ɔkpɛ lɛma ɔbla kamɛ.” Batii Kpinwu Di Samaria Lafũ Yesu Baanu.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, Samaria batii kpinwu niakye ni okpoo nwu nkpo lafũ Yesu baanu.
Diekye ɔsanko nwu nkpo latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ɛɛtɔkɔ mi lɛsaa biala ntooyibla lɛnya nii.” Nioso obe wɔ di Samaria batii nwu nkpo lawa ni Yesu nfũ yi, baatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ asiɛ ma diɔkyɛ, nioso aasiɛ di ɔkyɛ lɛma ayi anyɔ.
Nioso batii bamba kpinwu lakple baafũ Yesu baanu, ta sɛlaa nɔɔ se aabuɛ ni oso.
Ni baatɔkɔ ɔsanko nwu alɛ, “Butoofũ buoonu nfɛ, diele di sɛlaa se fɛɛtɔkɔ wo ni oso, diekye awo bamu loo butoonu nwɔ ɔlaa, butootofo kafɔɔ bulɛ, nwaako nnwɔɔ ninle kayi ka mmle dikitɛ.” Yesu Layɔɔsa Abaa Ɔnɔɔfotii Onwii Obi Ofiɛ.
Di Yesu lale ni ayi anyɔ ninfa, ni aadie aasifi Galilea kasɔ suoto nɛ.
Nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ aabuɛ alɛ, “Mámbu Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ kuonwii di nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ okpoo.” Kafɔɔ obe wɔ di Yesu labuo ni Galilea, batii nwu ninfa lafũ nwɔ osie kanya, diekye obe wɔ baakyɛ ni Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii kalekɔ di Yerusalem yi, baanya asaa ya amuu aabla ni ninfa.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lakple aasifi Kana di Galilea kasɔ, di lɛba le ayɔ ntu aabla ni nta nɛ.
Abaa ɔnɔɔfotii onwii lawɛ ninfa di Kapernaum di obi nɔɔ suɔtɔbi latoofiɛ nii.
Obe wɔ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lanu alɛ Yesu ntookple di Yudea ɛɛwa ni Galilea, ni aakyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ aalaatikiti nwɔ lekoto alɛ awa abayɔɔsa obi nɔɔ nwu nkpo nikoloo ni okpi ofiɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nse biɛ́nya sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ ku atuosaa mínfũ bianu.” Ninfɛ di ɔnɔɔfotii nwu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, lekoto wa wla fabanyu obi nii nwu mmle okle anamakpi ni.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔɔkyɛ, obi lɛfɔ nwu nkpo mawɛ nkpa.” Ni di ɔnɔɔfotii nwu nkpo lafũ Yesu ɔlaa wɔ aatɔkɔ nwɔ ni aanu, ni aasifi nɛ.
Obe wɔ nfɛ akyɛ di osuku oosifi ni leyo, ni baakpɛntɛ nɔɔ lawa baabakyakako nwɔ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ obi lɛfɔ nwu nkpo ntɔɔtaka di ofiɛ.
Ninfɛ aakaalɛ ma alɛ ɔmɛmbe kamɛ aataka di ofiɛ?
Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Kɔsa kakũ olomu onwii kamɛ di lɛwɔɔfɔ ofiɛ nwu nkpo layɔɔ nwɔ.” Ninfɛ di obisɔ nwu nkpo ote lanyuma alɛ, di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ tutuutu di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Obi lɛfɔ nwu nkpo mawɛ nkpa.” Nkpo oso ɔnɔɔfotii wɔ mmle ku leyo nɔɔ kamɛ batii bamuu lafũ Yesu baanu.
Nle mmle niale ɔkpɛ wɔ niabla ni ɔkpɛ nyɔɔfa di Yesu labla ni di obe wɔ aakye Yudea aawa ni Galilea kasɔ nɛ.
Yesu Layɔɔsa Otii Onwii Ofiɛ Di Lɛpanta Ninwii Ɔlɔɔkɔ.
Nle mmle sɛmaa, Yesu lakple aakyɛ Yerusalem di obe wɔ di Yuda batii kole ni dii lɛma ninwii.
Di bafoso kayoko ɔlɔɔkɔ di Yerusalem, lɛpanta ninwii nte manlɛɛ ni Betesda di Hebri sele kamɛ.
Bɛɛpɛ akpanta anɔɔ beekyisa lɛpanta nwu nkpo.
Bafiɛtɛ ɔlambu kplɛ late di akpanta nwu nkpo kalɔ baale ni banumbiɛtɛ ku mba di nkpaa lɛma lekpi nii ku mba niekpi ni kakyɛkakyɛ.
Baate baasoko ntu nwu nkpo ɔbakaa.
(Diekye Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ onwii nwa amabakaa ntu nwu nkpo di obe obe.
Fiɛtɛ lele niɛkasa obuo di ntu nwu nkpo kamɛ di obe wɔ di Yaa tɔkyɛntɛ lɛbabakaa mi nii, ofiɛ lele kule, kunyɔɔ fiɛtɛ nwu nkpo.)
Osuɔtɔ onwii lawɛ ninfa aatoofiɛ ni alɛɛ afosi atiɛ alɛɛ anɛ amu.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lanyɔɔ nii, aatofo alɛ osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle ntoote diofiɛ diɛklɛ.
Nioso aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Foomiɛ falɛ ofiɛ lɛfɔ nwu nkpo kuyɔɔ fɔ?” Ninfɛ di fiɛtɛ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, otii kuonwii nnaa mi abakyakaakoe an-yɔ mi ankpee ni di lɛpanta nwu nkpo kamɛ nse bɛɛbakaa ntu nwu.
Nse kɔkpɛ nlɛ kanaabuo yi, otii bamba nle mi katũ, anka mi ɔlaabuo.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Taka!
Faayɔ ɔkla lɛfɔ, faakyɛ.” Nfanwu ofiɛ layɔɔ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo, aayɔ ɔkla nɔɔ, aakyako ɔkyɛ.
Dii le di ɔlaa wɔ mmle lawa nii, Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi diale.
Nkpo oso Yuda batii banɔɔfotii latɔkɔ osuɔtɔ nwu di Yesu layɔɔsa ni ofiɛ alɛ, “Miɛ Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi dile, kufiofa loo diɛta osuku alɛ faaklee ɔkla lɛfɔ.” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ niɛyɔɔsɛɛ ni ofiɛ niɛtɔkɔ mi alɛ n-yɔ ɔkla nii ninkyɛ.” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Owe ninle otii nwu niɛtɔkɔfɔ alɛ, ‘Yɔ ɔkla lɛfɔ faakyɛ ni’?” Kafɔɔ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo baayɔɔsa ni ofiɛ dieye otii wɔ di Yesu nle nii.
Diekye batii dikudi niawɛ ninfa nkpo, Yesu kafɔɔ ntooyu ma kaamɛ.
Di nni nkpo sɛmaa, Yesu lanya osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo di Yaa Olekatakɔ, ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nyu lo!
Nunua fatoosie nii, tansimbla okpile.
Nse diele nkpo, ni lɛsaa le ninlenke ni nle mmle nikamabla fɔ.” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lasifi aalaatɔkɔ Yuda batii banɔɔfotii nwu nkpo alɛ, Yesu ninle otii nwu nkpo niayɔɔsa nwɔ ni ofiɛ.
Nkpo oso Yuda batii nwu nkpo lakyako Yesu otikanko, diekye Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto aayɔɔsa nwɔ ofiɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Obe lele Teemi kɔbla ɔkpɛ, nkpo oso dikpe ni amii lɛbla.” Ɔlaa wɔ mmle aabuɛ ni lakple diata alɛ Yuda batii banɔɔfotii lamiɛ osie kanya alɛ boolo nwɔ.
Diele alɛ aataalɛ ni Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi kufiofa nwu nkpo lete oso, kafɔɔ aabuɛ alɛ Yaa ninle nwɔ Kote.
Ni nle mmle kotuo alɛ, oonyu suoto nɔɔ alɛ manko Yaa bakyɛkyɛ.
Yaa Lɛyɔ Osie Ɛɛta Obi Nwu Nkpo.
Nioso Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, Yaa Obi nwu dilaafuo lɛsalɛsaa ɔbla di nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ lɛsaa le ɛɛnya Ote kɔbla nii, nni ambla nɛ.
Diekye Ote nwu mbɔmbɔ Obi nwu.
Nioso lɛsaa lele di Ote nwu omu kɔbla, aantuo Obi nwu nimuu.
Abatuo nwɔ bia asaa kplɛ ya ninlenke ni n-ya mmle alɛ bamuu lee dibabla ye yaaa.
Fɛ mmle okle di Ote nwu nsɛnkɛsa bakpi anta ma ni nkpa yi, nkpo okle kafɔɔ di Obi nwu nta mba eediki ni nkpa nɛ.
Ote nwu nkpo omu nínkanko otii kuonwii.
Kafɔɔ ɛɛyɔ lɛkanko biala eekpee di Obi nwu nkpo nnɛɛ kamɛ niimu alɛ, batii bamuu kabu Obi nwu nkpo, fɛ mmle okle boobu ni Ote.
Otii lele ninambu Obi nwu nkpo yi, ni aambu Ote wɔ kafɔɔ niekyesee nwɔ nii.
“Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, otii lele nienu mi ɔlaa, eefũ otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ eenu yi, akpe nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Blabakanko nwɔ, kafɔɔ atoofe kuukpi kamɛ, eebuo nkpa fɔle nwu kamɛ kofokofoko.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye, obe kɔwa, obe nwu nkpo kafɔɔ ntɔɔwa kofokofoko di bakpi manu ni Yaa Obi nwu nkpo sɛlɔ, mba nimanu nii, mataka mansiɛ nkpa.
Fɛ mmle okle di Ote nwu nkpo omu ninle ni nkpa kataakɔ yi, nkpo okle kafɔɔ ɛɛbla Obi nɔɔ nwu alɛ aale nkpa kataakɔ nɛ.
Ɛɛtɔɔ osuku alɛ aakanko, diekye Otii Obi nwu ale.
“Bitanta nle mmle labla ye ɔkpɛ.
Diekye obe kɔwa di bakpi bamuu manu nwɔ ni sɛlɔ, mandie di sɛkya lɛma kamɛ.
Mba niɛbla ni dibiene mataka mansiɛ nkpa, mba kafɔɔ niɛbla ni sikpile babataka manfũ lɛpɔɔ olo.
Yohane Ladiki Yesu Kanya.
“Ninfuo lɛsalɛsaa kuninwii ɔbla di ami omu osie nii kamɛ.
Nkanko di mmle okle lete di Yaa lɛtɔkɔ mi ni kanya.
Nkpo oso lɛkanko nii lewo.
Diekye nimmbla nle ninlɛ mi nii, kafɔɔ nle ninlɛ ni otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ.
“Nse lediki suoto nii kanya yi, ni suoto nii kanya odiki nwu nkpo diewo nimu.
Kafɔɔ otii onwii nkpe oodiki mi ni suoto kanya, n-ye kafɔɔ nlɛ, kanya ka oodiki ni di suoto nii nte nkpo.
“Biekpee batii bɛɛkyɛ Yohane nfũ bɛɛlaakaalɛ nwɔ sɛlaa beekyeko suoto nii, ɛɛtɔkɔ ma kafɔɔ ɔlaa nwɔ ninte ni nkpo.
Diele kafɔɔ alɛ komiɛ otii kaayi ka mmle alɛ aadiki mi kanya.
Lebuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle alɛ biawɛ didiki.
Yohane late fɛ kandiɛ baasɔ aayila aatɔɔkpa nii, biatuna bilɛ biɔnya ni suoto lɛyɔɔ di lɛkpa nɔɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ di obe kakui kamɛ.
“Kafɔɔ ami yi, suoto kanya ka ninkpe mi kodiki ni lɛtaka katoo dilenke nka di Yohane ladiki nii.
Diekye sɛkpɛ se di Teemi lekpee mi ni di nnɛɛ kamɛ alɛ kabla nloo ni kɔbla ni kotuo alɛ, nnwɔɔ niekpee mi kɔtɔ.
Teemi wɔ kafɔɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ, nikodiki mi suoto kanya.
Diidii biinu nwɔ sɛlɔ ee binyɔɔ kafɔɔ anu ku anu.
Bieemufũ ɔlaa nɔɔ nwu nkpo kafɔɔ bikpee di situ lee kamɛ.
Diekye bieefũ otii wɔ eekpee ye ni binu.
Biotekete Kɔkpana Klekle Akũ kamɛ sɛlaa obe lele ku disibu bilɛ bibawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Kɔkpana nwu nkpo kafɔɔ kodiki mi suoto kanya.
Kafɔɔ biesĩ bilɛ bilɔɔwa ɔkyɛ nii alɛ kata ye nkpa.
“Noomiɛ batii kɔlɛɛ kaasɔ ka mmle suoto, diekye n-ye batii ba okle bile nii, n-ye kafɔɔ nlɛ binaa lɛbɔmbɔ biɛta Yaa di situ lee kamɛ.
Lɛwa di Teemi leyooto kamɛ kafɔɔ biefũ mi.
Kafɔɔ nse otii bamba lɛwa di leyooto nɔɔ nimu kamɛ yi, bibafukuti nnɛɛ lee minfũ nwɔ.
Lɛ dibabla fiɛ bibafuo mi ofũ onu, di obe wɔ biomiɛ kɔlɛɛ minkyeko ni aye bamu bawo nfũ, minoomiɛ kɔlɛɛ bikyeko ni nwɔ lete ninle ni Yaa nfũ?
“Bitanyu bilɛ ami ninle otii wɔ nimalo ye lɛpɔɔ nta ni Teemi.
Kafɔɔ Mose wɔ kufiofa bietika ni anu nimalo ye lɛpɔɔ!
Nse nwaako biefũ Mose bienu yi, nse bitabafũ mi kafɔɔ minnu, diekye ami suoto di Mose nwu nkpo lɛkpana asaa eekyeko.
Kafɔɔ di obe wɔ minanfũ lɛsaa le ɛɛkpana ni binu nii, lɛ dibabla fiɛ bibafũ sɛlaa se kobuɛ ni minnu?”
Yesu Lata Batii Nkpe Nnɔɔ Alesaa Baale Baamiɛ.
Di nni nkpo sɛmaa, Yesu lataalɛ lekpo le manlɛɛ ni Galilea lekpo, obe owo kafɔɔ manlɛɛ ni Tiberia lekpo aasifi kakyɛ nyɔɔfa.
Batii kpinwu latikanko nwɔ diekye baanya sɛkpɛ kplɛ se aabla aayɔɔsa ni mba niatoofiɛ ni sifiɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ layie baasifi kobokote osi baalaasiɛ kaasɔ ninfa.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ Yuda batii Okpi Diisi Ofe Dii ole bee ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ.
Obe wɔ di Yesu latakatɛsa anu aanyu aanya alɛ batii dikudi kpinwu kɔwa ni ɔkyɛ nɔɔ yi, ni aakaalɛ Filipo alɛ, “Ɔfɛ bubawɛ alesaa munya munta batii ba mmle nwu nkpo manle?” Yesu labuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle alɛ ɔɔyɔ ansɔ Filipo annyu, diekye nnwɔɔ omu aye lɛsaa le ɔwa ni ɔbabla.
Ninfɛ di Filipo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nse buɔyɔ bia batii alafa anyɔ dii kɔkpɛnto buɔɔya alesaa buɔta batii ba mmle nkpo bamuu yi, dilabawo ma bale bia kafui kafui!” Ninfɛ di Yesu tikankotɛ nɔɔ onwii kaamɛ lɛma ninle ni Andrea, Simon Petro obilɛma, labuɛ alɛ, “Okosopo onwii nsi ninfũ akle ni abloblo kudi anɔɔ ku kɔkpaku kɔnyɔ.
Kafɔɔ be di nle mmle mabla banankpantii ba mmle nwu nkpo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bita batii nwu nkpo bamuu basiɛ kaasɔ.” Sɛfa kɔɔnle lɛkɛtɛɛ kpinwu lawɛ ninfa.
Batii nwu nkpo bamuu lasiɛ kaasɔ.
Basuɔtɔ ba niawɛ ni kaamɛ lɛma labla fɛ batii nkpe nnɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu lafũ bloblo nwu nkpo, ni aapɛ Yaa sɛfa, ni aasɛ aata batii nwu nkpo bamuu niasiɛ ni ninfa nɛ.
Nkpo okle kafɔɔ aasɛ kɔkpaku nwu nkpo aata bamuu lɛma, obiala lawɛ aawee fɛ mmle okle oomiɛ nii.
Di obe wɔ bamuu lɛma batoole beemiɛ nii, Yesu latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bisiisa kɔkyɛɛkɔkyɛɛ nwu nkpo niebu ni alɛ kukanwii dilalalaa.” Nkpo oso baasiisa bloblo akudi anɔɔ nwu nkpo baatii nwu lale ni kɔkyɛɛkɔkyɛɛ nɔɔ kuayii lefosi nkyikyɛ nnyɔ pɔ.
Obe wɔ baatii nwu nkpo lanya ɔkpɛ wɔ mmle niabla ni ɔkpɛ di Yesu labla nii, baabuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako, nnya nwɔ mmle ninle Yaa Ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ wɔ nikɔwa ni kayi ka mmle nɛ.” Yesu latofo alɛ boomiɛ alɛ bamufũ nwɔ osie kanya bayɔ nwɔ base ɔka.
Nkpo oso aadie ma kaamɛ lete nɔɔ aakple aasifi abokote suoto.
Yesu Lakyɛ Di Ntu Osi.
Obe wɔ kɔɔtɔɔfɔ lawo nii, Yesu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lasoo baakyɛ lekpo kotoko.
Ninfɛ baayie baabuo di oklo kamɛ, baataalɛ baakple baakyɔɔ anu Kapernaum nɛ.
Kale laloo, kafɔɔ Yesu diikple awa ɔkyɛ lɛma.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, kofɛɛfɔ siene kunwii lakyako ɔfɛ, lekpo ntu nwu nkpo kafɔɔ lakyako ɔkpɛ osie kanya.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, basaateketetɛ nwu ntɔɔwa oklo di ntu nwu osi bɛɛkyɛ fɛ akɔ atiɛ diɔkyɛ ni di lɛɛnafa kamɛ, ni baanya Yesu nkyɛ di ntu osi ɔɔwa oklo nwu nfũ nɛ.
Nni nkpo oso, ɔfɔɔ lasifi ma!
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bitanyɛkɛ!
Ami dile.” Ni di otu lɛma late nɛ.
Ni baakpaa Yesu baakpee di oklo kamɛ nɛ.
Nfanwu, ni baadu nfũ boofe ni nɛ.
Batii Nwu Nkpo Lawolaa Yesu.
Obe wɔ kaale lasɛ nii, batii ba niasiɛ ni di lekpo nwu kakyɛ nyɔɔfa, baatofo alɛ oklo onwii niayila di lekpo nwu kotoko.
Baatofo kafɔɔ alɛ Yesu ditasiɛ di nwu nkpo kaamɛ aakyakaa ku basaateketetɛ nɔɔ fiɛ baayefe osuku.
Diekye basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lete niabuo nwu kaamɛ baasifi.
Di obe nwu kamɛ, seklo bamba se niakye ni Tiberia okpoo lawa siabayila di lekpo kotoko, di lɛba le niɛtɛɛtɛɛ ni nfũ baatii nwu nkpo lale ni bloblo di obe wɔ di Saate lapɛ ni Yaa sɛfa.
Nkpo oso, obe wɔ di batii nwu nkpo lanya alɛ Yesu ee basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nnaa ni ninfa oso, baabuo di seklo nwu nkpo kamɛ baasifi Kapernaum baalaatoowolaa nwɔ.
Yesu Ninle Alesaa Ya Ninta Ni Nkpa.
Obe wɔ baatii nwu lanya ni Yesu di lekpo nwu nkpo kakyɛ nyɔɔfa, ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, ɔmɛmbe fɛɛwa nfũ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bloblo wɔ lata ye biale biamiɛ ni oso biowolaa mi.
Diele sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ bianya labla ni kasɔ bienu ni oso.
Bitankpɛ biata alesaa ya nimalalaa nii, kafɔɔ bikpɛ bita alesaa ya ninkpe ɛɛta ni nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Nnya ninle alesaa ya di Otii Obi nwu kamata ye ni nɛ.
Diekye nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ di Yaa Ote lese lɛnɛɛ eediki ni nɛ.” Nioso batii nwu lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Ni be ninle lɛsaa le buabla ni diatuo alɛ buɔbla ni Yaa dibiesaa?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Lɛsaa le di Yaa komiɛ alɛ bibla ni ninle alɛ, biafũ otii wɔ eekyesee ni minnu.” Ninfɛ baakple baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be ninle ɔkpɛ wɔ niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ fababla fantuo alɛ buafũ fɔ munnu ni?
Nwu ninle ɔmɛnle?
Waawa loo anɛ lale alesaa ya manlɛɛ ni mana di ɔfaafuu kamɛ, fɛ mmle okle di Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ ni alɛ, ‘Aata ma alesaa ya niekye ni Osi baale.’ ” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, diele Mose niata ye alesaa ya niekye ni osi biale.
Kafɔɔ Teemi ninta ye alesaa amuamu ya niekye ni osi.
Diekye alesaa ya di Yaa lɛta ni ninle otii wɔ niekye osi ɛɛwa ni, ɔɔta ni batii kaayi nkpa.” Nkpo oso baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Saate, ta wo alesaa ya mmle nwu nkpo obe lele.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ami ninle alesaa nwu nkpo ninkpe ni nkpa nɛ.
Otii lele niɛwa ɔkyɛ nii, diidii kɔka dilabaklee nwɔ.
Otii lele kafɔɔ niefũ mi eenu, diidii otukɔnsɔ dilabaklee nwɔ.
Kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bitɔɔnyɛɛ, kafɔɔ biloofũ mi binu.
Otii lele di Teemi lɛyɔ ɛɛtɛɛ kamawa ɔkyɛ nii.
Olele kafɔɔ niɛwa ɔkyɛ nii namasĩ nwɔ diidii.
Diekye diele okye lekye osi lewa nlɛ kɔbabla ami omu dibiesaa.
Kafɔɔ ɔwa lɛwa nlɛ kɔbabla otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ dibiesaa.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ dibiesaa dile alɛ, batii ba bamuu ɛɛyɔ ɛɛtɛɛ nii, kuonwii lɛma dilaayu, kafɔɔ alɛ kasɛnkɛsa bamuu lɛma mansiɛ nkpa di dii yɛntɛle nwu nkpo suoto.
Diekye lɛsaa le di Teemi komiɛ ni ninle alɛ batii ba bamuu niɛnya ni Obi nwu, beefũ kafɔɔ beenu nii kawɛ nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Ni masɛnkɛsa ma mansiɛ nkpa di dii yɛntɛle nwu nkpo suoto.” Nfa nfɛ di Yuda batii nwu lakye kasɔ baatoonwununuu nwɔ di suoto nɛ, diekye aabuɛ alɛ, “Ami ninle alesaa ya niakye osi lawa ni nɛ.” Nkpo oso baakaalɛ alɛ, “Diele Yesu wɔ mmle ninle Yosef obi nwu nkpo nɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?
Buye nwɔ ote ku ɔya de!
Lɛ nfɛ diɛwa fiɛ oobuɛ alɛ nnwɔɔ niekye osi ɛɛwa?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bidiɛ ɔkakatɛ di kamɛ lee.
Otii kuonwii dilabafuo ɔkyɛ nii ɔwa diediki Teemi wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ niɛnanfi nwɔ ɛɛwako ɔkyɛ nii.
Alɛ ami kasɛnkɛsa nwɔ ansiɛ nkpa di dii yɛntɛle nwu nkpo suoto.
Yaa ɔlaa babuɛtɛtɛ onwii lɛkpana alɛ, ‘Yaa omu nimatuo batii bamuu asaa.’ Nkpo oso, otii lele niɛkyɔɔ Ote nwu nkpo atoko, eetekete asaa eekyeko ɔkyɛ nɔɔ, anwa ɔkyɛ nii.
Nle mmle dilootuo alɛ otii biala ntɔɔnya Ote nwu nkpo.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ niekye ni Yaa nfũ ninle otii wɔ lete nintɔɔnya ni Ote nwu.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii wɔ niefũ eenu nii, nkpe nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo.
Ami ninle alesaa ya ninta ni nkpa nɛ.
Waawa lee anɛ lale alesaa ya manlɛɛ ni mana di ɔfaafuu kamɛ, kafɔɔ baakpi.
Kafɔɔ alesaa ya niekye osi ɛɛwa nii nle n-ya okle alɛ otii lele niele nya, ɔlɔbakpi.
Ami ninle alesaa ya ninkpe ni nkpa niakye osi aawa ni nɛ.
Nse otii owo lele alesaa ya mmle, abasiɛ nkpa ninnaa ni kaloo.
Alesaa ya mmle ninle suoto nii sina nɛ.
Nsĩ kamayɔ nta alɛ kayi ka mmle batii kawɛ nkpa nɛ.” Nle mmle oso Yuda batii nwu nkpo lakye kasɔ baatɔɔnanfi ɔlaa osie kanya kaamɛ lɛma alɛ, “Lɛ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle mayɔ suoto sina nɔɔ anta wo alɛ bule?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, nse biele Otii Obi nwu suoto sina, binyi nwɔ ntɔ, ni bilabawɛ nkpa di kamɛ lee.
Otii lele niele suoto nii sina nwu, eenyi ntɔ nii nwu nkpo kafɔɔ, ni akpe nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo, ni kamasɛnkɛsa nwɔ ansiɛ nkpa di dii yɛntɛle nwu nkpo suoto.
Diekye suoto nii sina nwu nkpo ninle alesaa nwu amuamu, ntɔ nii nwu kafɔɔ ninle dinyinsaa nimunimu.
Otii lele niele mi suoto sina nwu eenyi mi ntɔ nwu kafɔɔ nsi mi kaamɛ, ami kafɔɔ nsi nwɔ kaamɛ.
Fɛ mmle okle di Teemi wɔ ninkpe ni nkpa lekpee mi ni kɔtɔ, di nnwɔɔ kamɛ nkpe ni nkpa oso yi, nkpo okle kafɔɔ di otii wɔ niele mi ni suoto sina kafɔɔ masiɛ nkpa ta ami oso nɛ.
Nya alesaa ya niakye osi aawa nii, aate fɛ nnyankpo okle di waawaa lee anɛ lale ni baakpi nii.
Nkpo oso otii lele niele alesaa ya mmle masiɛ nkpa ninnaa ni kaloo.” Asaa ya mmle di Yesu labuɛ aatuo asaa di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ di Kapernaum nɛ.
Yesu Labuɛ Sɛlaa Se Ninta Ni Nkpa Be Ninaa Ni Kaloo.
Obe wɔ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kpinwu lanu ni sɛlaa se mmle yi, baabuɛ alɛ, “Asaatuo ya mmle nkpe osie!
Owe nimafuo nya ofũ?” Otii kuonwii ditatɔkɔ Yesu ɔlaa kuonwii kafɔɔ aatofo alɛ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ latoonwununu di sɛlaa se mmle suoto.
Nioso aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Sɛlaa se mmle kototofo ye di atokoɛ?
Ni se diɛwa alɛ biɛɛnya Otii Obi nwu kokple ansifi osi di lɛba le aawɛ ni saa mɔ, ni lɛ dibate ye?
Lɛsaa le ninta ni nkpa ninle Yaa Ninwuna nɛ.
Otii osie nwu diesi di lɛsalɛsaa kuninwii kamɛ.
Sɛlaa se ntoobuɛ lɛta ye ni ninwako Yaa Ninwuna nkpa.
Kafɔɔ batii kpinwu kaamɛ lee diefũ banu.” Yesu labuɛ sɛlaa se mmle diekye kaasɔ kakyekɔ aatofo batii ba ninamafũ banu nii, ku otii wɔ nimadiki nwɔ anta nii.
Ninfɛ aakple aabuɛ alɛ, “Nle mmle oso latɔkɔ ye nlɛ otii kuonwii dilabafuo ɔkyɛ nii ɔwa diediki Ote nwu nkpo nietuo nwɔ osuku.” Nle mmle oso Yesu basaateketetɛ nɔɔ kpinwu lakple nkpaamaa, batasintuna alɛ bootikanko nwɔ.
Nkpo oso, Yesu lamunikĩi aakaalɛ batɔkyɛntɛ nɔɔ lefosi banyɔ nwu nkpo kafɔɔ alɛ, “Aye kafɔɔ biomiɛ bilɛ bikple nkpaamaa ɛɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?” Ninfɛ di Simon Petro ladiki kanya alɛ, “Saate, owe nfũ nfɛ buofe?
Afɔ ninkpe sɛlaa se ninta ni nkpa be ninnaa ni kaaloo.
Nunua, butoofũ buonu buɔnya kafɔɔ buɔtɛnsũ bulɛ afɔ ninle Otii Klekle wɔ niekye ni Yaa nfũ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ami niediki lefosi batii lee banyɔ, kafɔɔ onwii nle Abonsam kaamɛ lee.” Yesu latoobuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle di Yuda suoto, nnwɔɔ niale Simon Iskariot obi nɛ.
Diekye di lefosi batii banyɔ nwu nkpo kamɛ, nnwɔɔ niadiki Yesu aata nɛ.
Yesu Lakyɛ Yuda Batii Akpanta Kalɔ Osiɛ Ayi Kalekɔ.
Di nle mmle sɛmaa, Yesu lakyɛ aakyi di Galilea kasɔ suoto.
Atamiɛ alɛ ɔɔkyɛ ankyi di Yudea kasɔ suoto.
Diekye, Yuda banɔɔfotii latoomiɛ osuku alɛ boolo nwɔ.
Di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ, Yuda batii akpanta kalɔ osiɛ ayi ole bee ntɔɔtɛɛtɛɛ.
Nkpo oso Yesu babilɛma latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Die ninfũ faatɔɔkyɛ Yudea kasɔ suoto alɛ basaateketetɛ lɛfɔ kanya fɔ ɔsaabla.
Diekye otii kuonwii ninkookaa lɛsaa le ɔɔbla nii nse oomiɛ alɛ batii batofo nwɔ nwaa.
Di obe wɔ fɔɔbla ni aasaa ya mmle nwu nkpo okle yi, diki suoto fatuo kayi batii bamuu baatofo fɔ!” Baatɔkɔ nwɔ sɛlaa se mmle diekye babilɛma suɔtɔbi bamu ditafũ nwɔ baanu.
Nfa nfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Obe nii diiwo.
Kafɔɔ aye yi, obe lele nkaatɛko ye.
Diekye aye yi, kayi ka mmle batii dilabafuo ye okyidi.
Kafɔɔ ami yi, beekyidi mi, diekye kodiki ntɔkɔ ma klekle nlɛ ɔsaabla lɛma diɛɛlɛ.
Aye yi, bitɔɔkyɛ Ayi nwu nkpo kalekɔ.
Ami nɔɔwa nfa, diekye obe nii diiwo saa.” Obe wɔ aatɔkɔ ma nkpo okle aaloo ni yi, nnwɔɔ omu aakple aasiɛ di Galilea ninfa.
Obe wɔ di babilɛma suɔtɔbi ntoosifi ni ayi nwu nkpo kalekɔ beeloo ni yi, Yesu kafɔɔ lakyɛ, atakyɛ alɛ batii banyɔɔ kafɔɔ aakyɛ di lɛwofa kamɛ.
Yuda batii banɔɔfotii latowolaa nwɔ di ayi nwu nkpo kalekɔ baatɔɔkaalɛ alɛ, “Ɔfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo nkpe?” Batii latoobuɛ sɛwɛɛwɛɛ baakakatɛ kpinwu di Yesu suoto.
Batii bawo labuɛ alɛ, “Otii biene ale.” Batii bamba kafɔɔ labuɛ alɛ, “Oowo!
Otii kpile ale.
Ɔɔkyɔnkyɔ batii anfenko di osuku kpile suoto.” Kafɔɔ otii kuonwii ditafuo odiki obuɛ osie kanya diekye baatɔɔyɛkɛ Yuda batii banɔɔfotii.
Yesu Lakyɛ Aalaatuo Asaa Di Yuda Batii Olekatakɔ.
Obe wɔ nfɛ di ayi nwu nkpo ole nfɛ kodu ni ntɛɛ yi, Yesu lakyɛ Yuda batii Olekatakɔ aalaatuo batii asaa.
Asaa nɔɔ otuo labla Yuda batii banɔɔfotii ɔkpɛ, ni baakaalɛ alɛ, “Lɛ diɛbla fiɛ di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle n-ye lɛsaa nkpo okle, di obe wɔ anankyɛ ni asaa kateketekɔ kukanwii?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Asaa ya kotuo ni diele ami omu asaa otuo ale.
Kafɔɔ Yaa wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ ale ale.
Otii lele nikomiɛ alɛ abla Yaa dibiesaa matofo nse asaa ya kotuo ni Yaa nfũ eekye ee ami omu osie nii kamɛ lɛyɔ kɔkakatɛ.
Otii lele ninkakatɛ di nnwɔɔ omu osie nɔɔ kamɛ yi, ni oomiɛ alɛ ayɔ katansa ata nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ suoto.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nikomiɛ alɛ atansa ni otii wɔ niekpee nwɔ ni kɔtɔ yi, ambla asaa di osuku kanya, ni aanlaa kafɔɔ.
Diele Mose niayɔ kufiofa nwu nkpo aata ye, sɛɛ lɛ?
Kafɔɔ otii kuonwii kaamɛ lee diloole kufiofa nwu nkpo.
Ni be oso biomiɛ bilɛ biloe?” Ninfɛ di batii nwu nkpo latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Ninwuna kpile ninsi fɔ kaamɛ!
Owe nikomiɛ alɛ alo fɔ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Lɛsaa ninwii le lɛbla, ninfɛ diɛbla bamuu lee yaaa nɛ.
Mose lakpee ye kufiofa alɛ biabudi babi lee asɔkɔsɔkɔ.
Kafɔɔ diele nnwɔɔ niakye kasɔ, waawa lee anɛ niakye kasɔ bia saa obe kamɛ.
Kafɔɔ mimbudi babi lee asɔkɔsɔkɔ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto.
Ni nse mimbudi babi lee asɔkɔsɔkɔ di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto alɛ bilaataalɛ Mose kufiofa nwu nkpo, ni be oso biɔnyakee ɔblɔ ta lɛyɔɔsa ni otii ofiɛ diɛyɔɔ nwɔ ni di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi suoto?
Nse biɔkanko yi, bitannyu otii di anu biaka lɛka!
Kafɔɔ yi, bika di mmle di ɔlaa nwu nte ni.” Batii Lakaalɛ Baanu Nse Yesu Ninle Kristo Nwu.
Ninfɛ di batii ba bawo niakye ni Yerusalem okpoo, baakaalɛ alɛ, “Diele osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle di Yuda banɔɔfotii komiɛ alɛ balo ni nɛ?
Binyu!
Nnwɔɔ nin-yɛ di lɛkpaka ɔɔkakatɛ nɛ!
Otii kuonwii kafɔɔ dilɔɔkaalɛ nwɔ ɔlaa kuonwii!
Sɛɛ kamɛ ntɔɔkpa ma klekle nfɛ alɛ nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo nwu nkpo?
Kafɔɔ nse Kristo nwu nkpo lɛwa yi, otii kuonwii dilabatofo nfũ eekye nii.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ mmle nnwɔɔ bamuu loo buye nfũ eekye nii.” Di obe wɔ di Yesu latootuo ni asaa di Olekatakɔ nwu nkpo ninfa yi, aatakatɛsa sɛlɔ katoo aakaalɛ alɛ, “Obuɛ biobuɛ bilɛ biye mi, biye nfũ kafɔɔ lekye ni?
Diele ami omu osie nii kamɛ lɛwa!
Otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ ninlaa.
Aye bieye nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ ami n-ye nwɔ.
Diekye ɔkyɛ nɔɔ lekye, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ niekpee mi kɔtɔ.” Nle mmle oso, baamiɛ alɛ boomufũ nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ otii kuonwii ditafuo nwɔ ɔkpanko, diekye obe nɔɔ diiwo.
Kafɔɔ kaamɛ lɛma batii bawo kpinwu lafũ nwɔ baanu baatɔɔkaalɛ alɛ, “Ni nse Kristo nwu nkpo lɛwa, ababla sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ɔkpɛ silenke ni nse di otii wɔ mmle lɛbla ni?” Farisi Batii Lakpee Basaa Nyuntɛ Alɛ Blaamufũ Yesu.
Di obe wɔ di Farisi batii lanu ni sɛlaa se baatii kobuɛ ni di Yesu suoto oso yi, baabla onwii ku olebatatɛ banɔɔfo, baakpee asaa banyuntɛ alɛ bakyɛ blaamufũ Yesu.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Makple nsiɛ di ɔkyɛ lee di obe kakui kamɛ, nni kamaa se ntoosifi otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ nfũ.
Bibawolaa mi kafɔɔ bilɔbanyɛɛ, diekye lɛba le kamasiɛ nii, bilɔbafuo nfa ɔwa.” Ninfɛ di Yuda batii nwu lakaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Ɔfɛ di otii wɔ mmle kofe oso fiɛ, bulɔbanyɔɔ?
Sɛɛ abasifi Hela batii sekpoo di nfũ baatii loo nsi ni anaatuo Hela batii asaa?
Be alaka di obe wɔ eebuɛ alɛ ‘Bibawolaa mi, kafɔɔ bilɔbanyɛɛ.
Nfũ kafɔɔ kamasiɛ nii, bilabafuo nfa ɔwa?’ ” Yesu Lakakatɛ Di Ninwuna Klekle Suoto.
Dii yɛntɛle le di ayi nwu nkpo boole kamɛ, dile dii finle, Yesu lataka aayila aatakatɛsa sɛlɔ katoo aabuɛ alɛ, “Otii lele di otukɔnsɔ nkle, awa ɔkyɛ nii, abanyi ntu.
Fɛ mmle okle di Kɔkpana Klekle lebuɛ ni di otii wɔ niefũ mi eenu ni suoto alɛ, ‘Ntu be nikɔtaa ninansɔɔ ni diidii, ninta alɛ otii nsiɛ ni nkpa, ntu nwu nkpo kamatoobiɛ nintoofe di otu nɔɔ kamɛ.’ ” Yesu labuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle di Ninwuna le baatii ba niefũ nwɔ beenu ni kamafũ ni suoto.
Diekye di obe nwu nkpo kamɛ yi, bayiyɔ Ninwuna nwu nkpo bata.
Diekye Yesu diibuo di Sɛka ole nɔɔ nwu nkpo lɛkpa kamɛ.
Batii Dikudi Nwu Nkpo Lasɛ Ta Yesu Oso.
Obe wɔ baatii nwu nkpo lanu ni Yesu sɛlaa se mmle yi, bawo kaamɛ lɛma labuɛ alɛ, “Nwaako Yaa Ɔlaa Buɛtɛtɛ nwu nkpo ninle otii wɔ mmle.” Babamba kafɔɔ labuɛ alɛ, “Nnwɔɔ ninle Kristo nwu nɛ.” Bawo kafɔɔ labuɛ alɛ, “Kristo nwu nkpo diele Galilea abadie ankye!
Diekye Kɔkpana Klekle Kukũ lebuɛ alɛ, Kristo nwu nkpo Ɔka Dawid leyo kamɛ abakye.
Babalofo nwɔ di Betlehem, di okpoo wɔ di Dawid lasiɛ nii.” Ta Yesu oso, batii nwu nkpo lasɛ.
Bawo lamiɛ alɛ boomufũ nwɔ, kafɔɔ otii kuonwii ditafuo nwɔ ɔkpanko.
Yuda Batii Banɔɔfotii Ditafũ Yesu Baanu.
Obe wɔ di Basaanyuntɛ nwu nkpo lakple baasifi ni Farisi batii ku olebatatɛ banɔɔfo nwu nkpo nfũ yi, baakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obe oso minammufũ nwɔ biwako?” Ninfɛ di basaanyuntɛ nwu nkpo latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Diidii buunu otii kuonwii akakatɛ nwaa fɛ mmle okle di osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lɛkakatɛ nii!” Ninfɛ di Farisi batii nwu nkpo lakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Aye kafɔɔ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo lɛkyɔnkyɔ ye?
Bitoyinu ɔnɔɔfotii owo ee Farisi otii owo ntoyifũ nwɔ eenu?
Batii dikudi le mmle nimuu dieye Mose kufiofa nwu nkpo.
Nkpo oso lɛkpaani ntikanko ma!” Farisi otii wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Nikodemo nintoyikyɛ ni Yesu nfũ lasiɛ ma kaamɛ, ninfɛ aakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Kufiofa loo lɛta osuku alɛ baalo otii lɛpɔɔ di obe wɔ manayilɛɛ nwɔ banu nwɔ ni kanya kamɛ ɔlaa di lɛsaa le ɛɛbla ni suoto?” Ninfɛ ninnwɔɔ kafɔɔ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ kafɔɔ Galilea feekye ɛɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?
Buo diakũ kamɛ fanyu!
Fabanya falɛ Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ kuonwii dilabakye Galilea awa diidii.” (Ninfɛ di obiala lɛma lasifi ayo lɛma nɛ.)
Baamufũ Ɔsanko Onwii Niadie Ni Ɔsa Kamaa Baawako Yesu Nfũ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu nnwɔɔ aasifi kobokote ko manlɛɛ ni Nnɔnyi Awoso Kobokote osi.
Obe wɔ kaale lasɛ ni ku kuyitatũ yi, Yesu lakple aasifi Yuda batii Olekatakɔ.
Ninfɛ di batii nwu nkpo bamuu lawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ babasiɛ baamana nwɔ baakyi, ni aasiɛ kaasɔ aakyako ma asaa otuo nɛ.
Ninfɛ di kufiofa asaa batuotɛ ku Farisi batii lakpaa ɔsanko onwii baamufũ oodie ni ɔsa kamaa nnɛɛ nnɛɛ baawako babase nwɔ di bamuu lɛma anu nɛ.
Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, buomufũ ɔsanko wɔ mmle nnɛɛ nnɛɛ osuɔtɔ bamba kotenko nwɔ.
Di kufiofa loo kanya yi, Mose lɛta wo osuku alɛ dikpe ni buasafɔ ɔsanko wɔ mmle okle afuɔ munlo.
Ni lɛ di afɔ foobuɛ?” Baakaalɛ Yesu ɔlaa wɔ mmle alɛ bɔɔyɔ manwolaa nwɔ kaanya mmle okle baalo nwɔ ni lɛpɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ ninfɛ aawa kasɔ aayɔ lɛnɛɛ nɔɔ aakyako asaa ɔkpana kaasɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ baayila ninfa bɔɔkaalɛ nwɔ ni akaalɛ yi, ninfɛ aatakatɛsa suoto aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Olele kaamɛ lee ninayibla okpile diidii yi, aaka nwɔ difuɔ oyu ɔsafɔ.” Ninfɛ aakple aawa kasɔ aayɔ lɛnɛɛ nɔɔ aakyako asaa ɔkpana kaasɔ nɛ.
Obe wɔ baanɔɔfo nwu nkpo lanu ni ɔlaa nwu yi, ni baakyako osifi onwii onwii fɛ mmle okle balekatũ batika ni nɛ.
Ni diabu Yesu ku ɔsanko nwu lete ninfa nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu latakatɛsa suoto, ni aakaalɛ ɔsanko nwu alɛ, “Ɔsanko, fɛ baatii nwu nkpo ntoofe?
Kuonwii lɛma diebu aalo fɔ ni lɛpɔɔ?” Ninfɛ di ɔsanko nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, oowo lo!” Nkpo oso, Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Nii ni ami kafɔɔ, noolo fɔ lɛpɔɔ.
Nioso, tɔɔkyɛ.
Kafɔɔ, taasinkple faalaasiɛ faatɔɔbla sikpile.” Yesu Ninle Kayi Ka Mmle Lɛkpa.
Di nni nkpo sɛmaa, Yesu lakple aabuɛ aatɔkɔ batii nwu nkpo alɛ, “Ami ninle kayi ka mmle lɛkpa.
Otii lele nietikanko mi, abawɛ lɛkpa le ninta ni nkpa.
Diidii kafɔɔ ɔlɔbakyɛ di ditunu kamɛ.” Ninfɛ di Farisi batii nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ omu lɛfɔ nikodiki suoto kanya.
Nkpo oso suoto lɛfɔ kanya odiki nwu nkpo diedie lɛsalɛsaa.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kuntɛ kodiki suoto kanya yi, suoto nii kanya nwu kodiki ni nte nkpo.
Diekye n-ye nfũ lekye nii, n-ye nfũ kafɔɔ kofe nii.
Aye bieye nfũ lekye nii, ee nfũ kofe nii.
Aye yi, sitiinyu kanya minkanko.
Kafɔɔ ami yi, ninkanko otii kuonwii.
Nse bia nlɛ kɔkanko yi, lɛkanko nii ntabakyɛ di osuku kanya.
Diekye diele lete nii ninkanko.
Teemi wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ, munko nwɔ ninkanko nɛ.
Bɛɛkpana di kufiofa lee kamɛ alɛ, nse batii banyɔ kanya nkaatɛ di ɔlaa owo suoto yi, ni ɔlaa nwu nte nkpo.
Ami yi, ndiki suoto nii kanya.
Teemi wɔ kafɔɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ kafɔɔ ndiki mi suoto kanya.” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Ɔfɛ di Teefɔ nwu nkpo nkpe?” Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Bieye mi.
Bieye Teemi kafɔɔ.
Diekye nse oye biye mi yi, nse bitabatofo Teemi kafɔɔ.” Yesu labuɛ sɛlaa se mmle di obe wɔ ootuo ni asaa di Yaa Olekatakɔ di lɛba le niɛtɛɛtɛɛ ni nfũ manta ni koto.
Kafɔɔ otii kuonwii ditafuo nwɔ omufũ diekye obe nɔɔ diiwo.
Yesu Latɔkɔ Yuda Banɔɔfotii Alɛ Bilabafuo Lɛba Le Kofe Ni Ɔkyɛ.
Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ami yi, kamasifi.
Bibawolaa mi, kafɔɔ bibakpi di sikple lee kamɛ.
Lɛba le kafɔɔ kofe nii bilabafuo nfa ɔwa.” Nioso Yuda batii banɔɔfotii lakaalɛ alɛ, “Suoto oofe olo oso oobuɛ alɛ, ‘Bilabafuo lɛba le kofe ni ɔwa’?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Aye yi, kasɔ ka mmle suoto biekye.
Kafɔɔ ami yi, osi lekye lɛwa.
Aye yi, kayi ka mmle batii bile.
Kafɔɔ ami yi, diele kayi ka mmle otii nle.
Nioso latɔkɔ ye nlɛ, bibakpi di sikpile lee kamɛ nɛ.
Nse biefũ binu bilɛ nle otii wɔ nnle nii, nwaako bibakpi di sikpile lee kamɛ.” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Owe fale?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Lɛsaa le lɛtɔkɔ ye kaasɔ kakyekɔ nlɛ nle ni yi, nni nwu kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ nle nɛ.
Nkpe sɛlaa kpinwu kabuɛ di suoto lee nlo ye ni lɛpɔɔ ta nkpa lee oso fiɛ.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɛ ninlaa.
Nioso ɔlaa wɔ lenu lekye ko ni ɔkyɛ nɔɔ yi, nwu lete lɛkya koyie nta kayi batii nɛ.” Batanu kasɔ alɛ Yesu yi, Ote suoto aatɔɔkakatɛ aatɔɔta ma.
Nioso aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Obe wɔ bibatakatɛsa ni Otii Obi nwu katoo yi, obe nwu nkpo bibatofo bilɛ ami ninle otii wɔ lebuɛ nlɛ nnle ni nɛ.
Nimbla lɛsalɛsaa kafɔɔ di ami omu osie nii kamɛ.
Lɛsaa le kafɔɔ di Teemi lekpeemi alɛ mbuɛ nii, nni nimbuɛ nɛ.
Otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ kafɔɔ nsikoe.
Aadiɛ mi lete, diekye obe lele mbla lɛsaa le nimbuo nwɔ ni anu.” Obe wɔ di Yesu labuɛ ni sɛlaa se mmle okle oso yi, batii kpinwu lafũ nwɔ baanu.
Yesu Ladiki Aatuo Batii Ba Ninle Ni Abraham Babi.
Nkpo oso Yesu latɔkɔ Yuda batii ba niafũ nwɔ baanu ni alɛ, “Nse biemufũ asaa otuo nii bieklee, ni nwaako basaateketetɛ nii bile.
Ni bibatofo nwaako ɔlaa nwu, ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo mata ye minwɛ kayaa.” Ninfɛ baatii nwu latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Abraham banantii bule, diidii kafɔɔ buukple otii kuonwii ɔlanle.
Ni be oso foobuɛ falɛ bubawɛ kayaa?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, otii lele nikɔbla okpile yi, ale ɔlanle ɛɛta okpile.
Ɔlanle nínle saate nɔɔ atesaa.
Kafɔɔ obi ninle ote atesaa obe lele.
Nkpo oso nse Yaa Obi nwu lɛtafɔ kayaa yi, ni fɛɛwɛ kayaa kamu kamu.
N-ye nlɛ Abraham banantii bile.
Kafɔɔ biomiɛ bilɛ bilo mi, diekye biloofũ asaa otuo nii ya kotuo ye ni binu.
Lɛsaa le di Teemi letuo mi ni yi, nni suoto kɔkakatɛ nɛ.
Aye kafɔɔ lɛsaa le di teeye lɛtɔkɔ ye ni yi, nni biɔbla nɛ.” Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Abraham ninle wo kote.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nse nwaako Abraham babi bile yi, bitababla asaa fɛ mmle okle aabla nii.
Kafɔɔ ami wɔ nikɔtɔkɔ ye ni nwaako ɔlaa nwu lenu lekyeko ni Yaa nfũ yi, ami biomiɛ bilɛ bilo nɛ.
Abraham ditabla nle mmle okle.
Asaa ya di teeye omu labla nii, nnya biɔbla nɛ.” Ninfɛ baatɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Buole basɔnɔbi.
Kote kunwii ninkpe wo, nkũ ninle Yaa nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nse nwaako Yaa ninle ye Kote yi, nse bitababɔmbɔ mi, diekye Yaa nfũ lekye lɛwa.
Ninwa ku ami omu osie, nnwɔɔ niekyesee mi.
Be oso minoonu lesaa le kobuɛ ni kasɔ?
Diekye ɔlaa nii kototofo ye di atoko.
Diekye teeye ninle Abonsam, nioso biomiɛ bilɛ bitikanko teeye dibiesaa nɛ.
Diayɔ ni bia kaasɔ kakyekɔ, batii lotɛ ale.
Diidii kafɔɔ ayitikanko onukwale, diekye onukwale diesi nwɔ kaamɛ.
Nse ɛɛlaa kafɔɔ nkpa nɔɔ letembi oodiki kayi antuo, diekye laatɛ ale.
Nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ ninle balaatɛ bamuu kote nɛ.
Ta ami kobuɛ ni onukwale oso, nkpo oso minoofũ mi binu nɛ.
Owe lee nkafuo mi okpile lɛpɔɔ olo?
Ni nse kobuɛ onukwale mɔ, be oso minoofũ mi binu?
Otii wɔ niekye ni Yaa nfũ yi, ankyɔɔ Yaa ɔlaa atoko.
Kafɔɔ, aye minankye ni Yaa nfũ oso yi, minkyɔɔ nwɔ ɔlaa atoko.” Yesu Ladiki Suoto Kanya Aata Yuda Batii.
Ninfɛ di Yuda batii nwu lakaalɛ Yesu alɛ, “Nse buobuɛ bulɛ Samaria otii fale, mmia kafɔɔ ninwuna kpile nsi fɔ kaamɛ, diele nwaako ɔlaa kule?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ninwuna kpile diesi mi kaamɛ.
Ami kɔyɔ dibu nta Teemi, kafɔɔ aye biɔlalaasa mi leyooto.
Noomiɛ dibu nta suoto.
Kafɔɔ otii onwii nkpe oomiɛ ni antɛɛ nii, nnwɔɔ kafɔɔ ninkanko di osuku kanya nɛ.
Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye, otii lele niɛkyɔɔ mi asaa otuo atoko dilabakpi diidii!” Ninfɛ di Yuda batii nwu nkpo latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Mia nfɛ butootofo nwaako bulɛ, ninwuna kpile ninsi fɔ nɛ.
Diekye Abraham lakpi, Yaa kanya badikitɛ kafɔɔ lakpi, kafɔɔ foobuɛ falɛ, otii lele niɛkyɔɔ fɔ asaa otuo atoko dilabakpi diidii!
Teewo Abraham lakpi, ni obuɛ foobuɛ falɛ fɛɛtaka katoo falenke nwɔ?
Yaa kanya badikitɛ kafɔɔ lakpi.
Ni ɔmɛntii okle foonyu falɛ fale?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nse nlɛ kɔtansa suoto yi, suoto nii ɔtansa nwu nkpo dilabadie lɛsalɛsaa.
Teemi ninle otii wɔ nikɔtansɛɛ nii, otii wɔ biobuɛ bilɛ nnwɔɔ ninle ye ni Yaa.
Mmia kafɔɔ bieye nwɔ.
Kafɔɔ ami n-ye nwɔ.
Nse lebuɛ nlɛ ninye nwɔ yi, ni ntookple laatɛ fɛle aye.
N-ye nwɔ, kɔkyɔɔ nwɔ kafɔɔ ɔlaa atoko.
Teeye Abraham lanya suoto lɛyɔɔ alɛ abanya ɔwabee nii.
Aanya nwu kafɔɔ, suoto layɔɔ nwɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yuda batii latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Fayifũ alɛɛ afosi anɔɔ, ni obuɛ foobuɛ falɛ fatɔɔnya Abraham nɛ?” Nfa nfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, fiɛ babalofo ni Abraham, ami nfɛ nkpe.” Obe wɔ aatɔkɔ ma ni ɔlaa nwu nkpo, ninfɛ baatii nwu nkpo layɔ afuɔ alɛ bɔɔsafɔ nwɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Yesu lawofasa suoto, ni aadie di Yaa Olekatakɔ nwu kamɛ ninfa aasifi nɛ.
Yesu Latikiti Numbiɛtɛ Anu.
Obe onwii kamɛ di Yesu lakyɛ aatoofe nii, aakyakako osuɔtɔ onwii niabiɛ ni anu, diayɔ ni bia kalofokɔ nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ lakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, owe niabla okpile oso beelofo osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle numbiɛtɛ?
Nnwɔɔ omu nɔɔ okpile kule ɛɛ, sɛɛ balofotɛ nɔɔ niabla okpile?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle anu ya niebiɛ nwɔ ni yi, diele nnwɔɔ niabla okpile ee balofotɛ nɔɔ niabla ni okpile oso.
Kafɔɔ eebiɛ anu alɛ baadiki Yaa osie mantuo batii diefe ni di suoto nɔɔ.
Di obe wɔ kaale diiloo nii, dikpe nii, buɔbla otii wɔ niekpee mi ni kɔtɔ ɔkpɛ.
Diekye kale kɔwa ɔbaloo di otii kuonwii dilabasinfuo ni ɔkpɛ ɔbla.
Di obe wɔ lɛnya nkpe ni kaayi ka mmle, ami ninle kayi ka mmle lɛkpa.” Obe wɔ di Yesu labuɛ nkpo aaloo nii, ni aatufa sita aakpete kaasɔ aanwɔtɔ kɔtɛ, ni aayɔ kɔtɛ nwu nkpo aafifia di osuɔtɔ nwu anu nɛ.
Ni aatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Tɔɔkyɛ falaafoto anu di lɛpanta le bɔɔlɛɛ ni Siloa kamɛ.” Siloa lɛsɔdiki ninle alɛ beekpee nwɔ.
Nkpo oso osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle lasifi aalaafoto anu.
Aapɛ aakple aawa nii, nfɛ ɔɔnya.
Ninfɛ di basiɛwo nɔɔ ku mba ninyɔɔ ansiɛ antɔɔkaalɛ ni asaa, latɔɔkaalɛ bawo alɛ, “Diele osuɔtɔ wɔ mmle ninsiɛ antɔɔkaalɛ ni asaa nɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?” Bawo labuɛ alɛ nnwɔɔ dile.
Bawo kafɔɔ labuɛ alɛ, “Oowo, diele nnwɔɔ dile.
Otii niedie nwɔ.” Nkpo oso, osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo omu labuɛ alɛ, “Ami dile!” Ninfɛ baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛ diɛwa fiɛ nfɛ fɔɔnya?” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Osuɔtɔ wɔ bɔɔlɛɛ ni Yesu nianwɔtɔ kɔtɛ aafifia mi di anu, ni aatɔkɔ mi alɛ, ntɔɔkyɛ Siloa ninaafoto anu, ninfɛ lasifi nɛ.
Lalaaloo ni anu ofoto, ni lakyako ɔnya nɛ.” Ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Ɔfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo nkpe?” Ni aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ninye.” Farisi Batii Lakaalɛ Numbiɛtɛ Nwu Alɛ Lɛ Diɛbla Fiɛ Nfɛ Ɔɔnya.
Ninfɛ baatii nwu lakpaa osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo di anu labiɛ ni baakyɛnko Farisi batii nfũ nɛ.
Dii le di Yesu lanwɔtɔ kɔtɛ aafifia ni di osuɔtɔ nwu anu aatikiti ni yi, Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi diale.
Nkpo oso Farisi batii kafɔɔ baakaalɛ osuɔtɔ nwu mmle diɛwa fiɛ nfɛ ɔɔnya nii.
Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Kɔtɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu lanwɔtɔ aafifia mi di anu ni lalaafoto anu nɛ.
Ni lɛkyako ɔnya nɛ.” Ninfɛ di Farisi batii nwu bawo labuɛ alɛ, “Otii wɔ niabla ni lɛsaa le mmle yi, diele Yaa nfũ eekye.
Diekye aabla di Lɛnyɛɛtɛyi kufiofa suoto.” Ninfɛ di bawo kafɔɔ labuɛ alɛ, “Kafɔɔ lɛ di kpile blatɛ kafuo sɛkpɛ se niɛbla ni ɔkpɛ ɔbla otuo?” Ninfɛ kaasɛ labuo di batii nwu nkpo ntɛɛ.
Nioso Farisi batii nwu lakple baakaalɛ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo alɛ, “Foobuɛ falɛ nnwɔɔ nietikiti fɔ ni anu, ni lɛ foobuɛ di suoto nɔɔ?” Ninfɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Yaa ɔlaa buɛtɛtɛ ale.” Bia nle Yuda batii nwu ditafuo ofũ onu alɛ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo numbiɛtɛ aale fiɛ atookple ɔɔnya, dialaase di obe wɔ baalɛɛ balofotɛ nɔɔ.
Ninfɛ baakaalɛ ma alɛ, “Obi lee ninle nwɔ nɛ?
Nnwɔɔ bilɛ bielofo ni numbiɛtɛ nɛ?
Ni lɛ diɛbla fiɛ nfɛ ɔɔnya?” Ninfɛ di balofotɛ nɔɔ ladiki kanya alɛ, “Buye bulɛ obi loo ale, buolofo ni numbiɛtɛ.
Kafɔɔ mmle diɛbla fiɛ nfɛ ɔɔnya nii, buoye.
Otii wɔ kafɔɔ nietikiti nwɔ ni anu yi, buoye nwɔ.
Nioso bikaalɛ nwɔ, atoomuɔ aafuo ni suoto kanya odiki!” Balofotɛ nwu labuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle diekye baatɔɔyɛkɛ Yuda batii banɔɔfotii nwu nkpo.
Diekye baabuɛ baatɛ alɛ otii lele niediki eebuɛ ku kanya nɔɔ alɛ Yesu ninle Kristo nwu nkpo yi, babadiki nwɔ di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ nwu.
Nkpo oso di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo balofotɛ nɔɔ lababuɛ alɛ, “Atoomuɔ aafuo ni suoto kanya odiki, bikaalɛ nwɔ.” Banɔɔfotii nwu lakple baalɛɛ osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo baalofo ni numbiɛtɛ lɛnyɔɔfa, baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ka di Yaa falɛ bababuɛ nwaako!
Awo buye bulɛ kpile blatɛ ninle otii wɔ nietikitifɔ ni anu!” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Kpile blatɛ ale woo, aale kpile blatɛ woo, ninye.
Lɛsaa le lete n-ye ni ninle alɛ, saa, anu labiɛ mi, kafɔɔ nunua nfɛ kɔnya!” Ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Be aablafɔ?
Lɛ aabla fiɛ aatikiti fɔ anu?” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ntɔɔtɔkɔ ye kofokofoko kafɔɔ biloonu.
Be oso biomiɛ bilɛ nkple ntɔkɔ ye?
Sɛɛ ayee biomiɛ bilɛ bikple nwɔ basaateketetɛ?” Ninfɛ di banɔɔfotii nwu nkpo lakpaani osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo baatɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Afɔ ko nikale nwɔ saateketetɛ.
Awo yi, Mose basaateketetɛ bule.
Buye bulɛ Yaa lakakatɛ aata Mose.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ mmle, buoye bia nfũ eekye nii!” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu ladiki kanya aabuɛ alɛ, “Ɔmɛnlaa ninle nwɔ?
Bieye nfũ eekye nii, kafɔɔ nnwɔɔ nietikiti mi anu nɛ!
Buye bulɛ Yaa ninkyɔɔ bakpileblatɛ atoko.
Kafɔɔ batii ba ninkyɔɔ nwɔ ni ɔlaa atoko mambla nwɔ ni dibiesaa, mma ankyɔɔ atoko nɛ.
Diɛyɔ ni kaayi ka mmle kasɔ kakyekɔ, diidii buunu bulɛ otii kuonwii letikiti otii wɔ beelofo ni numbiɛtɛ anu.
Nse otii wɔ mmle diele Yaa nfũ eekye, alaafuo lɛsalɛsaa le mmle ɔbla.” Ninfɛ di banɔɔfotii nwu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Beelofofɔ di sikpile kamɛ feemuɔ!
Afɔ nikomiɛ falɛ fatuo wo asaa ɛɛ, sɛɛ lɛ?” Ninfɛ baadiki nwɔ di Yuda batii kasiisakɔ nwu nɛ.
Batii Bawo Konyu Alɛ Bɔɔnya Asaa Klekle.
Yesu lanu alɛ baadiki osuɔtɔ nwu di kasiisakɔ lɛma kamɛ.
Nioso, aanyɔɔ nii, ni aakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Feefũ Otii Obi nwu feenu?” Ninfɛ di osuɔtɔ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Ɔnɔɔfo, tɔkɔ mi otiikle wɔ ale ni, mmle okle kafũ nwɔ nnu ni.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Fatɔɔnyɔɔ kofokofoko.
Nnwɔɔ ninle otii wɔ nikɔkakatɛkofɔ ni nɛ.” Ni di osuɔtɔ nwu labuɛ alɛ, “Saate, lefũ lenu!” Ninfɛ aapɛ akunkyi di Yesu katũ aatansa nwɔ nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu labuɛ alɛ, “Lɛwa kayi ka mmle nlɛ kɔmakanko alɛ, batii ba di anu lebiɛ ni ka-nya.
Alɛ mba nikɔnya ni kafɔɔ anu kabiɛ ma.” Farisi batii ba niawɛ ni ninfa lanu ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu labuɛ nii, ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Beeye!
Awo kafɔɔ banumbiɛtɛ bule?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Nse banumbiɛtɛ bile yi, se biekpi lɛpɔɔ.
Kafɔɔ di obe wɔ biobuɛ bilɛ biɔnya ni kamaa, biekpi lɛpɔɔ.”
Bafoso Kpatɛ Biene Nlolaa Bafoso Annyu.
Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, otii lele ninanfe di kayoko abuo lefosoyo nwu nkpo kamɛ, eeyie di kɔba nwu suoto eebuo yi, yu ku asaa lalaasatɛ ale.
Kafɔɔ otii wɔ nimafe ni di kayoko nwu nkpo ambuo nii, nnwɔɔ ninle bafoso nwu kpatɛ omu nɛ.
Kayoko nyuntɛ nsɛkɛtɛ kayoko antɔɔ.
Bafoso nwu nkpo nnu nwɔ sɛlɔ.
Nse ɛɛlɛɛ ma ku leyooto le eetika ma nii, ankpaa ma andieko.
Nse ɛɛkpaa ma eedieko yi, anleko ma katũ, bafoso nwu nkpo ntikanko nwɔ, diekye baye nwɔ sɛlɔ.
Blɔbatikanko otii bamba, babatoso nwɔ, diekye baaye nwɔ sɛlɔ.” Yesu lapɛ ma lɛkpa le mmle, kafɔɔ batanu lɛsaa le aatɔkɔ ma ni kasɔ.
Yesu Ninle Bafoso Kpatɛ Biene Nwu.
Nkpo oso Yesu lakple aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Nwaako kɔtɔkɔ ye nlɛ, ami ninle kayoko nwu nkpo lɛta bafoso nwu nɛ.
Batii ba bamuu niale mi katũ baawa nii, bayu ku asaa balalaasatɛ baale.
Nkpo oso bafoso nwu nkpo ditanu ma sɛlɔ.
Ami ninle kayoko nwu nkpo.
Otii lele niefe di suoto nii eebuo, abawɛ nkpa.
Ababuo andie, anwɛ alesaa biene kalekɔ.
Yu nnwɔɔ ɔwa anwa amayu, anlo, anlalasa asaa.
Kafɔɔ ami ɔwa lɛwa nlɛ batii kawɛ nkpa, nkpa be niewo ni niimu kamɛ.
“Ami ninle bafosokpatɛ biene nwu letuna nlɛ kokpi ni baafoso nwu nkpo disi nɛ.
Otii wɔ beefũ kooto kanya ɔɔkpa ni bafoso, baafoso nwu nkpo diele nnwɔɔ omu bale oso, nse ɛɛnya ɔkplɛle kɔwa yi, antoso andiɛ bafoso nwu nkpo.
Nkpo oso, ɔkplɛle nwu mmufũ bafoso nwu nkpo, ansamiisa ma ta aale ni bafoso nwu nkpo kpatɛ omu omu oso.
Otii wɔ mmle ntoso ansifi, diekye koto kanya beefũ nwɔ ɔɔbla ɔkpɛ nwu nkpo.
Diekye bafoso nwu nkpo ɔlaa dietika nwɔ di otu.
-“Ami ninle bafosokpatɛ biene nwu.
Fɛ mmle okle di Teete n-ye mi, di ami kafɔɔ n-ye nwɔ nii, nkpo okle kafɔɔ n-ye bafoso nii, mma kafɔɔ baye mi nɛ.
Ni letuna nlɛ kokpi diisi lɛma nɛ.
Bafoso bamba nkpe bale mi ni bale manansi ni di bafoso kɔba ko mmle kamɛ.
Dikpe ni lɛkpaa ma lɛwako bɛɛbanu mi sɛlɔ, bamuu lɛma beekple bafoso banwii, beesiɛ di bafosokpatɛ onwii kalɔ.
“Teete mbɔmbɔ mi, diekye letuna nlɛ kɔyɔ nkpa nii nta, sɛmaa, ninkple nfũ mi.
Diele otii kuonwii niefũ mi nkpa ninnɛɛ, kafɔɔ ami omu nietuna nlɛ kɔyɔ nta.
Nwaako, nkpe osuku n-yɔ nkpa nii nta, nkpe osuku kafɔɔ nkple nfũ mi.
Nle mmle di Teemi lekpee mi alɛ mbla nɛ.” Yesu sɛlaa se mmle aabuɛ ni oso, kasɛ lakple kaabuo di Yuda batii ntɛɛ.
Batii kpinwu kaamɛ lɛma latoobuɛ alɛ, “Ninwuna kpile ninsi nwɔ kaamɛ.
Oobuo afĩi kafɔɔ!
Be oso nfɛ buakple munyila muntɔɔkyɔɔ nwɔ atoko?” Kafɔɔ batii bamba latoobuɛ alɛ, “Otii wɔ di ninwuna kpile nsi nii, dilaafuo ɔkakatɛ fɛ mmle!
Lɛ nfɛ di ninwuna kpile mafuo ɔta alɛ numbiɛtɛ nnya?” Yuda Batii Lasĩ Yesu Ofũ Onu.
Yuda batii latoole dii lɛma le manlɛɛ ni Olekatakɔ Okleklesa Dii, baatɔɔta Yaa di Yerusalem.
Lɛwɔɔfɔ obe kamɛ diale.
Ni di Yesu lakyɛ aatoofe di Yaa Olekatakɔ lɛba le bɔɔlɛɛ ni Salomo ablalakyi nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yuda batii labamana nwɔ baakyi, ni baakaalɛ nwɔ alɛ, “Lɛ oso feediɛ wo buobu diisi nkpo?
Tɔkɔ wo!
Kubio afɔ ninle Kristo nwu nkpo?” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ntɔɔtɔkɔ ye ɔlaa wɔ mmle kofokofoko, kafɔɔ biloofũ mi binu.
Asaa ya kɔbla nfe ni di Teemi osie kamɛ kodiki mi suoto kanya fiɛ.
Kafɔɔ biloofũ binu, diekye biekye bafoso nii nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Bafoso nii nnu mi sɛlɔ.
N-ye ma, mma kafɔɔ batikankoe.
Nioso lɛta ma nkpa be ninnaa ni kaloo, blɔbawɔɔ diidii.
Kuonwii kafɔɔ dilabafuo ma ɔkpafɛ ofũ mi ninnɛɛ kamɛ.
Teemi niɛyɔ ma eekpee mi di nnɛɛ kamɛ, eemuɔ kafɔɔ alenke lɛsaa biala.
Kuonwii kafɔɔ dilabafuo ma ɔkpafɛ ofũ di Teete nnɛɛ kamɛ diidii.
Ami ku Teete, onwii bule.” Ninfɛ di Yuda batii nwu nkpo lakple baayɔ afuɔ alɛ bɔɔsafɔ Yesu nɛ.
Ninfɛ di Yesu labuɛ aatɔkɔ ma alɛ, “Ntɔɔbla sɛkpɛ biene kpinwu di anu lee letuo ye, nse di Teete lekpee mi alɛ mbla nii.
Ɔmɛnle suoto oso biomiɛ bilɛ bisafɔ mi afuɔ?” Ninfɛ di Yuda batii nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Buloomiɛ bulɛ busafɔ fɔ afuɔ di ɔkpɛ biene kuonwii suoto, kafɔɔ mbusuo ɔlaa wɔ feebuɛ ni oso!
Diekye otii ko fale kafɔɔ fɔɔbla suoto falɛ Yaa fale!” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Bɛɛkpana di kufiofa lee Kukũ kamɛ alɛ, Yaa lebuɛ alɛ, ‘Bite fɛ Yaa.’ Buye kafɔɔ bulɛ, ɔlaa wɔ Kɔɔkpana Klekle lebuɛ nii, kute nkpo obe lele.
Yaa kafɔɔ lalɛɛ batii ba niafũ ni ɔlaa biene nwu alɛ, ‘Bite fɛ Yaa.’ Kafɔɔ ami yi, Teete niediki mi eekpee mi kayi ka mmle.
Ni be oso nfɛ buobuɛ bilɛ, lebuɛ mbusuo ɔlaa ta lebuɛ nlɛ Yaa Obi nle?
Nse diele lɛsaa le di Teemi komiɛ alɛ mbla ni kɔbla yi, ni bitanfũ mi bianu.
Kafɔɔ nse nni kɔbla yi, kuntɛ biefũ mi binu yi, ni biefũ sɛkpɛ se kɔbla ni binu.
Ni bibatofo, minnu kasɔ kafɔɔ bilɛ, Teete nwu nkpo nsi mi kaamɛ, ami kafɔɔ nsi nwɔ kaamɛ.” Yuda batii nwu nkpo lamiɛ alɛ bookple mammufũ Yesu, kafɔɔ aadie ma kaamɛ aasifi.
Ni di Yesu lasifi aakple aalaataalɛ Yordan okle, aasifi lɛba le di Yohane Yaa Ntu Kpeesatɛ latookpeesa ni batii Yaa ntu saa, aalaasiɛ ninfa.
Batii kpinwu lawa ɔkyɛ nɔɔ bababuɛ alɛ, “Yohane ditabla ɔkpɛ wɔ niabla ni ɔkpɛ kuonwii aatuo.
Kafɔɔ sɛlaa se simuu aabuɛ ni di otii wɔ mmle suoto lɛwa kaanya nkpo.” Ninfɛ baatii kpinwu lafũ Yesu baanu ninfa nɛ.
Lasaro Lakpi.
Osuɔtɔ onwii baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Lasaro lakye okpoo wɔ baatɔɔlɛɛ ni Betania, latoofiɛ.
Babilɛma sankobi banyɔ banwii niale ni Maria ku Marta kafɔɔ lasiɛ di okpoo nwu nkpo kamɛ.
Maria wɔ mmle niale otii wɔ niayɔ nɔnyi kɔnɔnkɔnɔ aakpete ni di Saate nkpaatũ aayɔ disi sinwini nɔɔ aasunsũ ni nɛ.
Obilɛma suɔtɔbi niale Lasaro wɔ niatoofiɛ ni nɛ.
Babilɛma sankobi nwu nkpo latika Yesu kanya alɛ, “Saate, siɛwo lɛfɔ bɔmbɔtɛ kofiɛ.” Obe wɔ di Yesu lanu ni kanya ka mmle, aabuɛ alɛ, “Lasaro ofiɛ wɔ mmle dilabale nwɔ kukpi kaloo.
Kafɔɔ nle mmle lɛwa kaanya alɛ baayɔ mantakatɛsaa Yaa leyooto katoo.
Diefe ni di nle mmle kamɛ kafɔɔ, baayɔ mantakatɛsa Yaa Obi nwu nkpo katoo.” Yesu labɔmbɔ Marta ku obilɛma sankobi ku Lasaro osie kanya.
Kafɔɔ aafũ kanya alɛ Lasaro kofiɛ nii, aasiɛ ninfũ aawɛ ni ayi anyɔ aakyakaa.
Nni nkpo sɛmaa, ni aatɔkɔ basaateketetɛ nɔɔ alɛ, “Bita bukple busifi Yudea nfɛ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ nwu nkpo ladiki kanya alɛ, “Saatuotɛ, kɔsanklo ko mmle di Yuda batii nwu nkpo ninfa lamiɛ alɛ bɔɔsafɔ fɔ afuɔ!
Ni fookple fammiɛ falɛ fɔɔkyɛ nfa nɛ?” Ninfɛ di Yesu ladiki kanya alɛ, “Diele lefosi ambombo anyɔ ninsi di dii kufĩ kamɛ?
Nse otii nkyɛ di dii kamɛ diɛkpa ni oso yi, ántuula.
Diekye kayi lɛkpa ntɔɔ antɔɔnya.
Kafɔɔ nse akyɛ ku kakyɛ yi, antuula.
Diekye, lɛkpa nsinnaa.” Obe wɔ di Yesu labuɛ ɔlaa wɔ mmle aaloo nii, aakple aabuɛ aakyakaa alɛ, “Siɛwo loo Lasaro kɔkyɔsĩi, kafɔɔ makyɛ naasɛnkɛsa nwɔ.” Ninfɛ di basaateketetɛ nɔɔ ladiki kanya alɛ, “Saate, nse ɔkyɔsĩi ɔɔkyɔsĩi yi, ni dibayɔɔ nwɔ.” Ɔlaa wɔ di Yesu latobuɛ ninle alɛ Lasaro ntookpi, kafɔɔ basaateketetɛ lanyu alɛ sɛkyɔsĩ fukuti suoto aatɔɔkakatɛ.
Nioso Yesu latɔkɔ ma aatikiti alɛ, “Lasaro ntookpi.
Kafɔɔ, aye oso, dilɛ alɛ ntawɛ ninfa fiɛ aakpi, ta mmle okle biafũ mi minnu nii.
Bita bukyɛ ɔkyɛ nɔɔ.” Ninfɛ di Toma wɔ bɔɔlɛɛni Lɛtabi latɔkɔ basaateketetɛ wo nɔɔ alɛ, “Bita awo kafɔɔ bukyɛ ku Saatuotɛ buɔlaakpi ku nnwɔɔ.” Yesu Ninle Ɔtaka Okye Baakpi Kamɛ Saate.
Obe wɔ di Yesu lakyɛ aalaabuo nii, aanu alɛ dii nwu nkpo niale dii naafa baakookaa ni Lasaro nɛ.
Diedie ni di Betania diesifi ni Yerusalem, ditakyo.
Lekyo kate fɛ akɔ anyɔ.
Nioso Yuda batii kpinwu lakyɛ alɛ bɔɔlaakpee Maria ku Marta kɔnɛɛ kaafutu, ta obilɛma suɔtɔbi nwu nkpo kukpi oso.
Obe wɔ di Marta lanu alɛ Yesu nfɛ kɔwa nii, ni aadie aalaakyako nwɔ nɛ.
Kafɔɔ Maria lasiɛ leeyo.
Ninfɛ di Marta latɔkɔ Yesu alɛ, “Saate, nse fɛ faanwɛ ninfũ se obiloo diekpi!
Kafɔɔ bia nle n-ye nlɛ, lɛsaa lele fɛɛkaalɛ Yaa, ababla anta fɔ.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Obilee mataka ansiɛ nkpa.” Ninfɛ di Marta ladiki kanya alɛ, “N-ye nlɛ abakple antaka di obe wɔ baakpi makple mantaka ni di Dii Yɛntɛle nwu nkpo suoto.” Ninfɛ di Yesu latɔkɔ nwɔ alɛ, “Ami ninle otii wɔ nintakatɛsa ni baakpi nta ma ni nkpa nɛ.
Otii lele niefũ mi eenu, kuntɛ eekpi, abasiɛ nkpa.
Otii lele kafɔɔ ninkpe nkpa eefũ mi eenu yi, diidii kafɔɔ ɔlɔbakpi.
Feefũ nle mmle feenu?” Obe wɔ di Yesu lakaalɛ nwɔ ni nkpo, ni di Marta ladiki kanya alɛ, “Yii, Saate, lefũ lenu nlɛ afɔ ninle Kristo, Yaa Obi wɔ beebuɛ bɛɛtɛ ni kofokofoko alɛ abawa ni kayi nɛ.” Yesu Lawi Kaku.
